| `Line 1:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2: ||१ महाभारते आदिपर्वम् ||` | "The First Book [Ādi Parva] of the Mahābhārata" |
| `Line 3:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5: अनुक्रमणीपर्व` | "The Chapter of Contents [Index section]" |
| `Line 6: १` | "1" |
| `Line 7:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 8:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 9: नारायणं नमस्कृत्य नरं चैव नरोत्तमम् |` | "Having bowed to Nārāyaṇa [Supreme deity] and also to Nara [divine sage], the best among men," |
| `Line 10: देवीं सरस्वतीं चैव ततो जयमुदीरयेत् ||०||` | "And to the goddess Sarasvatī [learning deity], then one should recite the Jaya [Victory epic]." |
| `Line 11:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 12: लोमहर्षणपुत्र उग्रश्रवाः सूतः पौराणिको नैमिषारण्ये शौनकस्य कुलपतेर्द्वादशवार्षिके सत्रे | ००१ |` | "Ugraśravās [fierce-eared], the son of Lomaharṣaṇa, a sūta [bard-chronicler], a reciter of ancient tales, came to the twelve-year sacrificial session of Śaunaka, the family head, in the Naimiṣa forest." |
| `Line 13:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 14: समासीनानभ्यगच्छद्ब्रह्मर्षीन्संशितव्रतान् |` | "He approached the Brahmarṣis [Brahmin sages] of strict vows who were seated together," |
| `Line 15: विनयावनतो भूत्वा कदाचित्सूतनन्दनः ||२||` | "The son of the sūta [bard], having bowed with humility, at one time." |
| `Line 16:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 17: तमाश्रममनुप्राप्तं नैमिषारण्यवासिनः |` | "The dwellers of the Naimiṣa forest [sacred grove], upon his arrival at the hermitage," |
| `Line 18: चित्राः श्रोतुं कथास्तत्र परिवव्रुस्तपस्विनः ||३||` | "The ascetics surrounded him there to hear wonderful stories." |
| `Line 19:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 20: अभिवाद्य मुनींस्तांस्तु सर्वानेव कृताञ्जलिः |` | "Having saluted all those sages with folded hands," |
| `Line 21: अपृच्छत्स तपोवृद्धिं सद्भिश्चैवाभिनन्दितः ||४||` | "He inquired about the progress of their austerities, and was welcomed by the virtuous ones." |
| `Line 22:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 23: अथ तेषूपविष्टेषु सर्वेष्वेव तपस्विषु |` | "Then, when all those ascetics were seated," |
| `Line 24: निर्दिष्टमासनं भेजे विनयाल्लोमहर्षणिः ||५||` | "The son of Lomaharṣaṇa [sūta] humbly took the seat assigned to him." |
| `Line 25:` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 26: सुखासीनं ततस्तं तु विश्रान्तमुपलक्ष्य च |` | "Then, observing him seated comfortably and rested," |
| `Line 27: अथापृच्छदृषिस्तत्र कश्चित्प्रस्तावयन्कथाः ||६||` | "A certain sage there asked him, initiating conversations. ||6||" |
| `Line 28: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 29: कुत आगम्यते सौते क्व चायं विहृतस्त्वया |` | "From where do you come, O Sūta [bard/narrator], and where have you spent your time," |
| `Line 30: कालः कमलपत्राक्ष शंसैतत्पृच्छतो मम ||७||` | "O lotus-eyed one, tell this to me who asks. ||7||" |
| `Line 31: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 32: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 33: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 34: जनमेजयस्य राजर्षेः सर्पसत्रे महात्मनः |` | "At the snake sacrifice of Janamejaya, the royal sage [rājarṣi] of great soul," |
| `Line 35: समीपे पार्थिवेन्द्रस्य सम्यक्पारिक्षितस्य च ||८||` | "In the presence of that lord of the earth, the worthy son of Parikshit. ||8||" |
| `Line 36: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 37: कृष्णद्वैपायनप्रोक्ताः सुपुण्या विविधाः कथाः |` | "Various most sacred stories narrated by Krishna Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa]," |
| `Line 38: कथिताश्चापि विधिवद्या वैशम्पायनेन वै ||९||` | "Were properly recited by Vaiśampāyana indeed. ||9||" |
| `Line 39: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 40: श्रुत्वाहं ता विचित्रार्था महाभारतसंश्रिताः |` | "Having heard those stories of wonderful meanings contained in the Mahābhārata," |
| `Line 41: बहूनि सम्परिक्रम्य तीर्थान्यायतनानि च ||१०||` | "And having visited many holy places [tīrthas] and temples, ||10||" |
| `Line 42: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 43: समन्तपञ्चकं नाम पुण्यं द्विजनिषेवितम् |` | "I went to that sacred place called Samantapañcaka [five lakes region], frequented by the twice-born [Brahmins]," |
| `Line 44: गतवानस्मि तं देशं युद्धं यत्राभवत्पुरा ||११||` | "That region where the battle took place long ago, ||11||" |
| `Line 45: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 46: पाण्डवानां कुरूणां च सर्वेषां च महीक्षिताम् ||११||` | "Between the Pāṇḍavas, the Kurus, and all the rulers of the earth. ||11||" |
| `Line 47: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 48: दिदृक्षुरागतस्तस्मात्समीपं भवतामिह |` | "Desiring to see you, I have come here from that place to your presence," |
| `Line 49: आयुष्मन्तः सर्व एव ब्रह्मभूता हि मे मताः ||१२||` | "Long-lived ones, all of you are indeed regarded by me as embodiments of Brahman [divine knowledge]. ||12||" |
| `Line 50: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 51: अस्मिन्यज्ञे महाभागाः सूर्यपावकवर्चसः |` | "In this sacrifice, the fortunate ones, with radiance like the sun and fire," |
| `Line 52: कृताभिषेकाः शुचयः कृतजप्या हुताग्नयः ||१३||` | "Having performed ablutions, pure, having completed prayers, having offered oblations to fire. ||13||" |
| `Line 53: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 54: भवन्त आसते स्वस्था ब्रवीमि किमहं द्विजाः ||१३||` | "You all are seated comfortably; what shall I speak, O twice-born [Brahmins]? ||13||" |
| `Line 55: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 56: पुराणसंश्रिताः पुण्याः कथा वा धर्मसंश्रिताः |` | "Stories based on the Puranas [ancient texts], virtuous tales based on dharma [righteousness]," |
| `Line 57: इतिवृत्तं नरेन्द्राणामृषीणां च महात्मनाम् ||१४||` | "Or the histories of kings and great-souled sages? ||14||" |
| `Line 58: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 59: ऋषय ऊचुः||` | "The sages said:" |
| `Line 60: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 61: द्वैपायनेन यत्प्रोक्तं पुराणं परमर्षिणा |` | "That which was narrated by Dvaipayana [Vyasa], the great sage," |
| `Line 62: सुरैर्ब्रह्मर्षिभिश्चैव श्रुत्वा यदभिपूजितम् ||१५||` | "Which, having heard, was revered by gods and brahmarshis [sage-seers]. ||15||" |
| `Line 63: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 64: तस्याख्यानवरिष्ठस्य विचित्रपदपर्वणः |` | "Of that most excellent narrative with its wonderful chapters and sections," |
| `Line 65: सूक्ष्मार्थन्याययुक्तस्य वेदार्थैर्भूषितस्य च ||१६||` | "Endowed with subtle meanings and logic, adorned with Vedic meanings. ||16||" |
| `Line 66: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 67: भारतस्येतिहासस्य पुण्यां ग्रन्थार्थसंयुताम् |` | "Of the Bharata [Mahabharata], the sacred history, complete with textual meaning," |
| `Line 68: संस्कारोपगतां ब्राह्मीं नानाशास्त्रोपबृंहिताम् ||१७||` | "Refined, divine, enriched with various scriptures. ||17||" |
| `Line 69: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 70: जनमेजयस्य यां राज्ञो वैशम्पायन उक्तवान् |` | "Which Vaishampayana narrated to King Janamejaya," |
| `Line 71: यथावत्स ऋषिस्तुष्ट्या सत्रे द्वैपायनाज्ञया ||१८||` | "That sage, properly, with joy, during the sacrifice, by the command of Dvaipayana [Vyasa]. ||18||" |
| `Line 72: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 73: वेदैश्चतुर्भिः समितां व्यासस्याद्भुतकर्मणः |` | "Harmonized with the four Vedas, of Vyasa of wonderful deeds," |
| `Line 74: संहितां श्रोतुमिच्छामो धर्म्यां पापभयापहाम् ||१९||` | "We wish to hear that compilation, righteous and removing the fear of sin. ||19||" |
| `Line 75: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 76: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 77: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 78: आद्यं पुरुषमीशानं पुरुहूतं पुरुष्टुतम् |` | "The primeval Person [Purusha], the Lord, the much-invoked, the much-praised," |
| `Line 79: ऋतमेकाक्षरं ब्रह्म व्यक्ताव्यक्तं सनातनम् ||२०||` | "The Truth, the one-syllabled Brahman [Absolute], the manifest and unmanifest, the eternal. ||20||" |
| `Line 80: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 81: असच्च सच्चैव च यद्विश्वं सदसतः परम् |` | "He who is both non-existence and existence, the universe, beyond both being and non-being," |
| `Line 82: परावराणां स्रष्टारं पुराणं परमव्ययम् ||२१||` | "The creator of the high and low, the ancient, the supreme and imperishable. ||21||" |
| `Line 83: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 84: मङ्गल्यं मङ्गलं विष्णुं वरेण्यमनघं शुचिम् |` | "The auspicious, the blessed Vishnu [all-pervading deity], the most excellent, the sinless, the pure," |
| `Line 85: नमस्कृत्य हृषीकेशं चराचरगुरुं हरिम् ||२२||` | "Having bowed to Hrishikesha [lord of senses], the teacher of the moving and unmoving, Hari [remover of obstacles]. ||22||" |
| `Line 86: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 87: महर्षेः पूजितस्येह सर्वलोके महात्मनः |` | "Of the great sage who is worshipped in this world, the great-souled one," |
| `Line 88: प्रवक्ष्यामि मतं कृत्स्नं व्यासस्यामिततेजसः ||२३||` | "I shall declare the complete doctrine of Vyāsa [compiler of Vedas] of immeasurable splendor. ||23||" |
| `Line 89: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 90: आचख्युः कवयः केचित्सम्प्रत्याचक्षते परे |` | "Some poets have narrated it, others are narrating it now," |
| `Line 91: आख्यास्यन्ति तथैवान्ये इतिहासमिमं भुवि ||२४||` | "And others will likewise narrate this history [itihāsa] on earth. ||24||" |
| `Line 92: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 93: इदं तु त्रिषु लोकेषु महज्ज्ञानं प्रतिष्ठितम् |` | "This great knowledge is established in the three worlds [triloka]," |
| `Line 94: विस्तरैश्च समासैश्च धार्यते यद्द्विजातिभिः ||२५||` | "Which is preserved by the twice-born [Brahmins] in detailed and condensed forms. ||25||" |
| `Line 95: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 96: अलङ्कृतं शुभैः शब्दैः समयैर्दिव्यमानुषैः |` | "Adorned with auspicious words, with divine and human conventions," |
| `Line 97: छन्दोवृत्तैश्च विविधैरन्वितं विदुषां प्रियम् ||२६||` | "Composed in various meters [chandas], dear to the learned. ||26||" |
| `Line 98: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 99: निष्प्रभेऽस्मिन्निरालोके सर्वतस्तमसावृते |` | "When this (universe) was without light, without illumination, covered with darkness on all sides," |
| `Line 100: बृहदण्डमभूदेकं प्रजानां बीजमक्षयम् ||२७||` | "There was one great cosmic egg [Brahmanda], the imperishable seed of all creatures. ||27||" |
| `Line 101: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 102: युगस्यादौ निमित्तं तन्महद्दिव्यं प्रचक्षते |` | "At the beginning of a yuga [cosmic age], they declare that great divine cause," |
| `Line 103: यस्मिंस्तच्छ्रूयते सत्यं ज्योतिर्ब्रह्म सनातनम् ||२८||` | "In which is heard that truth, the luminous eternal Brahman [absolute reality]. ||28||" |
| `Line 104: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 105: अद्भुतं चाप्यचिन्त्यं च सर्वत्र समतां गतम् |` | "Wondrous and inconceivable, having reached equality everywhere," |
| `Line 106: अव्यक्तं कारणं सूक्ष्मं यत्तत्सदसदात्मकम् ||२९||` | "The unmanifest, subtle cause, which is the essence of both being and non-being. ||29||" |
| `Line 107: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 108: यस्मात्पितामहो जज्ञे प्रभुरेकः प्रजापतिः |` | "From which was born the grandfather [Brahma], the one lord, Prajapati [lord of creatures]," |
| `Line 109: ब्रह्मा सुरगुरुः स्थाणुर्मनुः कः परमेष्ठ्यथ ||३०||` | "Brahma, the preceptor of gods, Sthanu [Shiva], Manu, Ka [Prajapati], and Paramesthi [supreme one]. ||30||" |
| `Line 110: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 111: प्राचेतसस्तथा दक्षो दक्षपुत्राश्च सप्त ये |` | "Then Prachetasa Daksha and his seven sons," |
| `Line 112: ततः प्रजानां पतयः प्राभवन्नेकविंशतिः ||३१||` | "From them arose twenty-one lords of creatures [Prajapatis]. ||31||" |
| `Line 113: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 114: पुरुषश्चाप्रमेयात्मा यं सर्वमृषयो विदुः |` | "And the Purusha [cosmic being] of immeasurable nature, whom all sages know," |
| `Line 115: विश्वेदेवास्तथादित्या वसवोऽथाश्विनावपि ||३२||` | "The Vishvedevas [universal gods], the Adityas [solar deities], the Vasus [elemental gods], and also the two Ashvins [divine physicians]. ||32||" |
| `Line 116: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 117: यक्षाः साध्याः पिशाचाश्च गुह्यकाः पितरस्तथा |` | "The Yakshas [wealth spirits], Sadhyas [celestial beings], Pisachas [fiends], Guhyakas [hidden beings], and also the Pitris [ancestors]," |
| `Line 118: ततः प्रसूता विद्वांसः शिष्टा ब्रह्मर्षयोऽमलाः ||३३||` | "Then were born the learned ones, the distinguished, pure Brahmarshis [sage-seers]. ||33||" |
| `Line 119: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 120: राजर्षयश्च बहवः सर्वैः समुदिता गुणैः |` | "And many Rajarshis [royal sages] endowed with all excellent qualities," |
| `Line 121: आपो द्यौः पृथिवी वायुरन्तरिक्षं दिशस्तथा ||३४||` | "Water, heaven, earth, wind, sky, and the directions as well. ||34||" |
| `Line 122: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 123: संवत्सरर्तवो मासाः पक्षाहोरात्रयः क्रमात् |` | "The year, seasons, months, fortnights, days and nights in sequence," |
| `Line 124: यच्चान्यदपि तत्सर्वं सम्भूतं लोकसाक्षिकम् ||३५||` | "And whatever else exists, all that has come into being, witnessed by the world. ||35||" |
| `Line 125: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 126: यदिदं दृश्यते किञ्चिद्भूतं स्थावरजङ्गमम् |` | "Whatever is seen here, any being, immovable or movable," |
| `Line 127: पुनः सङ्क्षिप्यते सर्वं जगत्प्राप्ते युगक्षये ||३६||` | "All is dissolved again, the entire world, when the end of the yuga [cosmic age] arrives. ||36||" |
| `Line 128: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 129: यथर्तावृतुलिङ्गानि नानारूपाणि पर्यये |` | "Just as the characteristics of seasons, of various forms, in their cycle," |
| `Line 130: दृश्यन्ते तानि तान्येव तथा भावा युगादिषु ||३७||` | "Are seen as the very same ones repeatedly, so are the states of existence at the beginning of each yuga [cosmic age]. ||37||" |
| `Line 131: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 132: एवमेतदनाद्यन्तं भूतसंहारकारकम् |` | "Thus this, without beginning or end, causing the dissolution of beings," |
| `Line 133: अनादिनिधनं लोके चक्रं सम्परिवर्तते ||३८||` | "The wheel [of time] without beginning or end revolves in the world. ||38||" |
| `Line 134: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 135: त्रयस्त्रिंशत्सहस्राणि त्रयस्त्रिंशच्छतानि च |` | "Thirty-three thousand, thirty-three hundred, and" |
| `Line 136: त्रयस्त्रिंशच्च देवानां सृष्टिः सङ्क्षेपलक्षणा ||३९||` | "Thirty-three gods - this is the creation in brief description. ||39||" |
| `Line 137: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 138: दिवस्पुत्रो बृहद्भानुश्चक्षुरात्मा विभावसुः |` | "The son of heaven, Brihadbhānu, Chakshuratma, Vibhāvasu [sun deity]," |
| `Line 139: सविता च ऋचीकोऽर्को भानुराशावहो रविः ||४०||` | "Savitā, Ṛchīka, Arka, Bhānu, Āśāvaha, Ravi [all solar deities]. ||40||" |
| `Line 140: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 141: पुत्रा विवस्वतः सर्वे मह्यस्तेषां तथावरः |` | "All are sons of Vivasvat [sun god], and Mahya is the youngest among them," |
| `Line 142: देवभ्राट्तनयस्तस्य तस्मात्सुभ्राडिति स्मृतः ||४१||` | "Devabhrāṭ's son was his, therefore he is known as Subhrāḍ. ||41||" |
| `Line 143: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 144: सुभ्राजस्तु त्रयः पुत्राः प्रजावन्तो बहुश्रुताः |` | "Subhrāja had three sons, prolific and highly learned," |
| `Line 145: दशज्योतिः शतज्योतिः सहस्रज्योतिरात्मवान् ||४२||` | "Daśajyoti, Śatajyoti, and the noble Sahasrajyoti. ||42||" |
| `Line 146: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 147: दश पुत्रसहस्राणि दशज्योतेर्महात्मनः |` | "Ten thousand sons were born to the great-souled Daśajyoti," |
| `Line 148: ततो दशगुणाश्चान्ये शतज्योतेरिहात्मजाः ||४३||` | "And ten times that number were the sons of Śatajyoti here. ||43||" |
| `Line 149: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 150: भूयस्ततो दशगुणाः सहस्रज्योतिषः सुताः |` | "And ten times more than that were the sons of Sahasrajyoti," |
| `Line 151: तेभ्योऽयं कुरुवंशश्च यदूनां भरतस्य च ||४४||` | "From them arose this lineage of the Kurus, of the Yadus [Krishna's clan], and of Bharata [ancient king]. ||44||" |
| `Line 152: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 153: ययातीक्ष्वाकुवंशश्च राजर्षीणां च सर्वशः |` | "And the lineages of Yayāti [legendary king] and Ikṣvāku [solar dynasty founder], and of all the royal sages [rājarṣis] completely," |
| `Line 154: सम्भूता बहवो वंशा भूतसर्गाः सविस्तराः ||४५||` | "Many lineages arose, and the detailed creation of beings. ||45||" |
| `Line 155: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 156: भूतस्थानानि सर्वाणि रहस्यं त्रिविधं च यत् |` | "All the abodes of beings, and the threefold mysteries [esoteric knowledge]," |
| `Line 157: वेदयोगं सविज्ञानं धर्मोऽर्थः काम एव च ||४६||` | "The application of Vedas with special knowledge, and dharma [righteousness], artha [wealth], and kāma [pleasure] as well. ||46||" |
| `Line 158: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 159: धर्मकामार्थशास्त्राणि शास्त्राणि विविधानि च |` | "The treatises on dharma, kāma, and artha, and various other treatises," |
| `Line 160: लोकयात्राविधानं च सम्भूतं दृष्टवानृषिः ||४७||` | "And the rules for worldly conduct, the sage saw all these manifested. ||47||" |
| `Line 161: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 162: इतिहासाः सवैयाख्या विविधाः श्रुतयोऽपि च |` | "Histories with their explanations, various sacred texts [śrutis] as well," |
| `Line 163: इह सर्वमनुक्रान्तमुक्तं ग्रन्थस्य लक्षणम् ||४८||` | "Here everything is enumerated, thus the characteristics of this work are described. ||48||" |
| `Line 164: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 165: विस्तीर्यैतन्महज्ज्ञानमृषिः सङ्क्षेपमब्रवीत् |` | "Having expanded this great knowledge, the sage spoke it in condensed form," |
| `Line 166: इष्टं हि विदुषां लोके समासव्यासधारणम् ||४९||` | "For in the world of the learned, the grasp of both concise and elaborate forms is desired. ||49||" |
| `Line 167: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 168: मन्वादि भारतं केचिदास्तीकादि तथापरे |` | "Some study the Bharata beginning with Manu [first man], others beginning with Āstīka [serpent sacrifice story]," |
| `Line 169: तथोपरिचराद्यन्ये विप्राः सम्यगधीयते ||५०||` | "And other Brahmins study it properly beginning with Uparicara [King Vasu]. ||50||" |
| `Line 170: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 171: विविधं संहिताज्ञानं दीपयन्ति मनीषिणः |` | "The wise illuminate the diverse knowledge of the Saṃhitās [collections]," |
| `Line 172: व्याख्यातुं कुशलाः केचिद्ग्रन्थं धारयितुं परे ||५१||` | "Some are skilled in explaining, others in memorizing the text. ||51||" |
| `Line 173: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 174: तपसा ब्रह्मचर्येण व्यस्य वेदं सनातनम् |` | "Having divided the eternal Veda through austerity and celibacy," |
| `Line 175: इतिहासमिमं चक्रे पुण्यं सत्यवतीसुतः ||५२||` | "The son of Satyavatī [Vyāsa] created this sacred history. ||52||" |
| `Line 176: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 177: पराशरात्मजो विद्वान्ब्रह्मर्षिः संशितव्रतः |` | "The learned son of Parāśara, a brahmarṣi [sage of highest order], of firm vows," |
| `Line 178: मातुर्नियोगाद्धर्मात्मा गाङ्गेयस्य च धीमतः ||५३||` | "By the command of his mother and of the wise Gāṅgeya [son of Gaṅgā], that righteous soul. ||53||" |
| `Line 179: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 180: क्षेत्रे विचित्रवीर्यस्य कृष्णद्वैपायनः पुरा |` | "In the field [wife] of Vicitravīrya, Kṛṣṇa Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] formerly," |
| `Line 181: त्रीनग्नीनिव कौरव्याञ्जनयामास वीर्यवान् ||५४||` | "Like three sacred fires, begot the Kauravya princes, that powerful sage. ||54||" |
| `Line 182: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 183: उत्पाद्य धृतराष्ट्रं च पाण्डुं विदुरमेव च |` | "Having begotten Dhṛtarāṣṭra, Pāṇḍu, and Vidura," |
| `Line 184: जगाम तपसे धीमान्पुनरेवाश्रमं प्रति ||५५||` | "The wise one went again to his hermitage for performing austerities. ||55||" |
| `Line 185: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 186: तेषु जातेषु वृद्धेषु गतेषु परमां गतिम् |` | "When they were born, had grown up, and had attained the supreme state [death]," |
| `Line 187: अब्रवीद्भारतं लोके मानुषेऽस्मिन्महानृषिः ||५६||` | "The great sage narrated the Bhārata in this world of humans. ||56||" |
| `Line 188: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 189: जनमेजयेन पृष्टः सन्ब्राह्मणैश्च सहस्रशः |` | "Being asked by Janamejaya and by thousands of Brāhmaṇas [priests]," |
| `Line 190: शशास शिष्यमासीनं वैशम्पायनमन्तिके ||५७||` | "He instructed his disciple Vaiśampāyana who was seated nearby. ||57||" |
| `Line 191: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 192: स सदस्यैः सहासीनः श्रावयामास भारतम् |` | "He, seated with the assembly members, recited the Bhārata," |
| `Line 193: कर्मान्तरेषु यज्ञस्य चोद्यमानः पुनः पुनः ||५८||` | "Being repeatedly requested during the intervals of the sacrifice. ||58||" |
| `Line 194: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 195: विस्तरं कुरुवंशस्य गान्धार्या धर्मशीलताम् |` | "The detailed account of the Kuru lineage, the righteousness of Gāndhārī [Dhritarashtra's wife]," |
| `Line 196: क्षत्तुः प्रज्ञां धृतिं कुन्त्याः सम्यग्द्वैपायनोऽब्रवीत् ||५९||` | "The wisdom of Kṣattṛ [Vidura] and the steadfastness of Kuntī—Dvaipāyana narrated all this properly. ||59||" |
| `Line 197: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 198: वासुदेवस्य माहात्म्यं पाण्डवानां च सत्यताम् |` | "The greatness of Vāsudeva [Krishna] and the truthfulness of the Pāṇḍavas," |
| `Line 199: दुर्वृत्तं धार्तराष्ट्राणामुक्तवान्भगवानृषिः ||६०||` | "The evil conduct of the sons of Dhṛtarāṣṭra—the venerable sage narrated. ||60||" |
| `Line 200: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 201: चतुर्विंशतिसाहस्रीं चक्रे भारतसंहिताम् |` | "He composed the Bhārata Saṃhitā [epic compilation] of twenty-four thousand verses," |
| `Line 202: उपाख्यानैर्विना तावद्भारतं प्रोच्यते बुधैः ||६१||` | "Without the sub-narratives, that much is called Bhārata by the wise. ||61||" |
| `Line 203: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 204: ततोऽध्यर्धशतं भूयः सङ्क्षेपं कृतवानृषिः |` | "Then the sage further composed a summary of one hundred and fifty," |
| `Line 205: अनुक्रमणिमध्यायं वृत्तान्तानां सपर्वणाम् ||६२||` | "An index chapter of the contents along with the Parvas [sections]. ||62||" |
| `Line 206: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 207: इदं द्वैपायनः पूर्वं पुत्रमध्यापयच्छुकम् |` | "This was first taught by Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] to his son Śuka," |
| `Line 208: ततोऽन्येभ्योऽनुरूपेभ्यः शिष्येभ्यः प्रददौ प्रभुः ||६३||` | "Then the master gave it to other suitable disciples. ||63||" |
| `Line 209: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 210: नारदोऽश्रावयद्देवानसितो देवलः पितृन् |` | "Nārada recited it to the gods, Asita Devala to the ancestors," |
| `Line 211: गन्धर्वयक्षरक्षांसि श्रावयामास वै शुकः ||६४||` | "And Śuka indeed recited it to the Gandharvas [celestial musicians], Yakṣas [wealth spirits], and Rākṣasas [demons]. ||64||" |
| `Line 212: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 213: दुर्योधनो मन्युमयो महाद्रुमः; स्कन्धः कर्णः शकुनिस्तस्य शाखाः |` | "Duryodhana is a great tree made of anger; Karṇa is its trunk, Śakuni its branches," |
| `Line 214: दुःशासनः पुष्पफले समृद्धे; मूलं राजा धृतराष्ट्रोऽमनीषी ||६५||` | "Duḥśāsana its abundant flowers and fruits; the unwise king Dhṛtarāṣṭra is its root. ||65||" |
| `Line 215: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 216: युधिष्ठिरो धर्ममयो महाद्रुमः; स्कन्धोऽर्जुनो भीमसेनोऽस्य शाखाः |` | "Yudhiṣṭhira is a great tree made of dharma [righteousness]; Arjuna is its trunk, Bhīmasena its branches," |
| `Line 217: माद्रीसुतौ पुष्पफले समृद्धे; मूलं कृष्णो ब्रह्म च ब्राह्मणाश्च ||६६||` | "The sons of Mādrī [Nakula and Sahadeva] are its abundant flowers and fruits; Kṛṣṇa, Brahman, and the Brāhmaṇas are its roots. ||66||" |
| `Line 218: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 219: पाण्डुर्जित्वा बहून्देशान्युधा विक्रमणेन च |` | "Pāṇḍu, having conquered many lands through battle and valor," |
| `Line 220: अरण्ये मृगयाशीलो न्यवसत्सजनस्तदा ||६७||` | "Then lived in the forest with his people, devoted to hunting. ||67||" |
| `Line 221: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 222: मृगव्यवायनिधने कृच्छ्रां प्राप स आपदम् |` | "He met with a terrible calamity due to intercourse while in the form of a deer [during hunting]," |
| `Line 223: जन्मप्रभृति पार्थानां तत्राचारविधिक्रमः ||६८||` | "From the birth of the Pārthas [sons of Pṛthā/Kuntī], there is the sequence of their conduct and rules. ||68||" |
| `Line 224: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 225: मात्रोरभ्युपपत्तिश्च धर्मोपनिषदं प्रति |` | "And the approach of their mothers regarding the secret doctrine of dharma [divine conception]," |
| `Line 226: धर्मस्य वायोः शक्रस्य देवयोश्च तथाश्विनोः ||६९||` | "Of Dharma [righteousness deity], Vayu [wind god], Shakra [Indra], and also of the two Ashvins [divine twins]. ||69||" |
| `Line 227: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 228: तापसैः सह संवृद्धा मातृभ्यां परिरक्षिताः |` | "They grew up with ascetics, protected by their mothers," |
| `Line 229: मेध्यारण्येषु पुण्येषु महतामाश्रमेषु च ||७०||` | "In sacred forests and in the great hermitages of sages. ||70||" |
| `Line 230: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 231: ऋषिभिश्च तदानीता धार्तराष्ट्रान्प्रति स्वयम् |` | "And then the sages themselves brought them to the sons of Dhritarashtra," |
| `Line 232: शिशवश्चाभिरूपाश्च जटिला ब्रह्मचारिणः ||७१||` | "The children, handsome, with matted hair, practicing celibacy [brahmacharya]. ||71||" |
| `Line 233: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 234: पुत्राश्च भ्रातरश्चेमे शिष्याश्च सुहृदश्च वः |` | "These are your sons, brothers, disciples, and friends," |
| `Line 235: पाण्डवा एत इत्युक्त्वा मुनयोऽन्तर्हितास्ततः ||७२||` | "These are the Pandavas," saying thus, the sages disappeared from there. ||72||" |
| `Line 236: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 237: तांस्तैर्निवेदितान्दृष्ट्वा पाण्डवान्कौरवास्तदा |` | "Seeing those Pandavas thus introduced, the Kauravas then," |
| `Line 238: शिष्टाश्च वर्णाः पौरा ये ते हर्षाच्चुक्रुशुर्भृशम् ||७३||` | "And the noble classes and citizens who were there, cried out loudly with joy. ||73||" |
| `Line 239: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 240: आहुः केचिन्न तस्यैते तस्यैत इति चापरे |` | "Some said, 'These are not his,' while others said, 'These are indeed his,'" |
| `Line 241: यदा चिरमृतः पाण्डुः कथं तस्येति चापरे ||७४||` | "And others said, 'Since Pandu died long ago, how can they be his?' ||74||" |
| `Line 242: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 243: स्वागतं सर्वथा दिष्ट्या पाण्डोः पश्याम सन्ततिम् |` | "'Welcome in every way! By good fortune we see the progeny of Pandu!'" |
| `Line 244: उच्यतां स्वागतमिति वाचोऽश्रूयन्त सर्वशः ||७५||` | "Voices saying 'Welcome!' were heard from all sides. ||75||" |
| `Line 245: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 246: तस्मिन्नुपरते शब्दे दिशः सर्वा विनादयन् |` | "When that sound subsided, resounding in all directions," |
| `Line 247: अन्तर्हितानां भूतानां निस्वनस्तुमुलोऽभवत् ||७६||` | "There arose a tumultuous sound of invisible beings. ||76||" |
| `Line 248: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 249: पुष्पवृष्टिः शुभा गन्धाः शङ्खदुन्दुभिनिस्वनाः |` | "A shower of flowers, auspicious fragrances, sounds of conches and drums," |
| `Line 250: आसन्प्रवेशे पार्थानां तदद्भुतमिवाभवत् ||७७||` | "Occurred at the entrance of the Parthas [sons of Pritha], and it was like a miracle. ||77||" |
| `Line 251: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 252: तत्प्रीत्या चैव सर्वेषां पौराणां हर्षसम्भवः |` | "And from that affection arose the joy of all the citizens," |
| `Line 253: शब्द आसीन्महांस्तत्र दिवस्पृक्कीर्तिवर्धनः ||७८||` | "There was a great sound there, reaching the heavens, enhancing their fame. ||78||" |
| `Line 254: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 255: तेऽप्यधीत्याखिलान्वेदाञ्शास्त्राणि विविधानि च |` | "Having studied all the Vedas and various śāstras [sacred texts]," |
| `Line 256: न्यवसन्पाण्डवास्तत्र पूजिता अकुतोभयाः ||७९||` | "The Pāṇḍavas lived there, honored and fearless. ||79||" |
| `Line 257: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 258: युधिष्ठिरस्य शौचेन प्रीताः प्रकृतयोऽभवन् |` | "The subjects were pleased with Yudhiṣṭhira's purity," |
| `Line 259: धृत्या च भीमसेनस्य विक्रमेणार्जुनस्य च ||८०||` | "With Bhīmasena's steadfastness and Arjuna's valor. ||80||" |
| `Line 260: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 261: गुरुशुश्रूषया कुन्त्या यमयोर्विनयेन च |` | "With Kuntī's service to elders and the twins' [Nakula-Sahadeva] humility," |
| `Line 262: तुतोष लोकः सकलस्तेषां शौर्यगुणेन च ||८१||` | "The entire world was satisfied with their heroic qualities. ||81||" |
| `Line 263: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 264: समवाये ततो राज्ञां कन्यां भर्तृस्वयंवराम् |` | "Then, in an assembly of kings, at a bride's self-choice ceremony [svayaṃvara]," |
| `Line 265: प्राप्तवानर्जुनः कृष्णां कृत्वा कर्म सुदुष्करम् ||८२||` | "Arjuna won Kṛṣṇā [Draupadī], having performed an extremely difficult feat. ||82||" |
| `Line 266: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 267: ततः प्रभृति लोकेऽस्मिन्पूज्यः सर्वधनुष्मताम् |` | "From then on, in this world, he was revered among all archers," |
| `Line 268: आदित्य इव दुष्प्रेक्ष्यः समरेष्वपि चाभवत् ||८३||` | "And became difficult to look at in battles, like the sun [Āditya]. ||83||" |
| `Line 269: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 270: स सर्वान्पार्थिवाञ्जित्वा सर्वांश्च महतो गणान् |` | "Having conquered all the kings and all the great hosts," |
| `Line 271: आजहारार्जुनो राज्ञे राजसूयं महाक्रतुम् ||८४||` | "Arjuna brought for the king the Rājasūya, the great sacrifice [royal consecration]. ||84||" |
| `Line 272: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 273: अन्नवान्दक्षिणावांश्च सर्वैः समुदितो गुणैः |` | "Abundant with food and gifts, endowed with all excellent qualities," |
| `Line 274: युधिष्ठिरेण सम्प्राप्तो राजसूयो महाक्रतुः ||८५||` | "The great Rājasūya sacrifice was performed by Yudhiṣṭhira. ||85||" |
| `Line 275: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 276: सुनयाद्वासुदेवस्य भीमार्जुनबलेन च |` | "Through the wise policy of Vāsudeva [Krishna] and by the strength of Bhīma and Arjuna," |
| `Line 277: घातयित्वा जरासन्धं चैद्यं च बलगर्वितम् ||८६||` | "Having caused the slaying of Jarāsandha and Chaidya [Shishupala] who was proud of his strength. ||86||" |
| `Line 278: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 279: दुर्योधनमुपागच्छन्नर्हणानि ततस्ततः |` | "Tributes came to Duryodhana from here and there," |
| `Line 280: मणिकाञ्चनरत्नानि गोहस्त्यश्वधनानि च ||८७||` | "Jewels, gold, gems, and wealth in the form of cows, elephants, and horses. ||87||" |
| `Line 281: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 282: समृद्धां तां तथा दृष्ट्वा पाण्डवानां तदा श्रियम् |` | "Seeing thus the abundant prosperity of the Pāṇḍavas at that time," |
| `Line 283: ईर्ष्यासमुत्थः सुमहांस्तस्य मन्युरजायत ||८८||` | "Great anger born of envy arose in him. ||88||" |
| `Line 284: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 285: विमानप्रतिमां चापि मयेन सुकृतां सभाम् |` | "And seeing the assembly hall resembling a celestial palace, beautifully constructed by Maya [demon architect]," |
| `Line 286: पाण्डवानामुपहृतां स दृष्ट्वा पर्यतप्यत ||८९||` | "Presented to the Pāṇḍavas, he was consumed with grief. ||89||" |
| `Line 287: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 288: यत्रावहसितश्चासीत्प्रस्कन्दन्निव सम्भ्रमात् |` | "Where he had been laughed at when he fell in confusion," |
| `Line 289: प्रत्यक्षं वासुदेवस्य भीमेनानभिजातवत् ||९०||` | "In the presence of Vāsudeva [Krishna], by Bhīma, as if he were of low birth. ||90||" |
| `Line 290: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 291: स भोगान्विविधान्भुञ्जन्रत्नानि विविधानि च |` | "He, though enjoying various pleasures and diverse jewels," |
| `Line 292: कथितो धृतराष्ट्रस्य विवर्णो हरिणः कृशः ||९१||` | "Was described to Dhṛtarāṣṭra as pale, agitated, and emaciated. ||91||" |
| `Line 293: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 294: अन्वजानात्ततो द्यूतं धृतराष्ट्रः सुतप्रियः |` | "Then Dhṛtarāṣṭra, loving his son, approved of the gambling match," |
| `Line 295: तच्छ्रुत्वा वासुदेवस्य कोपः समभवन्महान् ||९२||` | "Hearing of this, great was the anger of Vāsudeva [Krishna]. ||92||" |
| `Line 296: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 297: नातिप्रीतमनाश्चासीद्विवादांश्चान्वमोदत |` | "He [Dhritarashtra] was not very pleased at heart, yet he approved of the disputes," |
| `Line 298: द्यूतादीननयान्घोरान्प्रवृद्धांश्चाप्युपैक्षत ||९३||` | "And overlooked the terrible injustices beginning with the gambling match that had grown out of control. ||93||" |
| `Line 299: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 300: निरस्य विदुरं द्रोणं भीष्मं शारद्वतं कृपम् |` | "Rejecting Vidura, Droṇa, Bhīṣma, Śāradvata [Kripa's father], and Kṛpa," |
| `Line 301: विग्रहे तुमुले तस्मिन्नहन्क्षत्रं परस्परम् ||९४||` | "In that tumultuous battle, the warriors [kṣatriyas] slew one another. ||94||" |
| `Line 302: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 303: जयत्सु पाण्डुपुत्रेषु श्रुत्वा सुमहदप्रियम् |` | "When the sons of Pandu were victorious, having heard this greatly unpleasant news," |
| `Line 304: दुर्योधनमतं ज्ञात्वा कर्णस्य शकुनेस्तथा ||९५||` | "And knowing the intentions of Duryodhana, Karna, and Shakuni as well, ||95||" |
| `Line 305: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 306: धृतराष्ट्रश्चिरं ध्यात्वा सञ्जयं वाक्यमब्रवीत् ||९५||` | "Dhritarashtra, after reflecting for a long time, spoke these words to Sanjaya. ||95||" |
| `Line 307: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 308: शृणु सञ्जय मे सर्वं न मेऽसूयितुमर्हसि |` | "Listen, Sanjaya, to all I say, and you should not find fault with me," |
| `Line 309: श्रुतवानसि मेधावी बुद्धिमान्प्राज्ञसंमतः ||९६||` | "You are learned, intelligent, and esteemed by the wise. ||96||" |
| `Line 310: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 311: न विग्रहे मम मतिर्न च प्रीये कुरुक्षये |` | "My mind is not inclined toward conflict, nor do I delight in the destruction of the Kurus," |
| `Line 312: न मे विशेषः पुत्रेषु स्वेषु पाण्डुसुतेषु च ||९७||` | "I have no preference between my own sons and the sons of Pandu. ||97||" |
| `Line 313: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 314: वृद्धं मामभ्यसूयन्ति पुत्रा मन्युपरायणाः |` | "My sons, devoted to anger, find fault with me, an old man," |
| `Line 315: अहं त्वचक्षुः कार्पण्यात्पुत्रप्रीत्या सहामि तत् ||९८||` | "But being blind, out of weakness and love for my sons, I endure it. ||98||" |
| `Line 316: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 317: मुह्यन्तं चानुमुह्यामि दुर्योधनमचेतनम् ||९८||` | "And I follow in delusion my deluded and senseless Duryodhana. ||98||" |
| `Line 318: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 319: राजसूये श्रियं दृष्ट्वा पाण्डवस्य महौजसः |` | "Having seen the prosperity of the mighty Pandava at the Rajasuya [royal sacrifice]," |
| `Line 320: तच्चावहसनं प्राप्य सभारोहणदर्शने ||९९||` | "And having experienced humiliation at the sight of the assembly hall, ||99||" |
| `Line 321: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 322: अमर्षितः स्वयं जेतुमशक्तः पाण्डवान्रणे |` | "Filled with intolerance, yet himself unable to defeat the Pandavas in battle," |
| `Line 323: निरुत्साहश्च सम्प्राप्तुं श्रियमक्षत्रियो यथा ||१००||` | "And lacking the energy to attain prosperity, like one who is not a kshatriya [warrior], ||100||" |
| `Line 324: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 325: गान्धारराजसहितश्छद्मद्यूतममन्त्रयत् ||१००||` | "Together with the king of Gandhara [Shakuni], he plotted the fraudulent game of dice. ||100||" |
| `Line 326: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 327: तत्र यद्यद्यथा ज्ञातं मया सञ्जय तच्छृणु |` | "Listen, Sanjaya, to what I have known there, in whatever way I have known it." |
| `Line 328: श्रुत्वा हि मम वाक्यानि बुद्ध्या युक्तानि तत्त्वतः ||१०१||` | "For having heard my words, which are endowed with wisdom and truth. ||101||" |
| `Line 329: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 330: ततो ज्ञास्यसि मां सौते प्रज्ञाचक्षुषमित्युत ||१०१||` | "Then you will know me, O charioteer's son [Sanjaya], as one who sees with the eye of wisdom. ||101||" |
| `Line 331: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 332: यदाश्रौषं धनुरायम्य चित्रं; विद्धं लक्ष्यं पातितं वै पृथिव्याम् |` | "When I heard that, drawing the marvelous bow, the target was pierced and made to fall on the earth," |
| `Line 333: कृष्णां हृतां पश्यतां सर्वराज्ञां; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०२||` | "And Krishnā [Draupadi] was dragged away in the sight of all kings; then, Sanjaya, I did not hope for victory. ||102||" |
| `Line 334: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 335: यदाश्रौषं द्वारकायां सुभद्रां; प्रसह्योढां माधवीमर्जुनेन |` | "When I heard that Subhadrā, the daughter of Mādhava [Krishna's family], was forcibly carried away from Dvārakā by Arjuna," |
| `Line 336: इन्द्रप्रस्थं वृष्णिवीरौ च यातौ; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०३||` | "And that the two Vrishni heroes [Krishna and Balarama] went to Indraprastha; then, Sanjaya, I did not hope for victory. ||103||" |
| `Line 337: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 338: यदाश्रौषं देवराजं प्रवृष्टं; शरैर्दिव्यैर्वारितं चार्जुनेन |` | "When I heard that the king of gods [Indra] showering (arrows) was repelled by Arjuna with divine arrows," |
| `Line 339: अग्निं तथा तर्पितं खाण्डवे च; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०४||` | "And that the fire god was satisfied in the Khāṇḍava forest; then, Sanjaya, I did not hope for victory. ||104||" |
| `Line 340: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 341: यदाश्रौषं हृतराज्यं युधिष्ठिरं; पराजितं सौबलेनाक्षवत्याम् |` | "When I heard that Yudhishthira was deprived of his kingdom, defeated by Soubala [Shakuni] in the game of dice," |
| `Line 342: अन्वागतं भ्रातृभिरप्रमेयै; स्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०५||` | "And was followed by his immeasurable brothers; then, Sanjaya, I did not hope for victory. ||105||" |
| `Line 343: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 344: यदाश्रौषं द्रौपदीमश्रुकण्ठीं; सभां नीतां दुःखितामेकवस्त्राम् |` | "When I heard that Draupadi, with tears in her throat, was brought to the assembly hall, distressed, wearing only a single garment," |
| `Line 345: रजस्वलां नाथवतीमनाथव; त्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०६||` | "In her monthly period, though having protectors, yet treated as if without protection; then, Sanjaya, I did not hope for victory. ||106||" |
| `Line 346: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 347: यदाश्रौषं विविधास्तात चेष्टा; धर्मात्मनां प्रस्थितानां वनाय |` | "When I heard, O dear one, of the various efforts of those righteous souls departing for the forest," |
| `Line 348: ज्येष्ठप्रीत्या क्लिश्यतां पाण्डवानां; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०७||` | "Of the Pāṇḍavas suffering out of devotion to their eldest brother; then, Sanjaya, I did not hope for victory. ||107||" |
| `Line 349: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 350: यदाश्रौषं स्नातकानां सहस्रै; रन्वागतं धर्मराजं वनस्थम् |` | "When I heard that Dharmarāja [Yudhishthira], dwelling in the forest, was followed by thousands of graduate students [Snātakas]," |
| `Line 351: भिक्षाभुजां ब्राह्मणानां महात्मनां; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०८||` | "Of the alms-eating Brahmins, the great souls; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||108||" |
| `Line 352: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 353: यदाश्रौषमर्जुनो देवदेवं; किरातरूपं त्र्यम्बकं तोष्य युद्धे |` | "When I heard that Arjuna had pleased the God of gods, Tryambaka [three-eyed Shiva] in the form of a Kirata [hunter], in battle," |
| `Line 354: अवाप तत्पाशुपतं महास्त्रं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१०९||` | "And obtained that mighty Pashupata [Shiva's weapon] weapon; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||109||" |
| `Line 355: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 356: यदाश्रौषं त्रिदिवस्थं धनञ्जयं; शक्रात्साक्षाद्दिव्यमस्त्रं यथावत् |` | "When I heard that Dhananjaya [Arjuna] was in heaven [Tridiva], properly learning divine weapons directly from Shakra [Indra]," |
| `Line 357: अधीयानं शंसितं सत्यसन्धं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११०||` | "He who is praised, truthful and steadfast in his vows; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||110||" |
| `Line 358: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 359: यदाश्रौषं वैश्रवणेन सार्धं; समागतं भीममन्यांश्च पार्थान् |` | "When I heard that Bhima and the other Parthas [Pandavas] had met with Vaishravana [Kubera]," |
| `Line 360: तस्मिन्देशे मानुषाणामगम्ये; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१११||` | "In that region inaccessible to humans; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||111||" |
| `Line 361: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 362: यदाश्रौषं घोषयात्रागतानां; बन्धं गन्धर्वैर्मोक्षणं चार्जुनेन |` | "When I heard of the capture of those who had gone on the Ghoshayatra [cattle expedition], by the Gandharvas, and their release by Arjuna," |
| `Line 363: स्वेषां सुतानां कर्णबुद्धौ रतानां; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११२||` | "Of my sons who relied on Karna's wisdom; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||112||" |
| `Line 364: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 365: यदाश्रौषं यक्षरूपेण धर्मं; समागतं धर्मराजेन सूत |` | "When I heard that Dharma [Yama] in the form of a Yaksha [supernatural being] had met with Dharmaraja [Yudhishthira], O charioteer," |
| `Line 366: प्रश्नानुक्तान्विब्रुवन्तं च सम्य; क्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११३||` | "And that he correctly answered all the questions asked; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||113||" |
| `Line 367: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 368: यदाश्रौषं मामकानां वरिष्ठा; न्धनञ्जयेनैकरथेन भग्नान् |` | "When I heard that the best of my warriors were defeated by Dhananjaya [Arjuna] alone in his chariot," |
| `Line 369: विराटराष्ट्रे वसता महात्मना; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११४||` | "By that great soul residing in the kingdom of Virata; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||114||" |
| `Line 370: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 371: यदाश्रौषं सत्कृतां मत्स्यराज्ञा; सुतां दत्तामुत्तरामर्जुनाय |` | "When I heard that the honored daughter of the Matsya king, Uttara, was given to Arjuna," |
| `Line 372: तां चार्जुनः प्रत्यगृह्णात्सुतार्थे; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११५||` | "And that Arjuna accepted her for his son's sake; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||115||" |
| `Line 373: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 374: यदाश्रौषं निर्जितस्याधनस्य; प्रव्राजितस्य स्वजनात्प्रच्युतस्य |` | "When I heard that Yudhishthira, who was defeated, made penniless, exiled, and separated from his kinsmen," |
| `Line 375: अक्षौहिणीः सप्त युधिष्ठिरस्य; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११६||` | "Had seven akshauhinis [large army divisions] at his command; then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||116||" |
| `Line 376: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 377: यदाश्रौषं नरनारायणौ तौ; कृष्णार्जुनौ वदतो नारदस्य |` | "When I heard from Narada's words that those two, Nara-Narayana [ancient sages], were Krishna and Arjuna," |
| `Line 378: अहं द्रष्टा ब्रह्मलोके सदेति; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११७||` | "That I would always see them in Brahmaloka [celestial realm], then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||117||" |
| `Line 379: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 380: यदाश्रौषं माधवं वासुदेवं; सर्वात्मना पाण्डवार्थे निविष्टम् |` | "When I heard that Madhava [Krishna], Vasudeva, was wholly devoted to the Pandavas' cause," |
| `Line 381: यस्येमां गां विक्रममेकमाहु; स्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११८||` | "He whose single stride is said to cover this earth, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||118||" |
| `Line 382: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 383: यदाश्रौषं कर्णदुर्योधनाभ्यां; बुद्धिं कृतां निग्रहे केशवस्य |` | "When I heard that Karna and Duryodhana had formed a plan to capture Keshava [Krishna]," |
| `Line 384: तं चात्मानं बहुधा दर्शयानं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||११९||` | "And that he revealed himself in multiple forms, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||119||" |
| `Line 385: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 386: यदाश्रौषं वासुदेवे प्रयाते; रथस्यैकामग्रतस्तिष्ठमानाम् |` | "When I heard that as Vasudeva [Krishna] departed, Pritha [Kunti] stood alone before his chariot," |
| `Line 387: आर्तां पृथां सान्त्वितां केशवेन; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२०||` | "Distressed Pritha was consoled by Keshava, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||120||" |
| `Line 388: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 389: यदाश्रौषं मन्त्रिणं वासुदेवं; तथा भीष्मं शान्तनवं च तेषाम् |` | "When I heard that Vasudeva was their counselor, and that Bhishma, son of Shantanu, was with them," |
| `Line 390: भारद्वाजं चाशिषोऽनुब्रुवाणं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२१||` | "And that Bharadvaja [Drona] pronounced blessings upon them, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||121||" |
| `Line 391: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 392: यदाश्रौषं कर्ण उवाच भीष्मं; नाहं योत्स्ये युध्यमाने त्वयीति |` | "When I heard that Karna said to Bhishma, 'I will not fight while you are fighting,'" |
| `Line 393: हित्वा सेनामपचक्राम चैव; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२२||` | "And that he left the army and departed, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||122||" |
| `Line 394: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 395: यदाश्रौषं वासुदेवार्जुनौ तौ; तथा धनुर्गाण्डिवमप्रमेयम् |` | "When I heard that those two, Vasudeva and Arjuna, along with the immeasurable Gandiva bow [divine weapon]," |
| `Line 396: त्रीण्युग्रवीर्याणि समागतानि; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२३||` | "These three of terrible prowess had come together, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||123||" |
| `Line 397: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 398: यदाश्रौषं कश्मलेनाभिपन्ने; रथोपस्थे सीदमानेऽर्जुने वै |` | "When I heard that Arjuna, overcome with dejection, was sinking down in his chariot," |
| `Line 399: कृष्णं लोकान्दर्शयानं शरीरे; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२४||` | "And Krishna revealed all the worlds within his body, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||124||" |
| `Line 400: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 401: यदाश्रौषं भीष्मममित्रकर्शनं; निघ्नन्तमाजावयुतं रथानाम् |` | "When I heard that Bhishma, the tormentor of foes, was destroying ten thousand chariots in battle," |
| `Line 402: नैषां कश्चिद्वध्यते दृश्यरूप; स्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२५||` | "Yet none of our visible warriors was being slain, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||125||" |
| `Line 403: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 404: यदाश्रौषं भीष्ममत्यन्तशूरं; हतं पार्थेनाहवेष्वप्रधृष्यम् |` | "When I heard that Bhishma, the extremely valiant one, unconquerable in battles, was slain by Partha [Arjuna]," |
| `Line 405: शिखण्डिनं पुरतः स्थापयित्वा; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२६||` | "After placing Shikhandi in front, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||126||" |
| `Line 406: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 407: यदाश्रौषं शरतल्पे शयानं; वृद्धं वीरं सादितं चित्रपुङ्खैः |` | "When I heard that the aged hero was lying on a bed of arrows, brought down by variegated-feathered shafts," |
| `Line 408: भीष्मं कृत्वा सोमकानल्पशेषां; स्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२७||` | "And that Bhishma had reduced the Somakas [Pandava allies] to a small remnant, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||127||" |
| `Line 409: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 410: यदाश्रौषं शान्तनवे शयाने; पानीयार्थे चोदितेनार्जुनेन |` | "When I heard that while the son of Shantanu [Bhishma] was lying wounded, Arjuna, being urged for water," |
| `Line 411: भूमिं भित्त्वा तर्पितं तत्र भीष्मं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२८||` | "Pierced the earth and satisfied Bhishma's thirst there, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||128||" |
| `Line 412: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 413: यदाश्रौषं शुक्रसूर्यौ च युक्तौ; कौन्तेयानामनुलोमौ जयाय |` | "When I heard that Venus and the Sun were favorably positioned for the victory of the sons of Kunti [Pandavas]," |
| `Line 414: नित्यं चास्माञ्श्वापदा व्याभषन्त; स्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१२९||` | "And that wild beasts were constantly frightening us, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||129||" |
| `Line 415: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 416: यदा द्रोणो विविधानस्त्रमार्गा; न्विदर्शयन्समरे चित्रयोधी |` | "When Drona, displaying various paths of weapons in battle, fighting wonderfully," |
| `Line 417: न पाण्डवाञ्श्रेष्ठतमान्निहन्ति; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३०||` | "Could not slay the foremost of the Pandavas, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||130||" |
| `Line 418: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 419: यदाश्रौषं चास्मदीयान्महारथा; न्व्यवस्थितानर्जुनस्यान्तकाय |` | "When I heard that our great warriors, who had positioned themselves to kill Arjuna," |
| `Line 420: संशप्तकान्निहतानर्जुनेन; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३१||` | "The Samsaptakas [oath-bound warriors], were slain by Arjuna, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||131||" |
| `Line 421: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 422: यदाश्रौषं व्यूहमभेद्यमन्यै; र्भारद्वाजेनात्तशस्त्रेण गुप्तम् |` | "When I heard that the formation, impenetrable to others, protected by the armed son of Bharadvaja [Drona]," |
| `Line 423: भित्त्वा सौभद्रं वीरमेकं प्रविष्टं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३२||` | "Was penetrated by the heroic son of Subhadra [Abhimanyu] who entered alone, then, O Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||132||" |
| `Line 424: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 425: यदाभिमन्युं परिवार्य बालं; सर्वे हत्वा हृष्टरूपा बभूवुः |` | "When all our warriors, having surrounded the young Abhimanyu, slew him and became joyful," |
| `Line 426: महारथाः पार्थमशक्नुवन्त; स्तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३३||` | "When the great warriors were unable to defeat Pārtha [Arjuna], then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||133||" |
| `Line 427: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 428: यदाश्रौषमभिमन्युं निहत्य; हर्षान्मूढान्क्रोशतो धार्तराष्ट्रान् |` | "When I heard the Dhārtarāṣṭras [Duryodhana's forces] shouting foolishly with joy after slaying Abhimanyu," |
| `Line 429: क्रोधं मुक्तं सैन्धवे चार्जुनेन; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३४||` | "And Arjuna's unleashed anger against Saindhava [Jayadratha], then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||134||" |
| `Line 430: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 431: यदाश्रौषं सैन्धवार्थे प्रतिज्ञां; प्रतिज्ञातां तद्वधायार्जुनेन |` | "When I heard the vow regarding Saindhava [Jayadratha], the pledge made by Arjuna for his slaying," |
| `Line 432: सत्यां निस्तीर्णां शत्रुमध्ये च तेन; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३५||` | "And that he fulfilled it truthfully in the midst of enemies, then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||135||" |
| `Line 433: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 434: यदाश्रौषं श्रान्तहये धनञ्जये; मुक्त्वा हयान्पाययित्वोपवृत्तान् |` | "When I heard that Dhanañjaya [Arjuna], whose horses were tired, released them, gave them water, and returned," |
| `Line 435: पुनर्युक्त्वा वासुदेवं प्रयातं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३६||` | "And then, yoking them again, proceeded with Vāsudeva [Krishna], then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||136||" |
| `Line 436: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 437: यदाश्रौषं वाहनेष्वाश्वसत्सु; रथोपस्थे तिष्ठता गाण्डिवेन |` | "When I heard that while the horses were resting, standing in his chariot with Gāṇḍīva [Arjuna's bow]," |
| `Line 438: सर्वान्योधान्वारितानर्जुनेन; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३७||` | "Arjuna warded off all the warriors, then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||137||" |
| `Line 439: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 440: यदाश्रौषं नागबलैर्दुरुत्सहं; द्रोणानीकं युयुधानं प्रमथ्य |` | "When I heard that Yuyudhāna [Sātyaki], having crushed Droṇa's formation that was formidable with elephant forces," |
| `Line 441: यातं वार्ष्णेयं यत्र तौ कृष्णपार्थौ; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३८||` | "That Vārṣṇeya [Sātyaki] went to where Krishna and Pārtha [Arjuna] were, then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||138||" |
| `Line 442: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 443: यदाश्रौषं कर्णमासाद्य मुक्तं; वधाद्भीमं कुत्सयित्वा वचोभिः |` | "When I heard that Bhīma, having encountered Karṇa, was released from death after being insulted with words," |
| `Line 444: धनुष्कोट्या तुद्य कर्णेन वीरं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१३९||` | "And that Karṇa struck the hero with the end of his bow, then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||139||" |
| `Line 445: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 446: यदा द्रोणः कृतवर्मा कृपश्च; कर्णो द्रौणिर्मद्रराजश्च शूरः |` | "When Droṇa, Kṛtavarman, Kṛpa, Karṇa, Droṇi [Ashvatthāma], and the heroic king of Madra [Shalya]," |
| `Line 447: अमर्षयन्सैन्धवं वध्यमानं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४०||` | "Could not prevent Saindhava [Jayadratha] from being slain, then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||140||" |
| `Line 448: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 449: यदाश्रौषं देवराजेन दत्तां; दिव्यां शक्तिं व्यंसितां माधवेन |` | "When I heard that the divine spear given by the king of gods [Indra] was thwarted by Mādhava [Krishna]," |
| `Line 450: घटोत्कचे राक्षसे घोररूपे; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४१||` | "When aimed at the terrifying rākṣasa [demon] Ghaṭotkaca, then, O Sañjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||141||" |
| `Line 451: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 452: यदाश्रौषं कर्णघटोत्कचाभ्यां; युद्धे मुक्तां सूतपुत्रेण शक्तिम् |` | "When I heard about the spear released by the son of a charioteer [Karna] in the battle between Karna and Ghatotkaca," |
| `Line 453: यया वध्यः समरे सव्यसाची; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४२||` | "By which the left-handed archer [Arjuna] was to be slain in battle, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||142||" |
| `Line 454: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 455: यदाश्रौषं द्रोणमाचार्यमेकं; धृष्टद्युम्नेनाभ्यतिक्रम्य धर्मम् |` | "When I heard that Drona, the teacher, alone was killed by Dhrishtadyumna, transgressing dharma [righteousness]," |
| `Line 456: रथोपस्थे प्रायगतं विशस्तं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४३||` | "Slain while seated in his chariot, having nearly given up his life, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||143||" |
| `Line 457: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 458: यदाश्रौषं द्रौणिना द्वैरथस्थं; माद्रीपुत्रं नकुलं लोकमध्ये |` | "When I heard that Nakula, son of Madri, standing in a chariot duel with Drona's son [Ashvatthama] before the world," |
| `Line 459: समं युद्धे पाण्डवं युध्यमानं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४४||` | "The Pandava fighting equally in battle, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||144||" |
| `Line 460: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 461: यदा द्रोणे निहते द्रोणपुत्रो; नारायणं दिव्यमस्त्रं विकुर्वन् |` | "When, after Drona was slain, his son [Ashvatthama] deployed the divine Narayana weapon [celestial missile]," |
| `Line 462: नैषामन्तं गतवान्पाण्डवानां; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४५||` | "Yet could not bring about the end of the Pandavas, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||145||" |
| `Line 463: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 464: यदाश्रौषं कर्णमत्यन्तशूरं; हतं पार्थेनाहवेष्वप्रधृष्यम् |` | "When I heard that Karna, the extremely valiant, unconquerable in battles, was slain by Partha [Arjuna]," |
| `Line 465: तस्मिन्भ्रातृणां विग्रहे देवगुह्ये; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४६||` | "In that mysterious conflict of brothers ordained by gods, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||146||" |
| `Line 466: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 467: यदाश्रौषं द्रोणपुत्रं कृपं च; दुःशासनं कृतवर्माणमुग्रम् |` | "When I heard that Drona's son [Ashvatthama], Kripa, Duhshasana, and the fierce Kritavarman," |
| `Line 468: युधिष्ठिरं शून्यमधर्षयन्तं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४७||` | "Were unable to overcome Yudhishthira when he was alone, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||147||" |
| `Line 469: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 470: यदाश्रौषं निहतं मद्रराजं; रणे शूरं धर्मराजेन सूत |` | "When I heard that the king of Madra [Shalya], valiant in battle, was slain by Dharmaraja [Yudhishthira], O charioteer," |
| `Line 471: सदा सङ्ग्रामे स्पर्धते यः स कृष्णं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४८||` | "He who always rivaled Krishna in combat, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||148||" |
| `Line 472: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 473: यदाश्रौषं कलहद्यूतमूलं; मायाबलं सौबलं पाण्डवेन |` | "When I heard that Soubala [Shakuni], the root cause of the gambling dispute, powerful in illusion," |
| `Line 474: हतं सङ्ग्रामे सहदेवेन पापं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१४९||` | "The sinful one, was slain in battle by Sahadeva, then, O Sanjaya, I despaired of victory. ||149||" |
| `Line 475: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 476: यदाश्रौषं श्रान्तमेकं शयानं; ह्रदं गत्वा स्तम्भयित्वा तदम्भः |` | "When I heard that the exhausted one was lying alone, having gone to the lake and frozen its waters," |
| `Line 477: दुर्योधनं विरथं भग्नदर्पं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१५०||` | "Duryodhana, chariotless and with broken pride - then, Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||150||" |
| `Line 478: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 479: यदाश्रौषं पाण्डवांस्तिष्ठमाना; न्गङ्गाह्रदे वासुदेवेन सार्धम् |` | "When I heard that the Pandavas were standing at the Ganga lake [sacred river pool] together with Vasudeva [Krishna]," |
| `Line 480: अमर्षणं धर्षयतः सुतं मे; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१५१||` | "Provoking my impatient son - then, Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||151||" |
| `Line 481: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 482: यदाश्रौषं विविधांस्तात मार्गा; न्गदायुद्धे मण्डलं सञ्चरन्तम् |` | "When I heard, dear one, about the various paths he was moving in circular patterns during the mace duel," |
| `Line 483: मिथ्या हतं वासुदेवस्य बुद्ध्या; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१५२||` | "And was falsely defeated by Vasudeva's [Krishna's] strategy - then, Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||152||" |
| `Line 484: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 485: यदाश्रौषं द्रोणपुत्रादिभिस्तै; र्हतान्पाञ्चालान्द्रौपदेयांश्च सुप्तान् |` | "When I heard that by Drona's son [Ashvatthama] and others, the sleeping Panchalas and Draupadi's sons were slain," |
| `Line 486: कृतं बीभत्समयशस्यं च कर्म; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१५३||` | "A horrible and inglorious deed was done - then, Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||153||" |
| `Line 487: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 488: यदाश्रौषं भीमसेनानुयातेन; अश्वत्थाम्ना परमास्त्रं प्रयुक्तम् |` | "When I heard that Ashvatthama, pursued by Bhimasena, discharged the supreme weapon," |
| `Line 489: क्रुद्धेनैषीकमवधीद्येन गर्भं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१५४||` | "And in anger destroyed the fetus with his reed-weapon [Brahmastra] - then, Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||154||" |
| `Line 490: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 491: यदाश्रौषं ब्रह्मशिरोऽर्जुनेन; मुक्तं स्वस्तीत्यस्त्रमस्त्रेण शान्तम् |` | "When I heard that the Brahma-weapon [divine missile] released by Arjuna neutralized the other weapon with a 'svasti' [blessing]," |
| `Line 492: अश्वत्थाम्ना मणिरत्नं च दत्तं; तदा नाशंसे विजयाय सञ्जय ||१५५||` | "And that Ashvatthama surrendered his jewel [head gem] - then, Sanjaya, I had no hope for victory. ||155||" |
| `Line 493: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 494: यदाश्रौषं द्रोणपुत्रेण गर्भे; वैराट्या वै पात्यमाने महास्त्रे |` | "When I heard that when Drona's son [Ashvatthama] directed the great weapon at the womb of Virata's daughter [Uttara]," |
| `Line 495: द्वैपायनः केशवो द्रोणपुत्रं; परस्परेणाभिशापैः शशाप ||१५६||` | "Dvaipayana [Vyasa] and Keshava [Krishna] cursed Drona's son with mutual curses - ||156||" |
| `Line 496: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 497: शोच्या गान्धारी पुत्रपौत्रैर्विहीना; तथा वध्वः पितृभिर्भ्रातृभिश्च |` | "Pitiable is Gandhari, bereft of sons and grandsons; likewise the daughters-in-law, of their fathers and brothers," |
| `Line 498: कृतं कार्यं दुष्करं पाण्डवेयैः; प्राप्तं राज्यमसपत्नं पुनस्तैः ||१५७||` | "The Pandavas have accomplished a difficult task; they have regained the kingdom without rivals. ||157||" |
| `Line 499: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 500: कष्टं युद्धे दश शेषाः श्रुता मे; त्रयोऽस्माकं पाण्डवानां च सप्त |` | "Alas! I have heard that only ten survived the war - three of ours and seven of the Pandavas," |
| `Line 501: द्व्यूना विंशतिराहताक्षौहिणीनां; तस्मिन्सङ्ग्रामे विग्रहे क्षत्रियाणाम् ॥१५८॥` | "Eighteen akshauhinis [army units] were destroyed in that battle, in that conflict of the kshatriyas [warrior class]. ||158||" |
| `Line 502: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 503: तमसा त्वभ्यवस्तीर्णो मोह आविशतीव माम् |` | "I am overcome by darkness, and delusion seems to enter me," |
| `Line 504: सञ्ज्ञां नोपलभे सूत मनो विह्वलतीव मे ॥१५९॥` | "I cannot maintain consciousness, O Suta [charioteer/bard], my mind seems to be bewildered. ||159||" |
| `Line 505: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 506: इत्युक्त्वा धृतराष्ट्रोऽथ विलप्य बहुदुःखितः |` | "Having spoken thus, Dhritarashtra then lamented, greatly distressed," |
| `Line 507: मूर्च्छितः पुनराश्वस्तः सञ्जयं वाक्यमब्रवीत् ॥१६०॥` | "Having fainted and regained consciousness, he spoke these words to Sanjaya. ||160||" |
| `Line 508: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 509: सञ्जयैवङ्गते प्राणांस्त्यक्तुमिच्छामि माचिरम् |` | "Sanjaya, in this situation, I wish to abandon my life without delay," |
| `Line 510: स्तोकं ह्यपि न पश्यामि फलं जीवितधारणे ॥१६१॥` | "For I see not even the slightest benefit in continuing to live. ||161||" |
| `Line 511: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 512: तं तथावादिनं दीनं विलपन्तं महीपतिम् |` | "To him who was speaking thus, miserable and lamenting, the ruler of the earth," |
| `Line 513: गावल्गणिरिदं धीमान्महार्थं वाक्यमब्रवीत् ॥१६२॥` | "Gavalgani [Sanjaya's patronymic] the wise one spoke these profound words. ||162||" |
| `Line 514: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 515: श्रुतवानसि वै राज्ञो महोत्साहान्महाबलान् |` | "You have indeed heard of kings of great enthusiasm and great strength," |
| `Line 516: द्वैपायनस्य वदतो नारदस्य च धीमतः ॥१६३॥` | "From the narrations of Dvaipayana [Vyasa] and the wise Narada. ||163||" |
| `Line 517: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 518: महत्सु राजवंशेषु गुणैः समुदितेषु च |` | "Born in great royal dynasties, endowed with excellent qualities," |
| `Line 519: जातान्दिव्यास्त्रविदुषः शक्रप्रतिमतेजसः ॥१६४॥` | "Born knowers of divine weapons, with splendor equal to Shakra [Indra]. ||164||" |
| `Line 520: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 521: धर्मेण पृथिवीं जित्वा यज्ञैरिष्ट्वाप्तदक्षिणैः |` | "Having conquered the earth righteously, having performed sacrifices with ample gifts," |
| `Line 522: अस्मिँल्लोके यशः प्राप्य ततः कालवशं गताः ॥१६५॥` | "Having attained fame in this world, they then succumbed to the power of time. ||165||" |
| `Line 523: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 524: वैन्यं महारथं वीरं सृञ्जयं जयतां वरम् |` | "Vainya [King Prithu] the great chariot-warrior, the heroic Srinjaya, foremost among conquerors," |
| `Line 525: सुहोत्रं रन्तिदेवं च कक्षीवन्तं तथौशिजम् ॥१६६॥` | "Suhotra, Rantideva, Kakshivanta, and also Aushija [Kakshivan's son]. ||166||" |
| `Line 526: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 527: बाह्लीकं दमनं शैब्यं शर्यातिमजितं जितम् |` | "Bāhlīka, Damana, Śaibya, Śaryāti, Ajita, Jita," |
| `Line 528: विश्वामित्रममित्रघ्नमम्बरीषं महाबलम् ||१६७||` | "Viśvāmitra the destroyer of enemies, Ambarīṣa of great strength. ||167||" |
| `Line 529: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 530: मरुत्तं मनुमिक्ष्वाकुं गयं भरतमेव च |` | "Marutta, Manu, Ikṣvāku, Gaya, and Bharata too," |
| `Line 531: रामं दाशरथिं चैव शशबिन्दुं भगीरथम् ||१६८||` | "And Rāma the son of Daśaratha, Śaśabindu, and Bhagīratha. ||168||" |
| `Line 532: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 533: ययातिं शुभकर्माणं देवैर्यो याजितः स्वयम् |` | "Yayāti of virtuous deeds, who was himself worshipped by the gods," |
| `Line 534: चैत्ययूपाङ्किता भूमिर्यस्येयं सवनाकरा ||१६९||` | "Whose land was marked with sacrificial posts [yūpa] and filled with sacred groves. ||169||" |
| `Line 535: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 536: इति राज्ञां चतुर्विंशन्नारदेन सुरर्षिणा |` | "Thus these twenty-four kings were by Nārada, the divine sage," |
| `Line 537: पुत्रशोकाभितप्ताय पुरा शैब्याय कीर्तिताः ||१७०||` | "Recounted in the past to Śaibya who was afflicted with grief for his son. ||170||" |
| `Line 538: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 539: तेभ्यश्चान्ये गताः पूर्वं राजानो बलवत्तराः |` | "And before them went other kings who were even mightier," |
| `Line 540: महारथा महात्मानो सर्वैः समुदिता गुणैः ||१७१||` | "Great chariot-warriors [maharathas], great souls, endowed with all excellent qualities. ||171||" |
| `Line 541: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 542: पूरुः कुरुर्यदुः शूरो विष्वगश्वो महाधृतिः |` | "Pūru, Kuru, Yadu, Śūra, Viṣvagaśva of great resolve," |
| `Line 543: अनेना युवनाश्वश्च ककुत्स्थो विक्रमी रघुः ||१७२||` | "Anena, Yuvanāśva, Kakutstha, and the valiant Raghu. ||172||" |
| `Line 544: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 545: विजिती वीतिहोत्रश्च भवः श्वेतो बृहद्गुरुः |` | "Vijitī, Vītihotra, Bhava, Śveta, Bṛhadguru," |
| `Line 546: उशीनरः शतरथः कङ्को दुलिदुहो द्रुमः ||१७३||` | "Uśīnara, Śataratha, Kaṅka, Duliduha, Druma. ||173||" |
| `Line 547: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 548: दम्भोद्भवः परो वेनः सगरः सङ्कृतिर्निमिः |` | "Dambhodbhava, Para, Vena, Sagara, Saṅkṛti, Nimi," |
| `Line 549: अजेयः परशुः पुण्ड्रः शम्भुर्देवावृधोऽनघः ||१७४||` | "Ajeya, Paraśu, Puṇḍra, Śambhu, Devāvṛdha the sinless one. ||174||" |
| `Line 550: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 551: देवाह्वयः सुप्रतिमः सुप्रतीको बृहद्रथः |` | "Devāhvaya, Supratima, Supratīka, Brihadratha," |
| `Line 552: महोत्साहो विनीतात्मा सुक्रतुर्नैषधो नलः ||१७५||` | "Mahotsāha, Vinītātmā, Sukratu, and Nala of Nishadha [famous king]. ||175||" |
| `Line 553: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 554: सत्यव्रतः शान्तभयः सुमित्रः सुबलः प्रभुः |` | "Satyavrata, Śāntabhaya, Sumitra, Subala, Prabhu," |
| `Line 555: जानुजङ्घोऽनरण्योऽर्कः प्रियभृत्यः शुभव्रतः ||१७६||` | "Jānujaṅgha, Anaraṇya, Arka, Priyabhṛtya, Śubhavrata. ||176||" |
| `Line 556: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 557: बलबन्धुर्निरामर्दः केतुशृङ्गो बृहद्बलः |` | "Balabandhu, Nirāmarda, Ketuśṛṅga, Brihadbala," |
| `Line 558: धृष्टकेतुर्बृहत्केतुर्दीप्तकेतुर्निरामयः ||१७७||` | "Dhṛṣṭaketu, Bṛhatketu, Dīptaketu, Nirāmaya. ||177||" |
| `Line 559: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 560: अविक्षित्प्रबलो धूर्तः कृतबन्धुर्दृढेषुधिः |` | "Avikṣit, Prabala, Dhūrta, Kṛtabandhu, Dṛḍheṣudhi," |
| `Line 561: महापुराणः सम्भाव्यः प्रत्यङ्गः परहा श्रुतिः ||१७८||` | "Mahāpurāṇa, Sambhāvya, Pratyaṅga, Parahā, Śruti. ||178||" |
| `Line 562: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 563: एते चान्ये च बहवः शतशोऽथ सहस्रशः |` | "These and many others, by hundreds and thousands," |
| `Line 564: श्रूयन्तेऽयुतशश्चान्ये सङ्ख्याताश्चापि पद्मशः ||१७९||` | "Are heard of in tens of thousands, and others counted by millions [padmas]. ||179||" |
| `Line 565: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 566: हित्वा सुविपुलान्भोगान्बुद्धिमन्तो महाबलाः |` | "Having abandoned vast enjoyments, these intelligent and mighty," |
| `Line 567: राजानो निधनं प्राप्तास्तव पुत्रैर्महत्तमाः ||१८०||` | "Greatest of kings have met their death at the hands of your sons. ||180||" |
| `Line 568: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 569: येषां दिव्यानि कर्माणि विक्रमस्त्याग एव च |` | "Whose divine deeds, valor, and generosity," |
| `Line 570: माहात्म्यमपि चास्तिक्यं सत्यता शौचमार्जवम् ||१८१||` | "As well as greatness, faith, truthfulness, purity, and straightforwardness, ||181||" |
| `Line 571: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 572: विद्वद्भिः कथ्यते लोके पुराणैः कविसत्तमैः |` | "Are spoken of in the world by the learned, by ancient [purāṇas] and excellent poets," |
| `Line 573: सर्वर्द्धिगुणसम्पन्नास्ते चापि निधनं गताः ||१८२||` | "They too, endowed with all prosperous qualities, have met their end. ||182||" |
| `Line 574: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 575: तव पुत्रा दुरात्मानः प्रतप्ताश्चैव मन्युना |` | "Your sons, evil-souled and consumed by anger," |
| `Line 576: लुब्धा दुर्वृत्तभूयिष्ठा न ताञ्शोचितुमर्हसि ||१८३||` | "They were greedy and mostly of bad conduct; you should not grieve for them. ||183||" |
| `Line 577: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 578: श्रुतवानसि मेधावी बुद्धिमान्प्राज्ञसंमतः |` | "You are learned, intelligent, wise, and respected by the wise." |
| `Line 579: येषां शास्त्रानुगा बुद्धिर्न ते मुह्यन्ति भारत ||१८४||` | "Those whose intellect follows the scriptures [śāstras] do not become deluded, O Bhārata [Dhritarashtra]. ||184||" |
| `Line 580: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 581: निग्रहानुग्रहौ चापि विदितौ ते नराधिप |` | "Punishment and favor are both known to you, O ruler of men." |
| `Line 582: नात्यन्तमेवानुवृत्तिः श्रूयते पुत्ररक्षणे ||१८५||` | "Excessive attachment is not prescribed in the protection of sons. ||185||" |
| `Line 583: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 584: भवितव्यं तथा तच्च नातः शोचितुमर्हसि |` | "What is destined to happen will happen thus; therefore you should not grieve." |
| `Line 585: दैवं प्रज्ञाविशेषेण को निवर्तितुमर्हति ||१८६||` | "Who can avert fate [divine will] even with exceptional wisdom? ||186||" |
| `Line 586: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 587: विधातृविहितं मार्गं न कश्चिदतिवर्तते |` | "No one can transgress the path ordained by the Creator [Vidhātṛ]." |
| `Line 588: कालमूलमिदं सर्वं भावाभावौ सुखासुखे ||१८७||` | "All this—existence and non-existence, happiness and sorrow—is rooted in Time [Kāla]. ||187||" |
| `Line 589: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 590: कालः पचति भूतानि कालः संहरति प्रजाः |` | "Time ripens all beings; Time destroys all creatures." |
| `Line 591: निर्दहन्तं प्रजाः कालं कालः शमयते पुनः ||१८८||` | "Time, which consumes all creatures, is itself pacified by Time again. ||188||" |
| `Line 592: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 593: कालो विकुरुते भावान्सर्वाँल्लोके शुभाशुभान् |` | "Time transforms all states in the world, both auspicious and inauspicious." |
| `Line 594: कालः सङ्क्षिपते सर्वाः प्रजा विसृजते पुनः ||१८९||` | "Time contracts all beings and creates them again. ||189||" |
| `Line 595: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 596: कालः सर्वेषु भूतेषु चरत्यविधृतः समः ||१८९||` | "Time moves among all beings, unrestrained and impartial. ||189||" |
| `Line 597: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 598: अतीतानागता भावा ये च वर्तन्ति साम्प्रतम् |` | "All conditions—past, future, and those existing at present—" |
| `Line 599: तान्कालनिर्मितान्बुद्ध्वा न सञ्ज्ञां हातुमर्हसि ||१९०||` | "Understanding them to be created by Time, you should not lose your composure. ||190||" |
| `Line 600: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 601: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 602: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 603: अत्रोपनिषदं पुण्यां कृष्णद्वैपायनोऽब्रवीत् |` | "Here, Krishna Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] spoke this sacred Upanishad [esoteric teaching]," |
| `Line 604: भारताध्ययनात्पुण्यादपि पादमधीयतः ||१९१||` | "Even for one who studies just a quarter of the holy Bhārata [Mahābhārata]. ||191||" |
| `Line 605: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 606: श्रद्दधानस्य पूयन्ते सर्वपापान्यशेषतः ||१९१||` | "For the one who has faith, all sins are purified completely. ||191||" |
| `Line 607: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 608: देवर्षयो ह्यत्र पुण्या ब्रह्मराजर्षयस्तथा |` | "Indeed, here the divine sages, the brahmarṣis [Brahmin sages] and rājarṣis [royal sages]," |
| `Line 609: कीर्त्यन्ते शुभकर्माणस्तथा यक्षमहोरगाः ||१९२||` | "Are glorified for their auspicious deeds, as well as the Yakṣas [demigods] and Mahoragas [great serpents]. ||192||" |
| `Line 610: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 611: भगवान्वासुदेवश्च कीर्त्यतेऽत्र सनातनः |` | "And Lord Vāsudeva [Krishna], the eternal one, is glorified here," |
| `Line 612: स हि सत्यमृतं चैव पवित्रं पुण्यमेव च ||१९३||` | "For he is truth, immortality, purity, and virtue indeed. ||193||" |
| `Line 613: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 614: शाश्वतं ब्रह्म परमं ध्रुवं ज्योतिः सनातनम् |` | "The eternal Brahman [Absolute], supreme, immutable, the eternal light," |
| `Line 615: यस्य दिव्यानि कर्माणि कथयन्ति मनीषिणः ||१९४||` | "Whose divine deeds the wise ones narrate. ||194||" |
| `Line 616: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 617: असत्सत्सदसच्चैव यस्माद्देवात्प्रवर्तते |` | "From which deity proceeds the unmanifest, the manifest, and that which is both manifest and unmanifest," |
| `Line 618: सन्ततिश्च प्रवृत्तिश्च जन्म मृत्युः पुनर्भवः ||१९५||` | "And continuity, activity, birth, death, and rebirth. ||195||" |
| `Line 619: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 620: अध्यात्मं श्रूयते यच्च पञ्चभूतगुणात्मकम् |` | "And what is heard as spiritual knowledge, composed of the qualities of the five elements," |
| `Line 621: अव्यक्तादि परं यच्च स एव परिगीयते ||१९६||` | "And that which is beyond the unmanifest beginning—He alone is celebrated. ||196||" |
| `Line 622: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 623: यत्तद्यतिवरा युक्ता ध्यानयोगबलान्विताः |` | "That which the best of ascetics [yatis], concentrated and endowed with the power of meditation yoga," |
| `Line 624: प्रतिबिम्बमिवादर्शे पश्यन्त्यात्मन्यवस्थितम् ||१९७||` | "See established in their own self, like a reflection in a mirror. ||197||" |
| `Line 625: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 626: श्रद्दधानः सदोद्युक्तः सत्यधर्मपरायणः |` | "One who is faithful, always diligent, and devoted to truth and righteousness," |
| `Line 627: आसेवन्निममध्यायं नरः पापात्प्रमुच्यते ||१९८||` | "A person who regularly studies this chapter is freed from sins. ||198||" |
| `Line 628: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 629: अनुक्रमणिमध्यायं भारतस्येममादितः |` | "This index chapter [anukramaṇi] of the Bharata from the beginning," |
| `Line 630: आस्तिकः सततं शृण्वन्न कृच्छ्रेष्ववसीदति ||१९९||` | "A believer [āstika] who constantly listens to it does not sink in difficulties. ||199||" |
| `Line 631: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 632: उभे सन्ध्ये जपन्किञ्चित्सद्यो मुच्येत किल्बिषात् |` | "One who recites even a little of it at both twilights [dawn and dusk] is immediately freed from sin," |
| `Line 633: अनुक्रमण्या यावत्स्यादह्ना रात्र्या च सञ्चितम् ||२००||` | "Whatever sins are accumulated during day and night, through the index [anukramaṇī]. ||200||" |
| `Line 634: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 635: भारतस्य वपुर्ह्येतत्सत्यं चामृतमेव च |` | "This is indeed the body of the Bharata, both truth and immortality," |
| `Line 636: नवनीतं यथा दध्नो द्विपदां ब्राह्मणो यथा ||२०१||` | "As butter is from curd, as the Brahmin is among bipeds [humans]. ||201||" |
| `Line 637: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 638: ह्रदानामुदधिः श्रेष्ठो गौर्वरिष्ठा चतुष्पदाम् |` | "As the ocean is the best among lakes, as the cow is the foremost among quadrupeds," |
| `Line 639: यथैतानि वरिष्ठानि तथा भारतमुच्यते ||२०२||` | "Just as these are the best, so is the Bharata declared to be. ||202||" |
| `Line 640: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 641: यश्चैनं श्रावयेच्छ्राद्धे ब्राह्मणान्पादमन्ततः |` | "Whoever recites this to Brahmins during a śrāddha [ancestral rite], even just a portion," |
| `Line 642: अक्षय्यमन्नपानं तत्पितृंस्तस्योपतिष्ठति ||२०३||` | "Inexhaustible food and drink reach his ancestors. ||203||" |
| `Line 643: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 644: इतिहासपुराणाभ्यां वेदं समुपबृंहयेत् |` | "One should supplement the Veda with Itihāsas [histories] and Purāṇas [ancient texts]," |
| `Line 645: बिभेत्यल्पश्रुताद्वेदो मामयं प्रतरिष्यति ||२०४||` | "The Veda fears one of little learning, thinking 'he will misinterpret me'. ||204||" |
| `Line 646: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 647: कार्ष्णं वेदमिमं विद्वाञ्श्रावयित्वार्थमश्नुते |` | "The learned one, having recited this Veda of Kṛṣṇa [Vyāsa's text], obtains wealth," |
| `Line 648: भ्रूणहत्याकृतं चापि पापं जह्यान्न संशयः ||२०५||` | "And even the sin of killing a fetus [brūṇahatyā] is abandoned, without doubt. ||205||" |
| `Line 649: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 650: य इमं शुचिरध्यायं पठेत्पर्वणि पर्वणि |` | "Whoever, being pure, recites this chapter at each parvan [sacred occasion]," |
| `Line 651: अधीतं भारतं तेन कृत्स्नं स्यादिति मे मतिः ||२०६||` | "The entire Bharata would be studied by him - this is my belief. ||206||" |
| `Line 652: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 653: यश्चेमं शृणुयान्नित्यमार्षं श्रद्धासमन्वितः |` | "And whoever listens to this sage-composed [ārṣa] text regularly with faith," |
| `Line 654: स दीर्घमायुः कीर्तिं च स्वर्गतिं चाप्नुयान्नरः ||२०७||` | "That person attains long life, fame, and the path to heaven [svargati]. ||207||" |
| `Line 655: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 656: चत्वार एकतो वेदा भारतं चैकमेकतः |` | "The four Vedas on one side and the Bharata alone on the other side," |
| `Line 657: समागतैः सुरर्षिभिस्तुलामारोपितं पुरा ||२०८||` | "Were placed on a scale by the assembled divine sages [surarṣi] in ancient times. ||208||" |
| `Line 658: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 659: महत्त्वे च गुरुत्वे च ध्रियमाणं ततोऽधिकम् ||२०८||` | "And in greatness and weight, it was held to be superior. ||208||" |
| `Line 660: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 661: महत्त्वाद्भारवत्त्वाच्च महाभारतमुच्यते |` | "Due to its greatness [mahattva] and weightiness [bhāravattva], it is called the Mahābhārata," |
| `Line 662: निरुक्तमस्य यो वेद सर्वपापैः प्रमुच्यते ||२०९||` | "One who knows this etymology [nirukta] is freed from all sins. ||209||" |
| `Line 663: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 664: तपो न कल्कोऽध्ययनं न कल्कः; स्वाभाविको वेदविधिर्न कल्कः |` | "Austerity is not impurity [kalka], study is not impurity; the natural Vedic procedure is not impurity;" |
| `Line 665: प्रसह्य वित्ताहरणं न कल्क; स्तान्येव भावोपहतानि कल्कः ||२१०||` | "Forcible taking of wealth is not impurity; these very things when corrupted by evil intent become impurity. ||210||" |
| `Line 666: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 668: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 669: ` | [Blank line] |
