| `Line 671: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 672: पर्वसंग्रहपर्व` | "Parvasaṃgraha Parva [Chapter summarizing sections]" |
| `Line 673: २` | "2" |
| `Line 674: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 675: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 676: ऋषय ऊचुः॥` | "The sages said:" |
| `Line 677: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 678: समन्तपञ्चकमिति यदुक्तं सूतनन्दन |` | "O Sūta-nandana [son of Sūta], what has been mentioned as Samantapañcaka [five lakes region]," |
| `Line 679: एतत्सर्वं यथान्यायं श्रोतुमिच्छामहे वयम् ॥१॥` | "All this we wish to hear properly in detail. ||1||" |
| `Line 680: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 681: सूत उवाच॥` | "Sūta said:" |
| `Line 682: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 683: शुश्रूषा यदि वो विप्रा ब्रुवतश्च कथाः शुभाः |` | "If you, O Vipras [learned Brahmins], wish to listen to auspicious stories from me," |
| `Line 684: समन्तपञ्चकाख्यं च श्रोतुमर्हथ सत्तमाः ॥२॥` | "Then you deserve to hear about the place called Samantapañcaka, O excellent ones. ||2||" |
| `Line 685: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 686: त्रेताद्वापरयोः सन्धौ रामः शस्त्रभृतां वरः |` | "At the junction of Tretā and Dvāpara [yugas/ages], Rāma [Paraśurāma], the best among weapon-bearers," |
| `Line 687: असकृत्पार्थिवं क्षत्रं जघानामर्षचोदितः ॥३॥` | "Repeatedly slaughtered the Kṣatriya [warrior] class, impelled by anger. ||3||" |
| `Line 688: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 689: स सर्वं क्षत्रमुत्साद्य स्ववीर्येणानलद्युतिः |` | "Having exterminated the entire Kṣatriya class by his own prowess, he who had the brilliance of fire," |
| `Line 690: समन्तपञ्चके पञ्च चकार रुधिरह्रदान् ॥४॥` | "Created five lakes of blood at Samantapañcaka. ||4||" |
| `Line 691: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 692: स तेषु रुधिराम्भस्सु ह्रदेषु क्रोधमूर्च्छितः |` | "In those lakes filled with bloody waters, overcome with rage," |
| `Line 693: पितृन्सन्तर्पयामास रुधिरेणेति नः श्रुतम् ॥५॥` | "He satisfied his ancestors with blood offerings - thus we have heard. ||5||" |
| `Line 694: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 695: अथर्चीकादयोऽभ्येत्य पितरो ब्राह्मणर्षभम् |` | "Then, approaching the bull among Brahmins [Paraśurāma], his ancestors led by Ṛcīka," |
| `Line 696: तं क्षमस्वेति सिषिधुस्ततः स विरराम ह ॥६॥` | "Restrained him saying, 'Desist from this,' and then he stopped. ||6||" |
| `Line 697: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 698: तेषां समीपे यो देशो ह्रदानां रुधिराम्भसाम् |` | "That region which is near those lakes of bloody waters," |
| `Line 699: समन्तपञ्चकमिति पुण्यं तत्परिकीर्तितम् ॥७॥` | "Is celebrated as the sacred Samantapañcaka. ||7||" |
| `Line 700: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 701: येन लिङ्गेन यो देशो युक्तः समुपलक्ष्यते |` | "By which characteristic a region is observed to be distinguished," |
| `Line 702: तेनैव नाम्ना तं देशं वाच्यमाहुर्मनीषिणः ||८||` | "By that very name that region should be called, say the wise ones. ||8||" |
| `Line 703: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 704: अन्तरे चैव सम्प्राप्ते कलिद्वापरयोरभूत् |` | "And when the interval between Kali [dark age] and Dvapara [third age] arrived," |
| `Line 705: समन्तपञ्चके युद्धं कुरुपाण्डवसेनयोः ||९||` | "At Samantapanchaka [five lakes region] occurred the war between the armies of the Kurus and Pandavas. ||9||" |
| `Line 706: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 707: तस्मिन्परमधर्मिष्ठे देशे भूदोषवर्जिते |` | "In that most righteous region, free from defects of the earth," |
| `Line 708: अष्टादश समाजग्मुरक्षौहिण्यो युयुत्सया ||१०||` | "Eighteen akshauhinis [army divisions] assembled with the desire to fight. ||10||" |
| `Line 709: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 710: एवं नामाभिनिर्वृत्तं तस्य देशस्य वै द्विजाः |` | "Thus the derivation of the name of that region, O twice-born [Brahmins]," |
| `Line 711: पुण्यश्च रमणीयश्च स देशो वः प्रकीर्तितः ||११||` | "That sacred and delightful region has been described to you. ||11||" |
| `Line 712: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 713: तदेतत्कथितं सर्वं मया वो मुनिसत्तमाः |` | "All this has been told by me to you, O best of sages," |
| `Line 714: यथा देशः स विख्यातस्त्रिषु लोकेषु विश्रुतः ||१२||` | "How that region became renowned, celebrated in the three worlds [heaven, earth, netherworld]. ||12||" |
| `Line 715: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 716: ऋषय ऊचुः||` | "The sages said:" |
| `Line 717: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 718: अक्षौहिण्य इति प्रोक्तं यत्त्वया सूतनन्दन |` | "What you have mentioned as 'akshauhinis', O son of Suta [bard/charioteer]," |
| `Line 719: एतदिच्छामहे श्रोतुं सर्वमेव यथातथम् ||१३||` | "We wish to hear all about this exactly as it is. ||13||" |
| `Line 720: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 721: अक्षौहिण्याः परीमाणं रथाश्वनरदन्तिनाम् |` | "The measure of an akshauhini in terms of chariots, horses, men, and elephants," |
| `Line 722: यथावच्चैव नो ब्रूहि सर्वं हि विदितं तव ||१४||` | "Tell us properly, for everything is known to you. ||14||" |
| `Line 723: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 724: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 725: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 726: एको रथो गजश्चैको नराः पञ्च पदातयः |` | "One chariot, one elephant, five men as foot-soldiers," |
| `Line 727: त्रयश्च तुरगास्तज्ज्ञैः पत्तिरित्यभिधीयते ||१५||` | "And three horses - by those who know, this is called a patti [basic military unit]. ||15||" |
| `Line 728: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 729: पत्तिं तु त्रिगुणामेतामाहुः सेनामुखं बुधाः |` | "The wise call three such pattis a senāmukha [battalion head]," |
| `Line 730: त्रीणि सेनामुखान्येको गुल्म इत्यभिधीयते ||१६||` | "Three senāmukhas are called one gulma [troop division]. ||16||" |
| `Line 731: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 732: त्रयो गुल्मा गणो नाम वाहिनी तु गणास्त्रयः |` | "Three gulmas are named a gaṇa [brigade], and three gaṇas are a vāhinī [division]," |
| `Line 733: स्मृतास्तिस्रस्तु वाहिन्यः पृतनेति विचक्षणैः ||१७||` | "Three vāhinīs are remembered by the discerning as a pṛtanā [army corps]. ||17||" |
| `Line 734: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 735: चमूस्तु पृतनास्तिस्रस्तिस्रश्चम्वस्त्वनीकिनी |` | "Three pṛtanās make a camū [army], and three camūs make an anīkinī [large army]," |
| `Line 736: अनीकिनीं दशगुणां प्राहुरक्षौहिणीं बुधाः ||१८||` | "The wise declare ten anīkinīs to be an akṣauhiṇī [complete army]. ||18||" |
| `Line 737: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 738: अक्षौहिण्याः प्रसङ्ख्यानं रथानां द्विजसत्तमाः |` | "The enumeration of chariots in an akṣauhiṇī, O best of twice-born [Brahmins]," |
| `Line 739: सङ्ख्यागणिततत्त्वज्ञैः सहस्राण्येकविंशतिः ||१९||` | "According to those who know the principles of numerical calculation, is twenty-one thousand. ||19||" |
| `Line 740: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 741: शतान्युपरि चैवाष्टौ तथा भूयश्च सप्ततिः |` | "And eight hundred, and furthermore seventy," |
| `Line 742: गजानां तु परीमाणमेतदेवात्र निर्दिशेत् ||२०||` | "The measure of elephants should be indicated as exactly the same here. ||20||" |
| `Line 743: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 744: ज्ञेयं शतसहस्रं तु सहस्राणि तथा नव |` | "It should be known that one hundred thousand and nine thousand," |
| `Line 745: नराणामपि पञ्चाशच्छतानि त्रीणि चानघाः ||२१||` | "And fifty and three hundred men, O sinless ones [sages]. ||21||" |
| `Line 746: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 747: पञ्चषष्टिसहस्राणि तथाश्वानां शतानि च |` | "Sixty-five thousand, and hundreds of horses," |
| `Line 748: दशोत्तराणि षट्प्राहुर्यथावदिह सङ्ख्यया ||२२||` | "Six hundred and ten more, they declare here according to the proper count. ||22||" |
| `Line 749: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 750: एतामक्षौहिणीं प्राहुः सङ्ख्यातत्त्वविदो जनाः |` | "This is what those who know the principles of enumeration declare to be an akṣauhiṇī [complete army]." |
| `Line 751: यां वः कथितवानस्मि विस्तरेण द्विजोत्तमाः ||२३||` | "Which I have narrated to you in detail, O best of the twice-born [Brahmins]. ||23||" |
| `Line 752: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 753: एतया सङ्ख्यया ह्यासन्कुरुपाण्डवसेनयोः |` | "According to this enumeration, the armies of the Kurus and Pandavas" |
| `Line 754: अक्षौहिण्यो द्विजश्रेष्ठाः पिण्डेनाष्टादशैव ताः ||२४||` | "Consisted of exactly eighteen akshauhinis [complete armies] in total, O foremost of the twice-born. ||24||" |
| `Line 755: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 756: समेतास्तत्र वै देशे तत्रैव निधनं गताः |` | "Assembled in that place, they met their destruction in that very place," |
| `Line 757: कौरवान्कारणं कृत्वा कालेनाद्भुतकर्मणा ||२५||` | "With the Kauravas as the cause, by Time [destiny] of wonderful deeds. ||25||" |
| `Line 758: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 759: अहानि युयुधे भीष्मो दशैव परमास्त्रवित् |` | "Bhishma, the supreme weapon-knower, fought for exactly ten days," |
| `Line 760: अहानि पञ्च द्रोणस्तु ररक्ष कुरुवाहिनीम् ||२६||` | "While Drona protected the Kuru army for five days. ||26||" |
| `Line 761: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 762: अहनी युयुधे द्वे तु कर्णः परबलार्दनः |` | "Karna, the tormentor of enemy forces, fought for two days," |
| `Line 763: शल्योऽर्धदिवसं त्वासीद्गदायुद्धमतः परम् ||२७||` | "Shalya was (commander) for half a day, and after that was the mace duel. ||27||" |
| `Line 764: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 765: तस्यैव तु दिनस्यान्ते हार्दिक्यद्रौणिगौतमाः |` | "At the end of that very day, Hardikya [Kritavarma], Drauni [Ashvatthama], and Gautama [Kripa]" |
| `Line 766: प्रसुप्तं निशि विश्वस्तं जघ्नुर्यौधिष्ठिरं बलम् ||२८||` | "Slew the sleeping, unsuspecting Pandava army at night. ||28||" |
| `Line 767: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 768: यत्तु शौनकसत्रे ते भारताख्यानविस्तरम् |` | "But in Shaunaka's sacrificial session, the detailed narration of the Bharata story" |
| `Line 769: आख्यास्ये तत्र पौलोममाख्यानं चादितः परम् ||२९||` | "I shall narrate there, beginning with the excellent Pauloma tale. ||29||" |
| `Line 770: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 771: विचित्रार्थपदाख्यानमनेकसमयान्वितम् |` | "A narrative with diverse meanings and words, containing many contexts," |
| `Line 772: अभिपन्नं नरैः प्राज्ञैर्वैराग्यमिव मोक्षिभिः ||३०||` | "Sought after by wise men, like detachment is by those seeking liberation. ||30||" |
| `Line 773: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 774: आत्मेव वेदितव्येषु प्रियेष्विव च जीवितम् |` | "Like the Self among things to be known, like life among things dear," |
| `Line 775: इतिहासः प्रधानार्थः श्रेष्ठः सर्वागमेष्वयम् ||३१||` | "This history [Mahabharata] with its principal meaning is the best among all scriptures. ||31||" |
| `Line 776: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 777: इतिहासोत्तमे ह्यस्मिन्नर्पिता बुद्धिरुत्तमा |` | "In this supreme historical narrative [itihāsa], the finest intellect has been invested," |
| `Line 778: स्वरव्यञ्जनयोः कृत्स्ना लोकवेदाश्रयेव वाक् ||३२||` | "Complete in vowels and consonants, like speech founded on worldly knowledge and Vedas. ||32||" |
| `Line 779: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 780: अस्य प्रज्ञाभिपन्नस्य विचित्रपदपर्वणः |` | "Of this wisdom-filled narrative with its diverse chapters and sections," |
| `Line 781: भारतस्येतिहासस्य श्रूयतां पर्वसङ्ग्रहः ||३३||` | "Listen to the summary of sections of the historical narrative [itihāsa] of Bharata. ||33||" |
| `Line 782: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 783: पर्वानुक्रमणी पूर्वं द्वितीयं पर्वसङ्ग्रहः |` | "First is the table of contents [Parvānukramaṇī], second is the summary of sections [Parvasaṅgraha]," |
| `Line 784: पौष्यं पौलोममास्तीकमादिवंशावतारणम् ||३४||` | "The Paushya, Pauloma, Āstīka, and the Descent of the First Dynasty [Ādivaṃśāvataraṇa]. ||34||" |
| `Line 785: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 786: ततः सम्भवपर्वोक्तमद्भुतं देवनिर्मितम् |` | "Then comes the marvelous divine-created section called Sambhava [Origin]," |
| `Line 787: दाहो जतुगृहस्यात्र हैडिम्बं पर्व चोच्यते ||३५||` | "The burning of the lac house is here, and the section called Hiḍimba is mentioned. ||35||" |
| `Line 788: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 789: ततो बकवधः पर्व पर्व चैत्ररथं ततः |` | "Then comes the section on the slaying of Baka, and then the Chaitraratha section," |
| `Line 790: ततः स्वयंवरं देव्याः पाञ्चाल्याः पर्व चोच्यते ||३६||` | "Then is mentioned the section on the self-choice [svayaṃvara] of the Panchala princess [Draupadi]. ||36||" |
| `Line 791: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 792: क्षत्रधर्मेण निर्जित्य ततो वैवाहिकं स्मृतम् |` | "Having conquered according to Kshatriya duty, then comes the section on marriage [Vaivāhika]," |
| `Line 793: विदुरागमनं पर्व राज्यलम्भस्तथैव च ||३७||` | "The section on Vidura's arrival, and likewise the obtaining of the kingdom. ||37||" |
| `Line 794: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 795: अर्जुनस्य वने वासः सुभद्राहरणं ततः |` | "Arjuna's dwelling in the forest, then the abduction of Subhadra," |
| `Line 796: सुभद्राहरणादूर्ध्वं ज्ञेयं हरणहारिकम् ||३८||` | "After the abduction of Subhadra, know the section called Haraṇahārika [Gifts after abduction]. ||38||" |
| `Line 797: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 799: सभापर्व ततः प्रोक्तं मन्त्रपर्व ततः परम् ||३९||` | "Then is declared the Assembly Hall section [Sabhāparva], and after that the Council section [Mantraparva]. ||39||" |
| `Line 800: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 802: पर्व दिग्विजयादूर्ध्वं राजसूयिकमुच्यते ||४०||` | "After the chapter of world conquest, the chapter concerning the Rājasūya [royal consecration] is described. ||40||" |
| `Line 803: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 805: द्यूतपर्व ततः प्रोक्तमनुद्यूतमतः परम् ||४१||` | "Then is described the Gambling chapter, and after that the Consequent Gambling chapter. ||41||" |
| `Line 806: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 808: ईश्वरार्जुनयोर्युद्धं पर्व कैरातसञ्ज्ञितम् ||४२||` | "The battle between Īśvara [Śiva] and Arjuna, the chapter known as Kirāta [hunter form of Śiva]. ||42||" |

| `Line 811: तीर्थयात्रा ततः पर्व कुरुराजस्य धीमतः ||४३||` | "Then the chapter of the pilgrimage of the wise Kuru king [Yudhiṣṭhira]. ||43||" |
| `Line 812: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 814: तथैवाजगरं पर्व विज्ञेयं तदनन्तरम् ||४४||` | "And likewise the Ajagara [python] chapter should be known thereafter. ||44||" |
| `Line 815: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 817: संवादश्च ततः पर्व द्रौपदीसत्यभामयोः ||४५||` | "And then the chapter of the conversation between Draupadī and Satyabhāmā. ||45||" |
| `Line 818: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 820: व्रीहिद्रौणिकमाख्यानं ततोऽनन्तरमुच्यते ||४६||` | "The story of the measure of rice [vrīhidroṇika] is described immediately after that. ||46||" |
| `Line 821: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 823: कुण्डलाहरणं पर्व ततः परमिहोच्यते ||४७||` | "The chapter of the taking of the earrings is described here after that. ||47||" |
| `Line 824: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 825: आरणेयं ततः पर्व वैराटं तदनन्तरम् |` | "Then the Āraṇeya chapter, and after that the Virāṭa chapter," |
| `Line 826: कीचकानां वधः पर्व पर्व गोग्रहणं ततः ||४८||` | "The section on the slaying of the Kīcakas [Matsya generals], and then the section on the cattle-raid [Go-grahaṇa]. ||48||" |
| `Line 827: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 829: उद्योगपर्व विज्ञेयमत ऊर्ध्वं महाद्भुतम् ||४९||` | "After this, the highly wonderful Udyoga Parva [Effort section] should be known. ||49||" |
| `Line 830: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 835: यानसन्धिस्ततः पर्व भगवद्यानमेव च ||५१||` | "Then the section on Yāna-sandhi [Preparation for march], and also the section on Bhagavad-yāna [Lord's journey]. ||51||" |
| `Line 836: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 838: निर्याणं पर्व च ततः कुरुपाण्डवसेनयोः ||५२||` | "And then the section on the marching forth of the armies of the Kurus and Pāṇḍavas. ||52||" |

| `Line 841: उलूकदूतागमनं पर्वामर्षविवर्धनम् ||५३||` | "The section on the arrival of Ulūka as messenger, which increases anger [provocation]. ||53||" |
| `Line 842: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 844: भीष्माभिषेचनं पर्व ज्ञेयमद्भुतकारणम् ||५४||` | "The section on the installation of Bhīṣma [as commander], which should be known as causing wonder. ||54||" |
| `Line 845: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 856: मोक्षो नारायणास्त्रस्य पर्वानन्तरमुच्यते ||५८||` | "The release of the Nārāyaṇāstra [divine weapon] is described in the section immediately following. ||58||" |
| `Line 857: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 859: ह्रदप्रवेशनं पर्व गदायुद्धमतः परम् ||५९||` | "The Hrada-praveshana Parva [lake-entering section] and after that the Gadāyuddha [mace battle section]. ||59||" |

| `Line 863: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 866: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 872: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 874: आपद्धर्मश्च पर्वोक्तं मोक्षधर्मस्ततः परम् ||६४||` | "And the Apad-dharma [emergency duties] section is described, followed by the Moksha-dharma [liberation principles]. ||64||" |

| `Line 877: स्वर्गारोहणिकं पर्व ततो भीष्मस्य धीमतः ||६५||` | "And then the Svargārohaṇika Parva [Ascent to Heaven section] of the wise Bhīṣhma. ||65||" |

| `Line 880: अनुगीता ततः पर्व ज्ञेयमध्यात्मवाचकम् ||६६||` | "Then should be known the Anugītā Parva [Subsequent Song section], which speaks of spiritual knowledge. ||66||" |
| `Line 881: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 883: नारदागमनं पर्व ततः परमिहोच्यते ||६७||` | "Then the section called Nāradāgamana [Nārada's Arrival] is described here next. ||67||" |
| `Line 884: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 886: महाप्रस्थानिकं पर्व स्वर्गारोहणिकं ततः ||६८||` | "The Mahāprasthānika Parva [Great Departure section], and then the Svargārohaṇika [Ascent to Heaven section]. ||68||" |

| `Line 889: भविष्यत्पर्व चाप्युक्तं खिलेष्वेवाद्भुतं महत् ||६९||` | "And also the Bhaviṣyat Parva [Future section] is mentioned, a great and wonderful supplement. ||69||" |
| `Line 890: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 891: एतत्पर्वशतं पूर्णं व्यासेनोक्तं महात्मना |` | "This complete hundred of sections was narrated by the great-souled Vyāsa," |
| `Line 892: यथावत्सूतपुत्रेण लोमहर्षणिना पुनः ||७०||` | "And then properly retold by the son of a sūta [bard], Lomaharṣaṇa. ||70||" |
| `Line 893: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 894: कथितं नैमिषारण्ये पर्वाण्यष्टादशैव तु |` | "Narrated in the Naimiṣāraṇya [Naimiṣa forest], these eighteen sections," |
| `Line 895: समासो भारतस्यायं तत्रोक्तः पर्वसङ्ग्रहः ||७१||` | "This is the summary of the Bhārata, the collection of sections described therein. ||71||" |
| `Line 896: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 897: पौष्ये पर्वणि माहात्म्यमुत्तङ्कस्योपवर्णितम् |` | "In the Pauṣya Parva [Pauṣya section], the greatness of Uttaṅka is described," |
| `Line 898: पौलोमे भृगुवंशस्य विस्तारः परिकीर्तितः ||७२||` | "In the Pauloma [Pauloma section], the expansion of Bhṛgu's lineage is celebrated. ||72||" |
| `Line 899: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 900: आस्तीके सर्वनागानां गरुडस्य च सम्भवः |` | "In the Āstīka [Āstīka section], the origin of all serpents and of Garuḍa [divine eagle]," |
| `Line 901: क्षीरोदमथनं चैव जन्मोच्छैःश्रवसस्तथा ||७३||` | "And the churning of the milk ocean [Kshīroda], as well as the birth of Uchchaihshravas [divine horse]. ||73||" |
| `Line 902: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 903: यजतः सर्पसत्रेण राज्ञः पारिक्षितस्य च |` | "And of King Parikshit performing the snake sacrifice [Sarpa-satra]," |
| `Line 904: कथेयमभिनिर्वृत्ता भारतानां महात्मनाम् ||७४||` | "This story is completed about the great-souled Bharatas [Kuru dynasty]. ||74||" |
| `Line 905: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 906: विविधाः सम्भवा राज्ञामुक्ताः सम्भवपर्वणि |` | "Various origins of kings are narrated in the Sambhava Parva [Book of Origins]," |
| `Line 907: अन्येषां चैव विप्राणामृषेर्द्वैपायनस्य च ||७५||` | "And of other Brahmins, and of the sage Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] as well. ||75||" |
| `Line 908: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 909: अंशावतरणं चात्र देवानां परिकीर्तितम् |` | "The descent of portions [incarnations] of the gods is described here," |
| `Line 910: दैत्यानां दानवानां च यक्षाणां च महौजसाम् ||७६||` | "Of the Daityas [demon class], Dānavas [demon class], and of the mighty Yakshas [wealth spirits]. ||76||" |
| `Line 911: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 912: नागानामथ सर्पाणां गन्धर्वाणां पतत्रिणाम् |` | "Of Nāgas [divine serpents] and serpents, of Gandharvas [celestial musicians] and of winged beings," |
| `Line 913: अन्येषां चैव भूतानां विविधानां समुद्भवः ||७७||` | "And the origin of various other beings as well. ||77||" |
| `Line 914: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 915: वसूनां पुनरुत्पत्तिर्भागीरथ्यां महात्मनाम् |` | "The rebirth of the great-souled Vasus [celestial deities] from Bhāgīrathī [Gangā]," |
| `Line 916: शन्तनोर्वेश्मनि पुनस्तेषां चारोहणं दिवि ||७८||` | "In the house of Shantanu, and their ascension again to heaven. ||78||" |
| `Line 917: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 918: तेजोंशानां च सङ्घाताद्भीष्मस्याप्यत्र सम्भवः |` | "From the collection of portions of splendor, the birth of Bhīshma here," |
| `Line 919: राज्यान्निवर्तनं चैव ब्रह्मचर्यव्रते स्थितिः ||७९||` | "And his renunciation of the kingdom, and establishment in the vow of celibacy [Brahmacharya]. ||79||" |
| `Line 920: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 921: प्रतिज्ञापालनं चैव रक्षा चित्राङ्गदस्य च |` | "And the keeping of his promise, and the protection of Chitrāngada," |
| `Line 922: हते चित्राङ्गदे चैव रक्षा भ्रातुर्यवीयसः ||८०||` | "And when Chitrāngada was slain, the protection of his younger brother. ||80||" |
| `Line 923: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 924: विचित्रवीर्यस्य तथा राज्ये सम्प्रतिपादनम् |` | "The establishment of Vichitravirya in the kingdom," |
| `Line 925: धर्मस्य नृषु सम्भूतिरणीमाण्डव्यशापजा ||८१||` | "The birth of Dharma [Yudhishthira] among men due to the curse of sage Māṇḍavya to Aṇi [Yama]. ||81||" |
| `Line 926: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 928: धृतराष्ट्रस्य पाण्डोश्च पाण्डवानां च सम्भवः ||८२||` | "The birth of Dhritarāshtra and Pāndu, and the origin of the Pāndavas. ||82||" |
| `Line 929: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 931: विदुरस्य च वाक्येन सुरुङ्गोपक्रमक्रिया ||८३||` | "And by Vidura's words, the construction of the underground passage. ||83||" |
| `Line 932: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 934: घटोत्कचस्य चोत्पत्तिरत्रैव परिकीर्तिता ||८४||` | "And the birth of Ghatotkaca is also narrated here. ||84||" |
| `Line 935: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 938: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 941: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 946: द्रौपद्या देवविहितो विवाहश्चाप्यमानुषः ||८८||` | "And Draupadī's divinely ordained marriage, which was superhuman. ||88||" |
| `Line 947: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 949: खाण्डवप्रस्थवासश्च तथा राज्यार्धशासनम् ||८९||` | "The dwelling at Khāṇḍavaprastha [city] and the ruling of half the kingdom. ||89||" |
| `Line 950: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 952: सुन्दोपसुन्दयोस्तत्र उपाख्यानं प्रकीर्तितम् ||९०||` | "And there the tale of Sunda and Upasunda was narrated. ||90||" |
| `Line 953: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 955: पुण्यतीर्थानुसंयानं बभ्रुवाहनजन्म च ||९१||` | "His pilgrimage to sacred places and the birth of Babhruvāhana [Arjuna's son]. ||91||" |
| `Line 956: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 958: वासुदेवस्यानुमते प्राप्ता चैव किरीटिना ||९२||` | "Was obtained by the diadem-wearer [Arjuna] with Vāsudeva's [Krishna's] consent. ||92||" |
| `Line 959: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 972: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 978: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 981: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 984: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 987: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 988: यत्रास्य मन्युरुद्भूतो येन द्यूतमकारयत् |` | "Where his anger arose, because of which he arranged the gambling match." |
| `Line 989: यत्र धर्मसुतं द्यूते शकुनिः कितवोऽजयत् ||१०१||` | "Where Shakuni, the deceitful gambler, defeated Dharma's son [Yudhishthira] in the game. ||101||" |
| `Line 990: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 992: तारयामास तांस्तीर्णाञ्ज्ञात्वा दुर्योधनो नृपः ||१०२||` | "King Duryodhana, knowing they had been saved, ||102||" |

| `Line 995: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 997: अध्यायाः सप्ततिर्ज्ञेयास्तथा द्वौ चात्र सङ्ख्यया ||१०३||` | "Seventy-two chapters are to be known here by count. ||103||" |
| `Line 998: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1001: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1003: पौरानुगमनं चैव धर्मपुत्रस्य धीमतः ||१०५||` | "And the following of the wise Dharmaputra [Yudhiṣṭhira] by the citizens. ||105||" |

| `Line 1009: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1014: युधिष्ठिरस्य चार्तस्य व्यसने परिदेवनम् ||१०८||` | "And the lamentation of the distressed Yudhiṣṭhira in his misfortune. ||108||" |

| `Line 1017: दमयन्त्याः स्थितिर्यत्र नलस्य व्यसनागमे ||१०९||` | "Where is described Damayantī's steadfastness during Nala's misfortune. ||109||" |

| `Line 1021: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1024: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1027: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1036: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1039: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1042: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1044: ताभ्यां च यत्र स मुनिर्यौवनं प्रतिपादितः ||११८||` | "And where that sage was restored to youth by those two. ||118||" |
| `Line 1045: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1047: पुत्रार्थमयजद्राजा लेभे पुत्रशतं च सः ||११९||` | "The king performed a sacrifice for sons and obtained a hundred sons. ||119||" |
| `Line 1048: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1049: अष्टावक्रीयमत्रैव विवादे यत्र बन्दिनम् |` | "Here also is the story of Aṣṭāvakra [eight-crooked sage], where in a debate with Bandin," |
| `Line 1050: विजित्य सागरं प्राप्तं पितरं लब्धवानृषिः ||१२०||` | "Having conquered him, the sage recovered his father who had gone to the ocean. ||120||" |
| `Line 1051: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1052: अवाप्य दिव्यान्यस्त्राणि गुर्वर्थे सव्यसाचिना |` | "Having obtained divine weapons by Savyasāchin [Arjuna] for his teacher's sake," |
| `Line 1053: निवातकवचैर्युद्धं हिरण्यपुरवासिभिः ||१२१||` | "The battle with the Nivātakavacas [demon clan], dwellers of Hiraṇyapura [golden city]. ||121||" |
| `Line 1054: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1056: घोषयात्रा च गन्धर्वैर्यत्र युद्धं किरीटिनः ||१२२||` | "The Ghoṣayātrā [cattle-station expedition] and where the battle of Kirīṭin [Arjuna] with the Gandharvas [celestial musicians] occurred. ||122||" |
| `Line 1057: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1059: जयद्रथेनापहारो द्रौपद्याश्चाश्रमान्तरात् ||१२३||` | "The abduction of Draupadī from the hermitage by Jayadratha. ||123||" |
| `Line 1060: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1063: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1065: व्रीहिद्रौणिकमाख्यानमैन्द्रद्युम्नं तथैव च ||१२५||` | "The tale of Vrīhidrauṇika [rice measure] and likewise that of Indradyumna. ||125||" |

| `Line 1068: रामायणमुपाख्यानमत्रैव बहुविस्तरम् ||१२६||` | "The narrative of the Rāmāyaṇa [Rama's journey] is also here in great detail. ||126||" |
| `Line 1069: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1072: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1074: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1076: अत्राध्यायशते द्वे तु सङ्ख्याते परमर्षिणा ||१२८||` | "Here, two hundred chapters have been enumerated by the great sage [paramarṣi]. ||128||" |
| `Line 1077: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1079: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1082: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1084: विराटनगरं गत्वा श्मशाने विपुलां शमीम् ||१३०||` | "where, having gone to Virāṭa's city, at a cremation ground, a large śamī tree [sacred tree] ||130||" |
| `Line 1085: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1087: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1090: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1093: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1095: अभिमन्युं समुद्दिश्य सौभद्रमरिघातिनम् ||१३३||` | "designating Abhimanyu, the son of Subhadrā, the slayer of foes. ||133||" |

| `Line 1099: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1104: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1106: उपप्लव्ये निविष्टेषु पाण्डवेषु जिगीषया ||१३६||` | "When the Pandavas were settled in Upaplavya with the desire for victory ||136||" |
| `Line 1107: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1109: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1112: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1113: अयुध्यमानमात्मानं मन्त्रिणं पुरुषर्षभौ |` | "'O best among men, myself non-fighting as an advisor,'" |
| `Line 1114: अक्षौहिणीं वा सैन्यस्य कस्य वा किं ददाम्यहम् ||१३८||` | "'Or an Akshauhini [large army unit] of troops - to whom shall I give what?' ||138||" |
| `Line 1115: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1118: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1121: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1123: प्रजागरः सम्प्रजज्ञे धृतराष्ट्रस्य चिन्तया ||१४१||` | "Sleeplessness arose in Dhritarashtra due to anxiety ||141||" |
| `Line 1124: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1127: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1130: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1133: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1135: स्वयमागाच्छमं कर्तुं नगरं नागसाह्वयम् ||१४५||` | "Himself came to make peace to the city called Nagasahvaya [Hastinapura]. ||145||" |
| `Line 1136: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1138: शमार्थं याचमानस्य पक्षयोरुभयोर्हितम् ||१४६||` | "Who was pleading for peace, for the benefit of both sides. ||146||" |
| `Line 1139: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1150: श्वोभाविनि महायुद्धे दूत्येन क्रूरवादिना ||१५०||` | "For the great battle to come tomorrow, as an envoy with harsh words. ||150||" |

| `Line 1162: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1177: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1180: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1182: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1184: यत्र संशप्तकाः पार्थमपनिन्यू रणाजिरात् ||१६०||` | "Where the Saṃśaptakas [oath-bound warriors] drew Pārtha [Arjuna] away from the battlefield. ||160||" |
| `Line 1185: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1187: सुप्रतीकेन नागेन सह शस्तः किरीटिना ||१६१||` | "Along with his elephant Supratīka, was slain by Kirīṭin [Arjuna]. ||161||" |
| `Line 1188: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1189: यत्राभिमन्युं बहवो जघ्नुर्लोकमहारथाः |` | "Where many great warriors of the world slew Abhimanyu," |
| `Line 1190: जयद्रथमुखा बालं शूरमप्राप्तयौवनम् ||१६२||` | "Led by Jayadratha, the brave youth who had not yet reached full maturity. ||162||" |
| `Line 1191: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1192: हतेऽभिमन्यौ क्रुद्धेन यत्र पार्थेन संयुगे |` | "Where, after Abhimanyu was slain, by the enraged Pārtha [Arjuna] in battle," |
| `Line 1193: अक्षौहिणीः सप्त हत्वा हतो राजा जयद्रथः ||१६३||` | "After slaying seven Akṣauhiṇīs [army units], King Jayadratha was killed. ||163||" |
| `Line 1194: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1196: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1197: अलम्बुसः श्रुतायुश्च जलसन्धश्च वीर्यवान् |` | "Alambusa, Śrutāyus, and the mighty Jalasandha," |
| `Line 1198: सौमदत्तिर्विराटश्च द्रुपदश्च महारथः ||१६४||` | "Saumadatti [Bhūriśravas], Virāṭa, and the great warrior Drupada, ||164||" |
| `Line 1199: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1200: घटोत्कचादयश्चान्ये निहता द्रोणपर्वणि ||१६४||` | "Ghaṭotkaca and others were slain in the Droṇa-parvan [Drona book]. ||164||" |
| `Line 1201: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1203: अस्त्रं प्रादुश्चकारोग्रं नारायणममर्षितः ||१६५||` | "Ashvatthama, enraged, unleashed the terrible Narayana [Vishnu's] weapon. ||165||" |
| `Line 1204: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1206: अत्र ते पृथिवीपालाः प्रायशो निधनं गताः ||१६६||` | "Wherein those rulers of the earth mostly met their death. ||166||" |
| `Line 1207: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1208: द्रोणपर्वणि ये शूरा निर्दिष्टाः पुरुषर्षभाः ||१६६||` | "Those heroes, the bulls among men, who are mentioned in the Drona Parva [book of Drona]. ||166||" |
| `Line 1209: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1211: अष्टौ श्लोकसहस्राणि तथा नव शतानि च ||१६७||` | "Eight thousand and nine hundred verses. ||167||" |
| `Line 1212: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1213: श्लोका नव तथैवात्र सङ्ख्यातास्तत्त्वदर्शिना |` | "And nine verses are counted here by the truth-seer [sage]," |
| `Line 1214: पाराशर्येण मुनिना सञ्चिन्त्य द्रोणपर्वणि ||१६८||` | "By the sage Parasharyeya [Vyasa], after careful consideration, in the Drona Parva. ||168||" |
| `Line 1215: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1217: सारथ्ये विनियोगश्च मद्रराजस्य धीमतः ||१६९||` | "And the appointment of the wise king of Madra [Shalya] as charioteer. ||169||" |

| `Line 1220: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1222: हंसकाकीयमाख्यानमत्रैवाक्षेपसंहितम् ||१७०||` | "The tale of the swan and crow is also included here with criticisms. ||170||" |
| `Line 1223: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1225: द्वैरथे यत्र पार्थेन हतः कर्णो महारथः ||१७१||` | "Where in single combat, Karna the great chariot-warrior was slain by Partha [Arjuna]. ||171||" |
| `Line 1226: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1228: एकोनसप्ततिः प्रोक्ता अध्यायाः कर्णपर्वणि ||१७२||` | "Sixty-nine chapters are said to be in the Karna-parva [Karna's book]. ||172||" |
| `Line 1229: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1231: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1233: हतप्रवीरे सैन्ये तु नेता मद्रेश्वरोऽभवत् ||१७३||` | "When the chief warriors were slain, the king of Madra [Shalya] became the leader. ||173||" |
| `Line 1234: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1236: विनाशः कुरुमुख्यानां शल्यपर्वणि कीर्त्यते ||१७४||` | "The destruction of the foremost Kurus is narrated in the Shalya-parva. ||174||" |
| `Line 1237: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1250: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1252: भग्नोरुं यत्र राजानं दुर्योधनममर्षणम् ||१७८||` | "Where the impatient king Duryodhana with broken thighs [was found]. ||178||" |
| `Line 1253: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1255: कृतवर्मा कृपो द्रौणिः सायाह्ने रुधिरोक्षिताः ||१७९||` | "Kritavarma, Kripa, and Droni [Ashvatthama], blood-spattered, in the evening. ||179||" |
| `Line 1256: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1258: अहत्वा सर्वपाञ्चालान्धृष्टद्युम्नपुरोगमान् ||१८०||` | "Not without slaying all the Panchalas led by Dhrishtadyumna, ||180||" |

| `Line 1261: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1267: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1273: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1276: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1308: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1310: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1313: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1315: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1318: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1320: यान्बुद्ध्वा पुरुषः सम्यक्सर्वज्ञत्वमवाप्नुयात् ||१९८||` | "Understanding which, a person may properly attain omniscience. ||198||" |
| `Line 1321: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1323: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1324: द्वादशं पर्व निर्दिष्टमेतत्प्राज्ञजनप्रियम् |` | "This twelfth Parva [section] is designated as dear to wise people," |
| `Line 1325: पर्वण्यत्र परिज्ञेयमध्यायानां शतत्रयम् ||१९९||` | "In this Parva [section], three hundred chapters are to be known. ||199||" |
| `Line 1326: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1327: त्रिंशच्चैव तथाध्याया नव चैव तपोधनाः ||१९९||` | "Thirty chapters and nine, O wealth of austerities [ascetics]. ||199||" |
| `Line 1328: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1329: श्लोकानां तु सहस्राणि कीर्तितानि चतुर्दश |` | "Fourteen thousand verses have been recited," |
| `Line 1330: पञ्च चैव शतान्याहुः पञ्चविंशतिसङ्ख्यया ||२००||` | "And five hundred and twenty-five verses, they say. ||200||" |
| `Line 1331: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1332: अत ऊर्ध्वं तु विज्ञेयमानुशासनमुत्तमम् |` | "After this should be known the excellent Anushasana [Instruction Parva]," |
| `Line 1333: यत्र प्रकृतिमापन्नः श्रुत्वा धर्मविनिश्चयम् ||२०१||` | "Where, having returned to his natural state after hearing the determination of dharma [righteousness], ||201||" |
| `Line 1334: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1335: भीष्माद्भागीरथीपुत्रात्कुरुराजो युधिष्ठिरः ||२०१||` | "From Bhishma, the son of Ganga [Bhagirathi], the Kuru king Yudhishthira. ||201||" |
| `Line 1336: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1337: व्यवहारोऽत्र कार्त्स्न्येन धर्मार्थीयो निदर्शितः |` | "Here the conduct related to dharma and artha [righteousness and prosperity] is fully demonstrated," |
| `Line 1338: विविधानां च दानानां फलयोगाः पृथग्विधाः ||२०२||` | "And the various fruits of different kinds of charity are described. ||202||" |
| `Line 1339: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1340: तथा पात्रविशेषाश्च दानानां च परो विधिः |` | "Also the special recipients and the supreme method of giving charity," |
| `Line 1341: आचारविधियोगश्च सत्यस्य च परा गतिः ||२०३||` | "And the rules of proper conduct, and the supreme path of truth. ||203||" |
| `Line 1342: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1343: एतत्सुबहुवृत्तान्तमुत्तमं चानुशासनम् |` | "This Anushasana [Instruction Parva] contains many narratives and is excellent," |
| `Line 1344: भीष्मस्यात्रैव सम्प्राप्तिः स्वर्गस्य परिकीर्तिता ||२०४||` | "Here is also described Bhishma's attainment of heaven [svarga]. ||204||" |
| `Line 1345: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1346: एतत्त्रयोदशं पर्व धर्मनिश्चयकारकम् |` | "This is the thirteenth Parva [book section], which establishes the certainty of dharma [righteousness]," |
| `Line 1347: अध्यायानां शतं चात्र षट्चत्वारिंशदेव च ||२०५||` | "It contains one hundred and forty-six chapters. ||205||" |
| `Line 1348: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1349: श्लोकानां तु सहस्राणि षट्सप्तैव शतानि च ||२०५||` | "And it contains six thousand and seven hundred verses. ||205||" |
| `Line 1350: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1351: ततोऽश्वमेधिकं नाम पर्व प्रोक्तं चतुर्दशम् |` | "Then the fourteenth section named Ashvamedha [horse sacrifice] Parva is described," |
| `Line 1352: तत्संवर्तमरुत्तीयं यत्राख्यानमनुत्तमम् ||२०६||` | "Where the excellent story of Samvarta and Marutta is told. ||206||" |
| `Line 1353: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1354: सुवर्णकोशसम्प्राप्तिर्जन्म चोक्तं परिक्षितः |` | "The acquisition of the golden treasury and the birth of Parikshit [Pandava grandson] are narrated," |
| `Line 1355: दग्धस्यास्त्राग्निना पूर्वं कृष्णात्सञ्जीवनं पुनः ||२०७||` | "Who was previously burnt by the fire of the weapon, and then revived by Krishna. ||207||" |
| `Line 1356: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1357: चर्यायां हयमुत्सृष्टं पाण्डवस्यानुगच्छतः |` | "The horse let loose for the ritual, followed by the Pandava [Arjuna]," |
| `Line 1358: तत्र तत्र च युद्धानि राजपुत्रैरमर्षणैः ||२०८||` | "And the battles fought here and there with wrathful princes. ||208||" |
| `Line 1359: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1360: चित्राङ्गदायाः पुत्रेण पुत्रिकाया धनञ्जयः |` | "Dhananjaya [Arjuna] with the son of Chitrangada, his putrika [appointed daughter]," |
| `Line 1361: सङ्ग्रामे बभ्रुवाहेन संशयं चात्र दर्शितः ||२०९||` | "Is shown in a perilous situation in battle with Babhruvahana. ||209||" |
| `Line 1362: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1363: अश्वमेधे महायज्ञे नकुलाख्यानमेव च ||२०९||` | "And also the story of Nakula in the great sacrifice of Ashvamedha. ||209||" |
| `Line 1364: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1365: इत्याश्वमेधिकं पर्व प्रोक्तमेतन्महाद्भुतम् |` | "Thus is described this wonderful Ashvamedha Parva," |
| `Line 1366: अत्राध्यायशतं त्रिंशत्त्रयोऽध्यायाश्च शब्दिताः ||२१०||` | "Here one hundred and thirty-three chapters are enumerated. ||210||" |
| `Line 1367: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1368: त्रीणि श्लोकसहस्राणि तावन्त्येव शतानि च |` | "Three thousand verses and as many hundreds," |
| `Line 1369: विंशतिश्च तथा श्लोकाः सङ्ख्यातास्तत्त्वदर्शिना ||२११||` | "And twenty verses are counted by the knower of truth [compiler]. ||211||" |
| `Line 1370: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1371: तत आश्रमवासाक्यं पर्व पञ्चदशं स्मृतम् |` | "Then comes the fifteenth section known as Ashramavasa [forest dwelling] Parva," |
| `Line 1372: यत्र राज्यं परित्यज्य गान्धारीसहितो नृपः ||२१२||` | "Where the king [Dhritarashtra], along with Gandhari, abandoning the kingdom, ||212||" |
| `Line 1373: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1374: धृतराष्ट्राश्रमपदं विदुरश्च जगाम ह ||२१२||` | "Went to the hermitage, and Vidura too went there. ||212||" |
| `Line 1375: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1376: यं दृष्ट्वा प्रस्थितं साध्वी पृथाप्यनुययौ तदा |` | "Seeing him departing, the virtuous Pritha [Kunti] followed him then," |
| `Line 1377: पुत्रराज्यं परित्यज्य गुरुशुश्रूषणे रता ||२१३||` | "Abandoning her sons' kingdom, devoted to serving the elders. ||213||" |
| `Line 1378: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1379: यत्र राजा हतान्पुत्रान्पौत्रानन्यांश्च पार्थिवान् |` | "Where the king saw his slain sons, grandsons, and other rulers," |
| `Line 1380: लोकान्तरगतान्वीरानपश्यत्पुनरागतान् ||२१४||` | "The heroes who had gone to the other world [afterlife], returned again. ||214||" |
| `Line 1381: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1382: ऋषेः प्रसादात्कृष्णस्य दृष्ट्वाश्चर्यमनुत्तमम् |` | "By the grace of the sage and Krishna, having seen the supreme wonder," |
| `Line 1383: त्यक्त्वा शोकं सदारश्च सिद्धिं परमिकां गतः ||२१५||` | "Abandoning grief, he along with his wife attained the highest perfection. ||215||" |
| `Line 1384: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1385: यत्र धर्मं समाश्रित्य विदुरः सुगतिं गतः |` | "Where Vidura, having taken refuge in dharma [righteousness], attained a good destination," |
| `Line 1386: सञ्जयश्च महामात्रो विद्वान्गावल्गणिर्वशी ||२१६||` | "And Sanjaya, the great minister, the wise Gavalgani, the self-controlled one. ||216||" |
| `Line 1387: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1388: ददर्श नारदं यत्र धर्मराजो युधिष्ठिरः |` | "Where Dharmaraja [righteous king] Yudhishthira saw Narada," |
| `Line 1389: नारदाच्चैव शुश्राव वृष्णीनां कदनं महत् ||२१७||` | "And from Narada he heard of the great destruction of the Vrishnis. ||217||" |
| `Line 1390: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1391: एतदाश्रमवासाख्यं पूर्वोक्तं सुमहाद्भुतम् |` | "This is the previously mentioned, very wonderful section called Ashramavasa [forest dwelling]," |
| `Line 1392: द्विचत्वारिंशदध्यायाः पर्वैतदभिसङ्ख्यया ||२१८||` | "This parva [section] consists of forty-two chapters by count. ||218||" |
| `Line 1393: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1394: सहस्रमेकं श्लोकानां पञ्च श्लोकशतानि च |` | "One thousand verses and five hundred verses," |
| `Line 1395: षडेव च तथा श्लोकाः सङ्ख्यातास्तत्त्वदर्शिना ||२१९||` | "And six verses have been counted by the knower of truth [sage]. ||219||" |
| `Line 1396: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1397: अतः परं निबोधेदं मौसलं पर्व दारुणम् |` | "After this, understand the terrible Mausala Parva [club section]," |
| `Line 1398: यत्र ते पुरुषव्याघ्राः शस्त्रस्पर्शसहा युधि ||२२०||` | "Where those tiger-like men [great warriors], who could withstand weapons in battle, ||220||" |
| `Line 1399: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1400: ब्रह्मदण्डविनिष्पिष्टाः समीपे लवणाम्भसः ||२२०||` | "Were crushed by Brahma's rod [divine punishment] near the salt waters [ocean]. ||220||" |
| `Line 1401: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1402: आपाने पानगलिता दैवेनाभिप्रचोदिताः |` | "In the drinking hall, intoxicated by drink, impelled by fate [divine will]," |
| `Line 1403: एरकारूपिभिर्वज्रैर्निजघ्नुरितरेतरम् ||२२१||` | "They struck one another with clubs [weapons] in the form of eraka grass. ||221||" |
| `Line 1404: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1405: यत्र सर्वक्षयं कृत्वा तावुभौ रामकेशवौ |` | "Where, after the destruction of all, both Rama [Balarama] and Keshava [Krishna]," |
| `Line 1406: नातिचक्रमतुः कालं प्राप्तं सर्वहरं समम् ||२२२||` | "Did not transgress the appointed time, the all-destroying [death] that comes equally to all. ||222||" |
| `Line 1407: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1408: यत्रार्जुनो द्वारवतीमेत्य वृष्णिविनाकृताम् |` | "Where Arjuna, coming to Dwaraka [Krishna's city] bereft of the Vrishnis [Krishna's clan]," |
| `Line 1409: दृष्ट्वा विषादमगमत्परां चार्तिं नरर्षभः ||२२३||` | "Seeing it, fell into despair and extreme grief, that bull among men [heroic Arjuna]. ||223||" |
| `Line 1410: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1411: स सत्कृत्य यदुश्रेष्ठं मातुलं शौरिमात्मनः |` | "He, having paid respects to the best of Yadus [Krishna's clan], his maternal uncle Shauri [Vasudeva]," |
| `Line 1412: ददर्श यदुवीराणामापाने वैशसं महत् ||२२४||` | "Witnessed in the drinking hall the great slaughter of the Yadu heroes. ||224||" |
| `Line 1413: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1414: शरीरं वासुदेवस्य रामस्य च महात्मनः |` | "The body of Vasudeva [Krishna] and of the great-souled Rama [Balarama]," |
| `Line 1415: संस्कारं लम्भयामास वृष्णीनां च प्रधानतः ||२२५||` | "He arranged the funeral rites for, and for the chief among the Vrishnis. ||225||" |
| `Line 1416: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1417: स वृद्धबालमादाय द्वारवत्यास्ततो जनम् |` | "Taking the elderly and children, and then the people of Dwaraka," |
| `Line 1418: ददर्शापदि कष्टायां गाण्डीवस्य पराभवम् ||२२६||` | "He witnessed in that terrible calamity the failure of Gandiva [Arjuna's bow]. ||226||" |
| `Line 1419: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1420: सर्वेषां चैव दिव्यानामस्त्राणामप्रसन्नताम् |` | "And the ineffectiveness of all divine weapons," |
| `Line 1421: नाशं वृष्णिकलत्राणां प्रभावानामनित्यताम् ||२२७||` | "The destruction of the Vrishni women, and the impermanence of powers [glories]. ||227||" |
| `Line 1422: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1423: दृष्ट्वा निर्वेदमापन्नो व्यासवाक्यप्रचोदितः |` | "Seeing this, he became despondent, and prompted by the words of Vyasa [sage-author]," |
| `Line 1424: धर्मराजं समासाद्य संन्यासं समरोचयेत् ||२२८||` | "Having approached Dharmaraja [Yudhishthira], he would recommend renunciation. ||228||" |
| `Line 1425: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1426: इत्येतन्मौसलं पर्व षोडशं परिकीर्तितम् |` | "Thus, this Mausala Parva [Club War chapter] is declared as the sixteenth," |
| `Line 1427: अध्यायाष्टौ समाख्याताः श्लोकानां च शतत्रयम् ||२२९||` | "Comprising eight chapters and three hundred verses. ||229||" |
| `Line 1428: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1429: महाप्रस्थानिकं तस्मादूर्ध्वं सप्तदशं स्मृतम् |` | "After that, the seventeenth is known as Mahaprasthanika [Great Departure chapter]," |
| `Line 1430: यत्र राज्यं परित्यज्य पाण्डवाः पुरुषर्षभाः ||२३०||` | "Where the Pandavas [sons of Pandu], those bulls among men, abandoning their kingdom, ||230||" |
| `Line 1431: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1432: द्रौपद्या सहिता देव्या सिद्धिं परमिकां गताः ||२३०||` | "Along with the divine Draupadi [Pandavas' wife], attained the supreme perfection. ||230||" |
| `Line 1433: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1434: अत्राध्यायास्त्रयः प्रोक्ताः श्लोकानां च शतं तथा |` | "Here three chapters are mentioned, as well as one hundred verses," |
| `Line 1435: विंशतिश्च तथा श्लोकाः सङ्ख्यातास्तत्त्वदर्शिना ||२३१||` | "And twenty verses are counted by the knower of truth [sage]. ||231||" |
| `Line 1436: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1437: स्वर्गपर्व ततो ज्ञेयं दिव्यं यत्तदमानुषम् |` | "Then should be known the Svarga Parva [Heaven chapter], which is divine and superhuman," |
| `Line 1438: अध्यायाः पञ्च सङ्ख्याताः पर्वैतदभिसङ्ख्यया ||२३२||` | "Five chapters are counted in this Parva [section] by enumeration. ||232||" |
| `Line 1439: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1440: श्लोकानां द्वे शते चैव प्रसङ्ख्याते तपोधनाः ||२३२||` | "And two hundred verses are counted, O wealth of austerities [ascetics]. ||232||" |
| `Line 1441: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1442: अष्टादशैवमेतानि पर्वाण्युक्तान्यशेषतः |` | "Thus these eighteen Parvas [major sections] have been described completely," |
| `Line 1443: खिलेषु हरिवंशश्च भविष्यच्च प्रकीर्तितम् ||२३३||` | "Among the supplements, the Harivamsha [Krishna's lineage] and the Bhavishya [future events] are proclaimed. ||233||" |
| `Line 1444: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1445: एतदखिलमाख्यातं भारतं पर्वसङ्ग्रहात् |` | "This entire Bharata [epic] has been narrated in the compilation of Parvas [sections]," |
| `Line 1446: अष्टादश समाजग्मुरक्षौहिण्यो युयुत्सया ||२३४||` | "Eighteen Akshauhinis [army units] came together with the desire to fight. ||234||" |
| `Line 1447: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1448: तन्महद्दारुणं युद्धमहान्यष्टादशाभवत् ||२३४||` | "That great and terrible war lasted for eighteen days. ||234||" |
| `Line 1449: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1450: यो विद्याच्चतुरो वेदान्साङ्गोपनिषदान्द्विजः |` | "That twice-born [Brahmin] who knows the four Vedas along with their Angas [auxiliary texts] and Upanishads [philosophical texts]," |
| `Line 1451: न चाख्यानमिदं विद्यान्नैव स स्याद्विचक्षणः ||२३५||` | "One who does not know this narrative cannot be considered wise. ||235||" |
| `Line 1452: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1453: श्रुत्वा त्विदमुपाख्यानं श्राव्यमन्यन्न रोचते |` | "After hearing this narrative, no other story worth hearing appeals," |
| `Line 1454: पुंस्कोकिलरुतं श्रुत्वा रूक्षा ध्वाङ्क्षस्य वागिव ||२३६||` | "Just as after hearing the male cuckoo's song, the harsh voice of a crow is displeasing. ||236||" |
| `Line 1455: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1456: इतिहासोत्तमादस्माज्जायन्ते कविबुद्धयः |` | "From this supreme history arise the intellects of poets," |
| `Line 1457: पञ्चभ्य इव भूतेभ्यो लोकसंविधयस्त्रयः ||२३७||` | "Just as from the five elements arise the three worlds [realms of existence]. ||237||" |
| `Line 1458: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1459: अस्याख्यानस्य विषये पुराणं वर्तते द्विजाः |` | "O twice-born [Brahmins], all Puranas [ancient texts] exist within the scope of this narrative," |
| `Line 1460: अन्तरिक्षस्य विषये प्रजा इव चतुर्विधाः ||२३८||` | "Just as the four kinds of beings exist within the realm of the sky. ||238||" |
| `Line 1461: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1462: क्रियागुणानां सर्वेषामिदमाख्यानमाश्रयः |` | "This narrative is the foundation of all actions and qualities," |
| `Line 1463: इन्द्रियाणां समस्तानां चित्रा इव मनःक्रियाः ||२३९||` | "Just as the varied activities of the mind are the basis of all the senses. ||239||" |
| `Line 1464: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 1469: उदयप्रेप्सुभिर्भृत्यैरभिजात इवेश्वरः ||२४१||` | "Just as a noble lord is relied upon by servants seeking prosperity. ||241||" |

| `Line 1488: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1489: जनमेजयः पारिक्षितः सह भ्रातृभिः कुरुक्षेत्रे दीर्घसत्रमुपास्ते |` | "Janamejaya, son of Parikshit, was performing a long sacrificial session [dīrgha-satra] at Kurukshetra [sacred battlefield] with his brothers." |
| `Line 1490: तस्य भ्रातरस्त्रयः श्रुतसेन उग्रसेनो भीमसेन इति | ००१ |` | "His three brothers were Shrutasena, Ugrasena, and Bhimasena. |001|" |
| `Line 1491: तेषु तत्सत्रमुपासीनेषु तत्र श्वाभ्यागच्छत्सारमेयः |` | "While they were engaged in that sacrifice, a dog [offspring of Sarama] came there." |
| `Line 1492: स जनमेजयस्य भ्रातृभिरभिहतो रोरूयमाणो मातुः समीपमुपागच्छत् | ००२ |` | "Beaten by Janamejaya's brothers, it went whimpering to its mother. |002|" |
| `Line 1493: तं माता रोरूयमाणमुवाच |` | "The mother said to it as it was whimpering:" |
| `Line 1494: किं रोदिषि |` | "Why are you crying?" |
| `Line 1495: केनास्यभिहत इति | ००३ |` | "By whom have you been beaten? |003|" |
| `Line 1496: स एवमुक्तो मातरं प्रत्युवाच |` | "Thus addressed, it replied to its mother:" |
| `Line 1497: जनमेजयस्य भ्रातृभिरभिहतोऽस्मीति | ००४ |` | "I have been beaten by Janamejaya's brothers. |004|" |
| `Line 1498: तं माता प्रत्युवाच |` | "The mother replied to it:" |
| `Line 1499: व्यक्तं त्वया तत्रापराद्धं येनास्यभिहत इति | ००५ |` | "Clearly you must have committed some offense there, for which you were beaten. |005|" |
| `Line 1500: स तां पुनरुवाच |` | "It said to her again:" |
| `Line 1501: नापराध्यामि किञ्चित् |` | "I have not committed any offense." |
| `Line 1502: नावेक्षे हवींषि नावलिह इति | ००६ |` | "I neither looked at the offerings nor licked them. ||6||" |
| `Line 1503: तच्छ्रुत्वा तस्य माता सरमा पुत्रशोकार्ता तत्सत्रमुपागच्छद्यत्र स जनमेजयः सह भ्रातृभिर्दीर्घसत्रमुपास्ते | ००७ |` | "Hearing that, his mother Saramā [divine hound], distressed by her son's pain, approached that sacrificial session where Janamejaya with his brothers was performing a long sacrifice [sattra]. ||7||" |
| `Line 1504: स तया क्रुद्धया तत्रोक्तः |` | "He was addressed there by her, who was angry:" |
| `Line 1505: अयं मे पुत्रो न किञ्चिदपराध्यति |` | "This son of mine has committed no offense." |
| `Line 1506: किमर्थमभिहत इति |` | "Why was he struck?" |
| `Line 1507: यस्माच्चायमभिहतोऽनपकारी तस्माददृष्टं त्वां भयमागमिष्यतीति | ००८ |` | "Since he was struck while being innocent, therefore an unforeseen danger shall come upon you. ||8||" |
| `Line 1508: स जनमेजय एवमुक्तो देवशुन्या सरमया दृढं सम्भ्रान्तो विषण्णश्चासीत् | ००९ |` | "Janamejaya, thus addressed by Saramā of divine lineage [celestial hound], became deeply disturbed and dejected. ||9||" |
| `Line 1509: स तस्मिन्सत्रे समाप्ते हास्तिनपुरं प्रत्येत्य पुरोहितमनुरूपमन्विच्छमानः परं यत्नमकरोद्यो मे पापकृत्यां शमयेदिति | ०१० |` | "After that sacrifice was completed, he returned to Hastināpura and made great effort to find a suitable priest who could pacify his sinful deed. ||10||" |
| `Line 1510: स कदाचिन्मृगयां यातः पारिक्षितो जनमेजयः कस्मिंश्चित्स्वविषयोद्देशे आश्रममपश्यत् | ०११ |` | "Once, while hunting, Janamejaya Pārikṣita [son of Parikshit] saw a hermitage in some region of his territory. ||11||" |
| `Line 1511: तत्र कश्चिदृषिरासां चक्रे श्रुतश्रवा नाम |` | "There, a certain sage named Śrutaśravā was residing." |
| `Line 1512: तस्याभिमतः पुत्र आस्ते सोमश्रवा नाम | ०१२ |` | "His beloved son named Somaśravā was staying there. ||12||" |
| `Line 1513: तस्य तं पुत्रमभिगम्य जनमेजयः पारिक्षितः पौरोहित्याय वव्रे | ०१३ |` | "Approaching that son of his, Janamejaya Pārikṣita requested him to become his priest. ||13||" |
| `Line 1514: स नमस्कृत्य तमृषिमुवाच |` | "He, having bowed to that sage, said:" |
| `Line 1515: भगवन्नयं तव पुत्रो मम पुरोहितोऽस्त्विति | ०१४ |` | "O venerable one, may this son of yours be my priest. ||14||" |
| `Line 1516: स एवमुक्तः प्रत्युवाच |` | "He, thus addressed, replied:" |
| `Line 1517: भो जनमेजय पुत्रोऽयं मम सर्प्यां जातः |` | "O Janamejaya, this son of mine was born from a serpent woman [nāga female]." |
| `Line 1518: महातपस्वी स्वाध्यायसम्पन्नो मत्तपोवीर्यसम्भृतो मच्छुक्रं पीतवत्यास्तस्याः कुक्षौ संवृद्धः |` | "He is of great austerity, accomplished in self-study, produced by my ascetic power, grown in the womb of her who drank my seed." |
| `Line 1519: समर्थोऽयं भवतः सर्वाः पापकृत्याः शमयितुमन्तरेण महादेवकृत्याम् |` | "He is capable of pacifying all your sinful deeds except those related to Mahādeva [Shiva]." |
| `Line 1520: अस्य त्वेकमुपांशुव्रतम् |` | "But he has one silent vow:" |
| `Line 1521: यदेनं कश्चिद्ब्राह्मणः कञ्चिदर्थमभियाचेत्तं तस्मै दद्यादयम् |` | "If any Brahmin should ask him for anything, he must give it to him." |
| `Line 1522: यद्येतदुत्सहसे ततो नयस्वैनमिति | ०१५ |` | "If you can endure this, then take him. ||15||" |

| `Line 1524: भगवंस्तथा भविष्यतीति | ०१६ |` | "O venerable one, so it shall be. ||16||" |
| `Line 1525: स तं पुरोहितमुपादायोपावृत्तो भ्रातृनुवाच |` | "Having accepted him as priest and returned, he said to his brothers:" |
| `Line 1526: मयायं वृत उपाध्यायः |` | "This teacher has been chosen by me." |

| `Line 1528: तेनैवमुक्ता भ्रातरस्तस्य तथा चक्रुः |` | "Thus instructed by him, his brothers did accordingly." |
