| `Line 1530: तं च देशं वशे स्थापयामास | ०१८ |` | "And he brought that region under his control. |018|" |
| `Line 1531: एतस्मिन्नन्तरे कश्चिदृषिर्धौम्यो नामायोदः |` | "During this time, there was a sage named Dhaumya Ayoda [revered teacher]." |
| `Line 1532: तस्य शिष्यास्त्रयो बभूवुरुपमन्युरारुणिर्वेदश्चेति | ०१९ |` | "He had three disciples: Upamanyu, Aruni, and Veda. |019|" |
| `Line 1533: स एकं शिष्यमारुणिं पाञ्चाल्यं प्रेषयामास |` | "He sent one disciple, Aruni of Panchala [region name], saying:" |
| `Line 1534: गच्छ केदारखण्डं बधानेति | ०२० |` | "Go and repair the breach in the field [kedara-khanda]. |020|" |
| `Line 1535: स उपाध्यायेन संदिष्ट आरुणिः पाञ्चाल्यस्तत्र गत्वा तत्केदारखण्डं बद्धुं नाशक्नोत् | ०२१ |` | "Instructed by his teacher, Aruni of Panchala went there but was unable to repair that breach in the field. |021|" |
| `Line 1536: स क्लिश्यमानोऽपश्यदुपायम् |` | "Struggling, he saw a solution." |
| `Line 1537: भवत्वेवं करिष्यामीति | ०२२ |` | "Let it be so, I will do this," he thought. |022|" |
| `Line 1538: स तत्र संविवेश केदारखण्डे |` | "He lay down in the breach of the field." |
| `Line 1539: शयाने तस्मिंस्तदुदकं तस्थौ | ०२३ |` | "As he lay there, the water stopped flowing. |023|" |
| `Line 1540: ततः कदाचिदुपाध्याय आयोदो धौम्यः शिष्यानपृच्छत् |` | "Then, after some time, the teacher Dhaumya Ayoda asked his disciples:" |
| `Line 1541: क्व आरुणिः पाञ्चाल्यो गत इति | ०२४ |` | "Where has Aruni of Panchala gone? |024|" |
| `Line 1542: ते प्रत्यूचुः |` | "They replied:" |
| `Line 1543: भगवतैव प्रेषितो गच्छ केदारखण्डं बधानेति | ०२५ |` | "He was sent by your reverence yourself, saying 'Go and repair the breach in the field.' |025|" |
| `Line 1544: स एवमुक्तस्ताञ्शिष्यान्प्रत्युवाच |` | "Having heard this, he said to those disciples:" |
| `Line 1545: तस्मात्सर्वे तत्र गच्छामो यत्र स इति | ०२६ |` | "Therefore, let us all go where he is. |026|" |
| `Line 1546: स तत्र गत्वा तस्याह्वानाय शब्दं चकार |` | "Having gone there, he called out to him:" |
| `Line 1547: भो आरुणे पाञ्चाल्य क्वासि |` | "O Aruni of Panchala, where are you?" |
| `Line 1548: वत्सैहीति | ०२७ |` | "Come here, my child! |027|" |
| `Line 1549: स तच्छ्रुत्वा आरुणिरुपाध्यायवाक्यं तस्मात्केदारखण्डात्सहसोत्थाय तमुपाध्यायमुपतस्थे |` | "Hearing those words of his teacher, Aruni suddenly rose up from that breach in the field and approached his teacher." |
| `Line 1550: प्रोवाच चैनम् |` | "And he said to him:" |
| `Line 1551: अयमस्म्यत्र केदारखण्डे निःसरमाणमुदकमवारणीयं संरोद्धुं संविष्टो भगवच्छब्दं श्रुत्वैव सहसा विदार्य केदारखण्डं भवन्तमुपस्थितः |` | "Here I am, lying in this field section to stop the unstoppable flowing water, when upon hearing the word 'Bhagavan [venerable one],' I suddenly broke through the field section and came before you." |
| `Line 1552: तदभिवादये भगवन्तम् |` | "Therefore, I pay my respects to you, O venerable one." |
| `Line 1553: आज्ञापयतु भवान् |` | "May you command me." |
| `Line 1554: किं करवाणीति | ०२८ |` | "What shall I do? ||28||" |
| `Line 1555: तमुपाध्यायोऽब्रवीत् |` | "The teacher said to him:" |
| `Line 1556: यस्माद्भवान्केदारखण्डमवदार्योत्थितस्तस्माद्भवानुद्दालक एव नाम्ना भविष्यतीति | ०२९ |` | "Since you have risen by breaking through (uddalana) the field section, therefore you shall be known by the name Uddālaka. ||29||" |
| `Line 1557: स उपाध्यायेनानुगृहीतः |` | "He was blessed by the teacher:" |
| `Line 1558: यस्मात्त्वया मद्वचोऽनुष्ठितं तस्माच्छ्रेयोऽवाप्स्यसीति |` | "Since you have followed my words, therefore you shall attain excellence." |
| `Line 1559: सर्वे च ते वेदाः प्रतिभास्यन्ति सर्वाणि च धर्मशास्त्राणीति | ०३० |` | "And all the Vedas and all the Dharmaśāstras [sacred law texts] will become clear to you. ||30||" |
| `Line 1560: स एवमुक्त उपाध्यायेनेष्टं देशं जगाम | ०३१ |` | "Having been thus addressed by the teacher, he went to a desired place. ||31||" |
| `Line 1561: अथापरः शिष्यस्तस्यैवायोदस्य धौम्यस्योपमन्युर्नाम | ०३२ |` | "Now, another student of that same Āyoda Dhaumya was named Upamanyu. ||32||" |
| `Line 1562: तमुपाध्यायः प्रेषयामास |` | "The teacher sent him:" |
| `Line 1563: वत्सोपमन्यो गा रक्षस्वेति | ०३३ |` | "O child Upamanyu, tend the cows. ||33||" |
| `Line 1564: स उपाध्यायवचनादरक्षद्गाः |` | "Following the teacher's words, he tended the cows." |
| `Line 1565: स चाहनि गा रक्षित्वा दिवसक्षयेऽभ्यागम्योपाध्यायस्याग्रतः स्थित्वा नमश्चक्रे | ०३४ |` | "And after tending the cows during the day, at sunset he returned, stood before his teacher, and paid his respects. ||34||" |
| `Line 1566: तमुपाध्यायः पीवानमपश्यत् |` | "The teacher saw that he was plump." |
| `Line 1567: उवाच चैनम् |` | "And he said to him:" |
| `Line 1568: वत्सोपमन्यो केन वृत्तिं कल्पयसि |` | "Child Upamanyu, how do you sustain yourself?" |
| `Line 1569: पीवानसि दृढमिति | ०३५ |` | "You are certainly plump. ||35||" |
| `Line 1570: स उपाध्यायं प्रत्युवाच |` | "He replied to the teacher:" |
| `Line 1571: भैक्षेण वृत्तिं कल्पयामीति | ०३६ |` | "I sustain myself by begging for alms. ||36||" |
| `Line 1572: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him:" |
| `Line 1573: ममानिवेद्य भैक्षं नोपयोक्तव्यमिति | ०३७ |` | "The alms should not be consumed without first offering them to me. ||37||" |
| `Line 1574: स तथेत्युक्त्वा पुनररक्षद्गाः |` | "Having said 'So be it,' he again tended the cows." |
| `Line 1575: रक्षित्वा चागम्य तथैवोपाध्यायस्याग्रतः स्थित्वा नमश्चक्रे | ०३८ |` | "And after tending them and returning, he stood before his teacher in the same way and paid his respects. ||38||" |
| `Line 1576: तमुपाध्यायस्तथापि पीवानमेव दृष्ट्वोवाच |` | "Seeing him still well-nourished, the teacher [upādhyāya] said to him:" |
| `Line 1577: वत्सोपमन्यो सर्वमशेषतस्ते भैक्षं गृह्णामि |` | "My child Upamanyu, I take all your alms [bhaikṣa] without exception," |
| `Line 1578: केनेदानीं वृत्तिं कल्पयसीति | ०३९ |` | "How are you now sustaining yourself? ||39||" |
| `Line 1579: स एवमुक्त उपाध्यायेन प्रत्युवाच |` | "Being thus addressed by the teacher, he replied:" |
| `Line 1580: भगवते निवेद्य पूर्वमपरं चरामि |` | "After offering to you, revered one, I go for a second round of begging," |
| `Line 1581: तेन वृत्तिं कल्पयामीति | ०४० |` | "By that I sustain myself. ||40||" |
| `Line 1582: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him:" |
| `Line 1583: नैषा न्याय्या गुरुवृत्तिः |` | "This is not a proper conduct toward a guru [teacher]," |
| `Line 1584: अन्येषामपि वृत्त्युपरोधं करोष्येवं वर्तमानः |` | "By acting this way, you also obstruct the livelihood of others," |
| `Line 1585: लुब्धोऽसीति | ०४१ |` | "You are greedy. ||41||" |
| `Line 1586: स तथेत्युक्त्वा गा अरक्षत् |` | "Having said 'so be it,' he tended the cows," |
| `Line 1587: रक्षित्वा च पुनरुपाध्यायगृहमागम्योपाध्यायस्याग्रतः स्थित्वा नमश्चक्रे | ०४२ |` | "And after tending them, he returned to the teacher's house, stood before the teacher and paid his respects. ||42||" |
| `Line 1588: तमुपाध्यायस्तथापि पीवानमेव दृष्ट्वा पुनरुवाच |` | "Seeing him still well-nourished, the teacher again said to him:" |
| `Line 1589: अहं ते सर्वं भैक्षं गृह्णामि न चान्यच्चरसि |` | "I take all your alms, and you do not go for a second round," |
| `Line 1590: पीवानसि |` | "Yet you are well-nourished," |
| `Line 1591: केन वृत्तिं कल्पयसीति | ०४३ |` | "How are you sustaining yourself? ||43||" |
| `Line 1592: स उपाध्यायं प्रत्युवाच |` | "He replied to the teacher:" |
| `Line 1593: भो एतासां गवां पयसा वृत्तिं कल्पयामीति | ०४४ |` | "Sir, I sustain myself with the milk of these cows. ||44||" |
| `Line 1594: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him:" |
| `Line 1595: नैतन्न्याय्यं पय उपयोक्तुं भवतो मयाननुज्ञातमिति | ०४५ |` | "It is not proper for you to consume milk without my permission. ||45||" |
| `Line 1596: स तथेति प्रतिज्ञाय गा रक्षित्वा पुनरुपाध्यायगृहानेत्य गुरोरग्रतः स्थित्वा नमश्चक्रे | ०४६ |` | "Having promised 'so be it,' he tended the cows and again, returning to the teacher's house, stood before the guru and paid his respects. ||46||" |
| `Line 1597: तमुपाध्यायः पीवानमेवापश्यत् |` | "The teacher saw him still well-nourished," |
| `Line 1598: उवाच चैनम् |` | "And said to him:" |
| `Line 1599: भैक्षं नाश्नासि न चान्यच्चरसि |` | "You do not eat alms, nor do you go for a second round," |
| `Line 1600: पयो न पिबसि |` | "You do not drink milk," |
| `Line 1601: पीवानसि |` | "You are fat [well-fed]," |
| `Line 1602: केन वृत्तिं कल्पयसीति | ०४७ |` | "By what means do you arrange your livelihood? ||47||" |
| `Line 1603: स एवमुक्त उपाध्यायं प्रत्युवाच |` | "Being thus addressed, he replied to the teacher," |
| `Line 1604: भोः फेनं पिबामि यमिमे वत्सा मातृणां स्तनं पिबन्त उद्गिरन्तीति | ०४८ |` | "Sir, I drink the foam which these calves regurgitate while drinking from their mothers' udders. ||48||" |
| `Line 1605: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him," |
| `Line 1606: एते त्वदनुकम्पया गुणवन्तो वत्साः प्रभूततरं फेनमुद्गिरन्ति |` | "These virtuous calves, out of compassion for you, regurgitate more foam," |
| `Line 1607: तदेवमपि वत्सानां वृत्त्युपरोधं करोष्येवं वर्तमानः |` | "Even so, by behaving this way, you are obstructing the livelihood of the calves," |
| `Line 1608: फेनमपि भवान्न पातुमर्हतीति | ०४९ |` | "You should not even drink the foam. ||49||" |
| `Line 1609: स तथेति प्रतिज्ञाय निराहारस्ता गा अरक्षत् |` | "Having promised 'so be it,' he tended the cows without taking any food," |
| `Line 1610: तथा प्रतिषिद्धो भैक्षं नाश्नाति न चान्यच्चरति |` | "Thus prohibited, he neither ate alms nor pursued anything else," |
| `Line 1611: पयो न पिबति |` | "He did not drink milk," |
| `Line 1612: फेनं नोपयुङ्क्ते | ०५० |` | "Nor did he consume the foam. ||50||" |
| `Line 1613: स कदाचिदरण्ये क्षुधार्तोऽर्कपत्राण्यभक्षयत् | ०५१ |` | "Once, tormented by hunger in the forest, he ate the leaves of the arka plant [milkweed]. ||51||" |
| `Line 1614: स तैरर्कपत्रैर्भक्षितैः क्षारकटूष्णविपाकिभिश्चक्षुष्युपहतोऽन्धोऽभवत् |` | "By eating those arka leaves, which have caustic, pungent, and hot properties, his eyes were damaged and he became blind," |
| `Line 1615: सोऽन्धोऽपि चङ्क्रम्यमाणः कूपेऽपतत् | ०५२ |` | "Though blind, while wandering about, he fell into a well. ||52||" |
| `Line 1616: अथ तस्मिन्ननागच्छत्युपाध्यायः शिष्यानवोचत् |` | "Then, when he did not return, the teacher said to his disciples," |
| `Line 1617: मयोपमन्युः सर्वतः प्रतिषिद्धः |` | "Upamanyu has been prohibited by me from all means of sustenance," |
| `Line 1618: स नियतं कुपितः |` | "He must certainly be angry," |
| `Line 1619: ततो नागच्छति चिरगतश्चेति | ०५३ |` | "That is why he does not return and has been gone so long. ||53||" |
| `Line 1620: स एवमुक्त्वा गत्वारण्यमुपमन्योराह्वानं चक्रे |` | "Having spoken thus, he went to the forest and called out to Upamanyu," |
| `Line 1621: भो उपमन्यो क्वासि |` | "O Upamanyu, where are you?" |
| `Line 1622: वत्सैहीति | ०५४ |` | "Come here, my child! ||54||" |
| `Line 1623: स तदाह्वानमुपाध्यायाच्छ्रुत्वा प्रत्युवाचोच्चैः |` | "Hearing that call from his teacher, he replied loudly," |
| `Line 1624: अयमस्मि भो उपाध्याय कूपे पतित इति | ०५५ |` | "Here I am, O teacher, fallen into a well! ||55||" |
| `Line 1625: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him," |
| `Line 1626: कथमसि कूपे पतित इति | ०५६ |` | "How did you fall into the well? |056|" |
| `Line 1627: स तं प्रत्युवाच |` | "He replied to him:" |
| `Line 1628: अर्कपत्राणि भक्षयित्वान्धीभूतोऽस्मि |` | "Having eaten arka [milkweed] leaves, I became blind." |
| `Line 1629: अतः कूपे पतित इति | ०५७ |` | "That is why I fell into the well. |057|" |
| `Line 1630: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him:" |
| `Line 1631: अश्विनौ स्तुहि |` | "Praise the Ashvins [divine physician twins]." |
| `Line 1632: तौ त्वां चक्षुष्मन्तं करिष्यतो देवभिषजाविति | ०५८ |` | "Those divine physicians will restore your eyesight. |058|" |
| `Line 1633: स एवमुक्त उपाध्यायेन स्तोतुं प्रचक्रमे देवावश्विनौ वाग्भिरृग्भिः | ०५९ |` | "Thus instructed by the teacher, he began to praise the divine Ashvins with words and Rig Vedic verses. |059|" |
| `Line 1634: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1635: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1636: प्र पूर्वगौ पूर्वजौ चित्रभानू; गिरा वा शंसामि तपनावनन्तौ |` | "I praise with my voice the foremost ones, the first-born, of brilliant light; the radiant ones, the boundless ones." |
| `Line 1637: दिव्यौ सुपर्णौ विरजौ विमाना; वधिक्षियन्तौ भुवनानि विश्वा ||६०||` | "The two divine, well-winged, stainless, immeasurable ones, who rule over all the worlds. ||60||" |
| `Line 1638: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1639: हिरण्मयौ शकुनी साम्परायौ; नासत्यदस्रौ सुनसौ वैजयन्तौ |` | "The two golden birds, companions in the journey; the truthful and miraculous ones, with beautiful noses, victorious." |
| `Line 1640: शुक्रं वयन्तौ तरसा सुवेमा; वभि व्ययन्तावसितं विवस्वत् ||६१||` | "Weaving brightness with speed, with excellent work; dispelling the darkness of the sun. ||61||" |
| `Line 1641: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1642: ग्रस्तां सुपर्णस्य बलेन वर्तिका; ममुञ्चतामश्विनौ सौभगाय |` | "The quail [bird] seized by the might of the eagle; the Ashvins released it for good fortune." |
| `Line 1643: तावत्सुवृत्तावनमन्त मायया; सत्तमा गा अरुणा उदावहन् ||६२||` | "Those two excellent ones bowed with their power; the most excellent reddish cows they brought forth. ||62||" |
| `Line 1644: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1645: षष्टिश्च गावस्त्रिशताश्च धेनव; एकं वत्सं सुवते तं दुहन्ति |` | "Three hundred and sixty cows give birth to one calf and they all milk it." |
| `Line 1646: नानागोष्ठा विहिता एकदोहना; स्तावश्विनौ दुहतो घर्ममुक्थ्यम् ||६३||` | "Though in different cow-pens, they yield milk at once; those Ashvins milk the praiseworthy ghee [clarified butter]. ||63||" |
| `Line 1647: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1648: एकां नाभिं सप्तशता अराः श्रिताः; प्रधिष्वन्या विंशतिरर्पिता अराः |` | "Seven hundred spokes are fixed in one hub; in another rim, twenty spokes are fixed." |
| `Line 1649: अनेमि चक्रं परिवर्ततेऽजरं; मायाश्विनौ समनक्ति चर्षणी ||६४||` | "The rimless wheel revolves without aging; the power of the Ashvins unites the people. ||64||" |
| `Line 1650: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1651: एकं चक्रं वर्तते द्वादशारं प्रधि; षण्णाभिमेकाक्षममृतस्य धारणम् |` | "One wheel revolves with twelve spokes, six naves, one axle, and it is the bearer of immortality [cosmic order]," |
| `Line 1652: यस्मिन्देवा अधि विश्वे विषक्ता; स्तावश्विनौ मुञ्चतो मा विषीदतम् ||६५||` | "In which all the gods are fixed; O Ashvins [divine twin physicians], release me, do not let me perish. ||65||" |
| `Line 1653: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1654: अश्विनाविन्द्रममृतं वृत्तभूयौ; तिरोधत्तामश्विनौ दासपत्नी |` | "The Ashvins, having become the protectors of immortal Indra; the Ashvins concealed the wife of Dāsa [demon/servant]," |
| `Line 1655: भित्त्वा गिरिमश्विनौ गामुदाचरन्तौ; तद्वृष्टमह्ना प्रथिता वलस्य ||६६||` | "Breaking the mountain, the Ashvins brought forth the cow [or earth]; that deed is celebrated day by day as the splitting of Vala [cave demon]. ||66||" |
| `Line 1656: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1657: युवां दिशो जनयथो दशाग्रे; समानं मूर्ध्नि रथया वियन्ति |` | "You two create the ten directions at the beginning; they spread out equally from the summit by your chariot," |
| `Line 1658: तासां यातमृषयोऽनुप्रयान्ति; देवा मनुष्याः क्षितिमाचरन्ति ||६७||` | "The sages follow your path through them; gods and humans move about on the earth. ||67||" |
| `Line 1659: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1660: युवां वर्णान्विकुरुथो विश्वरूपां; स्तेऽधिक्षियन्ति भुवनानि विश्वा |` | "You two create colors of various forms; they pervade all the worlds," |
| `Line 1661: ते भानवोऽप्यनुसृताश्चरन्ति; देवा मनुष्याः क्षितिमाचरन्ति ||६८||` | "Those rays of light move about being followed; gods and humans move about on the earth. ||68||" |
| `Line 1662: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1663: तौ नासत्यावश्विनावामहे वां; स्रजं च यां बिभृथः पुष्करस्य |` | "We invoke you two, the Nāsatyas [truthful ones], the Ashvins; and the garland of the lotus that you both wear," |
| `Line 1664: तौ नासत्यावमृतावृतावृधा; वृते देवास्तत्प्रपदेन सूते ||६९||` | "Those two Nāsatyas, immortal, promoters of truth; by their guidance the gods bring forth creation. ||69||" |
| `Line 1665: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1666: मुखेन गर्भं लभतां युवानौ; गतासुरेतत्प्रपदेन सूते |` | "May the young ones receive the embryo through the mouth; when life has departed, it gives birth through that guidance," |
| `Line 1667: सद्यो जातो मातरमत्ति गर्भ; स्तावश्विनौ मुञ्चथो जीवसे गाः ||७०||` | "As soon as born, the embryo consumes its mother; O Ashvins, you release the cows [or rays/life] for living. ||70||" |
| `Line 1668: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1669: एवं तेनाभिष्टुतावश्विनावाजग्मतुः |` | "Thus praised by him, the Ashvins arrived," |
| `Line 1670: आहतुश्चैनम् |` | "And said to him," |
| `Line 1671: प्रीतौ स्वः |` | "We are pleased," |
| `Line 1672: एष तेऽपूपः |` | "Here is a cake for you," |
| `Line 1673: अशानैनमिति | ०७१ |` | "Eat it. |71|" |
| `Line 1674: स एवमुक्तः प्रत्युवाच |` | "He, thus addressed, replied," |
| `Line 1675: नानृतमूचतुर्भवन्तौ |` | "You two do not speak untruth," |
| `Line 1676: न त्वहमेतमपूपमुपयोक्तुमुत्सहे अनिवेद्य गुरव इति | ०७२ |` | "But I cannot bring myself to eat this cake without informing my teacher. |072|" |
| `Line 1677: ततस्तमश्विनावूचतुः |` | "Then the Ashvins [divine twin physicians] said to him:" |
| `Line 1678: आवाभ्यां पुरस्ताद्भवत उपाध्यायेनैवमेवाभिष्टुताभ्यामपूपः प्रीताभ्यां दत्तः |` | "Previously, your teacher himself offered a cake to us when we were pleased by his praises." |
| `Line 1679: उपयुक्तश्च स तेनानिवेद्य गुरवे |` | "And he consumed it without informing his own teacher." |
| `Line 1680: त्वमपि तथैव कुरुष्व यथा कृतमुपाध्यायेनेति | ०७३ |` | "You should also do just as your teacher did. |073|" |
| `Line 1681: स एवमुक्तः पुनरेव प्रत्युवाचैतौ |` | "Having been thus addressed, he again replied to them:" |
| `Line 1682: प्रत्यनुनये भवन्तावश्विनौ |` | "I beg your pardon, O Ashvins." |
| `Line 1683: नोत्सहेऽहमनिवेद्योपाध्यायायोपयोक्तुमिति | ०७४ |` | "I cannot bring myself to consume this without informing my teacher. |074|" |
| `Line 1684: तमश्विनावाहतुः |` | "The Ashvins said to him:" |
| `Line 1685: प्रीतौ स्वस्तवानया गुरुवृत्त्या |` | "We are pleased with your praise and this devotion to your teacher." |
| `Line 1686: उपाध्यायस्य ते कार्ष्णायसा दन्ताः |` | "Your teacher's teeth are of iron." |
| `Line 1687: भवतो हिरण्मया भविष्यन्ति |` | "Yours shall become golden." |
| `Line 1688: चक्षुष्मांश्च भविष्यसि |` | "And you shall regain your sight." |
| `Line 1689: श्रेयश्चावाप्स्यसीति | ०७५ |` | "And you shall attain prosperity. |075|" |
| `Line 1690: स एवमुक्तोऽश्विभ्यां लब्धचक्षुरुपाध्यायसकाशमागम्योपाध्यायमभिवाद्याचचक्षे |` | "Thus addressed by the Ashvins, having regained his sight, he went to his teacher, greeted him, and told him everything." |
| `Line 1691: स चास्य प्रीतिमानभूत् | ०७६ |` | "And the teacher was pleased with him. |076|" |
| `Line 1692: आह चैनम् |` | "And he said to him:" |
| `Line 1693: यथाश्विनावाहतुस्तथा त्वं श्रेयोऽवाप्स्यसीति |` | "As the Ashvins have said, so shall you attain prosperity." |
| `Line 1694: सर्वे च ते वेदाः प्रतिभास्यन्तीति | ०७७ |` | "And all the Vedas [sacred texts] shall become clear to you. |077|" |
| `Line 1695: एषा तस्यापि परीक्षोपमन्योः | ०७८ |` | "This was the test of Upamanyu as well. |078|" |
| `Line 1696: अथापरः शिष्यस्तस्यैवायोदस्य धौम्यस्य वेदो नाम | ०७९ |` | "Now, another disciple of that same Ayoda Dhaumya was named Veda. |079|" |
| `Line 1697: तमुपाध्यायः संदिदेश |` | "The teacher instructed him:" |
| `Line 1698: वत्स वेद इहास्यताम् |` | "Dear Veda, stay here." |
| `Line 1699: भवता मद्गृहे कञ्चित्कालं शुश्रूषमाणेन भवितव्यम् |` | "You must serve in my house for some time." |
| `Line 1700: श्रेयस्ते भविष्यतीति | ०८० |` | "It will be beneficial for you. |080|" |
| `Line 1701: स तथेत्युक्त्वा गुरुकुले दीर्घकालं गुरुशुश्रूषणपरोऽवसत् |` | "Having said 'so be it,' he lived in the teacher's household for a long time, devoted to serving his guru." |
| `Line 1702: गौरिव नित्यं गुरुषु धूर्षु नियुज्यमानः शीतोष्णक्षुत्तृष्णादुःखसहः सर्वत्राप्रतिकूलः | ०८१ |` | "Like an ox, constantly engaged in heavy tasks by his teachers, enduring the suffering of cold, heat, hunger and thirst, never being contrary in any situation. |081|" |
| `Line 1703: तस्य महता कालेन गुरुः परितोषं जगाम |` | "After a long time, his teacher became completely satisfied with him." |
| `Line 1704: तत्परितोषाच्च श्रेयः सर्वज्ञतां चावाप |` | "And from that satisfaction, he attained excellence and omniscience." |
| `Line 1705: एषा तस्यापि परीक्षा वेदस्य | ०८२ |` | "This was also his test by Veda [sage/teacher]. |082|" |
| `Line 1706: स उपाध्यायेनानुज्ञातः समावृत्तस्तस्माद्गुरुकुलवासाद्गृहाश्रमं प्रत्यपद्यत |` | "Having been permitted by his teacher, he completed his education and departed from the teacher's residence to enter the householder stage [gṛhastha āśrama]." |
| `Line 1707: तस्यापि स्वगृहे वसतस्त्रयः शिष्या बभूवुः | ०८३ |` | "While living in his own house, he too had three disciples. |083|" |
| `Line 1708: स शिष्यान्न किञ्चिदुवाच |` | "He did not say anything to his disciples." |
| `Line 1709: कर्म वा क्रियतां गुरुशुश्रूषा वेति |` | "Neither 'perform this work' nor 'serve the teacher.'" |
| `Line 1710: दुःखाभिज्ञो हि गुरुकुलवासस्य शिष्यान्परिक्लेशेन योजयितुं नेयेष | ०८४ |` | "For having known the hardships of living in a teacher's household, he did not wish to subject his disciples to such suffering. |084|" |
| `Line 1711: अथ कस्यचित्कालस्य वेदं ब्राह्मणं जनमेजयः पौष्यश्च क्षत्रियावुपेत्योपाध्यायं वरयां चक्रतुः | ०८५ |` | "Then after some time, Janamejaya and Paushya, two Kshatriyas [warrior class], approached Veda the Brahmin and chose him as their teacher. |085|" |
| `Line 1712: स कदाचिद्याज्यकार्येणाभिप्रस्थित उत्तङ्कं नाम शिष्यं नियोजयामास |` | "Once, when departing for a sacrificial ceremony, he instructed his disciple named Uttanka:" |
| `Line 1713: भो उत्तङ्क यत्किञ्चिदस्मद्गृहे परिहीयते तदिच्छाम्यहमपरिहीणं भवता क्रियमाणमिति | ०८६ |` | "O Uttanka, whatever needs to be maintained in our house, I wish that you would keep it all in good order. |086|" |
| `Line 1714: स एवं प्रतिसमादिश्योत्तङ्कं वेदः प्रवासं जगाम | ०८७ |` | "Having given these instructions to Uttanka, Veda went away on his journey. |087|" |
| `Line 1715: अथोत्तङ्को गुरुशुश्रूषुर्गुरुनियोगमनुतिष्ठमानस्तत्र गुरुकुले वसति स्म | ०८८ |` | "Then Uttanka, eager to serve his teacher and following his instructions, continued to live in the teacher's household. |088|" |
| `Line 1716: स वसंस्तत्रोपाध्यायस्त्रीभिः सहिताभिराहूयोक्तः |` | "While living there, he was called and told by the teacher's wives together:" |
| `Line 1717: उपाध्यायिनी ते ऋतुमती |` | "Your teacher's wife is in her fertile period [menstruating]." |
| `Line 1718: उपाध्यायश्च प्रोषितः |` | "And the teacher is away from home." |
| `Line 1719: अस्या यथायमृतुर्वन्ध्यो न भवति तथा क्रियताम् |` | "Act in such a way that her fertile period does not go in vain." |
| `Line 1720: एतद्विषीदतीति | ०८९ |` | "She is distressed about this. |089|" |
| `Line 1721: स एवमुक्तस्ताः स्त्रियः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Having been told this, he replied to those women:" |
| `Line 1722: न मया स्त्रीणां वचनादिदमकार्यं कार्यम् |` | "I should not do this improper act at the word of women." |
| `Line 1723: न ह्यहमुपाध्यायेन संदिष्टः |` | "For I have not been instructed by my teacher to do this." |
| `Line 1724: अकार्यमपि त्वया कार्यमिति | ०९० |` | "That even improper acts should be done by me. |090|" |
| `Line 1725: तस्य पुनरुपाध्यायः कालान्तरेण गृहानुपजगाम तस्मात्प्रवासात् |` | "After some time, his teacher returned home from that journey." |
| `Line 1726: स तद्वृत्तं तस्याशेषमुपलभ्य प्रीतिमानभूत् | ०९१ |` | "He, having learned all about that incident, became pleased. |091|" |
| `Line 1727: उवाच चैनम् |` | "And he said to him:" |
| `Line 1728: वत्सोत्तङ्क किं ते प्रियं करवाणीति |` | "My child Uttanka, what may I do that would please you?" |
| `Line 1729: धर्मतो हि शुश्रूषितोऽस्मि भवता |` | "For I have been served by you according to dharma [righteous duty]." |
| `Line 1730: तेन प्रीतिः परस्परेण नौ संवृद्धा |` | "Through that, affection between us has grown." |
| `Line 1731: तदनुजाने भवन्तम् |` | "Therefore, I give you permission." |
| `Line 1732: सर्वामेव सिद्धिं प्राप्स्यसि |` | "You will attain complete success." |
| `Line 1733: गम्यतामिति | ०९२ |` | "You may go. |092|" |
| `Line 1734: स एवमुक्तः प्रत्युवाच |` | "He, thus addressed, replied:" |
| `Line 1735: किं ते प्रियं करवाणीति |` | "What may I do that would please you?" |
| `Line 1736: एवं ह्याहुः | ०९३ |` | "For thus they say: |093|" |
| `Line 1737: यश्चाधर्मेण विब्रूयाद्यश्चाधर्मेण पृच्छति | ०९४ |` | "He who speaks unrighteously and he who questions unrighteously, |094|" |
| `Line 1738: तयोरन्यतरः प्रैति विद्वेषं चाधिगच्छति |` | "One of them perishes and incurs hatred." |
| `Line 1739: सोऽहमनुज्ञातो भवता इच्छामीष्टं ते गुर्वर्थमुपहर्तुमिति | ०९५ |` | "I, having been permitted by you, wish to bring you a desired guru-dakṣiṇā [teacher's fee]. |095|" |
| `Line 1740: तेनैवमुक्त उपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Thus addressed by him, the teacher replied:" |
| `Line 1741: वत्सोत्तङ्क उष्यतां तावदिति | ०९६ |` | "My child Uttanka, wait for now. |096|" |
| `Line 1742: स कदाचित्तमुपाध्यायमाहोत्तङ्कः |` | "Once, Uttanka said to that teacher:" |
| `Line 1743: आज्ञापयतु भवान् |` | "May you command me." |
| `Line 1744: किं ते प्रियमुपहरामि गुर्वर्थमिति | ०९७ |` | "What pleasing thing may I bring you as guru-dakṣiṇā [teacher's fee]? |097|" |
| `Line 1745: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him:" |
| `Line 1746: वत्सोत्तङ्क बहुशो मां चोदयसि गुर्वर्थमुपहरेयमिति |` | "My child Uttanka, you repeatedly urge me saying 'I should bring something as guru-dakṣiṇā [teacher's fee].'" |
| `Line 1747: तद्गच्छ |` | "Therefore, go." |
| `Line 1748: एनां प्रविश्योपाध्यायिनीं पृच्छ किमुपहरामीति |` | "Go to my wife and ask her, 'What should I bring?'" |
| `Line 1749: एषा यद्ब्रवीति तदुपहरस्वेति | ०९८ |` | "Whatever she says, bring that. |098|" |
| `Line 1750: स एवमुक्त उपाध्यायेनोपाध्यायिनीमपृच्छत् |` | "He, thus instructed by the teacher, asked the teacher's wife:" |
| `Line 1751: भवत्युपाध्यायेनास्म्यनुज्ञातो गृहं गन्तुम् |` | "I have been permitted by your honorable teacher to go home." |
| `Line 1752: तदिच्छामीष्टं ते गुर्वर्थमुपहृत्यानृणो गन्तुम् |` | "Therefore, I wish to bring a suitable gift for the teacher and depart free from debt." |
| `Line 1753: तदाज्ञापयतु भवती |` | "So please instruct me, respected lady [teacher's wife]." |
| `Line 1754: किमुपहरामि गुर्वर्थमिति | ०९९ |` | "What should I bring as a gift for the teacher? |099|" |
| `Line 1755: सैवमुक्तोपाध्यायिन्युत्तङ्कं प्रत्युवाच |` | "Thus addressed, the teacher's wife replied to Uttanka:" |
| `Line 1756: गच्छ पौष्यं राजानम् |` | "Go to King Paushya." |
| `Line 1757: भिक्षस्व तस्य क्षत्रियया पिनद्धे कुण्डले |` | "Request the earrings worn by his queen [Kshatriya woman]." |
| `Line 1758: ते आनयस्व |` | "Bring those here." |
| `Line 1759: इतश्चतुर्थेऽहनि पुण्यकं भविता |` | "Four days from now there will be an auspicious ceremony [punyaka]." |
| `Line 1760: ताभ्यामाबद्धाभ्यां ब्राह्मणान्परिवेष्टुमिच्छामि |` | "I wish to serve the Brahmins while wearing those earrings." |
| `Line 1761: शोभमाना यथा ताभ्यां कुण्डलाभ्यां तस्मिन्नहनि सम्पादयस्व |` | "Ensure that I am adorned with those earrings on that day." |
| `Line 1762: श्रेयो हि ते स्यात्क्षणं कुर्वत इति | १०० |` | "It will be auspicious for you if you accomplish this task. |100|" |
| `Line 1763: स एवमुक्त उपाध्यायिन्या प्रातिष्ठतोत्तङ्कः |` | "Thus instructed by the teacher's wife, Uttanka set forth." |
| `Line 1764: स पथि गच्छन्नपश्यदृषभमतिप्रमाणं तमधिरूढं च पुरुषमतिप्रमाणमेव | १०१ |` | "While going along the path, he saw an enormous bull and a man of enormous size mounted on it. |101|" |
| `Line 1765: स पुरुष उत्तङ्कमभ्यभाषत |` | "That man addressed Uttanka:" |
| `Line 1766: उत्तङ्कैतत्पुरीषमस्य ऋषभस्य भक्षयस्वेति | १०२ |` | "Uttanka, eat this dung of this bull. |102|" |
| `Line 1767: स एवमुक्तो नैच्छत् | १०३ |` | "Thus addressed, he refused. |103|" |
| `Line 1768: तमाह पुरुषो भूयः |` | "The man spoke to him again:" |
| `Line 1769: भक्षयस्वोत्तङ्क |` | "Eat it, Uttanka." |
| `Line 1770: मा विचारय |` | "Do not hesitate." |
| `Line 1771: उपाध्यायेनापि ते भक्षितं पूर्वमिति | १०४ |` | "Your teacher also ate it before. |104|" |
| `Line 1772: स एवमुक्तो बाढमित्युक्त्वा तदा तदृषभस्य पुरीषं मूत्रं च भक्षयित्वोत्तङ्कः प्रतस्थे यत्र स क्षत्रियः पौष्यः | १०५ |` | "Thus addressed, saying 'Very well,' Uttanka then ate the dung and urine of that bull and proceeded to where King Paushya was. |105|" |
| `Line 1773: तमुपेत्यापश्यदुत्तङ्क आसीनम् |` | "Approaching, Uttanka saw him seated." |
| `Line 1774: स तमुपेत्याशीर्भिरभिनन्द्योवाच |` | "He approached him, greeted him with blessings, and said:" |
| `Line 1775: अर्थी भवन्तमुपगतोऽस्मीति | १०६ |` | "I have come to you as a petitioner. |106|" |
| `Line 1776: स एनमभिवाद्योवाच |` | "He, having greeted him, said:" |
| `Line 1777: भगवन्पौष्यः खल्वहम् |` | "Venerable sir, I am indeed Paushya." |
| `Line 1778: किं करवाणीति | १०७ |` | "What shall I do for you? ||107||" |
| `Line 1779: तमुवाचोत्तङ्कः |` | "Uttanka said to him:" |
| `Line 1780: गुर्वर्थे कुण्डलाभ्यामर्थ्यागतोऽस्मीति ये ते क्षत्रियया पिनद्धे कुण्डले ते भवान्दातुमर्हतीति | १०८ |` | "I have come to request the earrings for my guru's sake. Those earrings worn by your Kshatriya [warrior-class wife], you should give them to me. ||108||" |
| `Line 1781: तं पौष्यः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Paushya replied to him:" |
| `Line 1782: प्रविश्यान्तःपुरं क्षत्रिया याच्यतामिति | १०९ |` | "Enter the inner chambers and request them from the Kshatriya lady. ||109||" |
| `Line 1783: स तेनैवमुक्तः प्रविश्यान्तःपुरं क्षत्रियां नापश्यत् | ११० |` | "Having been thus instructed by him, he entered the inner chambers but did not see the Kshatriya lady. ||110||" |
| `Line 1784: स पौष्यं पुनरुवाच |` | "He again said to Paushya:" |
| `Line 1785: न युक्तं भवता वयमनृतेनोपचरितुम् |` | "It is not proper for you to treat us with falsehood." |
| `Line 1786: न हि ते क्षत्रियान्तःपुरे संनिहिता |` | "Your Kshatriya wife is not present in the inner chambers." |
| `Line 1787: नैनां पश्यामीति | १११ |` | "I do not see her. ||111||" |
| `Line 1788: स एवमुक्तः पौष्यस्तं प्रत्युवाच |` | "Thus addressed, Paushya replied to him:" |
| `Line 1789: सम्प्रति भवानुच्छिष्टः |` | "At present you are ucchishta [ritually impure from eating]." |
| `Line 1790: स्मर तावत् |` | "Think about it for a moment." |
| `Line 1791: न हि सा क्षत्रिया उच्छिष्टेनाशुचिना वा शक्या द्रष्टुम् |` | "Indeed, that Kshatriya lady cannot be seen by someone who is ucchishta or impure." |
| `Line 1792: पतिव्रतात्वादेषा नाशुचेर्दर्शनमुपैतीति | ११२ |` | "Because of her devotion to her husband, she does not appear before one who is impure. ||112||" |
| `Line 1793: अथैवमुक्त उत्तङ्कः स्मृत्वोवाच |` | "Then, thus addressed, Uttanka, after reflecting, said:" |
| `Line 1794: अस्ति खलु मयोच्छिष्टेनोपस्पृष्टं शीघ्रं गच्छता चेति | ११३ |` | "Indeed, I did touch something while being ucchishta and while walking quickly. ||113||" |
| `Line 1795: तं पौष्यः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Paushya replied to him:" |
| `Line 1796: एतत्तदेवं हि |` | "That is indeed so." |
| `Line 1797: न गच्छतोपस्पृष्टं भवति न स्थितेनेति | ११४ |` | "One should not touch anything while walking, nor while standing still. ||114||" |
| `Line 1798: अथोत्तङ्कस्तथेत्युक्त्वा प्राङ्मुख उपविश्य सुप्रक्षालितपाणिपादवदनोऽशब्दाभिर् हृदयङ्गमाभिरद्भिरुपस्पृश्य त्रिः पीत्वा द्विः परिमृज्य खान्यद्भिरुपस्पृश्यान्तःपुरं प्रविश्य तां क्षत्रियामपश्यत् | ११५ |` | "Then Uttanka, saying 'So be it,' sat facing east, thoroughly washed his hands, feet, and face, sipped water that was silent and pleasing to the heart three times, wiped twice, touched the bodily apertures with water, entered the inner chambers, and saw that Kshatriya lady. ||115||" |
| `Line 1799: सा च दृष्ट्वैवोत्तङ्कमभ्युत्थायाभिवाद्योवाच |` | "And she, upon seeing Uttanka, rose up, greeted him, and said:" |
| `Line 1800: स्वागतं ते भगवन् |` | "Welcome to you, venerable sir." |
| `Line 1801: आज्ञापय किं करवाणीति | ११६ |` | "Command me, what shall I do? |116|" |
| `Line 1802: स तामुवाच |` | "He said to her:" |
| `Line 1803: एते कुण्डले गुर्वर्थं मे भिक्षिते दातुमर्हसीति | ११७ |` | "You should give me these two earrings which I am begging for my teacher's sake. |117|" |
| `Line 1804: सा प्रीता तेन तस्य सद्भावेन पात्रमयमनतिक्रमणीयश्चेति मत्वा ते कुण्डले अवमुच्यास्मै प्रायच्छत् | ११८ |` | "She, pleased by his sincerity and thinking 'he is a worthy recipient who should not be refused,' removed those earrings and gave them to him. |118|" |
| `Line 1805: आह चैनम् |` | "And she said to him:" |
| `Line 1806: एते कुण्डले तक्षको नागराजः प्रार्थयति |` | "Takshaka, the king of serpents [nāga lord], desires these earrings." |
| `Line 1807: अप्रमत्तो नेतुमर्हसीति | ११९ |` | "You should carry them with vigilance. |119|" |
| `Line 1808: स एवमुक्तस्तां क्षत्रियां प्रत्युवाच |` | "He, thus addressed, replied to that Kshatriya woman:" |
| `Line 1809: भवति सुनिर्वृता भव |` | "Lady, be at ease," |
| `Line 1810: न मां शक्तस्तक्षको नागराजो धर्षयितुमिति | १२० |` | "Takshaka, the king of serpents, is not capable of harming me. |120|" |
| `Line 1811: स एवमुक्त्वा तां क्षत्रियामामन्त्र्य पौष्यसकाशमागच्छत् | १२१ |` | "Having spoken thus and taking leave of that Kshatriya woman, he went to Paushya. |121|" |
| `Line 1812: स तं दृष्ट्वोवाच |` | "Seeing him, he said:" |
| `Line 1813: भोः पौष्य प्रीतोऽस्मीति | १२२ |` | "O Paushya, I am pleased. |122|" |
| `Line 1814: तं पौष्यः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Paushya replied to him:" |
| `Line 1815: भगवंश्चिरस्य पात्रमासाद्यते |` | "Venerable sir, after a long time a worthy recipient has arrived," |
| `Line 1816: भवांश्च गुणवानतिथिः |` | "And you are a virtuous guest." |
| `Line 1817: तत्करिष्ये श्राद्धम् |` | "Therefore, I will perform a śrāddha [ancestral rite]." |
| `Line 1818: क्षणः क्रियतामिति | १२३ |` | "Please wait a moment. |123|" |
| `Line 1819: तमुत्तङ्कः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Uttanka replied to him:" |
| `Line 1820: कृतक्षण एवास्मि |` | "I have already waited enough," |
| `Line 1821: शीघ्रमिच्छामि यथोपपन्नमन्नमुपहृतं भवतेति | १२४ |` | "I wish for food to be served quickly, whatever is readily available. |124|" |
| `Line 1822: स तथेत्युक्त्वा यथोपपन्नेनान्नेनैनं भोजयामास | १२५ |` | "He, saying 'so be it,' fed him with whatever food was available. |125|" |
| `Line 1823: अथोत्तङ्कः शीतमन्नं सकेशं दृष्ट्वा अशुच्येतदिति मत्वा पौष्यमुवाच |` | "Then Uttanka, seeing the food was cold and contained hair, thinking 'this is impure,' said to Paushya:" |
| `Line 1824: यस्मान्मे अशुच्यन्नं ददासि तस्मदन्धो भविष्यसीति | १२६ |` | "Because you give me impure food, therefore you shall become blind. |126|" |
| `Line 1825: तं पौष्यः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Paushya replied to him:" |
| `Line 1826: यस्मात्त्वमप्यदुष्टमन्नं दूषयसि तस्मादनपत्यो भविष्यसीति | १२७ |` | "Since you too defame food that is not defiled, therefore you shall be childless. |127|" |
| `Line 1827: सोऽथ पौष्यस्तस्याशुचिभावमन्नस्यागमयामास | १२८ |` | "Then Paushya [the teacher] verified the impurity of that food. |128|" |
| `Line 1828: अथ तदन्नं मुक्तकेश्या स्त्रियोपहृतं सकेशमशुचि मत्वोत्तङ्कं प्रसादयामास |` | "Then, realizing that the food brought by a woman with loose hair contained hair and was impure, he appeased Uttanka." |
| `Line 1829: भगवन्नज्ञानादेतदन्नं सकेशमुपहृतं शीतं च |` | "Venerable sir, through ignorance this food was brought with hair in it and cold." |
| `Line 1830: तत्क्षामये भवन्तम् |` | "For that I beg your pardon." |
| `Line 1831: न भवेयमन्ध इति | १२९ |` | "May I not become blind. |129|" |
| `Line 1832: तमुत्तङ्कः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Uttanka replied to him:" |
| `Line 1833: न मृषा ब्रवीमि |` | "I do not speak falsely." |
| `Line 1834: भूत्वा त्वमन्धो नचिरादनन्धो भविष्यसीति |` | "You will become blind, but before long you will regain your sight." |
| `Line 1835: ममापि शापो न भवेद्भवता दत्त इति | १३० |` | "And may the curse given by you to me not take effect. |130|" |
| `Line 1836: तं पौष्यः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Paushya replied to him:" |
| `Line 1837: नाहं शक्तः शापं प्रत्यादातुम् |` | "I am not able to take back the curse." |
| `Line 1838: न हि मे मन्युरद्याप्युपशमं गच्छति |` | "For my anger has not yet subsided." |
| `Line 1839: किं चैतद्भवता न ज्ञायते यथा | १३१ |` | "And do you not know this, that: |131|" |
| `Line 1840: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1841: नावनीतं हृदयं ब्राह्मणस्य; वाचि क्षुरो निहितस्तीक्ष्णधारः |` | "The heart of a Brahmin is like butter, but a sharp-edged razor is placed in his speech." |
| `Line 1842: विपरीतमेतदुभयं क्षत्रियस्य; वाङ्नावनीती हृदयं तीक्ष्णधारम् ||१३२||` | "For a Kshatriya [warrior class], both these are reversed: his speech is like butter, but his heart has a sharp edge. ||132||" |
| `Line 1843: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1844: इति |` | "Thus." |
| `Line 1845: तदेवं गते न शक्तोऽहं तीक्ष्णहृदयत्वात्तं शापमन्यथा कर्तुम् |` | "This being so, I am unable, due to my sharp-heartedness, to alter that curse." |
| `Line 1846: गम्यतामिति | १३३ |` | "You may go. |133|" |
| `Line 1847: तमुत्तङ्कः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Uttanka replied to him:" |
| `Line 1848: भवताहमन्नस्याशुचिभावमागमय्य प्रत्यनुनीतः |` | "After verifying the impurity of the food, you have apologized to me." |
| `Line 1849: प्राक्च तेऽभिहितम् |` | "And previously you said to me:" |
| `Line 1850: यस्माददुष्टमन्नं दूषयसि तस्मादनपत्यो भविष्यसीति |` | "'Since you defame food that is not defiled, therefore you shall be childless.'" |
| `Line 1851: दुष्टे चान्ने नैष मम शापो भविष्यतीति | १३४ |` | "And if the food is spoiled, this curse of mine will not take effect. |134|" |
| `Line 1852: साधयामस्तावदित्युक्त्वा प्रातिष्ठतोत्तङ्कस्ते कुण्डले गृहीत्वा | १३५ |` | "Saying 'Let me accomplish this first,' Uttanka set out, taking those earrings. |135|" |
| `Line 1853: सोऽपश्यत्पथि नग्नं श्रमणमागच्छन्तं मुहुर्मुहुर्दृश्यमानमदृश्यमानं च |` | "On the way, he saw a naked ascetic [śramaṇa] approaching, who kept appearing and disappearing repeatedly." |
| `Line 1854: अथोत्तङ्कस्ते कुण्डले भूमौ निक्षिप्योदकार्थं प्रचक्रमे | १३६ |` | "Then Uttanka, placing those earrings on the ground, proceeded to get water. |136|" |
| `Line 1855: एतस्मिन्नन्तरे स श्रमणस्त्वरमाण उपसृत्य ते कुण्डले गृहीत्वा प्राद्रवत् |` | "Meanwhile, that ascetic hurriedly approached, took those earrings, and ran away." |
| `Line 1856: तमुत्तङ्कोऽभिसृत्य जग्राह |` | "Uttanka pursued him and caught him." |
| `Line 1857: स तद्रूपं विहाय तक्षकरूपं कृत्वा सहसा धरण्यां विवृतं महाबिलं विवेश | १३७ |` | "He, abandoning that form and assuming the form of Takshaka [serpent king], suddenly entered a large hole that opened in the earth. |137|" |
| `Line 1858: प्रविश्य च नागलोकं स्वभवनमगच्छत् |` | "And having entered the realm of serpents [nāgaloka], he went to his own abode." |
| `Line 1859: तमुत्तङ्कोऽन्वाविवेश तेनैव बिलेन |` | "Uttanka followed him through that same hole." |
| `Line 1860: प्रविश्य च नागानस्तुवदेभिः श्लोकैः | १३८ |` | "And having entered, he praised the serpents with these verses. |138|" |
| `Line 1861: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1862: य ऐरावतराजानः सर्पाः समितिशोभनाः |` | "Those serpent kings of Airāvata lineage [noble serpent clan], who adorn assemblies," |
| `Line 1863: वर्षन्त इव जीमूताः सविद्युत्पवनेरिताः ||१३९||` | "Are like rain clouds driven by wind with lightning. ||139||" |
| `Line 1864: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1865: सुरूपाश्च विरूपाश्च तथा कल्माषकुण्डलाः |` | "Both beautiful and misshapen, as well as those with spotted coils," |
| `Line 1866: आदित्यवन्नाकपृष्ठे रेजुरैरावतोद्भवाः ||१४०||` | "The descendants of Airāvata shine in the heavens like the sun. ||140||" |
| `Line 1867: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1868: बहूनि नागवर्त्मानि गङ्गायास्तीर उत्तरे |` | "Many are the paths of serpents on the northern bank of the Ganges," |
| `Line 1869: इच्छेत्कोऽर्कांशुसेनायां चर्तुमैरावतं विना ||१४१||` | "Who would wish to move in the army of sun's rays without Airāvata? ||141||" |
| `Line 1870: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1871: शतान्यशीतिरष्टौ च सहस्राणि च विंशतिः |` | "Eighty-eight hundreds and twenty thousand," |
| `Line 1872: सर्पाणां प्रग्रहा यान्ति धृतराष्ट्रो यदेजति ||१४२||` | "Serpents move as attendants when Dhritarashtra [serpent king] stirs. ||142||" |
| `Line 1873: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1874: ये चैनमुपसर्पन्ति ये च दूरं परं गताः |` | "Those who approach him and those who have gone far away," |
| `Line 1875: अहमैरावतज्येष्ठभ्रातृभ्योऽकरवं नमः ||१४३||` | "I offer salutations to the elder brothers of Airāvata. ||143||" |
| `Line 1876: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1877: यस्य वासः कुरुक्षेत्रे खाण्डवे चाभवत्सदा |` | "Whose dwelling was always in Kurukshetra [sacred battlefield] and in Khandava [forest region]," |
| `Line 1878: तं काद्रवेयमस्तौषं कुण्डलार्थाय तक्षकम् ||१४४||` | "I praised that Kadraveya [son of Kadru], Takshaka [serpent king], for the purpose of obtaining the earrings. ||144||" |
| `Line 1879: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1880: तक्षकश्चाश्वसेनश्च नित्यं सहचरावुभौ |` | "Both Takshaka and Ashvasena [serpent prince], always companions together," |
| `Line 1881: कुरुक्षेत्रे निवसतां नदीमिक्षुमतीमनु ||१४५||` | "Dwelled in Kurukshetra along the river Ikshumati [sugarcane river]. ||145||" |
| `Line 1882: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1883: जघन्यजस्तक्षकस्य श्रुतसेनेति यः श्रुतः |` | "The youngest son of Takshaka, who was known as Shrutasena [famed army]," |
| `Line 1884: अवसद्यो महद्द्युम्नि प्रार्थयन्नागमुख्यताम् ||१४६||` | "Who dwelled in Mahaddyumni [great splendor], aspiring for leadership among the serpents. ||146||" |
| `Line 1885: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1886: करवाणि सदा चाहं नमस्तस्मै महात्मने ||१४६||` | "I always offer my salutations to that great soul. ||146||" |
| `Line 1887: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1888: एवं स्तुवन्नपि नागान्यदा ते कुण्डले नालभदथापश्यत्स्त्रियौ तन्त्रे अधिरोप्य पटं वयन्त्यौ | १४७ |` | "Even while praising the serpents thus, when he did not obtain those earrings, he then saw two women weaving cloth on a loom. |147|" |
| `Line 1889: तस्मिंश्च तन्त्रे कृष्णाः सिताश्च तन्तवः |` | "And on that loom were black and white threads," |
| `Line 1890: चक्रं चापश्यत्षड्भिः कुमारैः परिवर्त्यमानम् |` | "And he saw a wheel being rotated by six youths," |
| `Line 1891: पुरुषं चापश्यद्दर्शनीयम् | १४८ |` | "And he saw a handsome person. |148|" |
| `Line 1892: स तान्सर्वांस्तुष्टाव एभिर्मन्त्रवादश्लोकैः | १४९ |` | "He praised all of them with these mantra-verses. |149|" |
| `Line 1893: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1894: त्रीण्यर्पितान्यत्र शतानि मध्ये; षष्टिश्च नित्यं चरति ध्रुवेऽस्मिन् |` | "Three hundred are fixed in the middle; and sixty move constantly in this fixed (wheel)," |
| `Line 1895: चक्रे चतुर्विंशतिपर्वयोगे; षड्यत्कुमाराः परिवर्तयन्ति ||१५०||` | "In this wheel with twenty-four junctions, which six youths rotate. ||150||" |
| `Line 1896: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1897: तन्त्रं चेदं विश्वरूपं युवत्यौ; वयतस्तन्तून्सततं वर्तयन्त्यौ |` | "This loom of universal form, the two young women weave the threads continuously," |
| `Line 1898: कृष्णान्सितांश्चैव विवर्तयन्त्यौ; भूतान्यजस्रं भुवनानि चैव ||१५१||` | "Turning the black and white threads, (representing) beings and worlds unceasingly. ||151||" |
| `Line 1899: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1900: वज्रस्य भर्ता भुवनस्य गोप्ता; वृत्रस्य हन्ता नमुचेर्निहन्ता |` | "The wielder of the thunderbolt [Indra], protector of the world, slayer of Vritra [demon], destroyer of Namuchi [demon]," |
| `Line 1901: कृष्णे वसानो वसने महात्मा; सत्यानृते यो विविनक्ति लोके ||१५२||` | "The great soul who wears dark garments, who distinguishes between truth and falsehood in the world. ||152||" |
| `Line 1902: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1903: यो वाजिनं गर्भमपां पुराणं; वैश्वानरं वाहनमभ्युपेतः |` | "Who has approached the ancient seed of waters, the horse, Vaishvanara [fire deity] as his vehicle," |
| `Line 1904: नमः सदास्मै जगदीश्वराय; लोकत्रयेशाय पुरंदराय ||१५३||` | "Salutations always to him, the lord of the universe, the ruler of the three worlds, the destroyer of cities [Indra]. ||153||" |
| `Line 1905: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 1906: ततः स एनं पुरुषः प्राह |` | "Then that person said to him," |
| `Line 1907: प्रीतोऽस्मि तेऽहमनेन स्तोत्रेण |` | "I am pleased with you by this hymn of praise." |
| `Line 1908: किं ते प्रियं करवाणीति | १५४ |` | "What shall I do that is pleasing to you? ||154||" |
| `Line 1909: स तमुवाच |` | "He said to him," |
| `Line 1910: नागा मे वशमीयुरिति | १५५ |` | "Let the serpents come under my control. ||155||" |
| `Line 1911: स एनं पुरुषः पुनरुवाच |` | "That person said to him again," |
| `Line 1912: एतमश्वमपाने धमस्वेति | १५६ |` | "Blow on this horse from behind [its rear]. ||156||" |
| `Line 1913: स तमश्वमपानेऽधमत् |` | "He blew on that horse from behind," |
| `Line 1914: अथाश्वाद्धम्यमानात्सर्वस्रोतोभ्यः सधूमा अर्चिषोऽग्नेर्निष्पेतुः | १५७ |` | "Then from the horse being blown upon, smoky flames of fire shot forth from all its openings. ||157||" |
| `Line 1915: ताभिर्नागलोको धूपितः | १५८ |` | "By those flames, the serpent world was fumigated. ||158||" |
| `Line 1916: अथ ससम्भ्रमस्तक्षकोऽग्नितेजोभयविषण्णस्ते कुण्डले गृहीत्वा सहसा स्वभवनान्निष्क्रम्योत्तङ्कमुवाच |` | "Then Takshaka [serpent king], agitated and distressed by the fear of the fire's power, suddenly took those earrings, came out of his abode, and said to Uttanka," |
| `Line 1917: एते कुण्डले प्रतिगृह्णातु भवानिति | १५९ |` | "Let your honor accept these earrings. ||159||" |
| `Line 1918: स ते प्रतिजग्राहोत्तङ्कः |` | "Uttanka accepted those earrings." |
| `Line 1919: कुण्डले प्रतिगृह्याचिन्तयत् |` | "Having received the earrings, he thought," |
| `Line 1920: अद्य तत्पुण्यकमुपाध्यायिन्याः |` | "Today is that auspicious day of my teacher's wife." |
| `Line 1921: दूरं चाहमभ्यागतः |` | "And I have come from afar." |
| `Line 1922: कथं नु खलु सम्भावयेयमिति | १६० |` | "How indeed shall I reach there in time? ||160||" |
| `Line 1923: तत एनं चिन्तयानमेव स पुरुष उवाच |` | "Then as he was thinking, that person said to him," |
| `Line 1924: उत्तङ्क एनमश्वमधिरोह |` | "Uttanka, mount this horse." |
| `Line 1925: एष त्वां क्षणादेवोपाध्यायकुलं प्रापयिष्यतीति | १६१ |` | "This will take you to your teacher's house in an instant. ||161||" |
| `Line 1926: स तथेत्युक्त्वा तमश्वमधिरुह्य प्रत्याजगामोपाध्यायकुलम् |` | "Having said 'so be it,' he mounted that horse and returned to his teacher's house." |
| `Line 1927: उपाध्यायिनी च स्नाता केशानावपयन्त्युपविष्टोत्तङ्को नागच्छतीति शापायास्य मनो दधे | १६२ |` | "And the teacher's wife, having bathed and sitting while drying her hair, set her mind to curse him thinking, 'Uttanka is not coming.' |162|" |
| `Line 1928: अथोत्तङ्कः प्रविश्य उपाध्यायिनीमभ्यवादयत् |` | "Then Uttanka, entering, greeted the teacher's wife." |
| `Line 1929: ते चास्यै कुण्डले प्रायच्छत् | १६३ |` | "And he presented the earrings to her. |163|" |
| `Line 1930: सा चैनं प्रत्युवाच |` | "And she replied to him:" |
| `Line 1931: उत्तङ्क देशे कालेऽभ्यागतः |` | "Uttanka, you have arrived at the right place and time." |
| `Line 1932: स्वागतं ते वत्स |` | "Welcome to you, my child." |
| `Line 1933: मनागसि मया न शप्तः |` | "You were not cursed by me, as you are innocent." |
| `Line 1934: श्रेयस्तवोपस्थितम् |` | "Good fortune has come to you." |
| `Line 1935: सिद्धिमाप्नुहीति | १६४ |` | "May you attain success. |164|" |
| `Line 1936: अथोत्तङ्क उपाध्यायमभ्यवादयत् |` | "Then Uttanka greeted his teacher." |
| `Line 1937: तमुपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "The teacher replied to him:" |
| `Line 1938: वत्सोत्तङ्क स्वागतं ते |` | "Child Uttanka, welcome to you." |
| `Line 1939: किं चिरं कृतमिति | १६५ |` | "Why did you take so long? |165|" |
| `Line 1940: तमुत्तङ्क उपाध्यायं प्रत्युवाच |` | "Uttanka replied to his teacher:" |
| `Line 1941: भोस्तक्षकेण नागराजेन विघ्नः कृतोऽस्मिन्कर्मणि |` | "Sir, Takshaka, the serpent king [nāga ruler], created an obstacle in this task." |
| `Line 1942: तेनास्मि नागलोकं नीतः | १६६ |` | "By him I was taken to the serpent world [nāgaloka]. |166|" |
| `Line 1943: तत्र च मया दृष्टे स्त्रियौ तन्त्रेऽधिरोप्य पटं वयन्त्यौ |` | "And there I saw two women weaving a cloth mounted on a loom." |
| `Line 1944: तस्मिंश्च तन्त्रे कृष्णाः सिताश्च तन्तवः |` | "And in that loom were black and white threads." |
| `Line 1945: किं तत् | १६७ |` | "What was that? |167|" |
| `Line 1946: तत्र च मया चक्रं दृष्टं द्वादशारम् |` | "And there I saw a wheel with twelve spokes." |
| `Line 1947: षट्चैनं कुमाराः परिवर्तयन्ति |` | "And six youths were turning it." |
| `Line 1948: तदपि किम् | १६८ |` | "What was that also? |168|" |
| `Line 1949: पुरुषश्चापि मया दृष्टः |` | "And a man was also seen by me." |
| `Line 1950: स पुनः कः | १६९ |` | "Who was he? |169|" |
| `Line 1951: अश्वश्चातिप्रमाणयुक्तः |` | "And the horse was of extraordinary size." |
| `Line 1952: स चापि कः | १७० |` | "And who was he? |170|" |
| `Line 1953: पथि गच्छता मया ऋषभो दृष्टः |` | "While traveling on the road, I saw a bull." |
| `Line 1954: तं च पुरुषोऽधिरूढः |` | "And a person was mounted on it." |
| `Line 1955: तेनास्मि सोपचारमुक्तः |` | "By him I was addressed with courtesy." |
| `Line 1956: उत्तङ्कास्य ऋषभस्य पुरीषं भक्षय |` | "Uttanka, eat the dung of this bull." |
| `Line 1957: उपाध्यायेनापि ते भक्षितमिति |` | "Your teacher has also eaten it, thus he said." |
| `Line 1958: ततस्तद्वचनान्मया तदृषभस्य पुरीषमुपयुक्तम् |` | "Then, following his words, I consumed the dung of that bull." |
| `Line 1959: तदिच्छामि भवतोपदिष्टं किं तदिति | १७१ |` | "I wish to know what was that which you instructed me about. |171|" |
| `Line 1960: तेनैवमुक्त उपाध्यायः प्रत्युवाच |` | "Thus addressed, the teacher replied:" |

| `Line 1963: यदपि तच्चक्रं द्वादशारं षट्कुमाराः परिवर्तयन्ति ते ऋतवः षट्संवत्सरश्चक्रम् |` | "That wheel with twelve spokes which six youths rotate is the wheel of six seasons and the year." |

| `Line 2098: निगदामि कथायुक्तं पुराणाश्रयसंयुतम् ॥६॥` | "I shall narrate to you, along with stories, supported by the Purāṇas [ancient texts]. ||6||" |

| `Line 2114: च्यवनत्वं परिख्यातं तन्ममाचक्ष्व पृच्छतः ||१०||` | "Came to be known as Cyavana, tell me that as I ask. ||10||" |

| `Line 2117: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2118: भृगोः सुदयिता भार्या पुलोमेत्यभिविश्रुता |` | "Bhṛgu's beloved wife was well-known as Pulomā," |
| `Line 2119: तस्यां गर्भः समभवद्भृगोर्वीर्यसमुद्भवः ||११||` | "In her a fetus was conceived, born of Bhṛgu's virility. ||11||" |
| `Line 2120: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2121: तस्मिन्गर्भे सम्भृतेऽथ पुलोमायां भृगूद्वह |` | "When that fetus was formed in Pulomā, O carrier of Bhṛgu's lineage," |
| `Line 2122: समये समशीलिन्यां धर्मपत्न्यां यशस्विनः ||१२||` | "At that time, in his virtuous and lawful wife of the illustrious one. ||12||" |
| `Line 2123: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2124: अभिषेकाय निष्क्रान्ते भृगौ धर्मभृतां वरे |` | "When Bhṛgu, the best among the upholders of dharma, went out for his ablutions," |
| `Line 2125: आश्रमं तस्य रक्षोऽथ पुलोमाभ्याजगाम ह ||१३||` | "A demon [rakṣas] then came to his hermitage, to Pulomā. ||13||" |
| `Line 2126: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2127: तं प्रविश्याश्रमं दृष्ट्वा भृगोर्भार्यामनिन्दिताम् |` | "Having entered that hermitage and seeing Bhṛgu's blameless wife," |

| `Line 2129: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 2131: न्यमन्त्रयत वन्येन फलमूलादिना तदा ||१५||` | "She welcomed him then with forest fruits, roots and other offerings. ||15||" |
| `Line 2132: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 2139: शंस मे कस्य भार्येयमग्ने पृष्ट ऋतेन वै |` | "Tell me truthfully, O Agni [fire god], when asked, whose wife is this?" |
| `Line 2140: सत्यस्त्वमसि सत्यं मे वद पावक पृच्छते ||१८||` | "You are truthful, so speak the truth to me who asks, O Pāvaka [fire god]. ||18||" |
| `Line 2141: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 2150: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 2153: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2155: साक्षिवत्पुण्यपापेषु सत्यं ब्रूहि कवे वचः ||२३||` | "Like a witness to virtuous and sinful deeds, speak the truth, O wise one. ||23||" |
| `Line 2156: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2158: सेयं यदि तथा मे त्वं सत्यमाख्यातुमर्हसि ||२४||` | "If she is the same, you should tell me the truth. ||24||" |
| `Line 2159: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2237: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2240: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2251: अग्निहोत्रेषु सत्रेषु क्रियास्वथ मखेषु च ||६||` | "In Agnihotra [fire sacrifices], in Satras [long rituals], in religious rites, and in sacrificial ceremonies. ||6||" |
| `Line 2252: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2253: वेदोक्तेन विधानेन मयि यद्धूयते हविः |` | "When oblations are offered into me according to the procedures prescribed in the Vedas," |
| `Line 2254: देवताः पितरश्चैव तेन तृप्ता भवन्ति वै ||७||` | "The deities and the ancestors indeed become satisfied by that. ||7||" |
| `Line 2255: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2256: आपो देवगणाः सर्वे आपः पितृगणास्तथा |` | "Water represents all the hosts of gods, and water represents the hosts of ancestors as well," |
| `Line 2257: दर्शश्च पौर्णमासश्च देवानां पितृभिः सह ||८||` | "The new moon (Darsha) and full moon (Paurnamasa) sacrifices are for gods along with the ancestors. ||8||" |
| `Line 2258: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2259: देवताः पितरस्तस्मात्पितरश्चापि देवताः |` | "Therefore, the deities are ancestors and the ancestors are also deities," |
| `Line 2260: एकीभूताश्च पूज्यन्ते पृथक्त्वेन च पर्वसु ||९||` | "They are worshipped as united and also separately during the sacred days [parvan]. ||9||" |
| `Line 2261: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2262: देवताः पितरश्चैव जुह्वते मयि यत्सदा |` | "Whatever is always offered to deities and ancestors through me," |
| `Line 2263: त्रिदशानां पितृणां च मुखमेवमहं स्मृतः ||१०||` | "Thus I am considered the mouth of the thirty gods [Tridasha] and the ancestors. ||10||" |
| `Line 2264: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2265: अमावास्यां च पितरः पौर्णमास्यां च देवताः |` | "On the new moon day, the ancestors, and on the full moon day, the deities," |
| `Line 2266: मन्मुखेनैव हूयन्ते भुञ्जते च हुतं हविः ||११||` | "Are invoked through my mouth alone, and they consume the offered oblations. ||11||" |
| `Line 2267: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2268: सर्वभक्षः कथं तेषां भविष्यामि मुखं त्वहम् ||११||` | "How shall I, becoming an eater of everything, remain their mouth? ||11||" |
| `Line 2269: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2270: चिन्तयित्वा ततो वह्निश्चक्रे संहारमात्मनः |` | "Having thought thus, Agni [fire deity] then withdrew himself," |
| `Line 2271: द्विजानामग्निहोत्रेषु यज्ञसत्रक्रियासु च ||१२||` | "From the Agnihotra of the twice-born [Brahmins] and from sacrificial ceremonies and rituals. ||12||" |
| `Line 2272: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2273: निरोङ्कारवषट्काराः स्वधास्वाहाविवर्जिताः |` | "Deprived of the sacred syllables Om and Vashat, and without the utterances of Svadha and Svaha [ritual exclamations]," |
| `Line 2274: विनाग्निना प्रजाः सर्वास्तत आसन्सुदुःखिताः ||१३||` | "Without fire, all creatures thereafter became extremely miserable. ||13||" |
| `Line 2275: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2276: अथर्षयः समुद्विग्ना देवान्गत्वाब्रुवन्वचः |` | "Then the sages, greatly distressed, went to the gods and spoke these words:" |
| `Line 2277: अग्निनाशात्क्रियाभ्रंशाद्भ्रान्ता लोकास्त्रयोऽनघाः ||१४||` | "Due to the disappearance of Agni [fire deity] and the cessation of rituals, the three worlds are confused, O sinless ones. ||14||" |
| `Line 2278: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2279: विधध्वमत्र यत्कार्यं न स्यात्कालात्ययो यथा ||१४||` | "Please arrange what needs to be done in this matter so that there is no delay beyond the proper time. ||14||" |
| `Line 2280: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2281: अथर्षयश्च देवाश्च ब्रह्माणमुपगम्य तु |` | "Then the sages and the gods, approaching Brahma [creator deity]," |
| `Line 2282: अग्नेरावेदयञ्शापं क्रियासंहारमेव च ||१५||` | "Informed him about the curse on Agni and the cessation of rituals. ||15||" |
| `Line 2283: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2284: भृगुणा वै महाभाग शप्तोऽग्निः कारणान्तरे |` | "O fortunate one, Agni was cursed by Bhrigu [sage] for a particular reason." |
| `Line 2285: कथं देवमुखो भूत्वा यज्ञभागाग्रभुक्तथा ||१६||` | "How can he, being the mouth of the gods and the primary consumer of sacrificial offerings, ||16||" |
| `Line 2286: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2287: हुतभुक्सर्वलोकेषु सर्वभक्षत्वमेष्यति ||१६||` | "The fire [Hutabhuk], who consumes offerings in all worlds, come to consume everything? ||16||" |
| `Line 2288: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2289: श्रुत्वा तु तद्वचस्तेषामग्निमाहूय लोककृत् |` | "Having heard their words, the creator of the world [Brahma] summoned Agni," |
| `Line 2290: उवाच वचनं श्लक्ष्णं भूतभावनमव्ययम् ||१७||` | "And spoke gentle words that were nurturing to beings and imperishable. ||17||" |
| `Line 2291: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2292: लोकानामिह सर्वेषां त्वं कर्ता चान्त एव च |` | "You are both the creator and the end of all these worlds," |
| `Line 2293: त्वं धारयसि लोकांस्त्रीन्क्रियाणां च प्रवर्तकः ||१८||` | "You sustain the three worlds and are the initiator of all rituals. ||18||" |
| `Line 2294: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2295: स तथा कुरु लोकेश नोच्छिद्येरन्क्रिया यथा ||१८||` | "Therefore, O lord of worlds, act in such a way that the rituals are not destroyed. ||18||" |
| `Line 2296: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2297: कस्मादेवं विमूढस्त्वमीश्वरः सन्हुताशनः |` | "Why are you so confused, being the lord, O consumer of offerings [Agni]?" |
| `Line 2298: त्वं पवित्रं यदा लोके सर्वभूतगतश्च ह ||१९||` | "When you are the purifier in the world and present in all beings, ||19||" |
| `Line 2299: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2300: न त्वं सर्वशरीरेण सर्वभक्षत्वमेष्यसि |` | "You shall not consume everything with your entire body." |
| `Line 2301: उपादानेऽर्चिषो यास्ते सर्वं धक्ष्यन्ति ताः शिखिन् ||२०||` | "When kindled, your flames will burn everything, O Fire [Agni]. ||20||" |
| `Line 2302: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2303: यथा सूर्यांशुभिः स्पृष्टं सर्वं शुचि विभाव्यते |` | "Just as everything touched by the sun's rays is perceived as pure," |
| `Line 2304: तथा त्वदर्चिर्निर्दग्धं सर्वं शुचि भविष्यति ||२१||` | "Similarly, everything burnt by your flames will become pure. ||21||" |
| `Line 2305: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2306: तदग्ने त्वं महत्तेजः स्वप्रभावाद्विनिर्गतम् |` | "Therefore, O Agni, with your great splendor emanating from your own power," |
| `Line 2307: स्वतेजसैव तं शापं कुरु सत्यमृषेर्विभो ||२२||` | "Make the sage's curse come true with your own radiance, O mighty one. ||22||" |
| `Line 2308: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2309: देवानां चात्मनो भागं गृहाण त्वं मुखे हुतम् ||२२||` | "And receive in your mouth the portion offered to the gods and yourself. ||22||" |
| `Line 2310: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2311: एवमस्त्विति तं वह्निः प्रत्युवाच पितामहम् |` | "So be it," the fire [Agni] replied to the Grandfather [Brahma]," |
| `Line 2312: जगाम शासनं कर्तुं देवस्य परमेष्ठिनः ||२३||` | "And went to execute the command of the supreme deity [Brahma]. ||23||" |
| `Line 2313: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2315: ऋषयश्च यथापूर्वं क्रियाः सर्वाः प्रचक्रिरे ||२४||` | "And the sages resumed all their rituals as before. ||24||" |
| `Line 2316: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2318: अग्निश्च परमां प्रीतिमवाप हतकल्मषः ||२५||` | "And Agni, freed from sin, attained supreme satisfaction. ||25||" |
| `Line 2319: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2320: एवमेष पुरावृत्त इतिहासोऽग्निशापजः |` | "Thus is this ancient tale about the curse of Agni," |
| `Line 2321: पुलोमस्य विनाशश्च च्यवनस्य च सम्भवः ||२६||` | "The destruction of Puloma and the birth of Chyavana. ||26||" |

| `Line 2331: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2332: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2333: स चापि च्यवनो ब्रह्मन्भार्गवोऽजनयत्सुतम् |` | "And that Cyavana, O Brahmin, a descendant of Bhṛgu [sage lineage], begot a son" |
| `Line 2334: सुकन्यायां महात्मानं प्रमतिं दीप्ततेजसम् ||१||` | "Through Sukanyā, a noble soul named Pramati, of brilliant splendor. ||1||" |
| `Line 2335: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2337: रुरुः प्रमद्वरायां तु शुनकं समजीजनत् ||२||` | "And Ruru, in turn, begot Śunaka through Pramadvarā. ||2||" |
| `Line 2338: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2339: तस्य ब्रह्मन्रुरोः सर्वं चरितं भूरितेजसः |` | "O Brahmin, the entire story of that Ruru of immense splendor," |
| `Line 2340: विस्तरेण प्रवक्ष्यामि तच्छृणु त्वमशेषतः ||३||` | "I shall narrate in detail; listen to it completely. ||3||" |
| `Line 2341: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2342: ऋषिरासीन्महान्पूर्वं तपोविद्यासमन्वितः |` | "There was once a great sage endowed with austerity and knowledge," |
| `Line 2343: स्थूलकेश इति ख्यातः सर्वभूतहिते रतः ||४||` | "Known as Sthūlakeśa [thick-haired sage], devoted to the welfare of all beings. ||4||" |
| `Line 2344: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2349: उत्ससर्ज यथाकालं स्थूलकेशाश्रमं प्रति ||६||` | "Abandoned that child in due time near the hermitage of Sthūlakeśa. ||6||" |
| `Line 2350: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2351: उत्सृज्य चैव तं गर्भं नद्यास्तीरे जगाम ह |` | "And having abandoned that embryo, she went to the bank of a river," |
| `Line 2352: कन्याममरगर्भाभां ज्वलन्तीमिव च श्रिया ||७||` | "A maiden resembling the child of immortals [celestial beings], radiant as if blazing with splendor. ||7||" |
| `Line 2353: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2355: स्थूलकेशः स तेजस्वी विजने बन्धुवर्जिताम् ||८||` | "Sthūlakeśa [thick-haired sage], that radiant one, (saw her) alone, without relatives, in a deserted place. ||8||" |
| `Line 2356: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2358: जग्राहाथ मुनिश्रेष्ठः कृपाविष्टः पुपोष च ||९||` | "The best of sages took her, filled with compassion, and nurtured her. ||9||" |
| `Line 2359: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2360: ववृधे सा वरारोहा तस्याश्रमपदे शुभा ||९||` | "That beautiful one with excellent hips grew up in his hermitage, auspicious. ||9||" |
| `Line 2361: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2362: प्रमदाभ्यो वरा सा तु सर्वरूपगुणान्विता |` | "She was the best among women, endowed with all forms of beauty and virtues," |
| `Line 2363: ततः प्रमद्वरेत्यस्या नाम चक्रे महानृषिः ||१०||` | "Therefore, the great sage named her Pramadvarā [best of delightful women]. ||10||" |
| `Line 2364: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2366: बभूव किल धर्मात्मा मदनानुगतात्मवान् ||११||` | "That righteous-souled one indeed became possessed by love [Madana's influence]. ||11||" |

| `Line 2376: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2378: पदा चैनं समाक्रामन्मुमूर्षुः कालचोदिता ||१५||` | "And stepped on it with her foot, about to die, impelled by fate [kāla-coditā]. ||15||" |
| `Line 2379: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2381: विषोपलिप्तान्दशनान्भृशमङ्गे न्यपातयत् ||१६||` | "Plunged its venom-coated fangs deeply into her body. ||16||" |

| `Line 2387: भूयो मनोहरतरा बभूव तनुमध्यमा ||१८||` | "The slender-waisted one appeared even more enchanting than before. ||18||" |

| `Line 2409: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2410: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2411: तेषु तत्रोपविष्टेषु ब्राह्मणेषु समन्ततः |` | "When those Brahmins were seated all around there," |
| `Line 2412: रुरुश्चुक्रोश गहनं वनं गत्वा सुदुःखितः ||१||` | "Ruru, deeply distressed, went to the dense forest and wailed. ||1||" |
| `Line 2413: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2414: शोकेनाभिहतः सोऽथ विलपन्करुणं बहु |` | "Struck by grief, he then lamented piteously many times," |
| `Line 2415: अब्रवीद्वचनं शोचन्प्रियां चिन्त्य प्रमद्वराम् ||२||` | "And spoke these words, grieving, thinking of his beloved Pramadvarā. ||2||" |
| `Line 2416: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2417: शेते सा भुवि तन्वङ्गी मम शोकविवर्धिनी |` | "She lies on the ground, that slender-limbed one, increasing my sorrow," |
| `Line 2418: बान्धवानां च सर्वेषां किं नु दुःखमतः परम् ||३||` | "What sorrow could be greater than this for all her relatives? ||3||" |
| `Line 2419: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2420: यदि दत्तं तपस्तप्तं गुरवो वा मया यदि |` | "If I have given charity, performed austerities, or if I have properly," |
| `Line 2421: सम्यगाराधितास्तेन सञ्जीवतु मम प्रिया ||४||` | "Worshipped my teachers, by that merit, may my beloved come back to life. ||4||" |
| `Line 2422: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2423: यथा जन्मप्रभृति वै यतात्माहं धृतव्रतः |` | "As I have been self-controlled and steadfast in my vows since birth," |
| `Line 2424: प्रमद्वरा तथाद्यैव समुत्तिष्ठतु भामिनी ||५||` | "So may Pramadvarā, that radiant lady, rise up this very day. ||5||" |
| `Line 2425: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2426: देवदूत उवाच||` | "The celestial messenger [Devadūta] said:" |
| `Line 2427: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2428: अभिधत्से ह यद्वाचा रुरो दुःखेन तन्मृषा |` | "O Ruru, what you speak with sorrow is false," |
| `Line 2429: न तु मर्त्यस्य धर्मात्मन्नायुरस्ति गतायुषः ||६||` | "O righteous one, a mortal whose lifespan has expired cannot have life again. ||6||" |
| `Line 2430: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2431: गतायुरेषा कृपणा गन्धर्वाप्सरसोः सुता |` | "This poor girl, daughter of a Gandharva [celestial musician] and an Apsara [celestial nymph], has exhausted her lifespan," |
| `Line 2432: तस्माच्छोके मनस्तात मा कृथास्त्वं कथञ्चन ||७||` | "Therefore, dear one, do not grieve in your mind in any way. ||7||" |
| `Line 2433: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2434: उपायश्चात्र विहितः पूर्वं देवैर्महात्मभिः |` | "A remedy for this has been ordained earlier by the great-souled gods," |
| `Line 2435: तं यदीच्छसि कर्तुं त्वं प्राप्स्यसीमां प्रमद्वराम् ||८||` | "If you wish to perform it, you will obtain this Pramadvara [beautiful maiden]. ||8||" |
| `Line 2436: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2437: रुरुरुवाच||` | "Ruru said:" |
| `Line 2438: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2439: क उपायः कृतो देवैर्ब्रूहि तत्त्वेन खेचर |` | "What remedy has been created by the gods? Tell me truthfully, O sky-traveler [celestial being]," |
| `Line 2440: करिष्ये तं तथा श्रुत्वा त्रातुमर्हति मां भवान् ||९||` | "Having heard it, I will perform it accordingly. You should save me. ||9||" |
| `Line 2441: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2442: देवदूत उवाच||` | "The celestial messenger said:" |
| `Line 2443: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2444: आयुषोऽर्धं प्रयच्छस्व कन्यायै भृगुनन्दन |` | "Give half of your lifespan to the maiden, O descendant of Bhrigu [sage lineage]," |
| `Line 2445: एवमुत्थास्यति रुरो तव भार्या प्रमद्वरा ||१०||` | "Thus, O Ruru, your wife Pramadvara will rise again. ||10||" |
| `Line 2446: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2447: रुरुरुवाच||` | "Ruru said:" |
| `Line 2448: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2449: आयुषोऽर्धं प्रयच्छामि कन्यायै खेचरोत्तम |` | "I give half of my lifespan to the maiden, O best of sky-travelers," |
| `Line 2450: शृङ्गाररूपाभरणा उत्तिष्ठतु मम प्रिया ||११||` | "Let my beloved rise again, adorned with beautiful ornaments. ||11||" |
| `Line 2451: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2452: सूत उवाच॥` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2453: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2454: ततो गन्धर्वराजश्च देवदूतश्च सत्तमौ |` | "Then the king of Gandharvas [celestial musicians] and the divine messenger, both excellent beings," |
| `Line 2455: धर्मराजमुपेत्येदं वचनं प्रत्यभाषताम् ॥१२॥` | "Approached Dharmarāja [Yama, death-god] and spoke these words. ||12||" |
| `Line 2456: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2457: धर्मराजायुषोऽर्धेन रुरोर्भार्या प्रमद्वरा |` | "By half the lifespan of Ruru, may Pramadvarā, Ruru's wife," |
| `Line 2458: समुत्तिष्ठतु कल्याणी मृतैव यदि मन्यसे ॥१३॥` | "Rise up again, the auspicious one, if you consider it proper even though she is dead. ||13||" |
| `Line 2459: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2460: धर्मराज उवाच॥` | "Dharmarāja [Yama, death-god] said:" |
| `Line 2461: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2462: प्रमद्वरा रुरोर्भार्या देवदूत यदीच्छसि |` | "If you wish, O divine messenger, that Pramadvarā, Ruru's wife," |
| `Line 2463: उत्तिष्ठत्वायुषोऽर्धेन रुरोरेव समन्विता ॥१४॥` | "May rise again, endowed with half the lifespan of Ruru himself. ||14||" |
| `Line 2464: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2465: सूत उवाच॥` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2466: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2467: एवमुक्ते ततः कन्या सोदतिष्ठत्प्रमद्वरा |` | "When this was said, then the maiden Pramadvarā rose up," |
| `Line 2468: रुरोस्तस्यायुषोऽर्धेन सुप्तेव वरवर्णिनी ॥१५॥` | "With half of Ruru's lifespan, as if from sleep, that fair-complexioned one. ||15||" |
| `Line 2469: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2470: एतद्दृष्टं भविष्ये हि रुरोरुत्तमतेजसः |` | "This was foreseen in the future indeed, that of Ruru of excellent splendor," |
| `Line 2471: आयुषोऽतिप्रवृद्धस्य भार्यार्थेऽर्धं ह्रसत्विति ॥१६॥` | "Half of his greatly increased lifespan would be diminished for the sake of his wife. ||16||" |
| `Line 2472: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2473: तत इष्टेऽहनि तयोः पितरौ चक्रतुर्मुदा |` | "Then, on an auspicious day, their parents joyfully performed," |
| `Line 2474: विवाहं तौ च रेमाते परस्परहितैषिणौ ॥१७॥` | "Their marriage, and the two enjoyed themselves, seeking each other's welfare. ||17||" |
| `Line 2475: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2476: स लब्ध्वा दुर्लभां भार्यां पद्मकिञ्जल्कसप्रभाम् |` | "Having obtained a rare wife, radiant like the pollen of a lotus," |
| `Line 2477: व्रतं चक्रे विनाशाय जिह्मगानां धृतव्रतः ||१८||` | "He, firm in his vows, made a vow to destroy the jihmaga [serpents/crooked-goers]. ||18||" |
| `Line 2478: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2479: स दृष्ट्वा जिह्मगान्सर्वांस्तीव्रकोपसमन्वितः |` | "Seeing any serpents, filled with intense anger," |
| `Line 2480: अभिहन्ति यथासन्नं गृह्य प्रहरणं सदा ||१९||` | "He would always strike them as they approached, having seized a weapon. ||19||" |
| `Line 2481: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2482: स कदाचिद्वनं विप्रो रुरुरभ्यागमन्महत् |` | "Once that Brahmin, Ruru, entered a great forest," |
| `Line 2483: शयानं तत्र चापश्यड्डुण्डुभं वयसान्वितम् ||२०||` | "And there he saw a Dundubha [snake species] lying, surrounded by crows. ||20||" |
| `Line 2484: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2485: तत उद्यम्य दण्डं स कालदण्डोपमं तदा |` | "Then, raising a staff resembling the rod of Kala [death god]," |
| `Line 2486: अभ्यघ्नद्रुषितो विप्रस्तमुवाचाथ डुण्डुभः ||२१||` | "The enraged Brahmin struck at it, whereupon the Dundubha spoke to him. ||21||" |
| `Line 2487: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2488: नापराध्यामि ते किञ्चिदहमद्य तपोधन |` | "I have not committed any offense against you today, O wealth of austerities [ascetic]," |
| `Line 2489: संरम्भात्तत्किमर्थं मामभिहंसि रुषान्वितः ||२२||` | "Why then do you strike me in anger, with such agitation? ||22||" |

| `Line 2500: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2501: मम प्राणसमा भार्या दष्टासीद्भुजगेन ह |` | "My wife, who was dear to me as life itself, was bitten by a serpent." |
| `Line 2502: तत्र मे समयो घोर आत्मनोरग वै कृतः ||१||` | "Therefore, I made a terrible vow to myself, O serpent, indeed. ||1||" |
| `Line 2503: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2504: हन्यां सदैव भुजगं यं यं पश्येयमित्युत |` | "That I would always kill any serpent that I might see." |
| `Line 2505: ततोऽहं त्वां जिघांसामि जीवितेन विमोक्ष्यसे ||२||` | "Therefore, I wish to kill you; you shall be released from life. ||2||" |
| `Line 2506: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2507: डुण्डुभ उवाच||` | "Dundubha said:" |
| `Line 2508: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2509: अन्ये ते भुजगा विप्र ये दशन्तीह मानवान् |` | "Different are those serpents, O Brahmin [twice-born], who bite humans here." |
| `Line 2510: डुण्डुभानहिगन्धेन न त्वं हिंसितुमर्हसि ||३||` | "By the mere scent of Dundubha snakes, you should not seek to harm me. ||3||" |
| `Line 2511: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2512: एकानर्थान्पृथगर्थानेकदुःखान्पृथक्सुखान् |` | "Some have one purpose, others have different purposes; some have one sorrow, others have different joys." |
| `Line 2513: डुण्डुभान्धर्मविद्भूत्वा न त्वं हिंसितुमर्हसि ||४||` | "Being knowledgeable in dharma [righteousness], you should not kill Dundubhas. ||4||" |
| `Line 2514: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2515: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2516: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2517: इति श्रुत्वा वचस्तस्य भुजगस्य रुरुस्तदा |` | "Having heard these words of that serpent, Ruru then," |
| `Line 2518: नावधीद्भयसंविग्न ऋषिं मत्वाथ डुण्डुभम् ||५||` | "Did not kill him, being struck with awe, thinking the Dundubha to be a sage. ||5||" |
| `Line 2519: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2520: उवाच चैनं भगवान्रुरुः संशमयन्निव |` | "And the venerable Ruru spoke to him, as if calming him," |
| `Line 2521: कामया भुजग ब्रूहि कोऽसीमां विक्रियां गतः ||६||` | "Please tell me, O serpent, who are you that has undergone this transformation? ||6||" |
| `Line 2522: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2524: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2525: अहं पुरा रुरो नाम्ना ऋषिरासं सहस्रपात् |` | "I was formerly a sage named Ruru, the thousand-footed [powerful sage]." |
| `Line 2526: सोऽहं शापेन विप्रस्य भुजगत्वमुपागतः ||७||` | "I have attained the state of a serpent due to the curse of a Vipra [Brahmin sage]. ||7||" |
| `Line 2527: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2529: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2531: कियन्तं चैव कालं ते वपुरेतद्भविष्यति ||८||` | "And for how long will you have this body? ||8||" |

| `Line 2544: भृशं संशितवाक्तात तपोबलसमन्वितः ||१||` | "Who was extremely sharp in speech, O dear one, endowed with the power of austerities. ||1||" |
| `Line 2545: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2546: स मया क्रीडता बाल्ये कृत्वा तार्णमथोरगम् |` | "In my childhood, while playing, I made a snake of grass," |
| `Line 2547: अग्निहोत्रे प्रसक्तः सन्भीषितः प्रमुमोह वै ||२||` | "And frightened him while he was engaged in his Agnihotra [fire ritual], causing him to faint. ||2||" |
| `Line 2548: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2549: लब्ध्वा च स पुनः सञ्ज्ञां मामुवाच तपोधनः |` | "And having regained consciousness, that Tapodhanah [ascetic] said to me," |
| `Line 2550: निर्दहन्निव कोपेन सत्यवाक्संशितव्रतः ||३||` | "As if burning with anger, that truthful speaker of firm vows: ||3||" |
| `Line 2551: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2552: यथावीर्यस्त्वया सर्पः कृतोऽयं मद्बिभीषया |` | "As you have made this serpent powerless out of fear of me," |
| `Line 2553: तथावीर्यो भुजङ्गस्त्वं मम कोपाद्भविष्यसि ||४||` | "So shall you, a serpent [snake-being], become powerless due to my anger. ||4||" |
| `Line 2554: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2555: तस्याहं तपसो वीर्यं जानमानस्तपोधन |` | "Knowing the power of his austerities, O wealth of austerities [ascetic one]," |
| `Line 2556: भृशमुद्विग्नहृदयस्तमवोचं वनौकसम् ||५||` | "With a greatly agitated heart, I spoke to that forest-dweller [hermit]. ||5||" |
| `Line 2557: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2558: प्रयतः सम्भ्रमाच्चैव प्राञ्जलिः प्रणतः स्थितः |` | "Earnestly, and with agitation, I stood with folded hands and bowed," |
| `Line 2559: सखेति हसतेदं ते नर्मार्थं वै कृतं मया ||६||` | "Saying 'Friend,' I said to him laughing, 'This was done by me merely in jest.' ||6||" |
| `Line 2560: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2561: क्षन्तुमर्हसि मे ब्रह्मञ्शापोऽयं विनिवर्त्यताम् |` | "'You should forgive me, O Brahmin [learned one], let this curse be withdrawn,'" |
| `Line 2562: सोऽथ मामब्रवीद्दृष्ट्वा भृशमुद्विग्नचेतसम् ||७||` | "Then he, seeing me with a greatly troubled mind, said to me: ||7||" |
| `Line 2563: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2564: मुहुरुष्णं विनिःश्वस्य सुसम्भ्रान्तस्तपोधनः |` | "Sighing hot breaths repeatedly, the greatly agitated ascetic [wealth of austerities]," |
| `Line 2565: नानृतं वै मया प्रोक्तं भवितेदं कथञ्चन ||८||` | "'What has been spoken by me cannot become untrue in any way. ||8||'" |
| `Line 2566: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2567: यत्तु वक्ष्यामि ते वाक्यं शृणु तन्मे धृतव्रत |` | "'But listen to these words that I will speak to you, O steadfast in vows," |
| `Line 2568: श्रुत्वा च हृदि ते वाक्यमिदमस्तु तपोधन ||९||` | "'Having heard, let these words be in your heart, O wealth of austerities [ascetic one]. ||9||'" |
| `Line 2569: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2570: उत्पत्स्यति रुरुर्नाम प्रमतेरात्मजः शुचिः |` | "'There will be born one named Ruru, the pure son of Pramati," |
| `Line 2571: तं दृष्ट्वा शापमोक्षस्ते भविता नचिरादिव ||१०||` | "'Upon seeing him, your release from the curse will happen without much delay. ||10||'" |
| `Line 2572: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2573: स त्वं रुरुरिति ख्यातः प्रमतेरात्मजः शुचिः |` | "'You are that Ruru, renowned thus, the pure son of Pramati," |
| `Line 2574: स्वरूपं प्रतिलभ्याहमद्य वक्ष्यामि ते हितम् ||११||` | "'Having regained my original form, I shall now tell you what is beneficial for you. ||11||'" |
| `Line 2575: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2576: अहिंसा परमो धर्मः सर्वप्राणभृतां स्मृतः |` | "Non-violence is remembered as the highest dharma [righteous duty] for all living beings." |
| `Line 2577: तस्मात्प्राणभृतः सर्वान्न हिंस्याद्ब्राह्मणः क्वचित् ||१२||` | "Therefore, a Brahmin should never harm any living being whatsoever. ||12||" |
| `Line 2578: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2579: ब्राह्मणः सौम्य एवेह जायतेति परा श्रुतिः |` | "A Brahmin is born in this world to be gentle - thus declares the highest scripture [Vedas]." |
| `Line 2580: वेदवेदाङ्गवित्तात सर्वभूताभयप्रदः ||१३||` | "O dear one, knower of Vedas and Vedāṅgas [auxiliary texts], he is the bestower of fearlessness to all beings. ||13||" |
| `Line 2581: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2582: अहिंसा सत्यवचनं क्षमा चेति विनिश्चितम् |` | "Non-violence, truthfulness, and forgiveness - this is firmly established" |
| `Line 2583: ब्राह्मणस्य परो धर्मो वेदानां धरणादपि ||१४||` | "As the highest dharma of a Brahmin, even more than the preservation of the Vedas. ||14||" |
| `Line 2584: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2586: दण्डधारणमुग्रत्वं प्रजानां परिपालनम् ||१५||` | "Wielding punishment, showing fierceness, and protecting the subjects. ||15||" |
| `Line 2587: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2589: जनमेजयस्य धर्मात्मन्सर्पाणां हिंसनं पुरा ||१६||` | "O righteous one, about Janamejaya's killing of serpents in the past. ||16||" |

| `Line 2592: तपोवीर्यबलोपेताद्वेदवेदाङ्गपारगात् ||१७||` | "Who was endowed with the power of austerities and strength, a master of the Vedas and Vedāṅgas. ||17||" |

| `Line 2635: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2636: किमर्थं राजशार्दूलः स राजा जनमेजयः |` | "For what purpose did that tiger among kings [great ruler], King Janamejaya," |
| `Line 2637: सर्पसत्रेण सर्पाणां गतोऽन्तं तद्वदस्व मे ||१||` | "Seek to destroy the serpents through the snake sacrifice? Tell me that. ||1||" |
| `Line 2638: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2639: आस्तीकश्च द्विजश्रेष्ठः किमर्थं जपतां वरः |` | "And for what purpose did Āstīka, the foremost of twice-born [Brahmin], best among chanters," |

| `Line 2653: आस्तीकस्य पुराणस्य ब्राह्मणस्य यशस्विनः ||५||` | "Of the ancient, illustrious brahmin Āstīka [snake ritual sage]. ||5||" |
| `Line 2654: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 2656: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2657: इतिहासमिमं वृद्धाः पुराणं परिचक्षते |` | "The elders describe this history as an ancient tale [purāṇa]," |
| `Line 2658: कृष्णद्वैपायनप्रोक्तं नैमिषारण्यवासिनः ||६||` | "Narrated by Kṛṣṇa Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa], O dwellers of Naimiṣāraṇya [sacred forest]. ||6||" |
| `Line 2659: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 2662: ` | "[Blank line]" |
