| `Line 2665: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2666: आस्तीकस्य पिता ह्यासीत्प्रजापतिसमः प्रभुः |` | "Āstīka's father was a lord equal to Prajāpati [creator deity]," |
| `Line 2667: ब्रह्मचारी यताहारस्तपस्युग्रे रतः सदा ||९||` | "A celibate with controlled diet, always engaged in severe austerities. ||9||" |
| `Line 2668: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2669: जरत्कारुरिति ख्यात ऊर्ध्वरेता महानृषिः |` | "Known as Jaratkāru, the great sage who preserved his vital fluid [celibate]," |
| `Line 2670: यायावराणां धर्मज्ञः प्रवरः संशितव्रतः ||१०||` | "Foremost among the wandering ascetics [yāyāvaras], knower of dharma, of firm vows. ||10||" |
| `Line 2671: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2672: अटमानः कदाचित्स स्वान्ददर्श पितामहान् |` | "Once while wandering, he saw his own forefathers," |
| `Line 2673: लम्बमानान्महागर्ते पादैरूर्ध्वैरधोमुखान् ||११||` | "Hanging in a great pit, with feet upward and faces downward. ||11||" |
| `Line 2674: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 2675: तानब्रवीत्स दृष्ट्वैव जरत्कारुः पितामहान् |` | "Upon seeing them, Jaratkāru addressed those forefathers," |
| `Line 2676: के भवन्तोऽवलम्बन्ते गर्तेऽस्मिन्वा अधोमुखाः ||१२||` | "Who are you hanging in this pit with your faces downward? ||12||" |
| `Line 2677: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2678: वीरणस्तम्बके लग्नाः सर्वतः परिभक्षिते |` | "Clinging to a reed grass [vīraṇa plant] stalk that is being gnawed all around," |
| `Line 2679: मूषकेन निगूढेन गर्तेऽस्मिन्नित्यवासिना ||१३||` | "By a hidden mouse that permanently dwells in this pit. ||13||" |
| `Line 2680: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2681: पितर ऊचुः||` | "The ancestors [pitṛs] said:" |
| `Line 2682: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2683: यायावरा नाम वयमृषयः संशितव्रताः |` | "We are ascetics known as Yāyāvaras [wandering sages], of strict vows," |
| `Line 2684: सन्तानप्रक्षयाद्ब्रह्मन्नधो गच्छाम मेदिनीम् ||१४||` | "Due to the extinction of our lineage, O Brahmin, we are descending to the earth. ||14||" |
| `Line 2685: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2686: अस्माकं सन्ततिस्त्वेको जरत्कारुरिति श्रुतः |` | "Our sole descendant is known as Jaratkāru," |
| `Line 2687: मन्दभाग्योऽल्पभाग्यानां तप एव समास्थितः ||१५||` | "Unfortunate one of the unfortunate, he is devoted only to austerities. ||15||" |
| `Line 2688: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2689: न स पुत्राञ्जनयितुं दारान्मूढश्चिकीर्षति |` | "That foolish one does not wish to take a wife to produce sons," |
| `Line 2690: तेन लम्बामहे गर्ते सन्तानप्रक्षयादिह ||१६||` | "Therefore we hang in this pit due to the extinction of our lineage. ||16||" |
| `Line 2691: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2692: अनाथास्तेन नाथेन यथा दुष्कृतिनस्तथा |` | "We are like orphans with that protector, just like evil-doers," |
| `Line 2693: कस्त्वं बन्धुरिवास्माकमनुशोचसि सत्तम ||१७||` | "Who are you who grieves for us like a relative, O excellent one? ||17||" |
| `Line 2694: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2696: किमर्थं चैव नः शोच्याननुकम्पितुमर्हसि ||१८||` | "And for what reason do you show compassion to us who are pitiable? ||18||" |
| `Line 2697: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2698: जरत्कारुरुवाच||` | "Jaratkāru said:" |
| `Line 2699: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2701: ब्रूत किं करवाण्यद्य जरत्कारुरहं स्वयम् ||१९||` | "Tell me what I should do today, I am Jaratkāru myself. ||19||" |
| `Line 2702: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2703: पितर ऊचुः||` | "The ancestors said:" |
| `Line 2704: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2705: यतस्व यत्नवांस्तात सन्तानाय कुलस्य नः |` | "Strive diligently, dear son, for the continuation of our lineage," |
| `Line 2706: आत्मनोऽर्थेऽस्मदर्थे च धर्म इत्येव चाभिभो ||२०||` | "For your own sake and for our sake, this is indeed dharma [righteous duty], O illustrious one. ||20||" |
| `Line 2707: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2708: न हि धर्मफलैस्तात न तपोभिः सुसञ्चितैः |` | "Not by the fruits of dharma, dear son, nor by well-accumulated austerities," |

| `Line 2710: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2711: तद्दारग्रहणे यत्नं सन्तत्यां च मनः कुरु |` | "Therefore, make effort to take a wife and set your mind on progeny," |
| `Line 2712: पुत्रकास्मन्नियोगात्त्वमेतन्नः परमं हितम् ||२२||` | "Son, by our command, this is our highest welfare. ||22||" |
| `Line 2713: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2714: जरत्कारुरुवाच||` | "Jaratkāru said:" |

| `Line 2716: न दारान्वै करिष्यामि सदा मे भावितं मनः |` | "I shall not take a wife, for my mind has always been thus resolved," |
| `Line 2717: भवतां तु हितार्थाय करिष्ये दारसङ्ग्रहम् ||२३||` | "But for your welfare, I shall take a wife. ||23||" |
| `Line 2718: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2719: समयेन च कर्ताहमनेन विधिपूर्वकम् |` | "I shall do so with this condition, according to proper procedure," |
| `Line 2720: तथा यद्युपलप्स्यामि करिष्ये नान्यथा त्वहम् ||२४||` | "Only if I find such a one shall I do it, not otherwise. ||24||" |
| `Line 2721: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2722: सनाम्नी या भवित्री मे दित्सिता चैव बन्धुभिः |` | "She who will be of the same name as mine and is offered by her relatives," |
| `Line 2723: भैक्षवत्तामहं कन्यामुपयंस्ये विधानतः ||२५||` | "Such a maiden, given like alms, I shall marry according to the rules. ||25||" |
| `Line 2724: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2725: दरिद्राय हि मे भार्यां को दास्यति विशेषतः |` | "For who would give a wife to a poor man like me, especially?" |
| `Line 2726: प्रतिग्रहीष्ये भिक्षां तु यदि कश्चित्प्रदास्यति ||२६||` | "I will accept alms only if someone offers them. ||26||" |
| `Line 2727: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2728: एवं दारक्रियाहेतोः प्रयतिष्ये पितामहाः |` | "Thus, for the sake of marriage, I will strive, O forefathers [ancestors]," |
| `Line 2729: अनेन विधिना शश्वन्न करिष्येऽहमन्यथा ||२७||` | "In this manner always, I will not act otherwise. ||27||" |
| `Line 2730: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2731: तत्र चोत्पत्स्यते जन्तुर्भवतां तारणाय वै |` | "And there a being will be born for your deliverance indeed," |
| `Line 2732: शाश्वतं स्थानमासाद्य मोदन्तां पितरो मम ||२८||` | "Having attained the eternal abode, may my ancestors [forefathers] rejoice. ||28||" |
| `Line 2733: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2734: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2735: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2736: ततो निवेशाय तदा स विप्रः संशितव्रतः |` | "Then, for settlement, that Brahmin of firm vows," |
| `Line 2737: महीं चचार दारार्थी न च दारानविन्दत ||२९||` | "Wandered the earth seeking a wife, but did not find a wife. ||29||" |
| `Line 2738: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2739: स कदाचिद्वनं गत्वा विप्रः पितृवचः स्मरन् |` | "Once, having gone to the forest, that Brahmin, remembering his ancestors' words," |
| `Line 2740: चुक्रोश कन्याभिक्षार्थी तिस्रो वाचः शनैरिव ||३०||` | "Called out, seeking a maiden as alms, uttering three words slowly. ||30||" |
| `Line 2741: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2742: तं वासुकिः प्रत्यगृह्णादुद्यम्य भगिनीं तदा |` | "Then Vāsuki [serpent king] approached him, bringing forward his sister," |
| `Line 2743: न स तां प्रतिजग्राह न सनाम्नीति चिन्तयन् ||३१||` | "But he did not accept her, thinking she was not of the same name. ||31||" |
| `Line 2744: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2745: सनाम्नीमुद्यतां भार्यां गृह्णीयामिति तस्य हि |` | "That he would accept a wife offered who had the same name as his," |
| `Line 2746: मनो निविष्टमभवज्जरत्कारोर्महात्मनः ||३२||` | "Was firmly fixed in the mind of the great-souled Jaratkāru [sage]. ||32||" |
| `Line 2747: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2748: तमुवाच महाप्राज्ञो जरत्कारुर्महातपाः |` | "The highly wise Jaratkāru of great austerities said to him," |
| `Line 2749: किंनाम्नी भगिनीयं ते ब्रूहि सत्यं भुजङ्गम ||३३||` | "What is the name of this sister of yours? Speak the truth, O serpent [nāga]. ||33||" |
| `Line 2750: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2751: वासुकिरुवाच||` | "Vāsuki [serpent king] said:" |
| `Line 2752: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2753: जरत्कारो जरत्कारुः स्वसेयमनुजा मम |` | "O Jaratkāru, this Jaratkāru is my younger sister," |
| `Line 2754: त्वदर्थं रक्षिता पूर्वं प्रतीच्छेमां द्विजोत्तम ||३४||` | "She has been preserved earlier for you; accept her, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin]. ||34||" |
| `Line 2755: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2756: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2757: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2758: मात्रा हि भुजगाः शप्ताः पूर्वं ब्रह्मविदां वर |` | "The serpents were previously cursed by their mother, O best of the knowers of Brahman [sages]," |
| `Line 2759: जनमेजयस्य वो यज्ञे धक्ष्यत्यनिलसारथिः ||३५||` | "In Janamejaya's sacrifice, the fire [lit: wind-charioteer] will burn you all. ||35||" |
| `Line 2760: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2761: तस्य शापस्य शान्त्यर्थं प्रददौ पन्नगोत्तमः |` | "For the pacification of that curse, the best of serpents [Vāsuki] gave" |
| `Line 2762: स्वसारमृषये तस्मै सुव्रताय तपस्विने ||३६||` | "His sister to that sage, who was of good vows and austere. ||36||" |
| `Line 2763: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2765: आस्तीको नाम पुत्रश्च तस्यां जज्ञे महात्मनः ||३७||` | "And a son named Āstīka was born to that great soul through her. ||37||" |
| `Line 2766: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2767: तपस्वी च महात्मा च वेदवेदाङ्गपारगः |` | "He was austere and noble-souled, master of the Vedas and Vedāṅgas [auxiliary texts]," |
| `Line 2768: समः सर्वस्य लोकस्य पितृमातृभयापहः ||३८||` | "Equal toward all beings, and remover of the fear of his fathers and mothers. ||38||" |
| `Line 2769: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2770: अथ कालस्य महतः पाण्डवेयो नराधिपः |` | "Then after a long time, the Pāṇḍava king [Janamejaya]," |
| `Line 2771: आजहार महायज्ञं सर्पसत्रमिति श्रुतिः ||३९||` | "Performed a great sacrifice known as the Serpent Sacrifice, as tradition tells. ||39||" |
| `Line 2772: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2773: तस्मिन्प्रवृत्ते सत्रे तु सर्पाणामन्तकाय वै |` | "When that sacrifice, meant for the destruction of serpents, was in progress," |
| `Line 2774: मोचयामास तं शापमास्तीकः सुमहायशाः ||४०||` | "Āstīka, of great fame, liberated them from that curse. ||40||" |
| `Line 2775: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2776: नागांश्च मातुलांश्चैव तथा चान्यान्स बान्धवान् |` | "And the Nāgas [serpent beings] who were his maternal uncles, as well as other relatives," |
| `Line 2777: पितृंश्च तारयामास सन्तत्या तपसा तथा ||४१||` | "And his ancestors - he delivered them all through his progeny and through austerities. ||41||" |
| `Line 2778: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2780: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2782: ऋषींश्च ब्रह्मचर्येण सन्तत्या च पितामहान् ||४२||` | "The sages through celibacy, and his forefathers through progeny. ||42||" |
| `Line 2783: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2785: जरत्कारुर्गतः स्वर्गं सहितः स्वैः पितामहैः ||४३||` | "Jaratkāru went to heaven together with his forefathers. ||43||" |

| `Line 2805: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2807: प्रीयामहे भृशं तात पितेवेदं प्रभाषसे ॥२॥` | "We are greatly pleased, dear one, as you speak like a father. ||2||" |
| `Line 2808: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2810: आचष्टैतद्यथाख्यानं पिता ते त्वं तथा वद ॥३॥` | "As your father narrated this story, so should you tell it. ||3||" |

| `Line 2815: यथा श्रुतं कथयतः सकाशाद्वै पितुर्मया ॥४॥` | "Just as I heard it from my father when he was narrating it. ||4||" |
| `Line 2816: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2817: पुरा देवयुगे ब्रह्मन्प्रजापतिसुते शुभे |` | "Long ago in the age of gods, O Brahmin, there were two auspicious daughters of Prajāpati [creator deity]," |
| `Line 2818: आस्तां भगिन्यौ रूपेण समुपेतेऽद्भुतेऽनघे ॥५॥` | "There were two sisters endowed with wonderful and flawless beauty. ||5||" |
| `Line 2819: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2820: ते भार्ये कश्यपस्यास्तां कद्रूश्च विनता च ह |` | "They were the wives of Kaśyapa [ancient sage], namely Kadrū and Vinatā," |
| `Line 2821: प्रादात्ताभ्यां वरं प्रीतः प्रजापतिसमः पतिः ॥६॥` | "Their husband, equal to Prajāpati, being pleased, granted them a boon. ||6||" |
| `Line 2822: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2823: कश्यपो धर्मपत्नीभ्यां मुदा परमया युतः ॥६॥` | "Kaśyapa, filled with supreme joy, to his righteous wives ||6||" |
| `Line 2824: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2825: वरातिसर्गं श्रुत्वैव कश्यपादुत्तमं च ते |` | "Having heard the excellent boon offered by Kaśyapa, they" |
| `Line 2826: हर्षादप्रतिमां प्रीतिं प्रापतुः स्म वरस्त्रियौ ||७||` | "The two excellent women experienced incomparable joy from happiness. ||7||" |
| `Line 2827: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2828: वव्रे कद्रूः सुतान्नागान्सहस्रं तुल्यतेजसः |` | "Kadrū chose a thousand serpent sons of equal splendor," |
| `Line 2829: द्वौ पुत्रौ विनता वव्रे कद्रूपुत्राधिकौ बले ||८||` | "While Vinatā chose two sons superior in strength to Kadrū's children. ||8||" |
| `Line 2830: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2831: ओजसा तेजसा चैव विक्रमेणाधिकौ सुतौ ||८||` | "Sons superior in vigor, brilliance, and valor. ||8||" |
| `Line 2832: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2833: तस्यै भर्ता वरं प्रादादध्यर्धं पुत्रमीप्सितम् |` | "Her husband granted her the desired boon of one and a half sons," |
| `Line 2834: एवमस्त्विति तं चाह कश्यपं विनता तदा ||९||` | "And Vinatā then said to Kaśyapa, 'So be it.' ||9||" |
| `Line 2835: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2836: कृतकृत्या तु विनता लब्ध्वा वीर्याधिकौ सुतौ |` | "Vinatā felt fulfilled having obtained two sons of superior strength," |
| `Line 2837: कद्रूश्च लब्ध्वा पुत्राणां सहस्रं तुल्यतेजसाम् ||१०||` | "And Kadrū having obtained a thousand sons of equal splendor. ||10||" |
| `Line 2838: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2841: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2843: जनयामास विप्रेन्द्र द्वे अण्डे विनता तदा ||१२||` | "While Vinatā, O best of Brahmins [Śaunaka], produced two eggs then. ||12||" |
| `Line 2844: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2846: सोपस्वेदेषु भाण्डेषु पञ्च वर्षशतानि च ||१३||` | "In warm vessels for five hundred years. ||13||" |
| `Line 2847: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2850: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2852: अण्डं बिभेद विनता तत्र पुत्रमदृक्षत ||१५||` | "Vinata broke the egg and there beheld her son. ||15||" |

| `Line 2858: शरीरेणासमग्रोऽद्य तस्माद्दासी भविष्यसि ||१७||` | "Incomplete in body today, therefore you shall become a slave. ||17||" |

| `Line 2861: एष च त्वां सुतो मातर्दास्यत्वान्मोक्षयिष्यति ||१८||` | "And this son, O mother, will free you from slavery. ||18||" |

| `Line 2901: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2903: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2904: ज्वलन्तमचलं मेरुं तेजोराशिमनुत्तमम् |` | "The blazing, immovable Mount Meru [cosmic mountain], an unsurpassed mass of splendor," |
| `Line 2905: आक्षिपन्तं प्रभां भानोः स्वशृङ्गैः काञ्चनोज्ज्वलैः ॥५॥` | "Eclipsing the radiance of the sun with its golden-brilliant peaks. ||5||" |
| `Line 2906: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2907: काञ्चनाभरणं चित्रं देवगन्धर्वसेवितम् |` | "Adorned with golden ornaments, marvelous, frequented by gods and gandharvas [celestial musicians]," |
| `Line 2908: अप्रमेयमनाधृष्यमधर्मबहुलैर्जनैः ॥६॥` | "Immeasurable and unapproachable by people abundant in unrighteousness. ||6||" |
| `Line 2909: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2910: व्यालैराचरितं घोरैर्दिव्यौषधिविदीपितम् |` | "Inhabited by fearsome serpents, illuminated by divine herbs," |
| `Line 2911: नाकमावृत्य तिष्ठन्तमुच्छ्रयेण महागिरिम् ॥७॥` | "The great mountain standing, covering heaven with its height. ||7||" |
| `Line 2912: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2913: अगम्यं मनसाप्यन्यैर्नदीवृक्षसमन्वितम् |` | "Inaccessible even in thought to others, filled with rivers and trees," |
| `Line 2914: नानापतगसङ्घैश्च नादितं सुमनोहरैः ॥८॥` | "And resounding with flocks of various enchanting birds. ||8||" |
| `Line 2915: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2916: तस्य पृष्ठमुपारुह्य बहुरत्नाचितं शुभम् |` | "Having ascended its peak, which was auspicious and studded with many jewels," |
| `Line 2917: अनन्तकल्पमुद्विद्धं सुराः सर्वे महौजसः ॥९॥` | "Eternally lofty and elevated, all the mighty gods [devas]. ||9||" |
| `Line 2918: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2919: ते मन्त्रयितुमारब्धास्तत्रासीना दिवौकसः |` | "Those heaven-dwellers, seated there, began to deliberate," |
| `Line 2920: अमृतार्थे समागम्य तपोनियमसंस्थिताः ॥१०॥` | "Having gathered for the sake of amrita [immortality nectar], established in austerities and observances. ||10||" |
| `Line 2921: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2922: तत्र नारायणो देवो ब्रह्माणमिदमब्रवीत् |` | "There, Nārāyaṇa [Vishnu] the god spoke this to Brahmā [creator deity]," |
| `Line 2923: चिन्तयत्सु सुरेष्वेवं मन्त्रयत्सु च सर्वशः ॥११॥` | "While the gods were thus pondering and deliberating in every way. ||11||" |
| `Line 2924: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2925: देवैरसुरसङ्घैश्च मथ्यतां कलशोदधिः |` | "Let the ocean of milk be churned by the gods and hosts of asuras [demons]," |
| `Line 2926: भविष्यत्यमृतं तत्र मथ्यमाने महोदधौ ||१२||` | "Amṛta [immortality nectar] will be produced there when the great ocean is churned. ||12||" |
| `Line 2927: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2928: सर्वौषधीः समावाप्य सर्वरत्नानि चैव हि |` | "Having obtained all herbs and all jewels indeed," |
| `Line 2929: मन्थध्वमुदधिं देवा वेत्स्यध्वममृतं ततः ||१३||` | "Churn the ocean, O gods, and you will obtain amṛta [immortality nectar] from it. ||13||" |

| `Line 2938: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2939: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 2940: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2941: ततोऽभ्रशिखराकारैर्गिरिशृङ्गैरलङ्कृतम् |` | "Then, adorned with mountain peaks resembling the summits of clouds," |
| `Line 2942: मन्दरं पर्वतवरं लताजालसमावृतम् ||१||` | "Mandara, the excellent mountain, covered with networks of creepers. ||1||" |
| `Line 2943: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2944: नानाविहगसङ्घुष्टं नानादंष्ट्रिसमाकुलम् |` | "Resounding with various birds, teeming with various wild beasts [fanged creatures]," |
| `Line 2945: किंनरैरप्सरोभिश्च देवैरपि च सेवितम् ||२||` | "Frequented by Kinnaras [half-human beings], Apsaras [celestial nymphs], and also by gods. ||2||" |
| `Line 2946: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2947: एकादश सहस्राणि योजनानां समुच्छ्रितम् |` | "Eleven thousand yojanas [ancient measure] in height," |
| `Line 2948: अधो भूमेः सहस्रेषु तावत्स्वेव प्रतिष्ठितम् ||३||` | "And established just as many thousands (of yojanas) below the earth. ||3||" |
| `Line 2949: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2950: तमुद्धर्तुं न शक्ता वै सर्वे देवगणास्तदा |` | "All the hosts of gods were then unable to uproot it," |
| `Line 2951: विष्णुमासीनमभ्येत्य ब्रह्माणं चेदमब्रुवन् ||४||` | "Having approached Vishnu [preserver deity] who was seated, and Brahma [creator deity], they said this. ||4||" |
| `Line 2952: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2953: भवन्तावत्र कुरुतां बुद्धिं नैःश्रेयसीं पराम् |` | "May both of you devise here the highest wisdom leading to supreme good," |
| `Line 2954: मन्दरोद्धरणे यत्नः क्रियतां च हिताय नः ||५||` | "And let efforts be made to lift Mount Mandara [sacred mountain] for our welfare. ||5||" |
| `Line 2955: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2956: तथेति चाब्रवीद्विष्णुर्ब्रह्मणा सह भार्गव |` | "Vishnu said 'So be it' along with Brahma, O Bhargava [descendant of Bhrigu]," |
| `Line 2957: ततोऽनन्तः समुत्थाय ब्रह्मणा परिचोदितः ||६||` | "Then Ananta [cosmic serpent Shesha] arose, urged by Brahma. ||6||" |
| `Line 2958: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2959: नारायणेन चाप्युक्तस्तस्मिन्कर्मणि वीर्यवान् ||६||` | "And instructed by Narayana [Vishnu] as well, the mighty one engaged in that task. ||6||" |
| `Line 2960: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2961: अथ पर्वतराजानं तमनन्तो महाबलः |` | "Then Ananta of great strength, the mighty one," |
| `Line 2962: उज्जहार बलाद्ब्रह्मन्सवनं सवनौकसम् ||७||` | "Forcibly lifted up that king of mountains, O Brahman, along with its forests and forest dwellers. ||7||" |
| `Line 2963: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2964: ततस्तेन सुराः सार्धं समुद्रमुपतस्थिरे |` | "Then, with it, the gods approached the ocean," |
| `Line 2965: तमूचुरमृतार्थाय निर्मथिष्यामहे जलम् ||८||` | "And said to him, 'For the sake of amrita [nectar of immortality], we will churn your waters.' ||8||" |
| `Line 2966: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2967: अपाम्पतिरथोवाच ममाप्यंशो भवेत्ततः |` | "Then the lord of waters [ocean] said, 'Let there be a share for me also from that,'" |
| `Line 2968: सोढास्मि विपुलं मर्दं मन्दरभ्रमणादिति ||९||` | "'I will endure the great churning from the rotation of Mandara.' ||9||" |
| `Line 2969: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2970: ऊचुश्च कूर्मराजानमकूपारं सुरासुराः |` | "And the gods and demons spoke to the king of tortoises, Akupara [cosmic turtle]," |
| `Line 2971: गिरेरधिष्ठानमस्य भवान्भवितुमर्हति ||१०||` | "'You should become the foundation of this mountain.' ||10||" |
| `Line 2972: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2973: कूर्मेण तु तथेत्युक्त्वा पृष्ठमस्य समर्पितम् |` | "The tortoise, having said 'So be it,' offered his back," |
| `Line 2974: तस्य शैलस्य चाग्रं वै यन्त्रेणेन्द्रोऽभ्यपीडयत् ||११||` | "And Indra [king of gods] with a machine pressed down the top of that mountain. ||11||" |
| `Line 2975: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2976: मन्थानं मन्दरं कृत्वा तथा नेत्रं च वासुकिम् |` | "Making Mount Mandara [cosmic mountain] the churning rod and Vāsuki [serpent king] the rope," |
| `Line 2977: देवा मथितुमारब्धाः समुद्रं निधिमम्भसाम् ||१२||` | "The gods began to churn the ocean, the repository of waters. ||12||" |
| `Line 2978: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2979: अमृतार्थिनस्ततो ब्रह्मन्सहिता दैत्यदानवाः ||१२||` | "Then, O Brahmin, the Daityas [demon class] and Dānavas [demon class], seeking immortality, joined together. ||12||" |
| `Line 2980: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2981: एकमन्तमुपाश्लिष्टा नागराज्ञो महासुराः |` | "The great Asuras [demons] grasped one end of the serpent king," |
| `Line 2982: विबुधाः सहिताः सर्वे यतः पुच्छं ततः स्थिताः ||१३||` | "While all the gods together stood at the tail end. ||13||" |
| `Line 2983: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2984: अनन्तो भगवान्देवो यतो नारायणस्ततः |` | "Where Lord Nārāyaṇa [Vishnu] was, there was Ananta [endless serpent]," |
| `Line 2985: शिर उद्यम्य नागस्य पुनः पुनरवाक्षिपत् ||१४||` | "Who, lifting the serpent's head, pulled it down again and again. ||14||" |
| `Line 2986: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2988: सधूमाः सार्चिषो वाता निष्पेतुरसकृन्मुखात् ||१५||` | "Smoky, fiery breaths repeatedly issued from his mouth. ||15||" |
| `Line 2989: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2990: ते धूमसङ्घाः सम्भूता मेघसङ्घाः सविद्युतः |` | "Those masses of smoke transformed into clouds with lightning," |
| `Line 2991: अभ्यवर्षन्सुरगणाञ्श्रमसन्तापकर्शितान् ||१६||` | "And rained upon the hosts of gods who were exhausted by fatigue and heat. ||16||" |
| `Line 2992: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2993: तस्माच्च गिरिकूटाग्रात्प्रच्युताः पुष्पवृष्टयः |` | "From the peak of that mountain, showers of flowers fell," |
| `Line 2994: सुरासुरगणान्माल्यैः सर्वतः समवाकिरन् ||१७||` | "Covering the hosts of gods and demons with garlands from all sides. ||17||" |
| `Line 2995: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 2997: उदधेर्मथ्यमानस्य मन्दरेण सुरासुरैः ||१८||` | "As the ocean was being churned by gods and demons using Mount Mandara. ||18||" |
| `Line 2998: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 2999: तत्र नानाजलचरा विनिष्पिष्टा महाद्रिणा |` | "There, various aquatic creatures, crushed by the great mountain," |
| `Line 3000: विलयं समुपाजग्मुः शतशो लवणाम्भसि ||१९||` | "Met their destruction by the hundreds in the salty waters. ||19||" |
| `Line 3001: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3002: वारुणानि च भूतानि विविधानि महीधरः |` | "And the mountain [Mandara] destroyed various aquatic creatures [water beings]" |
| `Line 3003: पातालतलवासीनि विलयं समुपानयत् ||२०||` | "And brought to destruction those dwelling in the depths of Pātāla [netherworld]. ||20||" |
| `Line 3004: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3005: तस्मिंश्च भ्राम्यमाणेऽद्रौ सङ्घृष्यन्तः परस्परम् |` | "And as that mountain was being rotated, rubbing against each other," |
| `Line 3006: न्यपतन्पतगोपेताः पर्वताग्रान्महाद्रुमाः ||२१||` | "Great trees with birds fell from the mountain peaks. ||21||" |
| `Line 3007: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3008: तेषां सङ्घर्षजश्चाग्निरर्चिर्भिः प्रज्वलन्मुहुः |` | "And the fire produced from their friction, repeatedly blazing with flames," |
| `Line 3009: विद्युद्भिरिव नीलाभ्रमावृणोन्मन्दरं गिरिम् ||२२||` | "Enveloped the Mandara mountain like lightning in dark clouds. ||22||" |
| `Line 3010: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3011: ददाह कुञ्जरांश्चैव सिंहांश्चैव विनिःसृतान् |` | "It burned the elephants and lions that had come out," |
| `Line 3012: विगतासूनि सर्वाणि सत्त्वानि विविधानि च ||२३||` | "And various other creatures, all deprived of their lives. ||23||" |
| `Line 3013: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3014: तमग्निममरश्रेष्ठः प्रदहन्तं ततस्ततः |` | "That fire which was burning everywhere, the foremost of immortals [Indra]," |
| `Line 3015: वारिणा मेघजेनेन्द्रः शमयामास सर्वतः ||२४||` | "Indra extinguished completely with water produced from clouds. ||24||" |
| `Line 3016: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3017: ततो नानाविधास्तत्र सुस्रुवुः सागराम्भसि |` | "Then various kinds of exudations flowed there into the ocean waters," |
| `Line 3018: महाद्रुमाणां निर्यासा बहवश्चौषधीरसाः ||२५||` | "The saps of great trees and many juices of medicinal herbs. ||25||" |
| `Line 3019: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3020: तेषाममृतवीर्याणां रसानां पयसैव च |` | "From those juices with the potency of amrita [nectar], and with the milk," |
| `Line 3021: अमरत्वं सुरा जग्मुः काञ्चनस्य च निःस्रवात् ||२६||` | "The gods attained immortality, and from the flow of gold. ||26||" |
| `Line 3022: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3023: अथ तस्य समुद्रस्य तज्जातमुदकं पयः |` | "Then that water of the ocean became milk," |
| `Line 3024: रसोत्तमैर्विमिश्रं च ततः क्षीरादभूद्घृतम् ||२७||` | "Mixed with the finest essences, and from that milk arose ghee [clarified butter]. ||27||" |
| `Line 3025: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3026: ततो ब्रह्माणमासीनं देवा वरदमब्रुवन् |` | "Then the gods addressed Brahmā [creator deity], who was seated, the bestower of boons," |
| `Line 3027: श्रान्ताः स्म सुभृशं ब्रह्मन्नोद्भवत्यमृतं च तत् ||२८||` | "We are extremely exhausted, O Brahmā, and that amṛta [immortality nectar] does not emerge. ||28||" |
| `Line 3028: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3029: ऋते नारायणं देवं दैत्या नागोत्तमास्तथा |` | "Without Nārāyaṇa [Vishnu], the daityas [demons] and the foremost nāgas [serpents] too," |
| `Line 3030: चिरारब्धमिदं चापि सागरस्यापि मन्थनम् ||२९||` | "This churning of the ocean has been going on for a long time. ||29||" |
| `Line 3031: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3032: ततो नारायणं देवं ब्रह्मा वचनमब्रवीत् |` | "Then Brahmā spoke these words to Lord Nārāyaṇa," |
| `Line 3033: विधत्स्वैषां बलं विष्णो भवानत्र परायणम् ||३०||` | "Grant them strength, O Viṣṇu, you are the ultimate refuge here. ||30||" |
| `Line 3034: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3035: विष्णुरुवाच||` | "Viṣṇu said:" |
| `Line 3036: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3037: बलं ददामि सर्वेषां कर्मैतद्ये समास्थिताः |` | "I shall give strength to all who are engaged in this task," |
| `Line 3038: क्षोभ्यतां कलशः सर्वैर्मन्दरः परिवर्त्यताम् ||३१||` | "Let the ocean be churned by all, let Mount Mandara be rotated. ||31||" |
| `Line 3039: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3040: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [narrator sage] said:" |
| `Line 3041: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3042: नारायणवचः श्रुत्वा बलिनस्ते महोदधेः |` | "Hearing Nārāyaṇa's words, those mighty ones, of the great ocean," |
| `Line 3043: तत्पयः सहिता भूयश्चक्रिरे भृशमाकुलम् ||३२||` | "Together, they again made its waters extremely agitated. ||32||" |
| `Line 3044: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3045: ततः शतसहस्रांशुः समान इव सागरात् |` | "Then, like the thousand-rayed one [sun], from the ocean," |
| `Line 3046: प्रसन्नभाः समुत्पन्नः सोमः शीतांशुरुज्ज्वलः ||३३||` | "Arose the radiant Soma [moon], with cool rays, of serene splendor. ||33||" |
| `Line 3047: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3048: श्रीरनन्तरमुत्पन्ना घृतात्पाण्डुरवासिनी |` | "Śrī [goddess of fortune] arose next, clad in white, from the ghee [clarified butter]," |
| `Line 3049: सुरा देवी समुत्पन्ना तुरगः पाण्डुरस्तथा ||३४||` | "The goddess Surā [wine deity] emerged, and also the white horse [Uccaiḥśravas]. ||34||" |
| `Line 3050: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3051: कौस्तुभश्च मणिर्दिव्य उत्पन्नोऽमृतसम्भवः |` | "And the divine Kaustubha gem emerged, born from the churning of the nectar [amrita]," |
| `Line 3052: मरीचिविकचः श्रीमान्नारायण उरोगतः ||३५||` | "Radiant with light rays, the glorious gem adorned the chest of Nārāyaṇa [Vishnu]. ||35||" |
| `Line 3053: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3054: श्रीः सुरा चैव सोमश्च तुरगश्च मनोजवः |` | "Śrī [goddess of fortune], Surā [goddess of wine], Soma [moon god], and the swift-minded horse [Uccaiḥśravas]," |
| `Line 3055: यतो देवास्ततो जग्मुरादित्यपथमाश्रिताः ||३६||` | "Went in the same direction as the gods, taking refuge in the path of Āditya [sun]. ||36||" |
| `Line 3056: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3057: धन्वन्तरिस्ततो देवो वपुष्मानुदतिष्ठत |` | "Then arose the handsome divine Dhanvantari [physician of gods]," |
| `Line 3058: श्वेतं कमण्डलुं बिभ्रदमृतं यत्र तिष्ठति ||३७||` | "Holding a white water-pot [kamaṇḍalu] in which the nectar [amrita] was contained. ||37||" |
| `Line 3059: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3060: एतदत्यद्भुतं दृष्ट्वा दानवानां समुत्थितः |` | "Seeing this most wonderful sight, there arose among the Dānavas [demons]," |
| `Line 3061: अमृतार्थे महान्नादो ममेदमिति जल्पताम् ||३८||` | "A great clamor for the nectar, as they shouted, 'This is mine!' ||38||" |
| `Line 3062: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3063: ततो नारायणो मायामास्थितो मोहिनीं प्रभुः |` | "Then Nārāyaṇa [Vishnu], the lord, resorted to his illusion [māyā], assuming the form of Mohinī [enchantress]," |
| `Line 3064: स्त्रीरूपमद्भुतं कृत्वा दानवानभिसंश्रितः ||३९||` | "Creating a wondrous female form, he approached the Dānavas. ||39||" |
| `Line 3065: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3066: ततस्तदमृतं तस्यै ददुस्ते मूढचेतसः |` | "Then those deluded-minded ones gave the nectar to her," |
| `Line 3067: स्त्रियै दानवदैतेयाः सर्वे तद्गतमानसाः ||४०||` | "All the Dānavas and Daityas [demon classes] gave it to the woman, their minds captivated by her. ||40||" |

| `Line 3076: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3077: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 3078: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3079: अथावरणमुख्यानि नानाप्रहरणानि च |` | "Then, taking up various shields and diverse weapons," |
| `Line 3080: प्रगृह्याभ्यद्रवन्देवान्सहिता दैत्यदानवाः ||१||` | "The united Daityas [demon class] and Dānavas [demon class] rushed against the gods. ||1||" |
| `Line 3081: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3082: ततस्तदमृतं देवो विष्णुरादाय वीर्यवान् |` | "Then the mighty god Viṣṇu [preserver deity], taking that amṛta [immortality nectar]," |
| `Line 3083: जहार दानवेन्द्रेभ्यो नरेण सहितः प्रभुः ||२||` | "Stole it from the Dānava lords, the Lord accompanied by Nara [divine sage]. ||2||" |
| `Line 3084: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3085: ततो देवगणाः सर्वे पपुस्तदमृतं तदा |` | "Then all the hosts of gods drank that amṛta," |
| `Line 3086: विष्णोः सकाशात्सम्प्राप्य सम्भ्रमे तुमुले सति ||३||` | "Having received it from Viṣṇu, while there was tumultuous confusion. ||3||" |
| `Line 3087: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3088: ततः पिबत्सु तत्कालं देवेष्वमृतमीप्सितम् |` | "Then, while the gods were drinking that desired nectar at that time," |
| `Line 3089: राहुर्विबुधरूपेण दानवः प्रापिबत्तदा ||४||` | "Rāhu [eclipse demon], a Dānava in the form of a god, also drank it then. ||4||" |
| `Line 3090: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3091: तस्य कण्ठमनुप्राप्ते दानवस्यामृते तदा |` | "When the nectar had reached the throat of that Dānava," |
| `Line 3092: आख्यातं चन्द्रसूर्याभ्यां सुराणां हितकाम्यया ||५||` | "It was reported by the Moon and Sun, out of desire for the welfare of the gods. ||5||" |
| `Line 3093: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3094: ततो भगवता तस्य शिरश्छिन्नमलङ्कृतम् |` | "Then the Lord cut off his adorned head," |
| `Line 3095: चक्रायुधेन चक्रेण पिबतोऽमृतमोजसा ||६||` | "With his discus weapon, while he was forcefully drinking the nectar. ||6||" |
| `Line 3096: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3097: तच्छैलशृङ्गप्रतिमं दानवस्य शिरो महत् |` | "That massive head of the Dānava, resembling a mountain peak," |
| `Line 3098: चक्रेणोत्कृत्तमपतच्चालयद्वसुधातलम् ||७||` | "Severed by the discus, fell down shaking the surface of the earth. ||7||" |
| `Line 3099: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3101: शाश्वतश्चन्द्रसूर्याभ्यां ग्रसत्यद्यापि चैव तौ ||८||` | "Eternally, he devours both the moon and sun, and even to this day continues to seize them. ||8||" |
| `Line 3102: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3103: विहाय भगवांश्चापि स्त्रीरूपमतुलं हरिः |` | "And then the Lord Hari [Vishnu], abandoning that incomparable female form," |
| `Line 3104: नानाप्रहरणैर्भीमैर्दानवान्समकम्पयत् ||९||` | "Made the Dānavas [demons] tremble with various terrifying weapons. ||9||" |
| `Line 3105: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3106: ततः प्रवृत्तः सङ्ग्रामः समीपे लवणाम्भसः |` | "Then commenced a battle near the salt waters [ocean]," |
| `Line 3107: सुराणामसुराणां च सर्वघोरतरो महान् ||१०||` | "Between the Suras [gods] and Asuras [demons], most terrible and great. ||10||" |
| `Line 3108: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3109: प्रासाः सुविपुलास्तीक्ष्णा न्यपतन्त सहस्रशः |` | "Massive sharp javelins fell by the thousands," |
| `Line 3110: तोमराश्च सुतीक्ष्णाग्राः शस्त्राणि विविधानि च ||११||` | "And lances with very sharp points, and various other weapons. ||11||" |
| `Line 3111: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3112: ततोऽसुराश्चक्रभिन्ना वमन्तो रुधिरं बहु |` | "Then the Asuras [demons], pierced by the discus, vomiting much blood," |
| `Line 3113: असिशक्तिगदारुग्णा निपेतुर्धरणीतले ||१२||` | "Broken by swords, spears, and maces, fell upon the surface of the earth. ||12||" |
| `Line 3114: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3115: छिन्नानि पट्टिशैश्चापि शिरांसि युधि दारुणे |` | "Heads severed by spears in that terrible battle," |
| `Line 3116: तप्तकाञ्चनजालानि निपेतुरनिशं तदा ||१३||` | "Adorned with heated golden ornaments, fell continuously then. ||13||" |
| `Line 3117: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3118: रुधिरेणावलिप्ताङ्गा निहताश्च महासुराः |` | "And the mighty Asuras [demons], slain with their limbs smeared with blood," |
| `Line 3119: अद्रीणामिव कूटानि धातुरक्तानि शेरते ||१४||` | "Lay like mountain peaks stained with red mineral deposits. ||14||" |
| `Line 3120: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3121: हाहाकारः समभवत्तत्र तत्र सहस्रशः |` | "Cries of distress arose here and there by the thousands," |
| `Line 3122: अन्योन्यं छिन्दतां शस्त्रैरादित्ये लोहितायति ||१५||` | "As they cut each other with weapons while the sun [Āditya] turned red. ||15||" |
| `Line 3123: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3124: परिघैश्चायसैः पीतैः संनिकर्षे च मुष्टिभिः |` | "With iron clubs gleaming yellow, and in close combat with fists," |
| `Line 3125: निघ्नतां समरेऽन्योन्यं शब्दो दिवमिवास्पृशत् ||१६||` | "The sound of them striking each other in battle seemed to touch the heavens. ||16||" |
| `Line 3126: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3127: छिन्धि भिन्धि प्रधावध्वं पातयाभिसरेति च |` | "Cut, split, charge forward, strike down, attack! - such [battle cries]" |
| `Line 3128: व्यश्रूयन्त महाघोराः शब्दास्तत्र समन्ततः ||१७||` | "Terrifying sounds were heard there from all directions. ||17||" |
| `Line 3129: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3130: एवं सुतुमुले युद्धे वर्तमाने भयावहे |` | "While this tumultuous and terrifying battle was raging," |
| `Line 3131: नरनारायणौ देवौ समाजग्मतुराहवम् ||१८||` | "The divine Nara and Nārāyaṇa [divine sages] arrived at the battlefield. ||18||" |
| `Line 3132: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3133: तत्र दिव्यं धनुर्दृष्ट्वा नरस्य भगवानपि |` | "There, seeing the divine bow of Nara, the Lord [Viṣṇu] himself" |
| `Line 3134: चिन्तयामास वै चक्रं विष्णुर्दानवसूदनम् ||१९||` | "Viṣṇu, the destroyer of demons, thought of his discus [Sudarśana]. ||19||" |
| `Line 3135: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3136: ततोऽम्बराच्चिन्तितमात्रमागतं; महाप्रभं चक्रममित्रतापनम् |` | "Then, merely by thinking of it, from the sky came the brilliant discus, the tormentor of enemies," |
| `Line 3137: विभावसोस्तुल्यमकुण्ठमण्डलं; सुदर्शनं भीममजय्यमुत्तमम् ||२०||` | "Equal to fire in brilliance, with unblunted rim, the terrifying, invincible, supreme Sudarśana [divine discus]. ||20||" |
| `Line 3138: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3139: तदागतं ज्वलितहुताशनप्रभं; भयङ्करं करिकरबाहुरच्युतः |` | "That arrived discus, blazing like fire, fearsome, Achyuta [Viṣṇu] with arms like elephant trunks" |
| `Line 3140: मुमोच वै चपलमुदग्रवेगव; न्महाप्रभं परनगरावदारणम् ||२१||` | "Released indeed the swift, tremendously forceful, brilliantly radiant, destroyer of enemy cities. ||21||" |
| `Line 3141: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3142: तदन्तकज्वलनसमानवर्चसं; पुनः पुनर्न्यपतत वेगवत्तदा |` | "That discus, with splendor equal to the fire of destruction, fell again and again with great speed then," |
| `Line 3143: विदारयद्दितिदनुजान्सहस्रशः; करेरितं पुरुषवरेण संयुगे ||२२||` | "Tearing apart thousands of Diti's and Danu's sons [demons], hurled by the hand of the supreme being in battle. ||22||" |
| `Line 3144: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3146: प्रवेरितं वियति मुहुः क्षितौ तदा; पपौ रणे रुधिरमथो पिशाचवत् ||२३||` | "Propelled repeatedly through the sky and on earth, it then drank blood in battle like a piśāca [flesh-eating spirit]. ||23||" |
| `Line 3147: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3149: महाबला विगलितमेघवर्चसः; सहस्रशो गगनमभिप्रपद्य ह ||२४||` | "The mighty ones, with splendor like dispersed clouds, thousands ascending to the sky indeed. ||24||" |
| `Line 3150: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3151: अथाम्बराद्भयजननाः प्रपेदिरे; सपादपा बहुविधमेघरूपिणः |` | "Then from the sky, terrifying clouds of various forms descended with trees;" |
| `Line 3152: महाद्रयः प्रविगलिताग्रसानवः; परस्परं द्रुतमभिहत्य सस्वनाः ||२५||` | "Great mountains with their peaks and summits crumbling, struck against each other swiftly with loud noise. ||25||" |
| `Line 3153: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3155: परस्परं भृशमभिगर्जतां मुहू; रणाजिरे भृशमभिसम्प्रवर्तिते ||२६||` | "As they repeatedly roared fiercely at each other, while the battlefield intensely raged on. ||26||" |
| `Line 3156: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3157: नरस्ततो वरकनकाग्रभूषणै; र्महेषुभिर्गगनपथं समावृणोत् |` | "Then Nara [Arjuna] covered the path of the sky with great arrows adorned with excellent golden tips;" |
| `Line 3158: विदारयन्गिरिशिखराणि पत्रिभि; र्महाभयेऽसुरगणविग्रहे तदा ||२७||` | "Splitting mountain peaks with feathered arrows, during that great terrifying battle with the hosts of asuras [demons]. ||27||" |
| `Line 3159: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3160: ततो महीं लवणजलं च सागरं; महासुराः प्रविविशुरर्दिताः सुरैः |` | "Then the great asuras [demons], tormented by the gods, entered the earth, the salt waters, and the ocean;" |
| `Line 3161: वियद्गतं ज्वलितहुताशनप्रभं; सुदर्शनं परिकुपितं निशाम्य च ||२८||` | "Having seen the Sudarshana [divine discus] blazing with the brilliance of fire, moving through the sky in great fury. ||28||" |
| `Line 3162: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3163: ततः सुरैर्विजयमवाप्य मन्दरः; स्वमेव देशं गमितः सुपूजितः |` | "Then, after the gods achieved victory, Mount Mandara [churning rod], duly worshipped, was returned to its own place;" |
| `Line 3164: विनाद्य खं दिवमपि चैव सर्वश; स्ततो गताः सलिलधरा यथागतम् ||२९||` | "After resounding through the sky and heaven in all directions, the clouds then departed as they had come. ||29||" |
| `Line 3165: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3166: ततोऽमृतं सुनिहितमेव चक्रिरे; सुराः परां मुदमभिगम्य पुष्कलाम् |` | "Then the gods, having obtained abundant joy, carefully secured the amrita [nectar of immortality];" |
| `Line 3167: ददौ च तं निधिममृतस्य रक्षितुं; किरीटिने बलभिदथामरैः सह ||३०||` | "And they gave that treasure of amrita [immortality nectar] to Kirīṭin [Indra, crown-wearer] to protect, along with Balabhid [Indra, destroyer of Bala] and the other gods. ||30||" |

| `Line 3178: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3179: एतत्ते सर्वमाख्यातममृतं मथितं यथा |` | "All this has been narrated to you about how the amṛta [immortality nectar] was churned," |
| `Line 3180: यत्र सोऽश्वः समुत्पन्नः श्रीमानतुलविक्रमः ||१||` | "During which that horse arose, the magnificent one of unparalleled prowess. ||1||" |
| `Line 3181: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3182: यं निशाम्य तदा कद्रूर्विनतामिदमब्रवीत् |` | "Upon seeing him, Kadrū [serpent mother] then said this to Vinatā [Garuḍa's mother]:" |
| `Line 3183: उच्चैःश्रवा नु किंवर्णो भद्रे जानीहि माचिरम् ||२||` | "What color is Uccaiḥśravā [divine horse], O blessed one? Find out without delay. ||2||" |
| `Line 3184: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3186: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3187: श्वेत एवाश्वराजोऽयं किं वा त्वं मन्यसे शुभे |` | "This king of horses is indeed white. What do you think, O auspicious one?" |
| `Line 3188: ब्रूहि वर्णं त्वमप्यस्य ततोऽत्र विपणावहे ||३||` | "Tell me what color you think it is, and then let us wager on it. ||3||" |
| `Line 3189: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3190: कद्रूरुवाच||` | "Kadrū said:" |
| `Line 3191: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3192: कृष्णवालमहं मन्ये हयमेनं शुचिस्मिते |` | "I think this horse has a black tail, O pure-smiling one," |
| `Line 3193: एहि सार्धं मया दीव्य दासीभावाय भामिनि ||४||` | "Come, wager with me for the state of servitude, O passionate one. ||4||" |
| `Line 3194: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3195: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta said:" |
| `Line 3196: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3197: एवं ते समयं कृत्वा दासीभावाय वै मिथः |` | "Having thus made an agreement between themselves for the state of servitude," |
| `Line 3198: जग्मतुः स्वगृहानेव श्वो द्रक्ष्याव इति स्म ह ||५||` | "They both went to their own homes, saying, 'We shall see tomorrow.' ||5||" |
| `Line 3199: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3200: ततः पुत्रसहस्रं तु कद्रूर्जिह्मं चिकीर्षती |` | "Then Kadrū, wishing to act deceitfully, commanded her thousand sons," |
| `Line 3201: आज्ञापयामास तदा वाला भूत्वाञ्जनप्रभाः ||६||` | "She then commanded them, having become dark-colored like collyrium [black eye cosmetic]. ||6||" |
| `Line 3202: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3203: आविशध्वं हयं क्षिप्रं दासी न स्यामहं यथा |` | "Enter the horse quickly so that I may not become a slave," |
| `Line 3204: तद्वाक्यं नान्वपद्यन्त ताञ्शशाप भुजङ्गमान् ||७||` | "They did not comply with that command, so she cursed those serpents. ||7||" |
| `Line 3205: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3206: सर्पसत्रे वर्तमाने पावको वः प्रधक्ष्यति |` | "During the serpent sacrifice [sarpa-satra], the fire will consume you," |
| `Line 3207: जनमेजयस्य राजर्षेः पाण्डवेयस्य धीमतः ||८||` | "The sacrifice of Janamejaya, the royal sage [rajarshi], descendant of Pandu, the wise one. ||8||" |
| `Line 3208: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3213: बहुत्वं प्रेक्ष्य सर्पाणां प्रजानां हितकाम्यया ||१०||` | "Considering the multitude of serpents, for the welfare of the people. ||10||" |
| `Line 3214: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3232: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3234: जग्मतुस्तुरगं द्रष्टुमुच्छैःश्रवसमन्तिकात् ||२||` | "Went to see the horse Uccaiḥśravas [divine steed] from nearby. ||2||" |
| `Line 3235: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3236: ददृशाते तदा तत्र समुद्रं निधिमम्भसाम् |` | "Then they saw there the ocean, the repository of waters," |
| `Line 3237: तिमिङ्गिलझषाकीर्णं मकरैरावृतं तथा ||३||` | "Filled with timiṅgila [whale-eaters] and fish, and likewise covered with makaras [sea monsters]. ||3||" |

| `Line 3240: उग्रैर्नित्यमनाधृष्यं कूर्मग्राहसमाकुलम् ||४||` | "Fierce, ever unconquerable, teeming with turtles and crocodiles. ||4||" |
| `Line 3241: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3242: आकरं सर्वरत्नानामालयं वरुणस्य च |` | "The source of all jewels and the abode of Varuṇa [water deity]," |
| `Line 3243: नागानामालयं रम्यमुत्तमं सरितां पतिम् ||५||` | "The pleasant dwelling of nāgas [serpent beings], the supreme lord of rivers. ||5||" |
| `Line 3244: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3246: भयङ्करं च सत्त्वानां पयसां निधिमर्णवम् ||६||` | "Terrifying to creatures, the ocean, the repository of waters. ||6||" |
| `Line 3247: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3248: शुभं दिव्यममर्त्यानाममृतस्याकरं परम् |` | "Auspicious, divine, the supreme source of amṛta [immortality nectar] for the immortals," |
| `Line 3249: अप्रमेयमचिन्त्यं च सुपुण्यजलमद्भुतम् ||७||` | "Immeasurable, inconceivable, with wonderfully pure waters. ||7||" |
| `Line 3250: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3251: घोरं जलचरारावरौद्रं भैरवनिस्वनम् |` | "Terrible with the roars of aquatic creatures, frightful with fearsome sounds," |
| `Line 3252: गम्भीरावर्तकलिलं सर्वभूतभयङ्करम् ||८||` | "Filled with deep whirlpools, causing fear to all beings. ||8||" |
| `Line 3253: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3255: वीचीहस्तैः प्रचलितैर्नृत्यन्तमिव सर्वशः ||९||` | "Dancing, as it were, everywhere with the moving hands of waves. ||9||" |
| `Line 3256: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3259: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3262: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3265: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3268: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3270: अगाधपारं विस्तीर्णमप्रमेयं सरित्पतिम् ||१४||` | "The lord of rivers, with unfathomable shores, vast and immeasurable. ||14||" |
| `Line 3271: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3273: अभिसार्यमाणमनिशं ददृशाते महार्णवम् ||१५||` | "They both beheld the great ocean being continuously approached. ||15||" |
| `Line 3274: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3275: गम्भीरं तिमिमकरोग्रसङ्कुलं तं; गर्जन्तं जलचररावरौद्रनादैः |` | "That deep ocean teeming with fierce whales and sea monsters; roaring with the terrible sounds of aquatic creatures;" |

| `Line 3277: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3279: पातालज्वलनशिखाविदीपितं तं; पश्यन्त्यौ द्रुतमभिपेततुस्तदानीम् ||१७||` | "Illuminated by the flames of the Pātāla [netherworld] fire; seeing it, they both swiftly flew toward it then. ||17||" |

| `Line 3299: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3320: अदूरादभ्युपेत्यैनं देवाः सर्षिगणास्तदा ||९||` | "Approaching him from nearby, the gods along with groups of sages, then. ||9||" |
| `Line 3321: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3324: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3325: बलोर्मिमान्साधुरदीनसत्त्वः; समृद्धिमान्दुष्प्रसहस्त्वमेव |` | "You are full of waves of strength, virtuous, of undaunted courage; prosperous and irresistible are you alone." |
| `Line 3326: तपः श्रुतं सर्वमहीनकीर्ते; अनागतं चोपगतं च सर्वम् ||११||` | "Austerities, learning, all are in you, O one of unfailing glory; everything past and future (is known to you). ||11||" |
| `Line 3327: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3328: त्वमुत्तमः सर्वमिदं चराचरं; गभस्तिभिर्भानुरिवावभाससे |` | "You are supreme, illuminating all this mobile and immobile universe with your rays, like the sun [Bhānu]," |
| `Line 3329: समाक्षिपन्भानुमतः प्रभां मुहु; स्त्वमन्तकः सर्वमिदं ध्रुवाध्रुवम् ||१२||` | "Repeatedly eclipsing the radiance of the sun, you are the destroyer [Antaka] of all this, both permanent and impermanent. ||12||" |
| `Line 3330: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3331: दिवाकरः परिकुपितो यथा दहे; त्प्रजास्तथा दहसि हुताशनप्रभ |` | "As the sun [Divākara] when enraged burns the creatures, so do you burn, O you who shine like fire [Hutāshana]," |
| `Line 3332: भयङ्करः प्रलय इवाग्निरुत्थितो; विनाशयन्युगपरिवर्तनान्तकृत् ||१३||` | "Terrifying like the fire risen at dissolution [pralaya], destroying, bringing an end to the cycle of ages. ||13||" |
| `Line 3333: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3351: मातुरन्तिकमागच्छत्परं तीरं महोदधेः ||१||` | "He came to his mother on the far shore of the great ocean. ||1||" |

| `Line 3354: अतीव दुःखसन्तप्ता दासीभावमुपागता ||२||` | "Extremely afflicted with sorrow, she had been reduced to the state of a slave. ||2||" |

| `Line 3363: पन्नगान्गरुडश्चापि मातुर्वचनचोदितः ||५||` | "And Garuḍa also carried the serpents, urged by his mother's words. ||5||" |

| `Line 3367: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3369: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3370: नमस्ते देवदेवेश नमस्ते बलसूदन |` | "Salutations to you, lord of lords of gods, salutations to you, destroyer of Bala [demon]," |
| `Line 3371: नमुचिघ्न नमस्तेऽस्तु सहस्राक्ष शचीपते ||७||` | "Slayer of Namuci [demon], salutations be to you, thousand-eyed one, lord of Śacī [Indra's wife]. ||7||" |
| `Line 3372: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3373: सर्पाणां सूर्यतप्तानां वारिणा त्वं प्लवो भव |` | "For the serpents scorched by the sun, be a shower with water," |
| `Line 3374: त्वमेव परमं त्राणमस्माकममरोत्तम ||८||` | "You alone are the supreme protection for us, O best of immortals. ||8||" |
| `Line 3375: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3376: ईशो ह्यसि पयः स्रष्टुं त्वमनल्पं पुरंदर |` | "You are capable of creating abundant waters, O Purandara [city-destroyer, Indra]," |
| `Line 3377: त्वमेव मेघस्त्वं वायुस्त्वमग्निर्वैद्युतोऽम्बरे ||९||` | "You yourself are the cloud, you are the wind, you are the lightning fire in the sky. ||9||" |
| `Line 3378: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3379: त्वमभ्रघनविक्षेप्ता त्वामेवाहुः पुनर्घनम् |` | "You are the disperser of dense clouds, and they call you again the cloud itself," |
| `Line 3380: त्वं वज्रमतुलं घोरं घोषवांस्त्वं बलाहकः ||१०||` | "You are the incomparable terrible thunderbolt, you are the thundering rain cloud. ||10||" |
| `Line 3381: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3382: स्रष्टा त्वमेव लोकानां संहर्ता चापराजितः |` | "You alone are the creator of worlds and the unconquered destroyer," |
| `Line 3383: त्वं ज्योतिः सर्वभूतानां त्वमादित्यो विभावसुः ||११||` | "You are the light of all beings, you are Aditya [sun deity], the radiant one. ||11||" |
| `Line 3384: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3385: त्वं महद्भूतमाश्चर्यं त्वं राजा त्वं सुरोत्तमः |` | "You are the great wondrous being, you are the king, you are the foremost among gods," |
| `Line 3386: त्वं विष्णुस्त्वं सहस्राक्षस्त्वं देवस्त्वं परायणम् ||१२||` | "You are Vishnu, you are Sahasraksha [thousand-eyed, Indra], you are the god, you are the supreme refuge. ||12||" |
| `Line 3387: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3389: त्वं मुहूर्तस्तिथिश्च त्वं लवस्त्वं वै पुनः क्षणः ||१३||` | "You are the muhurta [time unit], the tithi [lunar day], you are the lava [time fraction], and indeed you are the kshana [moment]. ||13||" |
| `Line 3390: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3393: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3467: पणं वितथमास्थाय सर्पैरुपधिना कृतम् ||९||` | "Due to a false wager deceitfully arranged by the serpents. ||9||" |

| `Line 3529: समुद्रकुक्षौ च विशोषयन्पयः; समीपगान्भूमिधरान्विचालयन् ||११||` | "Drying up the waters in the ocean's belly, and shaking the nearby mountains [earth-bearers]. ||11||" |
| `Line 3530: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3531: ततः स चक्रे महदाननं तदा; निषादमार्गं प्रतिरुध्य पक्षिराट् |` | "Then the king of birds [Garuḍa] made a huge mouth, blocking the path of the Niṣādas," |
| `Line 3532: ततो निषादास्त्वरिताः प्रवव्रजु; र्यतो मुखं तस्य भुजङ्गभोजिनः ||१२||` | "Then the Niṣādas hurriedly rushed toward the mouth of that serpent-eater. ||12||" |
| `Line 3533: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3535: सहस्रशः पवनरजोभ्रमोहिता; महानिलप्रचलितपादपे वने ||१३||` | "By thousands, confused by the wind-blown dust, in a forest where trees swayed in the great wind. ||13||" |
| `Line 3536: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3538: निषूदयन्बहुविधमत्स्यभक्षिणो; बुभुक्षितो गगनचरेश्वरस्तदा ||१४||` | "Closed his mouth, destroying the many fish-eating ones, that hungry lord of sky-travelers [birds] then. ||14||" |

| `Line 3548: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 3549: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3550: तस्य कण्ठमनुप्राप्तो ब्राह्मणः सह भार्यया |` | "A Brāhmaṇa [priest] along with his wife reached his throat," |
| `Line 3551: दहन्दीप्त इवाङ्गारस्तमुवाचान्तरिक्षगः ||१||` | "Burning brightly like a coal, the sky-traveler [Garuda] spoke to him. ||1||" |
| `Line 3552: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3553: द्विजोत्तम विनिर्गच्छ तूर्णमास्यादपावृतात् |` | "O best of the twice-born [Brahmin], quickly come out from this opened mouth." |
| `Line 3554: न हि मे ब्राह्मणो वध्यः पापेष्वपि रतः सदा ||२||` | "For a Brahmin is not to be killed by me, even if he is always engaged in sins. ||2||" |
| `Line 3555: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3556: ब्रुवाणमेवं गरुडं ब्राह्मणः समभाषत |` | "To Garuda speaking thus, the Brahmin replied:" |
| `Line 3557: निषादी मम भार्येयं निर्गच्छतु मया सह ||३||` | "This Nishadi [tribal woman] is my wife; let her come out with me. ||3||" |
| `Line 3558: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3560: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3562: तूर्णं सम्भावयात्मानमजीर्णं मम तेजसा ||४||` | "Quickly save yourself, undigested by my fiery energy. ||4||" |
| `Line 3563: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3567: वर्धयित्वा च गरुडमिष्टं देशं जगाम ह ||५||` | "And after blessing Garuda, he went to his desired place. ||5||" |
| `Line 3568: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3570: वितत्य पक्षावाकाशमुत्पपात मनोजवः ||६||` | "Spread his wings in the sky and flew up with the speed of mind. ||6||" |
| `Line 3571: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3573: अहं हि सर्पैः प्रहितः सोममाहर्तुमुद्यतः ||७||` | "I have been sent by the serpents and am prepared to bring the Soma [divine elixir]. ||7||" |
| `Line 3574: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3576: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3578: न च मे तृप्तिरभवद्भक्षयित्वा सहस्रशः ||८||` | "But I did not feel satisfaction even after devouring thousands. ||8||" |

| `Line 3583: कश्यप उवाच||` | "Kaśyapa said:" |
| `Line 3584: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3585: आसीद्विभावसुर्नाम महर्षिः कोपनो भृशम् |` | "There was a great sage named Vibhāvasu who was extremely irascible," |
| `Line 3586: भ्राता तस्यानुजश्चासीत्सुप्रतीको महातपाः ||१०||` | "And he had a younger brother named Supratīka, of great austerity. ||10||" |
| `Line 3587: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3588: स नेच्छति धनं भ्रात्रा सहैकस्थं महामुनिः |` | "That great sage did not wish to keep wealth together with his brother," |
| `Line 3589: विभागं कीर्तयत्येव सुप्रतीकोऽथ नित्यशः ||११||` | "And Supratīka constantly spoke about division (of property). ||11||" |
| `Line 3590: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3591: अथाब्रवीच्च तं भ्राता सुप्रतीकं विभावसुः |` | "Then his brother Vibhāvasu said to Supratīka," |
| `Line 3592: विभागं बहवो मोहात्कर्तुमिच्छन्ति नित्यदा ||१२||` | "Many people, out of delusion, always desire to make divisions. ||12||" |
| `Line 3593: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3594: ततो विभक्ता अन्योन्यं नाद्रियन्तेऽर्थमोहिताः ||१२||` | "Then, once divided, they do not respect each other, deluded by wealth. ||12||" |
| `Line 3595: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3596: ततः स्वार्थपरान्मूढान्पृथग्भूतान्स्वकैर्धनैः |` | "Then, knowing them to be foolish, self-interested, and separated with their own wealth," |
| `Line 3597: विदित्वा भेदयन्त्येतानमित्रा मित्ररूपिणः ||१३||` | "Enemies in the guise of friends divide them further. ||13||" |
| `Line 3598: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3599: विदित्वा चापरे भिन्नानन्तरेषु पतन्त्यथ |` | "And others, knowing them to be divided, attack them at the first opportunity," |
| `Line 3600: भिन्नानामतुलो नाशः क्षिप्रमेव प्रवर्तते ||१४||` | "For those who are divided, unparalleled destruction quickly follows. ||14||" |
| `Line 3601: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3602: तस्माच्चैव विभागार्थं न प्रशंसन्ति पण्डिताः |` | "Therefore, the learned ones do not praise division [separation] for the sake of wealth," |
| `Line 3603: गुरुशास्त्रे निबद्धानामन्योन्यमभिशङ्किनाम् ||१५||` | "Among those bound by the teacher's instructions who are suspicious of one another. ||15||" |
| `Line 3604: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3605: नियन्तुं न हि शक्यस्त्वं भेदतो धनमिच्छसि |` | "You cannot be restrained, you desire wealth through division," |
| `Line 3606: यस्मात्तस्मात्सुप्रतीक हस्तित्वं समवाप्स्यसि ||१६||` | "Therefore, O Supratīka, you shall attain the state of an elephant. ||16||" |
| `Line 3607: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3608: शप्तस्त्वेवं सुप्रतीको विभावसुमथाब्रवीत् |` | "Being thus cursed, Supratīka then said to Vibhāvasu [fire deity]," |
| `Line 3609: त्वमप्यन्तर्जलचरः कच्छपः सम्भविष्यसि ||१७||` | "You too shall become a turtle dwelling in water. ||17||" |
| `Line 3610: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3611: एवमन्योन्यशापात्तौ सुप्रतीकविभावसू |` | "Thus due to mutual curses, Supratīka and Vibhāvasu," |
| `Line 3612: गजकच्छपतां प्राप्तावर्थार्थं मूढचेतसौ ||१८||` | "Attained the states of elephant and turtle, deluded in mind for the sake of wealth. ||18||" |
| `Line 3613: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3615: परस्परद्वेषरतौ प्रमाणबलदर्पितौ ||१९||` | "They remained engaged in mutual hatred, proud of their immense strength. ||19||" |
| `Line 3616: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3619: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3621: उत्थितोऽसौ महाकायः कृत्स्नं सङ्क्षोभयन्सरः ||२१||` | "That huge-bodied one rose up, agitating the entire lake. ||21||" |

| `Line 3689: तेजोवीर्यबलोपेतं मनोमारुतरंहसम् ||६||` | "Endowed with splendor, prowess and strength, swift as mind and wind. ||6||" |
| `Line 3690: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3691: शैलशृङ्गप्रतीकाशं ब्रह्मदण्डमिवोद्यतम् |` | "Resembling a mountain peak, like the raised staff of Brahma [creator deity]," |
| `Line 3692: अचिन्त्यमनभिज्ञेयं सर्वभूतभयङ्करम् ||७||` | "Inconceivable, unknowable, terrifying to all beings. ||7||" |
| `Line 3693: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3694: मायावीर्यधरं साक्षादग्निमिद्धमिवोद्यतम् |` | "Possessing magical powers, like a blazing fire risen up," |
| `Line 3695: अप्रधृष्यमजेयं च देवदानवराक्षसैः ||८||` | "Unapproachable and unconquerable by gods, dānavas [demons], and rākṣasas [ogres]. ||8||" |
| `Line 3696: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3697: भेत्तारं गिरिशृङ्गाणां नदीजलविशोषणम् |` | "Breaker of mountain peaks, dryer of river waters," |
| `Line 3698: लोकसंलोडनं घोरं कृतान्तसमदर्शनम् ||९||` | "Terribly agitating the worlds, appearing like Death [Kṛtānta] himself. ||9||" |
| `Line 3699: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3700: तमागतमभिप्रेक्ष्य भगवान्कश्यपस्तदा |` | "Seeing him arrived, the venerable Kaśyapa then," |
| `Line 3701: विदित्वा चास्य सङ्कल्पमिदं वचनमब्रवीत् ||१०||` | "Having understood his intention, (Kaśyapa) spoke these words. ||10||" |
| `Line 3702: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3703: पुत्र मा साहसं कार्षीर्मा सद्यो लप्स्यसे व्यथाम् |` | "Son, do not act rashly, lest you immediately experience pain," |
| `Line 3704: मा त्वा दहेयुः सङ्क्रुद्धा वालखिल्या मरीचिपाः ||११||` | "Let not the angry Vālakhilyas [thumb-sized sages], the descendants of Marīci, burn you. ||11||" |
| `Line 3705: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3706: प्रसादयामास स तान्कश्यपः पुत्रकारणात् |` | "Kaśyapa then appeased them for the sake of his son," |
| `Line 3707: वालखिल्यांस्तपःसिद्धानिदमुद्दिश्य कारणम् ||१२||` | "The Vālakhilyas, perfected through austerities, addressing this reason. ||12||" |
| `Line 3708: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3709: प्रजाहितार्थमारम्भो गरुडस्य तपोधनाः |` | "O wealth of austerities [ascetics], Garuḍa's endeavor is for the welfare of beings," |
| `Line 3710: चिकीर्षति महत्कर्म तदनुज्ञातुमर्हथ ||१३||` | "He wishes to perform a great deed, please grant him permission for that. ||13||" |
| `Line 3711: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3712: एवमुक्ता भगवता मुनयस्ते समभ्ययुः |` | "Thus addressed by the venerable one, those sages departed," |
| `Line 3713: मुक्त्वा शाखां गिरिं पुण्यं हिमवन्तं तपोर्थिनः ||१४||` | "Leaving the branch, they went to the sacred mountain Himavat [Himalayas], seeking austerities. ||14||" |
| `Line 3714: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3715: ततस्तेष्वपयातेषु पितरं विनतात्मजः |` | "Then, after they had departed, the son of Vinatā [Garuḍa]," |
| `Line 3716: शाखाव्याक्षिप्तवदनः पर्यपृच्छत कश्यपम् ||१५||` | "With his mouth still holding the branch, asked Kaśyapa. ||15||" |
| `Line 3717: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3718: भगवन्क्व विमुञ्चामि तरुशाखामिमामहम् |` | "Venerable one, where should I release this tree branch?" |
| `Line 3719: वर्जितं ब्राह्मणैर्देशमाख्यातु भगवान्मम ||१६||` | "Let the venerable one tell me of a place uninhabited by Brahmins. ||16||" |
| `Line 3720: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3721: ततो निष्पुरुषं शैलं हिमसंरुद्धकन्दरम् |` | "Then, of a mountain uninhabited by humans, with its caverns blocked by snow," |
| `Line 3722: अगम्यं मनसाप्यन्यैस्तस्याचख्यौ स कश्यपः ||१७||` | "Inaccessible even in thought to others, Kaśyapa told him. ||17||" |
| `Line 3723: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3724: तं पर्वतमहाकुक्षिमाविश्य मनसा खगः |` | "Entering mentally into the great hollow of that mountain, the bird [Garuḍa]," |
| `Line 3725: जवेनाभ्यपतत्तार्क्ष्यः सशाखागजकच्छपः ||१८||` | "Tārkṣya [Garuḍa] swiftly flew there with the branch, elephant, and tortoise. ||18||" |
| `Line 3726: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3727: न तां वध्रः परिणहेच्छतचर्मा महानणुः |` | "The great minute one [Garuḍa], with skin like a hundred shields, could not encircle that vast branch," |
| `Line 3728: शाखिनो महतीं शाखां यां प्रगृह्य ययौ खगः ||१९||` | "The mighty branch of the tree which the bird [Garuḍa] had seized and carried away. ||19||" |
| `Line 3729: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3730: ततः स शतसाहस्रं योजनान्तरमागतः |` | "Then he, having traveled a distance of one hundred thousand yojanas [distance measure]," |
| `Line 3731: कालेन नातिमहता गरुडः पततां वरः ||२०||` | "In a time not too long, Garuḍa, the best among those who fly. ||20||" |
| `Line 3732: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3733: स तं गत्वा क्षणेनैव पर्वतं वचनात्पितुः |` | "Having reached that mountain in an instant, as per his father's instruction," |
| `Line 3734: अमुञ्चन्महतीं शाखां सस्वनां तत्र खेचरः ||२१||` | "The sky-traveler [Garuḍa] released that great branch there with a loud noise. ||21||" |
| `Line 3735: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3736: पक्षानिलहतश्चास्य प्राकम्पत स शैलराट् |` | "Struck by the wind from his wings, that king of mountains trembled," |
| `Line 3737: मुमोच पुष्पवर्षं च समागलितपादपः ||२२||` | "And with trees sliding down, it released a shower of flowers. ||22||" |
| `Line 3738: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3739: शृङ्गाणि च व्यशीर्यन्त गिरेस्तस्य समन्ततः |` | "And the peaks of that mountain shattered all around," |
| `Line 3740: मणिकाञ्चनचित्राणि शोभयन्ति महागिरिम् ||२३||` | "Adorned with jewels and gold, they beautified the great mountain. ||23||" |
| `Line 3741: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3742: शाखिनो बहवश्चापि शाखयाभिहतास्तया |` | "And many trees, struck by that branch," |
| `Line 3743: काञ्चनैः कुसुमैर्भान्ति विद्युत्वन्त इवाम्बुदाः ||२४||` | "Shone with golden flowers like lightning-filled clouds. ||24||" |
| `Line 3744: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3745: ते हेमविकचा भूयो युक्ताः पर्वतधातुभिः |` | "Those trees, with golden blossoms, combined with the mountain minerals," |
| `Line 3746: व्यराजञ्शाखिनस्तत्र सूर्यांशुप्रतिरञ्जिताः ||२५||` | "Shone there, colored by the rays of the sun. ||25||" |
| `Line 3747: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3748: ततस्तस्य गिरेः शृङ्गमास्थाय स खगोत्तमः |` | "Then, perching on the peak of that mountain, that best of birds [Garuḍa]," |
| `Line 3749: भक्षयामास गरुडस्तावुभौ गजकच्छपौ ||२६||` | "Garuḍa devoured both the elephant and the tortoise. ||26||" |
| `Line 3750: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3751: ततः पर्वतकूटाग्रादुत्पपात मनोजवः |` | "Then, with the speed of thought, he flew up from the mountain peak," |
| `Line 3752: प्रावर्तन्ताथ देवानामुत्पाता भयवेदिनः ||२७||` | "And then began ominous portents for the gods, foretelling danger. ||27||" |
| `Line 3753: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3754: इन्द्रस्य वज्रं दयितं प्रजज्वाल व्यथान्वितम् |` | "Indra's [king of gods] beloved thunderbolt blazed forth in agitation," |
| `Line 3755: सधूमा चापतत्सार्चिर्दिवोल्का नभसश्च्युता ||२८||` | "And a meteor fell from the sky with smoke and flames. ||28||" |
| `Line 3756: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3757: तथा वसूनां रुद्राणामादित्यानां च सर्वशः |` | "Likewise, of the Vasus [elemental deities], Rudras [storm gods], and Adityas [solar deities] completely," |
| `Line 3758: साध्यानां मरुतां चैव ये चान्ये देवतागणाः ||२९||` | "Of the Sadhyas [celestial beings], Maruts [wind gods], and all other groups of deities, ||29||" |
| `Line 3759: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3760: स्वं स्वं प्रहरणं तेषां परस्परमुपाद्रवत् ||२९||` | "Their respective weapons rushed against each other. ||29||" |
| `Line 3761: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3762: अभूतपूर्वं सङ्ग्रामे तदा देवासुरेऽपि च |` | "Unprecedented even in the battles between gods and demons," |
| `Line 3763: ववुर्वाताः सनिर्घाताः पेतुरुल्काः समन्ततः ||३०||` | "Winds blew with thunderclaps, and meteors fell from all directions. ||30||" |
| `Line 3764: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3765: निरभ्रमपि चाकाशं प्रजगर्ज महास्वनम् |` | "Though cloudless, the sky thundered with a great sound," |
| `Line 3766: देवानामपि यो देवः सोऽप्यवर्षदसृक्तदा ||३१||` | "And he who is the god of gods [Parjanya/rain deity] rained blood then. ||31||" |
| `Line 3767: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3768: मम्लुर्माल्यानि देवानां शेमुस्तेजांसि चैव हि |` | "The garlands of the gods withered, and their splendors dimmed," |
| `Line 3769: उत्पातमेघा रौद्राश्च ववर्षुः शोणितं बहु ||३२||` | "And portentous, terrible clouds rained much blood. ||32||" |
| `Line 3770: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3771: रजांसि मुकुटान्येषामुत्थितानि व्यधर्षयन् ||३२||` | "Rising dust defiled their crowns. ||32||" |
| `Line 3772: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3773: ततस्त्राससमुद्विग्नः सह देवैः शतक्रतुः |` | "Then, agitated with fear, Shatakratu [Indra, performer of hundred sacrifices] along with the gods," |
| `Line 3774: उत्पातान्दारुणान्पश्यन्नित्युवाच बृहस्पतिम् ||३३||` | "Seeing these terrible portents, spoke thus to Brihaspati [preceptor of gods]. ||33||" |
| `Line 3775: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3776: किमर्थं भगवन्घोरा महोत्पाताः समुत्थिताः |` | "For what reason, O lord, have these terrible great calamities arisen?" |
| `Line 3777: न च शत्रुं प्रपश्यामि युधि यो नः प्रधर्षयेत् ॥३४॥` | "And I do not see any enemy who could overpower us in battle. ||34||" |
| `Line 3778: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3779: बृहस्पतिरुवाच॥` | "Bṛhaspati [preceptor of gods] said:" |
| `Line 3780: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3781: तवापराधाद्देवेन्द्र प्रमादाच्च शतक्रतो |` | "Due to your offense, O Devendra [lord of gods], and due to your negligence, O Śatakratu [Indra]," |
| `Line 3782: तपसा वालखिल्यानां भूतमुत्पन्नमद्भुतम् ॥३५॥` | "By the austerities of the Vālakhilyas [thumb-sized sages], a wonderful being has been born. ||35||" |
| `Line 3783: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3784: कश्यपस्य मुनेः पुत्रो विनतायाश्च खेचरः |` | "A son of sage Kaśyapa and Vinatā, who travels through the sky," |
| `Line 3785: हर्तुं सोममनुप्राप्तो बलवान्कामरूपवान् ॥३६॥` | "Has arrived to steal the Soma [divine elixir], powerful and able to assume any form at will. ||36||" |
| `Line 3786: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3788: सर्वं सम्भावयाम्यस्मिन्नसाध्यमपि साधयेत् ॥३७॥` | "I believe he can accomplish everything, even that which is impossible. ||37||" |
| `Line 3789: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3790: सूत उवाच॥` | "Sūta [bard narrator] said:" |
| `Line 3791: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3792: श्रुत्वैतद्वचनं शक्रः प्रोवाचामृतरक्षिणः |` | "Hearing these words, Śakra [Indra] spoke to the guardians of the amṛta [nectar]:" |
| `Line 3793: महावीर्यबलः पक्षी हर्तुं सोममिहोद्यतः ॥३८॥` | "A bird of great power and strength is prepared to steal the Soma here. ||38||" |
| `Line 3794: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3795: युष्मान्सम्बोधयाम्येष यथा स न हरेद्बलात् |` | "I alert you all so that he may not take it away by force." |
| `Line 3796: अतुलं हि बलं तस्य बृहस्पतिरुवाच मे ॥३९॥` | "For his strength is unmatched, Bṛhaspati has told me. ||39||" |
| `Line 3797: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3799: परिवार्यामृतं तस्थुर्वज्री चेन्द्रः शतक्रतुः ॥४०॥` | "They stood surrounding the amṛta, along with the thunderbolt-wielding Indra, Śatakratu. ||40||" |
| `Line 3800: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3802: काञ्चनानि विचित्राणि वैडूर्यविकृतानि च ||४१||` | "Made of gold, variegated, and adorned with cat's eye gems [vaidūrya]. ||41||" |
| `Line 3803: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3805: शिततीक्ष्णाग्रधाराणि समुद्यम्य सहस्रशः ||४२||` | "With sharp, pointed edges, raising them by the thousands. ||42||" |
| `Line 3806: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3808: चक्राणि परिघांश्चैव त्रिशूलानि परश्वधान् ||४३||` | "Discuses, iron clubs, tridents, and battle-axes. ||43||" |
| `Line 3809: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3810: शक्तीश्च विविधास्तीक्ष्णाः करवालांश्च निर्मलान् |` | "Various sharp spears [śakti weapons] and gleaming swords," |
| `Line 3811: स्वदेहरूपाण्यादाय गदाश्चोग्रप्रदर्शनाः ||४४||` | "Taking forms suited to their bodies, and maces of fearsome appearance. ||44||" |
| `Line 3812: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3813: तैः शस्त्रैर्भानुमद्भिस्ते दिव्याभरणभूषिताः |` | "With those radiant weapons, adorned with divine ornaments," |
| `Line 3814: भानुमन्तः सुरगणास्तस्थुर्विगतकल्मषाः ||४५||` | "The radiant hosts of gods stood, free from impurities. ||45||" |
| `Line 3815: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3816: अनुपमबलवीर्यतेजसो; धृतमनसः परिरक्षणेऽमृतस्य |` | "Of incomparable strength, valor and splendor; with minds fixed on protecting the amrita [nectar of immortality]," |
| `Line 3817: असुरपुरविदारणाः सुरा; ज्वलनसमिद्धवपुःप्रकाशिनः ||४६||` | "The gods, destroyers of demon cities; their bodies blazing like kindled fire. ||46||" |
| `Line 3818: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3819: इति समरवरं सुरास्थितं; परिघसहस्रशतैः समाकुलम् |` | "Thus the gods stood ready for excellent battle; crowded with hundreds of thousands of iron clubs," |
| `Line 3820: विगलितमिव चाम्बरान्तरे; तपनमरीचिविभासितं बभौ ||४७||` | "As if flowing in the midst of the sky; shining with the rays of the sun, they gleamed. ||47||" |

| `Line 3830: शौनक उवाच||` | "Shaunaka said:" |
| `Line 3831: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3832: कोऽपराधो महेन्द्रस्य कः प्रमादश्च सूतज |` | "What was the offense of Mahendra [great Indra], and what was his negligence, O son of Suta?" |
| `Line 3833: तपसा वालखिल्यानां सम्भूतो गरुडः कथम् ||१||` | "How was Garuda born through the austerities of the Valakhilyas [thumb-sized sages]? ||1||" |
| `Line 3834: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3835: कश्यपस्य द्विजातेश्च कथं वै पक्षिराट्सुतः |` | "And how did the king of birds become the son of Kashyapa, the lord of the twice-born [Brahmin]?" |
| `Line 3836: अधृष्यः सर्वभूतानामवध्यश्चाभवत्कथम् ||२||` | "How did he become invincible and unkillable by all beings? ||2||" |
| `Line 3837: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3838: कथं च कामचारी स कामवीर्यश्च खेचरः |` | "And how did he become one who moves at will, with strength as desired, and a sky-traveler [bird]?" |
| `Line 3839: एतदिच्छाम्यहं श्रोतुं पुराणे यदि पठ्यते ||३||` | "I wish to hear this, if it is recited in the Purana [ancient text]. ||3||" |
| `Line 3840: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3841: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta said:" |
| `Line 3842: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3843: विषयोऽयं पुराणस्य यन्मां त्वं परिपृच्छसि |` | "This subject about which you are questioning me is indeed from the Purana," |
| `Line 3844: शृणु मे वदतः सर्वमेतत्सङ्क्षेपतो द्विज ||४||` | "Listen as I tell you everything about this in brief, O twice-born [Brahmin]. ||4||" |
| `Line 3845: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3846: यजतः पुत्रकामस्य कश्यपस्य प्रजापतेः |` | "When Kashyapa, the Prajapati [lord of creatures], was performing a sacrifice desiring a son," |
| `Line 3847: साहाय्यमृषयो देवा गन्धर्वाश्च ददुः किल ||५||` | "The sages, gods, and Gandharvas [celestial musicians] indeed gave their assistance. ||5||" |
| `Line 3848: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3849: तत्रेध्मानयने शक्रो नियुक्तः कश्यपेन ह |` | "There, Shakra [Indra] was appointed by Kashyapa to bring the sacrificial firewood," |
| `Line 3850: मुनयो वालखिल्याश्च ये चान्ये देवतागणाः ||६||` | "As were the sages, the Valakhilyas [thumb-sized sages], and other groups of deities. ||6||" |
| `Line 3851: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3852: शक्रस्तु वीर्यसदृशमिध्मभारं गिरिप्रभम् |` | "Shakra [Indra], however, lifted a load of firewood befitting his strength, massive as a mountain," |
| `Line 3853: समुद्यम्यानयामास नातिकृच्छ्रादिव प्रभुः ||७||` | "The lord carried it without much difficulty, as it seemed. ||7||" |
| `Line 3854: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3855: अथापश्यदृषीन्ह्रस्वानङ्गुष्ठोदरपर्वणः |` | "Then he saw tiny sages, with bodies the size of a thumb-joint," |
| `Line 3856: पलाशवृन्तिकामेकां सहितान्वहतः पथि ||८||` | "Carrying together a single palāśa [flame tree] leaf-stalk on the path. ||8||" |
| `Line 3857: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3858: प्रलीनान्स्वेष्विवाङ्गेषु निराहारांस्तपोधनान् |` | "These ascetics, rich in austerities, were fasting and seemed almost absorbed into their own bodies," |
| `Line 3859: क्लिश्यमानान्मन्दबलान्गोष्पदे सम्प्लुतोदके ||९||` | "Struggling with little strength, in water collected in a cow's footprint. ||9||" |
| `Line 3860: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3861: तांश्च सर्वान्स्मयाविष्टो वीर्योन्मत्तः पुरंदरः |` | "And Purandara [Indra], filled with pride and intoxicated with his own strength," |
| `Line 3862: अवहस्यात्यगाच्छीघ्रं लङ्घयित्वावमन्य च ||१०||` | "Laughed at them all, quickly passed by, leaping over them with contempt. ||10||" |
| `Line 3863: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3864: तेऽथ रोषसमाविष्टाः सुभृशं जातमन्यवः |` | "Then they, filled with intense anger, greatly enraged," |
| `Line 3865: आरेभिरे महत्कर्म तदा शक्रभयङ्करम् ||११||` | "Began a great ritual then, terrifying to Shakra [Indra]. ||11||" |
| `Line 3866: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3867: जुहुवुस्ते सुतपसो विधिवज्जातवेदसम् |` | "Those great ascetics offered oblations according to ritual into Jātavedas [fire deity]," |

| `Line 3869: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3870: कामवीर्यः कामगमो देवराजभयप्रदः |` | "One with desired strength, moving at will, causing fear to the king of gods," |
| `Line 3871: इन्द्रोऽन्यः सर्वदेवानां भवेदिति यतव्रताः ||१३||` | "Let there be another Indra of all the gods - thus (prayed) those of controlled vows. ||13||" |
| `Line 3872: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3873: इन्द्राच्छतगुणः शौर्ये वीर्ये चैव मनोजवः |` | "A hundred times greater than Indra in valor and strength, swift as thought," |
| `Line 3874: तपसो नः फलेनाद्य दारुणः सम्भवत्विति ||१४||` | "By the fruit of our austerities, let a formidable one be born today. ||14||" |
| `Line 3875: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3876: तद्बुद्ध्वा भृशसन्तप्तो देवराजः शतक्रतुः |` | "Understanding that, the king of gods, Śatakratu [Indra, hundred sacrifices], became greatly distressed," |
| `Line 3877: जगाम शरणं तत्र कश्यपं संशितव्रतम् ||१५||` | "And went there for refuge to Kaśyapa of firm vows. ||15||" |
| `Line 3878: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3879: तच्छ्रुत्वा देवराजस्य कश्यपोऽथ प्रजापतिः |` | "Hearing that from the king of gods, Kaśyapa, the Prajāpati [lord of creatures]," |
| `Line 3880: वालखिल्यानुपागम्य कर्मसिद्धिमपृच्छत ||१६||` | "Approached the Vālakhilyas [thumb-sized sages] and asked about the success of their undertaking. ||16||" |
| `Line 3881: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3882: एवमस्त्विति तं चापि प्रत्यूचुः सत्यवादिनः |` | "And those truth-speaking ones replied to him, 'Let it be so,'" |
| `Line 3883: तान्कश्यप उवाचेदं सान्त्वपूर्वं प्रजापतिः ||१७||` | "Then Kaśyapa, the Prajāpati, spoke these conciliatory words to them: ||17||" |
| `Line 3884: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3885: अयमिन्द्रस्त्रिभुवने नियोगाद्ब्रह्मणः कृतः |` | "This Indra has been appointed in the three worlds by the command of Brahma," |
| `Line 3886: इन्द्रार्थं च भवन्तोऽपि यत्नवन्तस्तपोधनाः ||१८||` | "And you too, rich in austerities, have been striving for the position of Indra. ||18||" |
| `Line 3887: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3888: न मिथ्या ब्रह्मणो वाक्यं कर्तुमर्हथ सत्तमाः |` | "O excellent ones, you should not render Brahma's words false," |
| `Line 3889: भवतां च न मिथ्यायं सङ्कल्पो मे चिकीर्षितः ||१९||` | "Nor do I wish to make your resolution fruitless. ||19||" |
| `Line 3890: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3891: भवत्वेष पतत्रीणामिन्द्रोऽतिबलसत्त्ववान् |` | "Let this one be the Indra of winged creatures, exceedingly powerful and strong," |
| `Line 3892: प्रसादः क्रियतां चैव देवराजस्य याचतः ||२०||` | "And let grace be shown to the king of gods who is beseeching you. ||20||" |
| `Line 3893: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3894: एवमुक्ताः कश्यपेन वालखिल्यास्तपोधनाः |` | "Thus addressed by Kaśyapa, the Vālakhilyas, rich in austerities," |
| `Line 3895: प्रत्यूचुरभिसम्पूज्य मुनिश्रेष्ठं प्रजापतिम् ||२१||` | "Replied, after duly honoring the foremost of sages, the Prajāpati: ||21||" |
| `Line 3896: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3897: इन्द्रार्थोऽयं समारम्भः सर्वेषां नः प्रजापते |` | "O Prajāpati, this undertaking of all of us was for the purpose of creating an Indra," |
| `Line 3898: अपत्यार्थं समारम्भो भवतश्चायमीप्सितः ||२२||` | "And this undertaking of yours is desired for the purpose of offspring. ||22||" |
| `Line 3899: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3900: तदिदं सफलं कर्म त्वया वै प्रतिगृह्यताम् |` | "Therefore, let this fruitful work be accepted by you." |
| `Line 3901: तथा चैव विधत्स्वात्र यथा श्रेयोऽनुपश्यसि ||२३||` | "And arrange here as you see what is best. ||23||" |
| `Line 3902: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3903: एतस्मिन्नेव काले तु देवी दाक्षायणी शुभा |` | "At this very time, the auspicious goddess Dākṣāyaṇī [daughter of Daksha]," |
| `Line 3904: विनता नाम कल्याणी पुत्रकामा यशस्विनी ||२४||` | "Named Vinatā, the virtuous and glorious one, desiring sons. ||24||" |
| `Line 3905: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3906: तपस्तप्त्वा व्रतपरा स्नाता पुंसवने शुचिः |` | "Having performed austerities, devoted to vows, bathed in the puṃsavana [male-child ceremony], purified," |
| `Line 3907: उपचक्राम भर्तारं तामुवाचाथ कश्यपः ||२५||` | "She approached her husband, and then Kaśyapa said to her. ||25||" |
| `Line 3908: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3909: आरम्भः सफलो देवि भवितायं तवेप्सितः |` | "This endeavor of yours, O goddess, will be fruitful as desired," |
| `Line 3910: जनयिष्यसि पुत्रौ द्वौ वीरौ त्रिभुवनेश्वरौ ||२६||` | "You will give birth to two heroic sons who will be lords of the three worlds. ||26||" |
| `Line 3911: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3913: भविष्यतो महाभागौ पुत्रौ ते लोकपूजितौ ||२७||` | "Your two sons will be greatly fortunate and worshipped by the worlds. ||27||" |
| `Line 3914: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3916: धार्यतामप्रमादेन गर्भोऽयं सुमहोदयः ||२८||` | "Bear this womb without negligence, for it will bring great prosperity. ||28||" |
| `Line 3917: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3918: एकः सर्वपतत्रीणामिन्द्रत्वं कारयिष्यति |` | "One will attain the position of Indra among all winged creatures," |
| `Line 3919: लोकसम्भावितो वीरः कामवीर्यो विहङ्गमः ||२९||` | "A hero respected by the worlds, a bird with strength according to his desire. ||29||" |
| `Line 3920: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3921: शतक्रतुमथोवाच प्रीयमाणः प्रजापतिः |` | "Then the pleased Prajāpati [creator deity] said to Śatakratu [Indra]," |
| `Line 3922: त्वत्सहायौ खगावेतौ भ्रातरौ ते भविष्यतः ||३०||` | "These two bird brothers will be your helpers. ||30||" |
| `Line 3923: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3924: नैताभ्यां भविता दोषः सकाशात्ते पुरंदर |` | "No harm will come to you from them, O Purandara [city-destroyer, Indra]," |
| `Line 3925: व्येतु ते शक्र सन्तापस्त्वमेवेन्द्रो भविष्यसि ||३१||` | "Let your anxiety depart, O Śakra [mighty one], you alone will remain Indra. ||31||" |
| `Line 3926: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3927: न चाप्येवं त्वया भूयः क्षेप्तव्या ब्रह्मवादिनः |` | "And you should not again insult the expounders of Brahman [Vedic scholars] in this manner," |
| `Line 3928: न चावमान्या दर्पात्ते वाग्विषा भृशकोपनाः ||३२||` | "Nor should you, out of pride, disrespect those who are verbally venomous and easily angered. ||32||" |
| `Line 3929: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3930: एवमुक्तो जगामेन्द्रो निर्विशङ्कस्त्रिविष्टपम् |` | "Thus addressed, Indra [king of gods] went without fear to Triviṣṭapa [heaven]," |
| `Line 3931: विनता चापि सिद्धार्था बभूव मुदिता तदा ||३३||` | "And Vinatā too, having accomplished her purpose, became joyful then. ||33||" |
| `Line 3932: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3933: जनयामास पुत्रौ द्वावरुणं गरुडं तथा |` | "She gave birth to two sons, Aruṇa and Garuḍa," |
| `Line 3934: अरुणस्तयोस्तु विकल आदित्यस्य पुरःसरः ||३४||` | "Of those two, Aruṇa was crippled and became the charioteer [forerunner] of Āditya [sun god]. ||34||" |
| `Line 3935: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 3937: तस्यैतत्कर्म सुमहच्छ्रूयतां भृगुनन्दन ||३५||` | "Listen to his great deed, O descendant of Bhṛgu [sage lineage]. ||35||" |

| `Line 3947: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
