| `Line 3949: ततस्तस्मिन्द्विजश्रेष्ठ समुदीर्णे तथाविधे |` | "Then, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin], when that mighty one arose," |
| `Line 3950: गरुत्मान्पक्षिराट्तूर्णं सम्प्राप्तो विबुधान्प्रति ||१||` | "Garutmān [Garuḍa], the king of birds, swiftly approached the gods. ||1||" |
| `Line 3951: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3952: तं दृष्ट्वातिबलं चैव प्राकम्पन्त समन्ततः |` | "Seeing him of extraordinary strength, they trembled all around," |
| `Line 3953: परस्परं च प्रत्यघ्नन्सर्वप्रहरणान्यपि ||२||` | "And all their weapons struck against each other. ||2||" |
| `Line 3954: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3955: तत्र चासीदमेयात्मा विद्युदग्निसमप्रभः |` | "There was one of immeasurable soul, with radiance like lightning and fire," |
| `Line 3956: भौवनः सुमहावीर्यः सोमस्य परिरक्षिता ||३||` | "Bhauvana [Earth-born], of great valor, the protector of Soma [moon deity]. ||3||" |
| `Line 3957: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3958: स तेन पतगेन्द्रेण पक्षतुण्डनखैः क्षतः |` | "He, wounded by that lord of birds [Garuda] with wings, beak, and talons," |
| `Line 3959: मुहूर्तमतुलं युद्धं कृत्वा विनिहतो युधि ||४||` | "After fighting an incomparable battle for a moment, was slain in combat. ||4||" |
| `Line 3960: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3961: रजश्चोद्धूय सुमहत्पक्षवातेन खेचरः |` | "And raising a great dust with the wind of his wings, the sky-traveler [Garuda]," |
| `Line 3962: कृत्वा लोकान्निरालोकांस्तेन देवानवाकिरत् ||५||` | "Making the worlds lightless, showered the gods with it. ||5||" |
| `Line 3963: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3964: तेनावकीर्णा रजसा देवा मोहमुपागमन् |` | "Covered with that dust, the gods became confused," |
| `Line 3965: न चैनं ददृशुश्छन्ना रजसामृतरक्षिणः ||६||` | "And the guardians of ambrosia [gods], being covered with dust, could not see him. ||6||" |
| `Line 3966: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3967: एवं संलोडयामास गरुडस्त्रिदिवालयम् |` | "Thus Garuda [divine eagle] agitated the abode of the three heavens [celestial realm]," |
| `Line 3968: पक्षतुण्डप्रहारैश्च देवान्स विददार ह ||७||` | "And with blows of his wings and beak, he tore the gods asunder. ||7||" |
| `Line 3969: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3970: ततो देवः सहस्राक्षस्तूर्णं वायुमचोदयत् |` | "Then the thousand-eyed god [Indra] quickly urged the wind," |
| `Line 3971: विक्षिपेमां रजोवृष्टिं तवैतत्कर्म मारुत ||८||` | "'Disperse this shower of dust; this is your task, O Wind [Maruta].' ||8||" |
| `Line 3972: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3973: अथ वायुरपोवाह तद्रजस्तरसा बली |` | "Then the mighty Wind swiftly carried away that dust," |
| `Line 3974: ततो वितिमिरे जाते देवाः शकुनिमार्दयन् ||९||` | "When the darkness was gone, the gods attacked the bird [Garuda]. ||9||" |
| `Line 3975: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3976: ननाद चोच्चैर्बलवान्महामेघरवः खगः |` | "The mighty bird [Garuda], with a sound like great thunder clouds, roared loudly," |
| `Line 3977: वध्यमानः सुरगणैः सर्वभूतानि भीषयन् ||१०||` | "While being attacked by hosts of gods, terrifying all beings. ||10||" |
| `Line 3978: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3979: उत्पपात महावीर्यः पक्षिराट्परवीरहा ||१०||` | "The king of birds [Garuda], of great prowess, slayer of enemy heroes, soared upward. ||10||" |
| `Line 3980: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3981: तमुत्पत्यान्तरिक्षस्थं देवानामुपरि स्थितम् |` | "As he flew up and positioned himself in the sky above the gods," |
| `Line 3982: वर्मिणो विबुधाः सर्वे नानाशस्त्रैरवाकिरन् ||११||` | "All the armored gods showered him with various weapons. ||11||" |
| `Line 3983: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3984: पट्टिशैः परिघैः शूलैर्गदाभिश्च सवासवाः |` | "With spears, iron clubs, tridents, and maces, the gods including Vāsava [Indra]," |
| `Line 3985: क्षुरान्तैर्ज्वलितैश्चापि चक्रैरादित्यरूपिभिः ||१२||` | "With razor-edged weapons, blazing discs shining like the sun. ||12||" |
| `Line 3986: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3987: नानाशस्त्रविसर्गैश्च वध्यमानः समन्ततः |` | "Though attacked from all sides with various weapons," |
| `Line 3988: कुर्वन्सुतुमुलं युद्धं पक्षिराण्न व्यकम्पत ||१३||` | "The king of birds, waging a fierce battle, did not waver. ||13||" |
| `Line 3989: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3990: विनर्दन्निव चाकाशे वैनतेयः प्रतापवान् |` | "Roaring in the sky, the mighty son of Vinatā [Garuda]," |
| `Line 3991: पक्षाभ्यामुरसा चैव समन्ताद्व्याक्षिपत्सुरान् ||१४||` | "Scattered the gods in all directions with his wings and chest. ||14||" |
| `Line 3992: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3993: ते विक्षिप्तास्ततो देवाः प्रजग्मुर्गरुडार्दिताः |` | "Those gods, thus scattered and tormented by Garuda, fled," |
| `Line 3994: नखतुण्डक्षताश्चैव सुस्रुवुः शोणितं बहु ||१५||` | "Wounded by his claws and beak, they bled profusely. ||15||" |
| `Line 3995: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3996: साध्याः प्राचीं सगन्धर्वा वसवो दक्षिणां दिशम् |` | "The Sādhyas [divine beings] with the Gandharvas fled to the east, the Vasus to the south," |
| `Line 3997: प्रजग्मुः सहिता रुद्रैः पतगेन्द्रप्रधर्षिताः ||१६||` | "They fled together with the Rudras, all harassed by the lord of birds. ||16||" |
| `Line 3998: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 3999: दिशं प्रतीचीमादित्या नासत्या उत्तरां दिशम् |` | "The Ādityas fled to the west, the Nāsatyas [Ashvins] to the north," |
| `Line 4000: मुहुर्मुहुः प्रेक्षमाणा युध्यमाना महौजसम् ||१७||` | "Repeatedly looking back while fighting the mighty one [Garuda]. ||17||" |
| `Line 4001: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4002: अश्वक्रन्देन वीरेण रेणुकेन च पक्षिणा |` | "With the heroic Ashvakranda, the bird Renuka," |
| `Line 4003: क्रथनेन च शूरेण तपनेन च खेचरः ||१८||` | "And with the valiant Krathana, and the sky-traveler [bird] Tapana. ||18||" |
| `Line 4004: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4005: उलूकश्वसनाभ्यां च निमेषेण च पक्षिणा |` | "And with Uluka and Shvasana, and with the bird Nimesha," |
| `Line 4006: प्ररुजेन च संयुद्धं चकार प्रलिहेन च ||१९||` | "He fought with Praruja and with Praliha as well. ||19||" |
| `Line 4007: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4008: तान्पक्षनखतुण्डाग्रैरभिनद्विनतासुतः |` | "The son of Vinata [Garuda] pierced them with the tips of his wings, claws, and beak," |
| `Line 4009: युगान्तकाले सङ्क्रुद्धः पिनाकीव महाबलः ||२०||` | "Like the mighty Pinaki [Shiva] enraged at the time of cosmic dissolution. ||20||" |
| `Line 4010: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4011: महावीर्या महोत्साहास्तेन ते बहुधा क्षताः |` | "Those of great valor and great enthusiasm were wounded by him in many ways," |
| `Line 4012: रेजुरभ्रघनप्रख्या रुधिरौघप्रवर्षिणः ||२१||` | "They shone like dense clouds, showering streams of blood. ||21||" |
| `Line 4013: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4014: तान्कृत्वा पतगश्रेष्ठः सर्वानुत्क्रान्तजीवितान् |` | "Having deprived all of them of their lives, the foremost of birds [Garuda]," |
| `Line 4015: अतिक्रान्तोऽमृतस्यार्थे सर्वतोऽग्निमपश्यत ||२२||` | "Advancing for the sake of amrita [nectar], saw fire on all sides. ||22||" |
| `Line 4016: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4017: आवृण्वानं महाज्वालमर्चिर्भिः सर्वतोऽम्बरम् |` | "Covering the sky on all sides with great flames and rays," |
| `Line 4018: दहन्तमिव तीक्ष्णांशुं घोरं वायुसमीरितम् ||२३||` | "Like the scorching fierce sun, stirred by the wind. ||23||" |
| `Line 4019: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4020: ततो नवत्या नवतीर्मुखानां; कृत्वा तरस्वी गरुडो महात्मा |` | "Then the mighty, great-souled Garuda, creating ninety times ninety mouths," |
| `Line 4021: नदीः समापीय मुखैस्ततस्तैः; सुशीघ्रमागम्य पुनर्जवेन ||२४||` | "Drank up rivers with those mouths, and then returned swiftly with speed. ||24||" |
| `Line 4022: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4023: ज्वलन्तमग्निं तममित्रतापनः; समास्तरत्पत्ररथो नदीभिः |` | "The tormentor of enemies [Garuda], whose chariot is his wings, extinguished the blazing fire with those rivers," |
| `Line 4024: ततः प्रचक्रे वपुरन्यदल्पं; प्रवेष्टुकामोऽग्निमभिप्रशाम्य ||२५||` | "Then, having quenched the fire, he made his body small, desiring to enter. ||25||" |

| `Line 4034: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 4035: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4036: जाम्बूनदमयो भूत्वा मरीचिविकचोज्ज्वलः |` | "Having become golden [jāmbūnada-gold], radiant with scattered light rays," |
| `Line 4037: प्रविवेश बलात्पक्षी वारिवेग इवार्णवम् ||१||` | "The bird forcefully entered, like a water-current entering the ocean. ||1||" |
| `Line 4038: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4039: स चक्रं क्षुरपर्यन्तमपश्यदमृतान्तिके |` | "He saw a wheel with razor-sharp edges near the amṛta [immortality nectar]," |
| `Line 4040: परिभ्रमन्तमनिशं तीक्ष्णधारमयस्मयम् ||२||` | "Revolving continuously, with sharp iron blades. ||2||" |
| `Line 4041: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4042: ज्वलनार्कप्रभं घोरं छेदनं सोमहारिणाम् |` | "Terrible, with the brilliance of fire and sun, a cutter of Soma [nectar] thieves," |
| `Line 4043: घोररूपं तदत्यर्थं यन्त्रं देवैः सुनिर्मितम् ||३||` | "That exceedingly fearsome device well-constructed by the gods. ||3||" |
| `Line 4044: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4045: तस्यान्तरं स दृष्ट्वैव पर्यवर्तत खेचरः |` | "Having seen the space between (the blades), the sky-traveler [bird] circled around," |
| `Line 4046: अरान्तरेणाभ्यपतत्सङ्क्षिप्याङ्गं क्षणेन ह ||४||` | "And darted between the spokes, contracting his body in an instant. ||4||" |
| `Line 4047: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4048: अधश्चक्रस्य चैवात्र दीप्तानलसमद्युती |` | "And below the wheel, with radiance equal to blazing fire," |
| `Line 4049: विद्युज्जिह्वौ महाघोरौ दीप्तास्यौ दीप्तलोचनौ ||५||` | "With lightning-like tongues, extremely terrifying, with blazing mouths and blazing eyes. ||5||" |
| `Line 4050: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4051: चक्षुर्विषौ महावीर्यौ नित्यक्रुद्धौ तरस्विनौ |` | "Two serpents with poison in their eyes, of great power, ever-angry, and energetic," |
| `Line 4052: रक्षार्थमेवामृतस्य ददर्श भुजगोत्तमौ ||६||` | "He saw these two excellent serpents [nāgas] stationed for the protection of the amṛta [immortality nectar]. ||6||" |
| `Line 4053: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4055: तयोरेकोऽपि यं पश्येत्स तूर्णं भस्मसाद्भवेत् ||७||` | "Whomever even one of them would look upon would instantly be reduced to ashes. ||7||" |
| `Line 4056: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4058: अदृष्टरूपस्तौ चापि सर्वतः पर्यकालयत् ||८||` | "And while remaining invisible, he observed them from all sides. ||8||" |
| `Line 4059: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4060: तयोरङ्गे समाक्रम्य वैनतेयोऽन्तरिक्षगः |` | "Vainateya [Garuḍa], the sky-traveler, attacking their bodies," |
| `Line 4061: आच्छिनत्तरसा मध्ये सोममभ्यद्रवत्ततः ||९||` | "Quickly cut through between them and then rushed toward the Soma [amṛta]. ||9||" |
| `Line 4062: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4063: समुत्पाट्यामृतं तत्तु वैनतेयस्ततो बली |` | "Having seized that amṛta, the mighty Vainateya [Garuḍa]," |
| `Line 4064: उत्पपात जवेनैव यन्त्रमुन्मथ्य वीर्यवान् ||१०||` | "Flew up with great speed, having broken the mechanism [container], the powerful one. ||10||" |
| `Line 4065: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4066: अपीत्वैवामृतं पक्षी परिगृह्याशु वीर्यवान् |` | "Without drinking the amṛta, the powerful bird quickly took it," |
| `Line 4067: अगच्छदपरिश्रान्त आवार्यार्कप्रभां खगः ||११||` | "The bird went, untired, with a radiance rivaling the sun. ||11||" |
| `Line 4068: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4069: विष्णुना तु तदाकाशे वैनतेयः समेयिवान् |` | "Then in the sky, Vainateya [Garuḍa] encountered Viṣṇu [preserver deity]," |
| `Line 4070: तस्य नारायणस्तुष्टस्तेनालौल्येन कर्मणा ||१२||` | "Nārāyaṇa [Viṣṇu] was pleased with him for that steadfast deed. ||12||" |
| `Line 4071: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4073: स वव्रे तव तिष्ठेयमुपरीत्यन्तरिक्षगः ||१३||` | "He chose: 'May I remain above you,' said the sky-traveler. ||13||" |
| `Line 4074: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4076: अजरश्चामरश्च स्याममृतेन विनाप्यहम् ||१४||` | "May I be ageless and immortal even without amṛta [nectar of immortality]. ||14||" |
| `Line 4077: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4079: भवतेऽपि वरं दद्मि वृणीतां भगवानपि ||१५||` | "I also give a boon to you; may the Lord also choose one. ||15||" |
| `Line 4080: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4083: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4085: विहङ्गमं सुरामित्रं हरन्तममृतं बलात् ||१७||` | "The bird who was an enemy of the gods, forcibly carrying away the amṛta [nectar]. ||17||" |
| `Line 4086: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4088: प्रहसञ्श्लक्ष्णया वाचा तथा वज्रसमाहतः ||१८||` | "Laughing, with smooth speech, though struck by the vajra [thunderbolt]: ||18||" |
| `Line 4089: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4090: ऋषेर्मानं करिष्यामि वज्रं यस्यास्थिसम्भवम् |` | "I will honor the sage whose bone became the vajra [thunderbolt]," |
| `Line 4091: वज्रस्य च करिष्यामि तव चैव शतक्रतो ||१९||` | "And I will honor the vajra [thunderbolt] and you too, O Śatakratu [Indra]. ||19||" |
| `Line 4092: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4094: न हि वज्रनिपातेन रुजा मेऽस्ति कदाचन ||२०||` | "For the strike of your vajra [thunderbolt] has caused me no pain whatsoever. ||20||" |
| `Line 4095: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4120: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4126: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4128: वहेयमपरिश्रान्तो विद्धीदं मे महद्बलम् ||५||` | "I could carry without fatigue - know this to be my great strength. ||5||" |
| `Line 4129: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4133: आह शौनक देवेन्द्रः सर्वभूतहितः प्रभुः ||६||` | "Spoke, O Śaunaka, the lord of gods [Indra], the master who is beneficial to all beings. ||6||" |
| `Line 4134: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4135: प्रतिगृह्यतामिदानीं मे सख्यमानन्त्यमुत्तमम् |` | "Accept now my eternal and supreme friendship," |
| `Line 4136: न कार्यं तव सोमेन मम सोमः प्रदीयताम् ||७||` | "You have no need for Soma [moon/elixir], (but) let the Soma be given to me. ||7||" |
| `Line 4137: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4138: अस्मांस्ते हि प्रबाधेयुर्येभ्यो दद्याद्भवानिमम् ||७||` | "Those to whom you would give this would indeed trouble us. ||7||" |
| `Line 4139: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4140: गरुड उवाच||` | "Garuḍa [divine eagle] said:" |
| `Line 4141: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4142: किञ्चित्कारणमुद्दिश्य सोमोऽयं नीयते मया |` | "For a certain purpose this Soma is being carried by me," |
| `Line 4143: न दास्यामि समादातुं सोमं कस्मैचिदप्यहम् ||८||` | "I will not give the Soma to anyone to take away. ||8||" |
| `Line 4144: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4145: यत्रेमं तु सहस्राक्ष निक्षिपेयमहं स्वयम् |` | "Where I myself would place this, O Thousand-eyed one [Indra]," |
| `Line 4146: त्वमादाय ततस्तूर्णं हरेथास्त्रिदशेश्वर ||९||` | "You may quickly take it from there, O Lord of the thirty (gods) [Indra]. ||9||" |
| `Line 4147: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4148: शक्र उवाच||` | "Śakra [Indra] said:" |
| `Line 4149: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4150: वाक्येनानेन तुष्टोऽहं यत्त्वयोक्तमिहाण्डज |` | "I am pleased with these words that you have spoken here, O egg-born [Garuḍa]," |
| `Line 4151: यदिच्छसि वरं मत्तस्तद्गृहाण खगोत्तम ||१०||` | "Whatever boon you desire from me, take it, O best of birds [Garuḍa]. ||10||" |
| `Line 4152: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4153: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 4154: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4155: इत्युक्तः प्रत्युवाचेदं कद्रूपुत्राननुस्मरन् |` | "Thus addressed, he replied this, remembering the sons of Kadrū [serpents]," |
| `Line 4156: स्मृत्वा चैवोपधिकृतं मातुर्दास्यनिमित्ततः ||११||` | "And recalling the deception that caused his mother's servitude. ||11||" |
| `Line 4157: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4158: ईशोऽहमपि सर्वस्य करिष्यामि तु तेऽर्थिताम् |` | "Though I am master of all, I will fulfill your request," |
| `Line 4159: भवेयुर्भुजगाः शक्र मम भक्ष्या महाबलाः ||१२||` | "Let the mighty serpents, O Śakra [Indra], become my food. ||12||" |
| `Line 4160: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4161: तथेत्युक्त्वान्वगच्छत्तं ततो दानवसूदनः |` | "Having said 'so be it,' the slayer of Dānavas [Indra] then followed him," |
| `Line 4162: हरिष्यामि विनिक्षिप्तं सोममित्यनुभाष्य तम् ||१३||` | "Saying to him, 'I will take away the Soma [nectar] once it is placed down.' ||13||" |
| `Line 4163: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4164: आजगाम ततस्तूर्णं सुपर्णो मातुरन्तिकम् |` | "Then Suparṇa [Garuḍa] quickly came to his mother's presence," |
| `Line 4165: अथ सर्पानुवाचेदं सर्वान्परमहृष्टवत् ||१४||` | "And then spoke these words to all the serpents, appearing extremely delighted. ||14||" |
| `Line 4166: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4167: इदमानीतममृतं निक्षेप्स्यामि कुशेषु वः |` | "This amṛta [nectar] I have brought, I will place on kuśa grass for you," |
| `Line 4168: स्नाता मङ्गलसंयुक्तास्ततः प्राश्नीत पन्नगाः ||१५||` | "After bathing and performing auspicious rites, then partake of it, O serpents. ||15||" |
| `Line 4169: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4170: अदासी चैव मातेयमद्यप्रभृति चास्तु मे |` | "And let my mother be free from servitude from this day forward," |
| `Line 4171: यथोक्तं भवतामेतद्वचो मे प्रतिपादितम् ||१६||` | "As you had promised, your word has been fulfilled by me. ||16||" |
| `Line 4172: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4173: ततः स्नातुं गताः सर्पाः प्रत्युक्त्वा तं तथेत्युत |` | "Then the serpents went to bathe, having replied to him, 'So be it'," |
| `Line 4174: शक्रोऽप्यमृतमाक्षिप्य जगाम त्रिदिवं पुनः ||१७||` | "And Śakra [Indra], having snatched away the nectar, returned to Tridiva [heaven]. ||17||" |
| `Line 4175: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4176: अथागतास्तमुद्देशं सर्पाः सोमार्थिनस्तदा |` | "Then the serpents, desiring Soma [sacred elixir], arrived at that place," |
| `Line 4177: स्नाताश्च कृतजप्याश्च प्रहृष्टाः कृतमङ्गलाः ||१८||` | "Bathed, having completed their prayers, delighted and having performed auspicious rites. ||18||" |
| `Line 4178: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4179: तद्विज्ञाय हृतं सर्पाः प्रतिमायाकृतं च तत् |` | "The serpents, discovering that it was stolen and replaced with an imitation," |
| `Line 4180: सोमस्थानमिदं चेति दर्भांस्ते लिलिहुस्तदा ||१९||` | "Thinking 'This is the place of Soma,' they licked the darbha grass [sacred grass] then. ||19||" |
| `Line 4181: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4182: ततो द्वैधीकृता जिह्वा सर्पाणां तेन कर्मणा |` | "Then by that action, the tongues of the serpents became split in two," |
| `Line 4183: अभवंश्चामृतस्पर्शाद्दर्भास्तेऽथ पवित्रिणः ||२०||` | "And those darbha grasses became purifiers from the touch of amrita [immortal nectar]. ||20||" |
| `Line 4184: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4185: ततः सुपर्णः परमप्रहृष्टवा; न्विहृत्य मात्रा सह तत्र कानने |` | "Then Suparna [Garuda], extremely delighted, having sported with his mother in that forest," |
| `Line 4186: भुजङ्गभक्षः परमार्चितः खगै; रहीनकीर्तिर्विनतामनन्दयत् ||२१||` | "The serpent-eater, highly honored by birds, of unfailing glory, brought joy to Vinata. ||21||" |
| `Line 4187: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4188: इमां कथां यः शृणुयान्नरः सदा; पठेत वा द्विजजनमुख्यसंसदि |` | "The man who always listens to this story or recites it in an assembly of eminent twice-born [Brahmins]," |
| `Line 4189: असंशयं त्रिदिवमियात्स पुण्यभा; ङ्महात्मनः पतगपतेः प्रकीर्तनात् ||२२||` | "Without doubt he goes to heaven, becoming a partaker of merit, from glorifying the great-souled lord of birds [Garuda]. ||22||" |

| `Line 4199: शौनक उवाच||` | "Shaunaka said:" |
| `Line 4200: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4201: भुजङ्गमानां शापस्य मात्रा चैव सुतेन च |` | "Of the serpents' curse by the mother and by the son," |
| `Line 4202: विनतायास्त्वया प्रोक्तं कारणं सूतनन्दन ||१||` | "You have explained the cause related to Vinatā [Garuḍa's mother], O joy of sūtas [bard/charioteer]. ||1||" |
| `Line 4203: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4204: वरप्रदानं भर्त्रा च कद्रूविनतयोस्तथा |` | "The granting of boons by the husband to both Kadrū [serpent mother] and Vinatā," |
| `Line 4205: नामनी चैव ते प्रोक्ते पक्षिणोर्वैनतेययोः ||२||` | "And you have mentioned the names of the two birds, sons of Vinatā [Garuḍa and Aruṇa]. ||2||" |
| `Line 4206: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4207: पन्नगानां तु नामानि न कीर्तयसि सूतज |` | "But you do not recite the names of the serpents [nāgas], O son of a sūta," |
| `Line 4208: प्राधान्येनापि नामानि श्रोतुमिच्छामहे वयम् ||३||` | "We wish to hear especially the names of the prominent ones. ||3||" |
| `Line 4209: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4210: सूत उवाच||` | "The Sūta [narrator] said:" |
| `Line 4211: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4212: बहुत्वान्नामधेयानि भुजगानां तपोधन |` | "Due to the multitude of names of the serpents, O wealth of austerities [sage]," |
| `Line 4213: न कीर्तयिष्ये सर्वेषां प्राधान्येन तु मे शृणु ||४||` | "I will not recite all of them, but listen to me about the prominent ones. ||4||" |
| `Line 4214: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4215: शेषः प्रथमतो जातो वासुकिस्तदनन्तरम् |` | "Śeṣa [cosmic serpent] was born first, then Vāsuki [king of serpents]," |
| `Line 4216: ऐरावतस्तक्षकश्च कर्कोटकधनञ्जयौ ||५||` | "Airāvata, Takṣaka [poison-fanged], and Karkoṭaka and Dhanañjaya. ||5||" |
| `Line 4217: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4218: कालियो मणिनागश्च नागश्चापूरणस्तथा |` | "Kāliya [Krishna's adversary], Maṇināga, and also the serpent Āpūraṇa," |
| `Line 4219: नागस्तथा पिञ्जरक एलापत्रोऽथ वामनः ||६||` | "And the serpent Piñjaraka, Elāpatra, and Vāmana [dwarf serpent]. ||6||" |
| `Line 4220: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4221: नीलानीलौ तथा नागौ कल्माषशबलौ तथा |` | "The serpents Nīla and Anīla, and likewise Kalmāṣa and Śabala," |
| `Line 4222: आर्यकश्चादिकश्चैव नागश्च शलपोतकः ||७||` | "Āryaka and Ādika, and the serpent Śalapotaka. ||7||" |
| `Line 4223: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4224: सुमनोमुखो दधिमुखस्तथा विमलपिण्डकः |` | "Sumanomukha, Dadhimukha [curd-faced], and also Vimalapiṇḍaka," |
| `Line 4225: आप्तः कोटनकश्चैव शङ्खो वालशिखस्तथा ||८||` | "Āpta, Koṭanaka, and also Śaṅkha [conch-like] and Vālaśikha. ||8||" |
| `Line 4226: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4227: निष्ठ्यूनको हेमगुहो नहुषः पिङ्गलस्तथा |` | "Niṣṭhyūnaka, Hemaguha, Nahuṣa [famous serpent king], and Piṅgala as well," |
| `Line 4228: बाह्यकर्णो हस्तिपदस्तथा मुद्गरपिण्डकः ||९||` | "Bāhyakarṇa, Hastipada, and also Mudgarapiṇḍaka. ||9||" |
| `Line 4229: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4230: कम्बलाश्वतरौ चापि नागः कालीयकस्तथा |` | "Kambala and Aśvatara, and also the serpent Kālīyaka [defeated by Krishna]," |
| `Line 4231: वृत्तसंवर्तकौ नागौ द्वौ च पद्माविति श्रुतौ ||१०||` | "The two serpents Vṛtta and Saṃvartaka, and the two known as Padma. ||10||" |
| `Line 4232: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4233: नागः शङ्खनकश्चैव तथा च स्फण्डकोऽपरः |` | "The serpent Śaṅkhanaka, and also another named Sphaṇḍaka," |
| `Line 4234: क्षेमकश्च महानागो नागः पिण्डारकस्तथा ||११||` | "And Kṣemaka the great serpent, and the serpent Piṇḍāraka as well. ||11||" |
| `Line 4235: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4236: करवीरः पुष्पदंष्ट्र एळको बिल्वपाण्डुकः |` | "Karavīra, Puṣpadaṃṣṭra, Eḷaka, Bilvapāṇḍuka," |
| `Line 4237: मूषकादः शङ्खशिराः पूर्णदंष्ट्रो हरिद्रकः ||१२||` | "Mūṣakāda, Śaṅkaśirā, Pūrṇadaṃṣṭra, and Haridrika. ||12||" |
| `Line 4238: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4239: अपराजितो ज्योतिकश्च पन्नगः श्रीवहस्तथा |` | "Aparājita, Jyotika, the serpent Śrīvaha as well," |
| `Line 4240: कौरव्यो धृतराष्ट्रश्च पुष्करः शल्यकस्तथा ||१३||` | "Kauravya, Dhṛtarāṣṭra [serpent king], Puṣkara, and Śalyaka as well. ||13||" |
| `Line 4241: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4242: विरजाश्च सुबाहुश्च शालिपिण्डश्च वीर्यवान् |` | "Virajā, Subāhu, and the mighty Śālipiṇḍa," |
| `Line 4243: हस्तिभद्रः पिठरको मुखरः कोणवासनः ||१४||` | "Hastibhadra, Piṭharaka, Mukhara, and Koṇavāsana. ||14||" |
| `Line 4244: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4245: कुञ्जरः कुररश्चैव तथा नागः प्रभाकरः |` | "Kuñjara, Kurara, and also the serpent Prabhākara," |
| `Line 4246: कुमुदः कुमुदाक्षश्च तित्तिरिर्हलिकस्तथा ||१५||` | "Kumuda, Kumudākṣa, Tittiri, and Halika as well. ||15||" |
| `Line 4247: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4248: कर्कराकर्करौ चोभौ कुण्डोदरमहोदरौ ||१५||` | "Both Karkara and Karkara, and Kuṇḍodara and Mahodara. ||15||" |
| `Line 4249: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4250: एते प्राधान्यतो नागाः कीर्तिता द्विजसत्तम |` | "These are the principal serpents [nāgas] mentioned, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin]," |
| `Line 4251: बहुत्वान्नामधेयानामितरे न प्रकीर्तिताः ||१६||` | "Due to the multitude of names, the others have not been mentioned. ||16||" |
| `Line 4252: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4253: एतेषां प्रसवो यश्च प्रसवस्य च सन्ततिः |` | "The offspring of these and the continuation of their progeny," |
| `Line 4254: असङ्ख्येयेति मत्वा तान्न ब्रवीमि द्विजोत्तम ||१७||` | "Considering them to be innumerable, I do not describe them, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin]. ||17||" |
| `Line 4255: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4256: बहूनीह सहस्राणि प्रयुतान्यर्बुदानि च |` | "Many thousands, millions, and hundreds of millions," |
| `Line 4257: अशक्यान्येव सङ्ख्यातुं भुजगानां तपोधन ||१८||` | "Are impossible to count of the serpents [bhujaga], O wealth of austerities [ascetic sage]. ||18||" |

| `Line 4267: शौनक उवाच||` | "Shaunaka said:" |
| `Line 4268: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4269: जाता वै भुजगास्तात वीर्यवन्तो दुरासदाः |` | "Born indeed were the serpents [bhujaga], O dear one, powerful and unapproachable," |
| `Line 4270: शापं तं त्वथ विज्ञाय कृतवन्तो नु किं परम् ||१||` | "After knowing that curse, what else did they do? ||1||" |
| `Line 4271: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4272: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta said:" |
| `Line 4273: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4274: तेषां तु भगवाञ्शेषस्त्यक्त्वा कद्रूं महायशाः |` | "Among them, the illustrious Lord Shesha [cosmic serpent], abandoning Kadru [serpent mother]," |
| `Line 4275: तपो विपुलमातस्थे वायुभक्षो यतव्रतः ||२||` | "Engaged in intense austerities, subsisting on air, with controlled vows. ||2||" |
| `Line 4276: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4277: गन्धमादनमासाद्य बदर्यां च तपोरतः |` | "Having reached Gandhamādana [fragrant mountain] and engaged in austerities at Badarī [sacred place]," |
| `Line 4278: गोकर्णे पुष्करारण्ये तथा हिमवतस्तटे ||३||` | "At Gokarṇa [cow's ear site], in Puṣkara forest, and likewise on the slopes of Himavat [Himalayas]. ||3||" |
| `Line 4279: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4280: तेषु तेषु च पुण्येषु तीर्थेष्वायतनेषु च |` | "In those various sacred pilgrimage places and temples," |
| `Line 4281: एकान्तशीली नियतः सततं विजितेन्द्रियः ||४||` | "Solitary in habit, disciplined, always with conquered senses [self-controlled]. ||4||" |
| `Line 4282: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4283: तप्यमानं तपो घोरं तं ददर्श पितामहः |` | "Performing severe austerities, him did Pitāmaha [Brahmā] behold," |
| `Line 4284: परिशुष्कमांसत्वक्स्नायुं जटाचीरधरं प्रभुम् ||५||` | "With dried-up flesh, skin and sinews, wearing matted locks and bark garments, the mighty one. ||5||" |
| `Line 4285: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4286: तमब्रवीत्सत्यधृतिं तप्यमानं पितामहः |` | "To him, steadfast in truth, performing austerities, Pitāmaha [Brahmā] spoke," |
| `Line 4287: किमिदं कुरुषे शेष प्रजानां स्वस्ति वै कुरु ||६||` | "What is this you are doing, Śeṣa [serpent deity]? Ensure the welfare of creatures. ||6||" |
| `Line 4288: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4289: त्वं हि तीव्रेण तपसा प्रजास्तापयसेऽनघ |` | "With your intense austerities, you are causing distress to creatures, O sinless one," |
| `Line 4290: ब्रूहि कामं च मे शेष यत्ते हृदि चिरं स्थितम् ||७||` | "Tell me your desire, Śeṣa, that which has long been established in your heart. ||7||" |
| `Line 4291: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4292: शेष उवाच||` | "Śeṣa said:" |
| `Line 4293: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4294: सोदर्या मम सर्वे हि भ्रातरो मन्दचेतसः |` | "All my brothers born of the same womb are dull-witted," |
| `Line 4295: सह तैर्नोत्सहे वस्तुं तद्भवाननुमन्यताम् ||८||` | "I cannot bear to live with them; may you approve of this. ||8||" |
| `Line 4296: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4297: अभ्यसूयन्ति सततं परस्परममित्रवत् |` | "They constantly envy each other like enemies," |
| `Line 4298: ततोऽहं तप आतिष्ठे नैतान्पश्येयमित्युत ||९||` | "Therefore I undertake these austerities so that I may not see them. ||9||" |
| `Line 4299: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4300: न मर्षयन्ति सततं विनतां ससुतां च ते |` | "They constantly cannot tolerate Vinatā [mother of Garuḍa] and her son," |
| `Line 4301: अस्माकं चापरो भ्राता वैनतेयः पितामह ||१०||` | "And our other brother is Vainateya [Garuda], O grandfather. ||10||" |
| `Line 4302: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4304: वरप्रदानात्स पितुः कश्यपस्य महात्मनः ||११||` | "Due to the boon granted by our father, the great-souled Kashyapa. ||11||" |
| `Line 4305: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4306: सोऽहं तपः समास्थाय मोक्ष्यामीदं कलेवरम् |` | "I, having undertaken austerities, will abandon this body," |
| `Line 4307: कथं मे प्रेत्यभावेऽपि न तैः स्यात्सह सङ्गमः ||१२||` | "How can I avoid association with them even after my death? ||12||" |
| `Line 4308: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4309: ब्रह्मोवाच||` | "Brahma [creator deity] said:" |
| `Line 4310: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4312: मातुश्चाप्यपराधाद्वै भ्रातृणां ते महद्भयम् ||१३||` | "And due to your mother's offense, there is great fear from your brothers. ||13||" |
| `Line 4313: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4314: कृतोऽत्र परिहारश्च पूर्वमेव भुजङ्गम |` | "A remedy for this has already been arranged, O serpent," |
| `Line 4315: भ्रातृणां तव सर्वेषां न शोकं कर्तुमर्हसि ||१४||` | "You should not grieve about all your brothers. ||14||" |
| `Line 4316: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4319: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4321: अतो भूयश्च ते बुद्धिर्धर्मे भवतु सुस्थिरा ||१६||` | "Therefore, may your mind be even more firmly established in dharma. ||16||" |
| `Line 4322: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4323: शेष उवाच||` | "Shesha [serpent king] said:" |
| `Line 4324: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4325: एष एव वरो मेऽद्य काङ्क्षितः प्रपितामह |` | "This alone is the boon I desire today, O great-grandfather," |
| `Line 4326: धर्मे मे रमतां बुद्धिः शमे तपसि चेश्वर ||१७||` | "May my mind delight in righteousness, tranquility, and austerity, O Lord [Ishvara]. ||17||" |

| `Line 4330: प्रीतोऽस्म्यनेन ते शेष दमेन प्रशमेन च |` | "I am pleased, O Shesha [serpent king], with your self-control and tranquility," |
| `Line 4331: त्वया त्विदं वचः कार्यं मन्नियोगात्प्रजाहितम् ||१८||` | "But you must carry out these words of mine, by my command, for the welfare of all creatures. ||18||" |
| `Line 4332: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4333: इमां महीं शैलवनोपपन्नां; ससागरां साकरपत्तनां च |` | "This earth, endowed with mountains and forests, with oceans, mines and cities," |
| `Line 4334: त्वं शेष सम्यक्चलितां यथाव; त्सङ्गृह्य तिष्ठस्व यथाचला स्यात् ||१९||` | "You, Shesha, should properly hold it when it shakes, supporting it so that it remains steady. ||19||" |

| `Line 4339: तथा महीं धारयितास्मि निश्चलां; प्रयच्छ तां मे शिरसि प्रजापते ||२०||` | "So shall I hold the earth steady; place it upon my head, O Prajapati [creator lord]. ||20||" |

| `Line 4344: इमां धरां धारयता त्वया हि मे; महत्प्रियं शेष कृतं भविष्यति ||२१||` | "By supporting this earth, O Shesha, you will have done me a great favor. ||21||" |

| `Line 4372: सूत उवाच॥` | "Sūta said:" |
| `Line 4373: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4374: मातुः सकाशात्तं शापं श्रुत्वा पन्नगसत्तमः |` | "Having heard that curse from his mother, the foremost of serpents," |
| `Line 4375: वासुकिश्चिन्तयामास शापोऽयं न भवेत्कथम् ॥१॥` | "Vāsuki pondered, 'How might this curse not come to pass?' ||1||" |
| `Line 4376: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4377: ततः स मन्त्रयामास भ्रातृभिः सह सर्वशः |` | "Then he consulted thoroughly with all his brothers," |
| `Line 4378: ऐरावतप्रभृतिभिर्ये स्म धर्मपरायणाः ||२||` | "With Airāvata and others who were devoted to righteousness. ||2||" |
| `Line 4379: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4380: वासुकिरुवाच||` | "Vāsuki [serpent king] said:" |
| `Line 4381: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4382: अयं शापो यथोद्दिष्टो विदितं वस्तथानघाः |` | "This curse as pronounced is known to you all, O sinless ones," |
| `Line 4383: तस्य शापस्य मोक्षार्थं मन्त्रयित्वा यतामहे ||३||` | "Let us consult together and strive for liberation from that curse. ||3||" |
| `Line 4384: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4385: सर्वेषामेव शापानां प्रतिघातो हि विद्यते |` | "For all curses, indeed, there exists a counteraction," |
| `Line 4386: न तु मात्राभिशप्तानां मोक्षो विद्येत पन्नगाः ||४||` | "But for those cursed by a mother, O serpents, there may be no release. ||4||" |
| `Line 4387: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4388: अव्ययस्याप्रमेयस्य सत्यस्य च तथाग्रतः |` | "In the presence of the imperishable, immeasurable, and truthful one," |
| `Line 4389: शप्ता इत्येव मे श्रुत्वा जायते हृदि वेपथुः ||५||` | "Hearing that we are cursed, trembling arises in my heart. ||5||" |
| `Line 4390: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4391: नूनं सर्वविनाशोऽयमस्माकं समुदाहृतः |` | "Surely this complete destruction of ours has been pronounced," |
| `Line 4392: न ह्येनां सोऽव्ययो देवः शपन्तीं प्रत्यषेधयत् ||६||` | "For that imperishable god did not restrain her when she was cursing. ||6||" |
| `Line 4393: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4394: तस्मात्संमन्त्रयामोऽत्र भुजगानामनामयम् |` | "Therefore, let us consult here about the welfare of the serpents," |
| `Line 4395: यथा भवेत सर्वेषां मा नः कालोऽत्यगादयम् ||७||` | "How it might be for all, lest this time of doom overtake us. ||7||" |
| `Line 4396: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4397: अपि मन्त्रयमाणा हि हेतुं पश्याम मोक्षणे |` | "Perhaps by consulting, we may see a means for liberation," |
| `Line 4398: यथा नष्टं पुरा देवा गूढमग्निं गुहागतम् ||८||` | "Just as the gods once found the lost fire hidden in a cave. ||8||" |
| `Line 4399: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 4400: यथा स यज्ञो न भवेद्यथा वापि पराभवेत् |` | "How that sacrifice might not take place, or how it might be defeated," |
| `Line 4401: जनमेजयस्य सर्पाणां विनाशकरणाय हि ||९||` | "For causing the destruction of serpents by Janamejaya [Pāṇḍava king]. ||9||" |
| `Line 4402: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4403: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard sage] said:" |
| `Line 4404: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4405: तथेत्युक्त्वा तु ते सर्वे काद्रवेयाः समागताः |` | "Having said 'so be it,' all those Kādraveyas [serpent sons] who had assembled," |
| `Line 4406: समयं चक्रिरे तत्र मन्त्रबुद्धिविशारदाः ||१०||` | "Made a plan there, being skilled in deliberative thinking. ||10||" |
| `Line 4407: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4408: एके तत्राब्रुवन्नागा वयं भूत्वा द्विजर्षभाः |` | "Some serpents there said, 'We shall become Brahmin [twice-born] bulls [eminent ones]," |
| `Line 4409: जनमेजयं तं भिक्षामो यज्ञस्ते न भवेदिति ||११||` | "And beg Janamejaya saying, 'Let this sacrifice not take place.'" ||11||" |
| `Line 4410: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4411: अपरे त्वब्रुवन्नागास्तत्र पण्डितमानिनः |` | "But other serpents there, considering themselves learned, said," |
| `Line 4412: मन्त्रिणोऽस्य वयं सर्वे भविष्यामः सुसंमताः ||१२||` | "We all shall become his highly respected ministers. ||12||" |
| `Line 4413: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4414: स नः प्रक्ष्यति सर्वेषु कार्येष्वर्थविनिश्चयम् |` | "He will ask us for decisive counsel in all matters," |
| `Line 4415: तत्र बुद्धिं प्रवक्ष्यामो यथा यज्ञो निवर्तते ||१३||` | "Then we shall give advice so that the sacrifice is stopped. ||13||" |
| `Line 4416: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4417: स नो बहुमतान्राजा बुद्ध्वा बुद्धिमतां वरः |` | "The king, foremost among the wise, considering us highly esteemed," |
| `Line 4418: यज्ञार्थं प्रक्ष्यति व्यक्तं नेति वक्ष्यामहे वयम् ||१४||` | "Will surely ask about the sacrifice, and we shall say 'no.' ||14||" |
| `Line 4419: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4420: दर्शयन्तो बहून्दोषान्प्रेत्य चेह च दारुणान् |` | "Showing many terrible faults both in this world and after death," |
| `Line 4421: हेतुभिः कारणैश्चैव यथा यज्ञो भवेन्न सः ||१५||` | "With reasons and arguments so that the sacrifice may not take place. ||15||" |
| `Line 4422: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4423: अथवा य उपाध्यायः क्रतौ तस्मिन्भविष्यति |` | "Or else, whoever will be the preceptor [teacher] in that sacrifice," |
| `Line 4424: सर्पसत्रविधानज्ञो राजकार्यहिते रतः ||१६||` | "Knowledgeable in the procedures of the serpent sacrifice, devoted to the king's welfare. ||16||" |
| `Line 4425: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4426: तं गत्वा दशतां कश्चिद्भुजगः स मरिष्यति |` | "Going there, some serpent [snake being] will bite him and die." |
| `Line 4427: तस्मिन्हते यज्ञकरे क्रतुः स न भविष्यति ||१७||` | "When that sacrificer [ritual performer] is killed, that sacrifice will not take place. ||17||" |
| `Line 4428: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4429: ये चान्ये सर्पसत्रज्ञा भविष्यन्त्यस्य ऋत्विजः |` | "And those others who are knowledgeable in serpent-sacrifices [snake rituals] who will be his priests," |
| `Line 4430: तांश्च सर्वान्दशिष्यामः कृतमेवं भविष्यति ||१८||` | "We shall bite all of them too, thus it will be accomplished. ||18||" |
| `Line 4431: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4432: तत्रापरेऽमन्त्रयन्त धर्मात्मानो भुजङ्गमाः |` | "There, other righteous-souled serpents [snake beings] counseled," |
| `Line 4433: अबुद्धिरेषा युष्माकं ब्रह्महत्या न शोभना ||१९||` | "This is unwise of you; killing a Brahmin [priest] is not auspicious. ||19||" |
| `Line 4434: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4435: सम्यक्सद्धर्ममूला हि व्यसने शान्तिरुत्तमा |` | "Indeed, the highest peace in calamity is rooted in proper righteousness [dharma]," |
| `Line 4436: अधर्मोत्तरता नाम कृत्स्नं व्यापादयेज्जगत् ||२०||` | "The predominance of unrighteousness [adharma] would destroy the entire world. ||20||" |
| `Line 4437: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4438: अपरे त्वब्रुवन्नागाः समिद्धं जातवेदसम् |` | "But other serpents [nāgas] said, 'The blazing fire [Jātavedas]," |
| `Line 4439: वर्षैर्निर्वापयिष्यामो मेघा भूत्वा सविद्युतः ||२१||` | "We shall extinguish with rains, becoming clouds with lightning.' ||21||" |
| `Line 4440: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4441: स्रुग्भाण्डं निशि गत्वा वा अपरे भुजगोत्तमाः |` | "Or other excellent serpents [snake lords] said, 'Going at night to the sacrificial vessels [ritual implements]," |
| `Line 4442: प्रमत्तानां हरन्त्वाशु विघ्न एवं भविष्यति ||२२||` | "Let them quickly steal them from the careless ones; thus there will be an obstacle.' ||22||" |
| `Line 4443: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4445: जनं दशन्तु वै सर्वमेवं त्रासो भविष्यति ||२३||` | "Bite all the people; thus there will be terror. ||23||" |
| `Line 4446: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4447: अथवा संस्कृतं भोज्यं दूषयन्तु भुजङ्गमाः |` | "Or let the serpents [snake beings] contaminate the prepared food," |
| `Line 4448: स्वेन मूत्रपुरीषेण सर्वभोज्यविनाशिना ||२४||` | "With their urine and feces that destroy all food. ||24||" |
| `Line 4449: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4450: अपरे त्वब्रुवंस्तत्र ऋत्विजोऽस्य भवामहे |` | "But others said there, 'Let us become the priests [ritual officiants] of his," |
| `Line 4451: यज्ञविघ्नं करिष्यामो दीयतां दक्षिणा इति ||२५||` | "We shall create an obstacle to the sacrifice, so let the sacrificial fee be given. ||25||" |
| `Line 4452: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4453: वश्यतां च गतोऽसौ नः करिष्यति यथेप्षितम् ||२५||` | "And having come under our control, he will do as we desire. ||25||" |
| `Line 4454: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4455: अपरे त्वब्रुवंस्तत्र जले प्रक्रीडितं नृपम् |` | "But others said there: 'Let us seize the king while he is sporting in the water," |
| `Line 4456: गृहमानीय बध्नीमः क्रतुरेवं भवेन्न सः ||२६||` | "Bring him to our abode and bind him; thus the sacrifice will not take place.' ||26||" |
| `Line 4457: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4462: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4630: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4631: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard sage] said:" |
| `Line 4632: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4633: अथ कालस्य महतः स मुनिः संशितव्रतः |` | "Then, after a long time, that sage of firm vows," |
| `Line 4634: तपस्यभिरतो धीमान्न दारानभ्यकाङ्क्षत ||६||` | "Engaged in austerities, the wise one did not desire a wife. ||6||" |
| `Line 4635: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4636: स ऊर्ध्वरेतास्तपसि प्रसक्तः; स्वाध्यायवान्वीतभयक्लमः सन् |` | "He, practicing celibacy [ūrdhvaretās], devoted to austerities, engaged in self-study, free from fear and fatigue," |
| `Line 4637: चचार सर्वां पृथिवीं महात्मा; न चापि दारान्मनसाप्यकाङ्क्षत् ||७||` | "The great soul wandered over the entire earth; and did not desire a wife even in his mind. ||7||" |
| `Line 4638: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4639: ततोऽपरस्मिन्सम्प्राप्ते काले कस्मिंश्चिदेव तु |` | "Then, at some later time," |
| `Line 4640: परिक्षिदिति विख्यातो राजा कौरववंशभृत् ||८||` | "A king named Parikshit, bearer of the Kuru lineage, became famous. ||8||" |
| `Line 4641: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4642: यथा पाण्डुर्महाबाहुर्धनुर्धरवरो भुवि |` | "Just as Pāṇḍu [father of Pāṇḍavas], the mighty-armed, the best of archers on earth," |
| `Line 4643: बभूव मृगयाशीलः पुरास्य प्रपितामहः ||९||` | "Was fond of hunting, so was his great-grandfather before him. ||9||" |
| `Line 4644: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4645: मृगान्विध्यन्वराहांश्च तरक्षून्महिषांस्तथा |` | "Piercing deer, boars, hyenas, and buffaloes," |
| `Line 4646: अन्यांश्च विविधान्वन्यांश्चचार पृथिवीपतिः ||१०||` | "And various other wild animals, the lord of the earth roamed about. ||10||" |
| `Line 4647: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4648: स कदाचिन्मृगं विद्ध्वा बाणेन नतपर्वणा |` | "Once, having pierced a deer with an arrow of curved joints," |
| `Line 4649: पृष्ठतो धनुरादाय ससार गहने वने ||११||` | "Taking his bow, he pursued it from behind into the dense forest. ||11||" |
| `Line 4650: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4651: यथा हि भगवान्रुद्रो विद्ध्वा यज्ञमृगं दिवि |` | "Just as the lord Rudra [Shiva], having pierced the sacrificial deer in heaven," |
| `Line 4652: अन्वगच्छद्धनुष्पाणिः पर्यन्वेषंस्ततस्ततः ||१२||` | "Followed it with bow in hand, searching here and there. ||12||" |
| `Line 4653: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4654: न हि तेन मृगो विद्धो जीवन्गच्छति वै वनम् |` | "For indeed, the deer pierced by him does not go living to the forest," |
| `Line 4655: पूर्वरूपं तु तन्नूनमासीत्स्वर्गगतिं प्रति ||१३||` | "But that was surely a foretoken regarding the path to heaven. ||13||" |
| `Line 4656: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4657: परिक्षितस्तस्य राज्ञो विद्धो यन्नष्टवान्मृगः ||१३||` | "For King Parikshit, the wounded deer that disappeared. ||13||" |
| `Line 4658: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4659: दूरं चापहृतस्तेन मृगेण स महीपतिः |` | "That ruler of the earth was led far away by that deer," |
| `Line 4660: परिश्रान्तः पिपासार्त आससाद मुनिं वने ||१४||` | "Exhausted and afflicted by thirst, he came upon a sage in the forest. ||14||" |
| `Line 4661: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4662: गवां प्रचारेष्वासीनं वत्सानां मुखनिःसृतम् |` | "Seated in the pastures of cows, (watching) what flowed from the mouths of calves," |
| `Line 4663: भूयिष्ठमुपयुञ्जानं फेनमापिबतां पयः ||१५||` | "Mostly consuming the foam of the milk they were drinking. ||15||" |
| `Line 4664: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4665: तमभिद्रुत्य वेगेन स राजा संशितव्रतम् |` | "Rushing quickly toward him, that king approached the sage of strict vows," |
| `Line 4666: अपृच्छद्धनुरुद्यम्य तं मुनिं क्षुच्छ्रमान्वितः ||१६||` | "And asked him, raising his bow, that sage, while afflicted with hunger and fatigue. ||16||" |
| `Line 4667: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4668: भो भो ब्रह्मन्नहं राजा परिक्षिदभिमन्युजः |` | "O Brahmin, I am King Parikshit, son of Abhimanyu," |
| `Line 4669: मया विद्धो मृगो नष्टः कच्चित्त्वं दृष्टवानसि ||१७||` | "A deer wounded by me has disappeared; have you perhaps seen it? ||17||" |
| `Line 4670: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4671: स मुनिस्तस्य नोवाच किञ्चिन्मौनव्रते स्थितः |` | "That sage did not say anything to him, being established in a vow of silence," |
| `Line 4672: तस्य स्कन्धे मृतं सर्पं क्रुद्धो राजा समासजत् ||१८||` | "The angry king placed a dead snake on his shoulders. ||18||" |
| `Line 4673: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4674: धनुष्कोट्या समुत्क्षिप्य स चैनं समुदैक्षत |` | "Lifting it with the end of his bow, and the sage looked at him," |
| `Line 4675: न च किञ्चिदुवाचैनं शुभं वा यदि वाशुभम् ||१९||` | "But did not say anything to him, whether good or bad. ||19||" |
| `Line 4676: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4677: स राजा क्रोधमुत्सृज्य व्यथितस्तं तथागतम् |` | "That king, abandoning his anger, distressed, seeing him in such a state," |
| `Line 4678: दृष्ट्वा जगाम नगरमृषिस्त्वास्ते तथैव सः ||२०||` | "Went back to his city, while the sage remained there in the same condition. ||20||" |
| `Line 4679: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4680: तरुणस्तस्य पुत्रोऽभूत्तिग्मतेजा महातपाः |` | "That sage had a young son of fierce energy and great austerity," |
| `Line 4681: शृङ्गी नाम महाक्रोधो दुष्प्रसादो महाव्रतः ||२१||` | "Named Śṛṅgī, who was very wrathful, difficult to please, and of great vows. ||21||" |
| `Line 4682: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4683: स देवं परमीशानं सर्वभूतहिते रतम् |` | "He worshipped the supreme lord, devoted to the welfare of all beings," |
| `Line 4684: ब्रह्माणमुपतस्थे वै काले काले सुसंयतः ||२२||` | "Brahmā [creator deity], at proper times, with great self-control. ||22||" |
| `Line 4685: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4686: स तेन समनुज्ञातो ब्रह्मणा गृहमेयिवान् ||२२||` | "Having been permitted by Brahmā, he returned home. ||22||" |
| `Line 4687: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4688: सख्योक्तः क्रीडमानेन स तत्र हसता किल |` | "There, he was told by a playful, laughing friend," |
| `Line 4689: संरम्भी कोपनोऽतीव विषकल्प ऋषेः सुतः ||२३||` | "He who was impetuous, extremely irascible, venomous-like, the sage's son. ||23||" |
| `Line 4690: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4691: ऋषिपुत्रेण नर्मार्थं कृशेन द्विजसत्तम ||२३||` | "By a thin sage's son in jest, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin]. ||23||" |
| `Line 4692: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4693: तेजस्विनस्तव पिता तथैव च तपस्विनः |` | "Your father, though powerful and an ascetic," |
| `Line 4694: शवं स्कन्धेन वहति मा शृङ्गिन्गर्वितो भव ||२४||` | "Carries a dead snake on his shoulder. O Śṛṅgī, do not be proud. ||24||" |
| `Line 4695: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4696: व्याहरत्स्वृषिपुत्रेषु मा स्म किञ्चिद्वचो वदीः |` | "Do not speak any words among the sons of sages," |
| `Line 4697: अस्मद्विधेषु सिद्धेषु ब्रह्मवित्सु तपस्विषु ||२५||` | "Among accomplished ones like us, knowers of Brahman [absolute reality], and ascetics. ||25||" |
| `Line 4698: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4699: क्व ते पुरुषमानित्वं क्व ते वाचस्तथाविधाः |` | "Where is your manly pride, where are your boastful words," |
| `Line 4700: दर्पजाः पितरं यस्त्वं द्रष्टा शवधरं तथा ||२६||` | "Born of arrogance, when you will see your father carrying a dead snake thus? ||26||" |

| `Line 4707: ३७` | "37" |
| `Line 4708: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4709: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4710: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 4711: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4712: एवमुक्तः स तेजस्वी शृङ्गी कोपसमन्वितः |` | "Thus addressed, that radiant Śṛṅgī [sage's son], filled with anger," |
| `Line 4713: मृतधारं गुरुं श्रुत्वा पर्यतप्यत मन्युना ||१||` | "Having heard that his teacher bore a dead snake, was consumed by wrath. ||1||" |
| `Line 4714: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4715: स तं कृशमभिप्रेष्क्य सूनृतां वाचमुत्सृजन् |` | "He, looking at Kṛśa [messenger], speaking gentle words," |
| `Line 4716: अपृच्छत कथं तातः स मेऽद्य मृतधारकः ||२||` | "Asked, 'How is my father today bearing a dead snake?' ||2||" |
| `Line 4717: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4718: कृश उवाच||` | "Kṛśa [messenger] said:" |
| `Line 4719: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4720: राज्ञा परिक्षिता तात मृगयां परिधावता |` | "By King Parikṣit [Abhimanyu's son], O dear one, while roaming on a hunt," |
| `Line 4721: अवसक्तः पितुस्तेऽद्य मृतः स्कन्धे भुजङ्गमः ||३||` | "A dead serpent was placed on your father's shoulder today. ||3||" |
| `Line 4722: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4723: शृङ्ग्युवाच||` | "Śṛṅgī [sage's son] said:" |
| `Line 4724: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4725: किं मे पित्रा कृतं तस्य राज्ञोऽनिष्टं दुरात्मनः |` | "What harm was done by my father to that evil-minded king?" |
| `Line 4726: ब्रूहि त्वं कृश तत्त्वेन पश्य मे तपसो बलम् ||४||` | "Tell me the truth, O Kṛśa, behold the power of my austerities. ||4||" |
| `Line 4727: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4728: कृश उवाच||` | "Kṛśa said:" |
| `Line 4729: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4730: स राजा मृगयां यातः परिक्षिदभिमन्युजः |` | "That king, Parikshit [son of Abhimanyu], went hunting," |
| `Line 4731: ससार मृगमेकाकी विद्ध्वा बाणेन पत्रिणा ||५||` | "He pursued a deer alone, having pierced it with a feathered arrow. ||5||" |
| `Line 4732: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4733: न चापश्यन्मृगं राजा चरंस्तस्मिन्महावने |` | "And the king did not see the deer while wandering in that great forest," |
| `Line 4734: पितरं ते स दृष्ट्वैव पप्रच्छानभिभाषिणम् ||६||` | "Upon seeing your father, he questioned him who was not speaking. ||6||" |
| `Line 4735: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4736: तं स्थाणुभूतं तिष्ठन्तं क्षुत्पिपासाश्रमातुरः |` | "To him who was standing still like a post, the king, afflicted by hunger, thirst, and fatigue," |
| `Line 4737: पुनः पुनर्मृगं नष्टं पप्रच्छ पितरं तव ||७||` | "Again and again asked your father about the lost deer. ||7||" |
| `Line 4738: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4739: स च मौनव्रतोपेतो नैव तं प्रत्यभाषत |` | "And he, observing a vow of silence, did not reply to him," |
| `Line 4740: तस्य राजा धनुष्कोट्या सर्पं स्कन्धे समासृजत् ||८||` | "The king placed a dead snake on his shoulders with the tip of his bow. ||8||" |
| `Line 4741: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4742: शृङ्गिंस्तव पिताद्यासौ तथैवास्ते यतव्रतः |` | "O Śṛṅgin [son of sage], your father even now sits there, steadfast in his vow," |
| `Line 4743: सोऽपि राजा स्वनगरं प्रतियातो गजाह्वयम् ||९||` | "And that king has returned to his city named Gajāhvaya [Hastinapura]. ||9||" |
| `Line 4744: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4745: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 4746: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4747: श्रुत्वैवमृषिपुत्रस्तु दिवं स्तब्ध्वेव विष्ठितः |` | "Having heard this, the sage's son stood as if frozen, staring at the sky," |
| `Line 4748: कोपसंरक्तनयनः प्रज्वलन्निव मन्युना ||१०||` | "With eyes reddened by anger, burning as it were with wrath. ||10||" |
| `Line 4749: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4750: आविष्टः स तु कोपेन शशाप नृपतिं तदा |` | "Possessed by anger, he then cursed the king," |
| `Line 4751: वार्युपस्पृश्य तेजस्वी क्रोधवेगबलात्कृतः ||११||` | "Having touched water, the radiant one was overcome by the force of anger. ||11||" |
| `Line 4752: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4753: शृङ्ग्युवाच||` | "Śṛṅgī [sage's son] said:" |
| `Line 4754: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4755: योऽसौ वृद्धस्य तातस्य तथा कृच्छ्रगतस्य च |` | "That sinful king who placed a dead snake on the shoulders of my elderly father who was in such a difficult state," |
| `Line 4756: स्कन्धे मृतमवास्राक्षीत्पन्नगं राजकिल्बिषी ||१२||` | "That sinful king placed a dead serpent on his shoulders. ||12||" |
| `Line 4757: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4758: तं पापमतिसङ्क्रुद्धस्तक्षकः पन्नगोत्तमः |` | "That sinful one, Takṣaka [serpent king], the foremost among serpents, extremely enraged," |
| `Line 4759: आशीविषस्तिग्मतेजा मद्वाक्यबलचोदितः ||१३||` | "The venomous one of fierce energy, impelled by the power of my words, ||13||" |
| `Line 4760: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4761: सप्तरात्रादितो नेता यमस्य सदनं प्रति |` | "Will, from today in seven nights, lead him to the abode of Yama [death god]," |
| `Line 4762: द्विजानामवमन्तारं कुरूणामयशस्करम् ||१४||` | "Him who insults the twice-born [Brahmins] and brings disgrace to the Kurus [royal dynasty]. ||14||" |
| `Line 4763: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4764: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 4765: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4766: इति शप्त्वा नृपं क्रुद्धः शृङ्गी पितरमभ्ययात् |` | "Having thus cursed the king in anger, Śṛṅgī went to his father," |
| `Line 4767: आसीनं गोचरे तस्मिन्वहन्तं शवपन्नगम् ||१५||` | "Who was sitting in that pasture, still bearing the dead snake. ||15||" |
| `Line 4768: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4769: स तमालक्ष्य पितरं शृङ्गी स्कन्धगतेन वै |` | "Seeing his father with the snake still on his shoulders," |
| `Line 4770: शवेन भुजगेनासीद्भूयः क्रोधसमन्वितः ||१६||` | "Śṛṅgī was again filled with anger. ||16||" |
| `Line 4771: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4772: दुःखाच्चाश्रूणि मुमुचे पितरं चेदमब्रवीत् |` | "Out of sorrow he shed tears and said this to his father," |
| `Line 4773: श्रुत्वेमां धर्षणां तात तव तेन दुरात्मना ||१७||` | "Having heard of this insult to you, father, by that wicked one, ||17||" |
| `Line 4774: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4775: राज्ञा परिक्षिता कोपादशपं तमहं नृपम् |` | "In anger I have cursed that king Parikṣit [Kuru king]," |
| `Line 4776: यथार्हति स एवोग्रं शापं कुरुकुलाधमः ||१८||` | "Thus that lowest of the Kuru family deserves this terrible curse. ||18||" |
| `Line 4777: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4778: सप्तमेऽहनि तं पापं तक्षकः पन्नगोत्तमः |` | "On the seventh day, Takshaka, the foremost of serpents [nāga king]," |
| `Line 4779: वैवस्वतस्य भवनं नेता परमदारुणम् ||१९||` | "Will lead that sinful one to the abode of Vaivasvata [Yama, death god], most terribly. ||19||" |
| `Line 4780: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4781: तमब्रवीत्पिता ब्रह्मंस्तथा कोपसमन्वितम् |` | "His father, filled with anger, said to him, O Brahman [sage]," |
| `Line 4782: न मे प्रियं कृतं तात नैष धर्मस्तपस्विनाम् ||२०||` | "You have not done what pleases me, my son; this is not the dharma [righteous duty] of ascetics. ||20||" |
| `Line 4783: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4784: वयं तस्य नरेन्द्रस्य विषये निवसामहे |` | "We live in the kingdom of that lord of men [king]," |
| `Line 4785: न्यायतो रक्षितास्तेन तस्य पापं न रोचये ||२१||` | "Justly protected by him; I do not approve of his being cursed. ||21||" |
| `Line 4786: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4787: सर्वथा वर्तमानस्य राज्ञो ह्यस्मद्विधैः सदा |` | "The king who always behaves properly toward people like us," |
| `Line 4788: क्षन्तव्यं पुत्र धर्मो हि हतो हन्ति न संशयः ||२२||` | "Should be forgiven, my son, for dharma [righteousness] when destroyed, destroys in return—there is no doubt. ||22||" |

| `Line 4791: न शक्नुयाम चरितुं धर्मं पुत्र यथासुखम् ||२३||` | "We would not be able to practice dharma [religious duties] comfortably, my son. ||23||" |
| `Line 4792: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4794: चरामो विपुलं धर्मं तेषां चांशोऽस्ति धर्मतः ||२४||` | "We practice extensive dharma [spiritual practices], and they receive a share of that merit. ||24||" |
| `Line 4795: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4813: शृङ्ग्युवाच||` | "Śṛṅgī said:" |

| `Line 4815: यद्येतत्साहसं तात यदि वा दुष्कृतं कृतम् |` | "Whether this was rashness, father, or whether an evil deed was done," |
| `Line 4816: प्रियं वाप्यप्रियं वा ते वागुक्ता न मृषा मया ||१||` | "Whether pleasing or displeasing to you, the words spoken by me are not false. ||1||" |

| `Line 4819: नाहं मृषा प्रब्रवीमि स्वैरेष्वपि कुतः शपन् ||२||` | "I do not speak falsely even in casual matters, how much less when pronouncing a curse? ||2||" |

| `Line 4822: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4823: जानाम्युग्रप्रभावं त्वां पुत्र सत्यगिरं तथा |` | "I know your terrible power, O son, and also that you speak the truth," |
| `Line 4824: नानृतं ह्युक्तपूर्वं ते नैतन्मिथ्या भविष्यति ||३||` | "You have never spoken falsehood before, and this will not prove false. ||3||" |

| `Line 4827: यथा स्याद्गुणसंयुक्तः प्राप्नुयाच्च महद्यशः ||४||` | "So that he may be endowed with virtues and attain great fame. ||4||" |

| `Line 4943: काश्यप उवाच||` | "Kaśyapa said:" |
| `Line 4944: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4945: अहं तं नृपतिं नाग त्वया दष्टमपज्वरम् |` | "I, O serpent, can make that king bitten by you free from fever [healed]," |
| `Line 4946: करिष्य इति मे बुद्धिर्विद्याबलमुपाश्रितः ||३९||` | "This is my conviction, relying on the power of my knowledge. ||39||" |

| `Line 4956: तक्षक उवाच||` | "Takshaka [serpent king] said:" |
| `Line 4957: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4958: दष्टं यदि मयेह त्वं शक्तः किञ्चिच्चिकित्सितुम् |` | "If you are able to heal anything that has been bitten by me here," |
| `Line 4959: ततो वृक्षं मया दष्टमिमं जीवय काश्यप ||१||` | "Then revive this tree that has been bitten by me, O Kashyapa. ||1||" |
| `Line 4960: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4961: परं मन्त्रबलं यत्ते तद्दर्शय यतस्व च |` | "Show the supreme power of your mantras and exert yourself," |
| `Line 4962: न्यग्रोधमेनं धक्ष्यामि पश्यतस्ते द्विजोत्तम ||२||` | "I will burn this banyan tree before your eyes, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin]. ||2||" |
| `Line 4963: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4964: काश्यप उवाच||` | "Kashyapa [sage] said:" |
| `Line 4965: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4966: दश नागेन्द्र वृक्षं त्वं यमेनमभिमन्यसे |` | "Bite this tree, O lord of serpents, which you have in mind," |
| `Line 4967: अहमेनं त्वया दष्टं जीवयिष्ये भुजङ्गम ||३||` | "I will revive it after it has been bitten by you, O serpent. ||3||" |
| `Line 4968: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4969: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta [narrator sage] said:" |
| `Line 4970: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4971: एवमुक्तः स नागेन्द्रः काश्यपेन महात्मना |` | "Thus addressed by the great-souled Kashyapa, that lord of serpents," |
| `Line 4972: अदशद्वृक्षमभ्येत्य न्यग्रोधं पन्नगोत्तमः ||४||` | "The foremost of serpents approached and bit the banyan tree. ||4||" |
| `Line 4973: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4974: स वृक्षस्तेन दष्टः सन्सद्य एव महाद्युते |` | "That tree, having been bitten by him, O greatly radiant one [addressing the listener]," |
| `Line 4975: आशीविषविषोपेतः प्रजज्वाल समन्ततः ||५||` | "Filled with the poison of the venomous snake, burst into flames all around. ||5||" |
| `Line 4976: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4977: तं दग्ध्वा स नगं नागः काश्यपं पुनरब्रवीत् |` | "After burning that tree, the nāga [serpent king] spoke again to Kāśyapa," |
| `Line 4978: कुरु यत्नं द्विजश्रेष्ठ जीवयैनं वनस्पतिम् ||६||` | "Make an effort, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin], to revive this tree. ||6||" |
| `Line 4979: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4980: भस्मीभूतं ततो वृक्षं पन्नगेन्द्रस्य तेजसा |` | "Then, the tree reduced to ashes by the serpent lord's power," |
| `Line 4981: भस्म सर्वं समाहृत्य काश्यपो वाक्यमब्रवीत् ||७||` | "Gathering all the ashes, Kāśyapa spoke these words: ||7||" |
| `Line 4982: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4983: विद्याबलं पन्नगेन्द्र पश्य मेऽस्मिन्वनस्पतौ |` | "O lord of serpents, behold the power of my knowledge on this tree," |
| `Line 4984: अहं सञ्जीवयाम्येनं पश्यतस्ते भुजङ्गम ||८||` | "I shall revive it before your eyes, O serpent. ||8||" |
| `Line 4985: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4986: ततः स भगवान्विद्वान्काश्यपो द्विजसत्तमः |` | "Then that venerable learned Kāśyapa, best among the twice-born [Brahmins]," |
| `Line 4987: भस्मराशीकृतं वृक्षं विद्यया समजीवयत् ||९||` | "Revived the tree that had been reduced to a heap of ashes through his knowledge. ||9||" |
| `Line 4988: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 4989: अङ्कुरं तं स कृतवांस्ततः पर्णद्वयान्वितम् |` | "He made it first into a sprout, then with two leaves," |
| `Line 4990: पलाशिनं शाखिनं च तथा विटपिनं पुनः ||१०||` | "Then with foliage, branches, and finally a complete tree again. ||10||" |
| `Line 4991: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4993: उवाच तक्षको ब्रह्मन्नेतदत्यद्भुतं त्वयि ||११||` | "Takṣaka said, 'O Brahmin, this is not surprising in you. ||11||'" |
| `Line 4994: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 4996: कं त्वमर्थमभिप्रेप्सुर्यासि तत्र तपोधन ||१२||` | "What purpose do you seek in going there, O wealth of austerities [ascetic]? ||12||" |
| `Line 4997: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5000: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5001: विप्रशापाभिभूते च क्षीणायुषि नराधिपे |` | "When the king is overwhelmed by a Brahmin's curse and his life-span is diminished," |

| `Line 5010: ततोऽहं विनिवर्तिष्ये गृहायोरगसत्तम ||१६||` | "Then I shall return home, O best of serpents [Takshaka]. ||16||" |

| `Line 5064: अस्तमभ्येति सविता विषादद्य न मे भयम् ||३०||` | "The sun is setting, and today I have no fear of poison. ||30||" |

| `Line 5106: शशास राज्यं कुरुपुङ्गवाग्रजो; यथास्य वीरः प्रपितामहस्तथा ||७||` | "Ruled the kingdom as the foremost of the Kuru bulls, just as his great-grandfather, the hero, had done. ||7||" |
| `Line 5107: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5108: ततस्तु राजानममित्रतापनं; समीक्ष्य ते तस्य नृपस्य मन्त्रिणः |` | "Then, observing that king, the scorcher of enemies, those ministers of the king," |
| `Line 5109: सुवर्णवर्माणमुपेत्य काशिपं; वपुष्टमार्थं वरयां प्रचक्रमुः ||८||` | "Approached Suvarnavarman, the king of Kashi, and sought the hand of Vapushtama [beautiful-bodied woman] for him. ||8||" |
| `Line 5110: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5111: ततः स राजा प्रददौ वपुष्टमां; कुरुप्रवीराय परीक्ष्य धर्मतः |` | "Then that king, having examined according to dharma, gave Vapushtama to the foremost of Kurus," |
| `Line 5112: स चापि तां प्राप्य मुदा युतोऽभव; न्न चान्यनारीषु मनो दधे क्वचित् ||९||` | "And he, having obtained her, was filled with joy, and never set his mind on any other woman. ||9||" |
| `Line 5113: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5114: सरःसु फुल्लेषु वनेषु चैव ह; प्रसन्नचेता विजहार वीर्यवान् |` | "In blooming lakes and forests, the mighty one sported with a cheerful mind," |
| `Line 5115: तथा स राजन्यवरो विजह्रिवा; न्यथोर्वशीं प्राप्य पुरा पुरूरवाः ||१०||` | "Thus that best of kings enjoyed himself, just as Pururavas had done in the past after obtaining Urvashi [celestial nymph]. ||10||" |
| `Line 5116: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5117: वपुष्टमा चापि वरं पतिं तदा; प्रतीतरूपं समवाप्य भूमिपम् |` | "And Vapushtama too, having obtained that excellent husband, the renowned king of the earth," |
| `Line 5118: भावेन रामा रमयां बभूव वै; विहारकालेष्ववरोधसुन्दरी ||११||` | "The beautiful lady of the inner chambers delighted him with her affection during times of recreation. ||11||" |

| `Line 5125: ४१` | "41" |
| `Line 5126: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5127: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5128: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5129: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5130: एतस्मिन्नेव काले तु जरत्कारुर्महातपाः |` | "At this very time, Jaratkāru of great austerities," |
| `Line 5131: चचार पृथिवीं कृत्स्नां यत्रसायङ्गृहो मुनिः ||१||` | "Wandered over the entire earth, the sage who had no home except where evening found him. ||1||" |
| `Line 5132: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5133: चरन्दीक्षां महातेजा दुश्चरामकृतात्मभिः |` | "Observing a vow difficult to perform by those of undisciplined minds, that greatly radiant one," |
| `Line 5134: तीर्थेष्वाप्लवनं कुर्वन्पुण्येषु विचचार ह ||२||` | "Bathing in sacred waters [tīrthas], wandered through holy places. ||2||" |
| `Line 5135: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5136: वायुभक्षो निराहारः शुष्यन्नहरहर्मुनिः |` | "Subsisting on air, without food, the sage growing drier day by day," |
| `Line 5137: स ददर्श पितृन्गर्ते लम्बमानानधोमुखान् ||३||` | "He saw his ancestors hanging in a pit, head downward. ||3||" |
| `Line 5138: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5139: एकतन्त्ववशिष्टं वै वीरणस्तम्बमाश्रितान् |` | "They were hanging by a single remaining thread, clinging to a clump of kusa grass [vīraṇa]," |
| `Line 5140: तं च तन्तुं शनैराखुमाददानं बिलाश्रयम् ||४||` | "And that thread was slowly being gnawed by a rat dwelling in a hole. ||4||" |
| `Line 5141: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5142: निराहारान्कृशान्दीनान्गर्तेऽऽर्तांस्त्राणमिच्छतः |` | "They were without food, emaciated, miserable, distressed in the pit, desiring rescue," |
| `Line 5143: उपसृत्य स तान्दीनान्दीनरूपोऽभ्यभाषत ||५||` | "Approaching those wretched ones, he, with a compassionate appearance, spoke to them. ||5||" |
| `Line 5144: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5145: के भवन्तोऽवलम्बन्ते वीरणस्तम्बमाश्रिताः |` | "Who are you who hang clinging to this clump of kusa grass," |
| `Line 5146: दुर्बलं खादितैर्मूलैराखुना बिलवासिना ||६||` | "Weakened by its roots being eaten by the rat dwelling in the hole? ||6||" |
| `Line 5147: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5148: वीरणस्तम्बके मूलं यदप्येकमिह स्थितम् |` | "Even the single root that remains here in this clump of kusa grass," |
| `Line 5149: तदप्ययं शनैराखुरादत्ते दशनैः शितैः ||७||` | "Even that this rat is slowly gnawing away with its sharp teeth. ||7||" |
| `Line 5150: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5151: छेत्स्यतेऽल्पावशिष्टत्वादेतदप्यचिरादिव |` | "It will be cut soon, as very little of it remains," |
| `Line 5152: ततः स्थ पतितारोऽत्र गर्ते अस्मिन्नधोमुखाः ||८||` | "Then you will fall headlong into this pit. ||8||" |
| `Line 5153: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5154: ततो मे दुःखमुत्पन्नं दृष्ट्वा युष्मानधोमुखान् |` | "Therefore, grief has arisen in me seeing you hanging head-downward," |
| `Line 5155: कृच्छ्रामापदमापन्नान्प्रियं किं करवाणि वः ||९||` | "Having fallen into this dire calamity. What pleasing thing may I do for you? ||9||" |
| `Line 5156: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5157: तपसोऽस्य चतुर्थेन तृतीयेनापि वा पुनः |` | "With a fourth of my austerities, or even with a third," |
| `Line 5158: अर्धेन वापि निस्तर्तुमापदं ब्रूत माचिरम् ||१०||` | "Or even with half, to rescue you from this calamity—tell me quickly. ||10||" |
| `Line 5159: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5160: अथवापि समग्रेण तरन्तु तपसा मम |` | "Or even with all of my austerities, may you all be rescued," |
| `Line 5161: भवन्तः सर्व एवास्मात्काममेवं विधीयताम् ||११||` | "Let it be done according to your desire. ||11||" |
| `Line 5162: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5163: पितर ऊचुः||` | "The ancestors [pitrs] said:" |
| `Line 5164: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5165: ऋद्धो भवान्ब्रह्मचारी यो नस्त्रातुमिहेच्छति |` | "Prosperous are you, O celibate [brahmachari], who wishes to rescue us here," |
| `Line 5166: न तु विप्राग्र्य तपसा शक्यमेतद्व्यपोहितुम् ||१२||` | "But, O foremost of Brahmins, this cannot be removed by austerities. ||12||" |
| `Line 5167: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5168: अस्ति नस्तात तपसः फलं प्रवदतां वर |` | "We have, dear son, the fruit of austerities, O best of speakers," |
| `Line 5169: सन्तानप्रक्षयाद्ब्रह्मन्पतामो निरयेऽशुचौ ||१३||` | "But due to the extinction of our lineage, O Brahmin, we are falling into an impure hell. ||13||" |
| `Line 5170: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5171: लम्बतामिह नस्तात न ज्ञानं प्रतिभाति वै |` | "As we hang here, dear son, our consciousness is indeed not clear," |
| `Line 5172: येन त्वां नाभिजानीमो लोके विख्यातपौरुषम् ||१४||` | "Due to which we do not recognize you, who is renowned for prowess in the world. ||14||" |
| `Line 5173: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5174: ऋद्धो भवान्महाभागो यो नः शोच्यान्सुदुःखितान् |` | "Prosperous are you, O fortunate one, who out of compassion," |
| `Line 5175: शोचस्युपेत्य कारुण्याच्छृणु ये वै वयं द्विज ||१५||` | "Grieves for us who are pitiable and greatly distressed. Listen to who we are, O twice-born [Brahmin]. ||15||" |
| `Line 5176: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5177: यायावरा नाम वयमृषयः संशितव्रताः |` | "We are sages called Yāyāvara [wandering ascetics], of strict vows," |
| `Line 5178: लोकात्पुण्यादिह भ्रष्टाः सन्तानप्रक्षयाद्विभो ||१६||` | "Fallen from the virtuous world to this place due to the extinction of our lineage, O mighty one. ||16||" |
| `Line 5179: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5180: प्रनष्टं नस्तपः पुण्यं न हि नस्तन्तुरस्ति वै |` | "Our ascetic merit is destroyed, for we truly have no lineage continuation," |
| `Line 5181: अस्ति त्वेकोऽद्य नस्तन्तुः सोऽपि नास्ति यथा तथा ||१७||` | "There is only one thread [descendant] of our line today, but he too is as good as non-existent. ||17||" |
| `Line 5182: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5183: मन्दभाग्योऽल्पभाग्यानां बन्धुः स किल नः कुले |` | "That unfortunate relative in our family of ill-fated ones," |
| `Line 5184: जरत्कारुरिति ख्यातो वेदवेदाङ्गपारगः ||१८||` | "Is known as Jaratkāru, master of the Vedas and Vedāṅgas [auxiliary texts]. ||18||" |
| `Line 5185: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5186: नियतात्मा महात्मा च सुव्रतः सुमहातपाः ||१८||` | "Self-controlled, noble-souled, of excellent vows, and of great austerities. ||18||" |
| `Line 5187: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5188: तेन स्म तपसो लोभात्कृच्छ्रमापादिता वयम् |` | "Due to his obsession with austerities, we have been brought to this miserable state," |
| `Line 5189: न तस्य भार्या पुत्रो वा बान्धवो वास्ति कश्चन ||१९||` | "He has neither wife, nor son, nor any relative whatsoever. ||19||" |
| `Line 5190: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5191: तस्माल्लम्बामहे गर्ते नष्टसञ्ज्ञा ह्यनाथवत् |` | "Therefore we hang in this pit, unconscious and helpless," |
| `Line 5192: स वक्तव्यस्त्वया दृष्ट्वा अस्माकं नाथवत्तया ||२०||` | "He should be told by you upon seeing him, as our protector. ||20||" |
| `Line 5193: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5194: पितरस्तेऽवलम्बन्ते गर्ते दीना अधोमुखाः |` | "Your forefathers hang in a pit, wretched and facing downward," |
| `Line 5195: साधु दारान्कुरुष्वेति प्रजायस्वेति चाभिभो ||२१||` | "'Please take a wife and produce offspring,' O powerful one. ||21||" |
| `Line 5196: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5197: कुलतन्तुर्हि नः शिष्टस्त्वमेवैकस्तपोधन ||२१||` | "For you alone remain as the thread of our family, O wealth of austerities [ascetic]. ||21||" |
| `Line 5198: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5199: यं तु पश्यसि नो ब्रह्मन्वीरणस्तम्बमाश्रितान् |` | "The reed grass clump you see us clinging to, O Brahmin," |
| `Line 5200: एषोऽस्माकं कुलस्तम्ब आसीत्स्वकुलवर्धनः ||२२||` | "This was the pillar of our family, once increasing our lineage. ||22||" |
| `Line 5201: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5202: यानि पश्यसि वै ब्रह्मन्मूलानीहास्य वीरुधः |` | "O Brahmin, these roots of this creeper that you see here," |
| `Line 5203: एते नस्तन्तवस्तात कालेन परिभक्षिताः ||२३||` | "These are our lifelines, dear one, being gradually consumed by Time [personified]. ||23||" |
| `Line 5204: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5205: यत्त्वेतत्पश्यसि ब्रह्मन्मूलमस्यार्धभक्षितम् |` | "And this root that you see, O Brahmin, half-eaten," |
| `Line 5206: तत्र लम्बामहे सर्वे सोऽप्येकस्तप आस्थितः ||२४||` | "On that we all hang, while that one [Jaratkaru] is engaged in austerities alone. ||24||" |
| `Line 5207: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5208: यमाखुं पश्यसि ब्रह्मन्काल एष महाबलः |` | "This rat that you see, O Brahmin, is Time [death personified], of great power," |
| `Line 5209: स तं तपोरतं मन्दं शनैः क्षपयते तुदन् ||२५||` | "It slowly gnaws away at him who is engaged in austerities, that slow-witted one. ||25||" |
| `Line 5210: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5211: जरत्कारुं तपोलुब्धं मन्दात्मानमचेतसम् ||२५||` | "Jaratkaru, who is obsessed with austerities, slow-minded and thoughtless. ||25||" |
| `Line 5212: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5213: न हि नस्तत्तपस्तस्य तारयिष्यति सत्तम |` | "Indeed, his austerities will not save us, O excellent one," |
| `Line 5214: छिन्नमूलान्परिभ्रष्टान्कालोपहतचेतसः ||२६||` | "With our roots cut, fallen down, our minds destroyed by Time [death]. ||26||" |
| `Line 5215: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5216: नरकप्रतिष्ठान्पश्यास्मान्यथा दुष्कृतिनस्तथा ||२६||` | "See us destined for hell, like evil-doers. ||26||" |
| `Line 5217: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5218: अस्मासु पतितेष्वत्र सह पूर्वैः पितामहैः |` | "When we have fallen here along with our forefathers," |
| `Line 5219: छिन्नः कालेन सोऽप्यत्र गन्ता वै नरकं ततः ||२७||` | "Cut off by Time [death], he too will then go to hell. ||27||" |
| `Line 5220: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5221: तपो वाप्यथवा यज्ञो यच्चान्यत्पावनं महत् |` | "Austerities, or sacrifices, or any other great purifying act," |
| `Line 5222: तत्सर्वं न समं तात सन्तत्येति सतां मतम् ||२८||` | "All that is not equal to progeny, dear one - this is the opinion of the virtuous. ||28||" |
| `Line 5223: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5224: स तात दृष्ट्वा ब्रूयास्त्वं जरत्कारुं तपस्विनम् |` | "Having seen this, dear one, you should tell the ascetic Jaratkaru," |
| `Line 5225: यथादृष्टमिदं चास्मै त्वयाख्येयमशेषतः ||२९||` | "This should be related to him by you completely, exactly as seen. ||29||" |
| `Line 5226: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5227: यथा दारान्प्रकुर्यात्स पुत्रांश्चोत्पादयेद्यथा |` | "How he should take a wife and how he should beget sons," |
| `Line 5228: तथा ब्रह्मंस्त्वया वाच्यः सोऽस्माकं नाथवत्तया ||३०||` | "Thus, O Brahmin [sage], you should tell him, for he is like a protector to us. ||30||" |

| `Line 5238: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5239: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5240: एतच्छ्रुत्वा जरत्कारुर्दुःखशोकपरायणः |` | "Hearing this, Jaratkāru, overwhelmed with grief and sorrow," |
| `Line 5241: उवाच स्वान्पितृन्दुःखाद्बाष्पसंदिग्धया गिरा ||१||` | "Spoke to his forefathers with a voice choked with tears due to sorrow. ||1||" |
| `Line 5242: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5244: तद्दण्डं धारयत मे दुष्कृतेरकृतात्मनः ||२||` | "Therefore, impose punishment on me, the evil-doer with an undisciplined self. ||2||" |
| `Line 5245: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5246: पितर ऊचुः||` | "The forefathers said:" |
| `Line 5247: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5248: पुत्र दिष्ट्यासि सम्प्राप्त इमं देशं यदृच्छया |` | "Son, fortunately you have arrived at this place by chance," |
| `Line 5249: किमर्थं च त्वया ब्रह्मन्न कृतो दारसङ्ग्रहः ||३||` | "But why, O Brahmin [sage], have you not taken a wife? ||3||" |
| `Line 5250: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5251: जरत्कारुरुवाच||` | "Jaratkāru said:" |
| `Line 5252: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5253: ममायं पितरो नित्यं हृद्यर्थः परिवर्तते |` | "O forefathers, this desire constantly revolves in my heart:" |
| `Line 5254: ऊर्ध्वरेताः शरीरं वै प्रापयेयममुत्र वै ||४||` | "That I should carry this body to the other world as one with preserved seed [celibate]. ||4||" |
| `Line 5255: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5256: एवं दृष्ट्वा तु भवतः शकुन्तानिव लम्बतः |` | "But having seen you hanging like birds," |
| `Line 5257: मया निवर्तिता बुद्धिर्ब्रह्मचर्यात्पितामहाः ||५||` | "My mind has been turned away from celibacy, O grandfathers. ||5||" |
| `Line 5258: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5259: करिष्ये वः प्रियं कामं निवेक्ष्ये नात्र संशयः |` | "I will fulfill your dear wish and will marry, there is no doubt about this," |
| `Line 5260: सनाम्नीं यद्यहं कन्यामुपलप्स्ये कदाचन ||६||` | "If I ever find a maiden who bears the same name as mine. ||6||" |
| `Line 5261: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5262: भविष्यति च या काचिद्भैक्षवत्स्वयमुद्यता |` | "And whoever she may be, she should come forward herself like alms," |
| `Line 5263: प्रतिग्रहीता तामस्मि न भरेयं च यामहम् ||७||` | "I will accept her, and she should be one whom I need not maintain. ||7||" |
| `Line 5264: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5265: एवंविधमहं कुर्यां निवेशं प्राप्नुयां यदि |` | "I would enter into such a marriage if I could obtain it," |
| `Line 5266: अन्यथा न करिष्ये तु सत्यमेतत्पितामहाः ||८||` | "Otherwise I will not do so; this is the truth, O grandfathers. ||8||" |
| `Line 5267: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5268: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5269: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5270: एवमुक्त्वा तु स पितृंश्चचार पृथिवीं मुनिः |` | "Having spoken thus to his forefathers, the sage wandered over the earth," |
| `Line 5271: न च स्म लभते भार्यां वृद्धोऽयमिति शौनक ||९||` | "But he did not find a wife, being considered old, O Śaunaka. ||9||" |
| `Line 5272: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5273: यदा निर्वेदमापन्नः पितृभिश्चोदितस्तथा |` | "When he became despondent, and was thus urged by his forefathers," |
| `Line 5274: तदारण्यं स गत्वोच्चैश्चुक्रोश भृशदुःखितः ||१०||` | "Then, going to the forest, he cried out loudly, deeply distressed. ||10||" |
| `Line 5275: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5276: यानि भूतानि सन्तीह स्थावराणि चराणि च |` | "Whatever beings exist here, both immovable and movable," |
| `Line 5277: अन्तर्हितानि वा यानि तानि शृण्वन्तु मे वचः ||११||` | "Or those that are hidden, let them all hear my words. ||11||" |
| `Line 5278: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5279: उग्रे तपसि वर्तन्तं पितरश्चोदयन्ति माम् |` | "While I was engaged in severe austerities, my ancestors [departed forefathers] urged me," |
| `Line 5280: निविशस्वेति दुःखार्तास्तेषां प्रियचिकीर्षया ||१२||` | "'Settle down,' they said, afflicted with sorrow. Desiring to please them, ||12||" |
| `Line 5281: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5282: निवेशार्थ्यखिलां भूमिं कन्याभैक्षं चरामि भोः |` | "For the purpose of marriage, I wander the entire earth seeking a maiden as alms, O sirs!" |
| `Line 5283: दरिद्रो दुःखशीलश्च पितृभिः संनियोजितः ||१३||` | "Poor and sorrowful, commissioned by my ancestors. ||13||" |
| `Line 5284: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5285: यस्य कन्यास्ति भूतस्य ये मयेह प्रकीर्तिताः |` | "Whichever being has a daughter among those I have addressed here," |
| `Line 5286: ते मे कन्यां प्रयच्छन्तु चरतः सर्वतोदिशम् ||१४||` | "Let them give me their daughter as I wander in all directions. ||14||" |
| `Line 5287: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5288: मम कन्या सनाम्नी या भैक्षवच्चोद्यता भवेत् |` | "A maiden who has the same name as mine, who would be offered like alms," |
| `Line 5289: भरेयं चैव यां नाहं तां मे कन्यां प्रयच्छत ||१५||` | "And whom I would not have to maintain—give me such a maiden. ||15||" |
| `Line 5290: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5291: ततस्ते पन्नगा ये वै जरत्कारौ समाहिताः |` | "Then those serpents [nāgas] who were intent on Jaratkāru," |
| `Line 5292: तामादाय प्रवृत्तिं ते वासुकेः प्रत्यवेदयन् ||१६||` | "Taking this information, reported it to Vāsuki [serpent king]. ||16||" |
| `Line 5293: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5294: तेषां श्रुत्वा स नागेन्द्रः कन्यां तां समलङ्कृताम् |` | "Hearing them, that lord of serpents, taking his well-adorned daughter," |
| `Line 5295: प्रगृह्यारण्यमगमत्समीपं तस्य पन्नगः ||१७||` | "Went to the forest, near that sage, the serpent [Vāsuki]. ||17||" |
| `Line 5296: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5297: तत्र तां भैक्षवत्कन्यां प्रादात्तस्मै महात्मने |` | "There, he offered that maiden like alms to that great soul," |
| `Line 5298: नागेन्द्रो वासुकिर्ब्रह्मन्न स तां प्रत्यगृह्णत ||१८||` | "Vāsuki, the lord of serpents, O Brahman, but he [Jaratkāru] did not accept her. ||18||" |
| `Line 5299: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5300: असनामेति वै मत्वा भरणे चाविचारिते |` | "Thinking that she was not of the same name, and also not considering the matter of maintenance," |
| `Line 5301: मोक्षभावे स्थितश्चापि द्वन्द्वीभूतः परिग्रहे ||१९||` | "Though established in the state of liberation, he became conflicted about accepting a wife. ||19||" |
| `Line 5302: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5303: ततो नाम स कन्यायाः पप्रच्छ भृगुनन्दन |` | "Then, O descendant of Bhrigu [sage lineage], he asked the name of the maiden," |
| `Line 5304: वासुके भरणं चास्या न कुर्यामित्युवाच ह ||२०||` | "And said to Vāsuki [serpent king], 'I shall not provide for her maintenance.' ||20||" |
