| `Line 5313: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5314: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5315: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5316: वासुकिस्त्वब्रवीद्वाक्यं जरत्कारुमृषिं तदा |` | "Then Vāsuki spoke these words to the sage Jaratkāru," |
| `Line 5317: सनामा तव कन्येयं स्वसा मे तपसान्विता ||१||` | "This maiden, my sister, endowed with austerities, has the same name as yours. ||1||" |
| `Line 5318: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5319: भरिष्यामि च ते भार्यां प्रतीच्छेमां द्विजोत्तम |` | "I shall maintain your wife; accept her, O best of the twice-born [Brahmin]," |
| `Line 5320: रक्षणं च करिष्येऽस्याः सर्वशक्त्या तपोधन ||२||` | "And I shall protect her with all my power, O wealth of austerities [ascetic sage]. ||2||" |
| `Line 5321: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5322: प्रतिश्रुते तु नागेन भरिष्ये भगिनीमिति |` | "When the serpent promised, 'I shall maintain my sister,'" |
| `Line 5323: जरत्कारुस्तदा वेश्म भुजगस्य जगाम ह ||३||` | "Then Jaratkāru went to the dwelling of the serpent. ||3||" |
| `Line 5324: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5325: तत्र मन्त्रविदां श्रेष्ठस्तपोवृद्धो महाव्रतः |` | "There, the foremost among knowers of mantras, advanced in austerities and of great vows," |
| `Line 5326: जग्राह पाणिं धर्मात्मा विधिमन्त्रपुरस्कृतम् ||४||` | "The righteous-souled one took her hand with proper mantras and rituals. ||4||" |
| `Line 5327: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5328: ततो वासगृहं शुभ्रं पन्नगेन्द्रस्य संमतम् |` | "Then to a bright dwelling place, approved by the serpent-lord [Vāsuki]," |
| `Line 5329: जगाम भार्यामादाय स्तूयमानो महर्षिभिः ||५||` | "He went, taking his wife, being praised by the great sages. ||5||" |
| `Line 5330: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5331: शयनं तत्र वै कॢप्तं स्पर्ध्यास्तरणसंवृतम् |` | "A bed was arranged there, covered with enviable bedding," |
| `Line 5332: तत्र भार्यासहायः स जरत्कारुरुवास ह ||६||` | "There Jaratkāru dwelt with his wife as his companion. ||6||" |
| `Line 5333: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5334: स तत्र समयं चक्रे भार्यया सह सत्तमः |` | "That excellent one made an agreement there with his wife," |
| `Line 5335: विप्रियं मे न कर्तव्यं न च वाच्यं कदाचन ||७||` | "'Nothing unpleasant should be done to me, nor should anything disagreeable ever be said. ||7||'" |
| `Line 5336: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5337: त्यजेयमप्रिये हि त्वां कृते वासं च ते गृहे |` | "'I would abandon you if anything unpleasant is done, and also my residence in your house,'" |
| `Line 5338: एतद्गृहाण वचनं मया यत्समुदीरितम् ||८||` | "'Accept these words that have been uttered by me.' ||8||" |
| `Line 5339: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5340: ततः परमसंविग्ना स्वसा नागपतेस्तु सा |` | "Then, extremely anxious, that sister of the serpent-lord [Vāsuki]," |
| `Line 5341: अतिदुःखान्विता वाचं तमुवाचैवमस्त्विति ||९||` | "Filled with great distress, said to him, 'Let it be so.' ||9||" |
| `Line 5342: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5343: तथैव सा च भर्तारं दुःखशीलमुपाचरत् |` | "And she served her husband, who was of a melancholy disposition," |
| `Line 5344: उपायैः श्वेतकाकीयैः प्रियकामा यशस्विनी ||१०||` | "With śvetakākīya methods [rare, special care], the illustrious one desiring to please him. ||10||" |
| `Line 5345: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5346: ऋतुकाले ततः स्नाता कदाचिद्वासुकेः स्वसा |` | "Then once, having bathed at the proper time [for conception], Vāsuki's sister," |
| `Line 5347: भर्तारं तं यथान्यायमुपतस्थे महामुनिम् ||११||` | "Approached her husband, the great sage, according to proper custom. ||11||" |
| `Line 5348: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5349: तत्र तस्याः समभवद्गर्भो ज्वलनसंनिभः |` | "There in her was conceived an embryo resembling fire," |
| `Line 5350: अतीव तपसा युक्तो वैश्वानरसमद्युतिः ||१२||` | "Endowed with great austerity, with radiance equal to Vaiśvānara [fire deity]. ||12||" |
| `Line 5351: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5352: शुक्लपक्षे यथा सोमो व्यवर्धत तथैव सः ||१२||` | "Just as the moon waxes during the bright fortnight [śuklapakṣa], so did he grow. ||12||" |
| `Line 5353: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5354: ततः कतिपयाहस्य जरत्कारुर्महातपाः |` | "Then after several days, Jaratkāru of great austerities [mahātapāḥ]," |
| `Line 5355: उत्सङ्गेऽस्याः शिरः कृत्वा सुष्वाप परिखिन्नवत् ||१३||` | "Placing his head on her lap, fell asleep as if exhausted. ||13||" |
| `Line 5356: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5357: तस्मिंश्च सुप्ते विप्रेन्द्रे सवितास्तमियाद्गिरिम् |` | "And while that foremost of Brahmins [viprendraḥ] was asleep, the sun was setting behind the mountain," |
| `Line 5358: अह्नः परिक्षये ब्रह्मंस्ततः साचिन्तयत्तदा ||१४||` | "At the end of the day, O Brahman, then she began to think. ||14||" |
| `Line 5359: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5360: वासुकेर्भगिनी भीता धर्मलोपान्मनस्विनी ||१४||` | "Vāsuki's sister, thoughtful and afraid of a violation of dharma [dharmalopa]. ||14||" |
| `Line 5361: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5362: किं नु मे सुकृतं भूयाद्भर्तुरुत्थापनं न वा |` | "What would be the right thing for me to do—to wake my husband or not?" |
| `Line 5363: दुःखशीलो हि धर्मात्मा कथं नास्यापराध्नुयाम् ||१५||` | "For he is righteous but easily disturbed—how might I not offend him? ||15||" |
| `Line 5364: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5365: कोपो वा धर्मशीलस्य धर्मलोपोऽथ वा पुनः |` | "Either the anger of this righteous one, or else the violation of dharma," |
| `Line 5366: धर्मलोपो गरीयान्वै स्यादत्रेत्यकरोन्मनः ||१६||` | "The violation of dharma would be more serious—thus she made up her mind. ||16||" |
| `Line 5367: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5368: उत्थापयिष्ये यद्येनं ध्रुवं कोपं करिष्यति |` | "If I wake him, he will surely become angry," |
| `Line 5369: धर्मलोपो भवेदस्य सन्ध्यातिक्रमणे ध्रुवम् ||१७||` | "But if the evening prayer time [sandhyā] passes, there will certainly be a violation of his dharma. ||17||" |
| `Line 5370: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5371: इति निश्चित्य मनसा जरत्कारुर्भुजङ्गमा |` | "Having thus decided in her mind, Jaratkāru of the serpent race [bhujaṅgamā]," |
| `Line 5372: तमृषिं दीप्ततपसं शयानमनलोपमम् ||१८||` | "To that sage of blazing austerities, who was sleeping, resembling fire [anala]," ||18||" |
| `Line 5373: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5374: उवाचेदं वचः श्लक्ष्णं ततो मधुरभाषिणी ||१८||` | "She then spoke these gentle words, that sweet-speaking one. ||18||" |
| `Line 5375: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5376: उत्तिष्ठ त्वं महाभाग सूर्योऽस्तमुपगच्छति |` | "Rise up, O fortunate one [blessed sage], the sun is setting." |
| `Line 5377: सन्ध्यामुपास्स्व भगवन्नपः स्पृष्ट्वा यतव्रतः ||१९||` | "O lord, perform your evening prayers after touching water, as one who observes strict vows. ||19||" |
| `Line 5378: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5379: प्रादुष्कृताग्निहोत्रोऽयं मुहूर्तो रम्यदारुणः |` | "This is the time for performing Agnihotra [fire ritual], a beautiful reddish moment," |
| `Line 5380: सन्ध्या प्रवर्तते चेयं पश्चिमायां दिशि प्रभो ||२०||` | "And this twilight proceeds in the western direction, O master. ||20||" |
| `Line 5381: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5382: एवमुक्तः स भगवाञ्जरत्कारुर्महातपाः |` | "Thus addressed, that venerable Jaratkāru of great austerities," |
| `Line 5383: भार्यां प्रस्फुरमाणोष्ठ इदं वचनमब्रवीत् ||२१||` | "With quivering lips, spoke these words to his wife. ||21||" |
| `Line 5384: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5385: अवमानः प्रयुक्तोऽयं त्वया मम भुजङ्गमे |` | "This disrespect has been shown to me by you, O serpent woman," |
| `Line 5386: समीपे ते न वत्स्यामि गमिष्यामि यथागतम् ||२२||` | "I shall not dwell near you; I shall depart as I came. ||22||" |
| `Line 5387: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5388: न हि तेजोऽस्ति वामोरु मयि सुप्ते विभावसोः |` | "O beautiful-thighed one, the sun [fire deity] has no power to set," |
| `Line 5389: अस्तं गन्तुं यथाकालमिति मे हृदि वर्तते ||२३||` | "At its appointed time while I am asleep - this is what I believe in my heart. ||23||" |
| `Line 5390: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5391: न चाप्यवमतस्येह वस्तुं रोचेत कस्यचित् |` | "And it would not please anyone who is disrespected to continue staying here," |
| `Line 5392: किं पुनर्धर्मशीलस्य मम वा मद्विधस्य वा ||२४||` | "How much less for one devoted to dharma [righteousness] like me or those like me? ||24||" |
| `Line 5393: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5395: अब्रवीद्भगिनी तत्र वासुकेः संनिवेशने ||२५||` | "The sister of Vāsuki spoke there in Vāsuki's dwelling. ||25||" |
| `Line 5396: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5397: नावमानात्कृतवती तवाहं प्रतिबोधनम् |` | "I did not wake you up out of disrespect," |
| `Line 5398: धर्मलोपो न ते विप्र स्यादित्येतत्कृतं मया ||२६||` | "I did this so that you, O Brahmin, would not neglect your religious duty. ||26||" |
| `Line 5399: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5400: उवाच भार्यामित्युक्तो जरत्कारुर्महातपाः |` | "Thus addressed, Jaratkāru of great austerities said to his wife," |
| `Line 5401: ऋषिः कोपसमाविष्टस्त्यक्तुकामो भुजङ्गमाम् ||२७||` | "The sage, filled with anger, desired to leave the serpent woman [Nāga wife]. ||27||" |
| `Line 5402: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5403: न मे वागनृतं प्राह गमिष्येऽहं भुजङ्गमे |` | "My speech has never uttered falsehood. I shall depart, O serpent woman," |
| `Line 5404: समयो ह्येष मे पूर्वं त्वया सह मिथः कृतः ||२८||` | "For this was the agreement previously made between us mutually. ||28||" |
| `Line 5405: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5406: सुखमस्म्युषितो भद्रे ब्रूयास्त्वं भ्रातरं शुभे |` | "I have dwelt happily here, O auspicious one. Tell your brother, O beautiful one," |
| `Line 5407: इतो मयि गते भीरु गतः स भगवानिति ||२९||` | "'After he left from here, O timid one, that venerable one has gone.' ||29||" |
| `Line 5408: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5409: त्वं चापि मयि निष्क्रान्ते न शोकं कर्तुमर्हसि ||२९||` | "And you too, after I have departed, should not grieve. ||29||" |
| `Line 5410: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5411: इत्युक्ता सानवद्याङ्गी प्रत्युवाच पतिं तदा |` | "Thus addressed, she of faultless limbs replied then to her husband," |
| `Line 5412: जरत्कारुं जरत्कारुश्चिन्ताशोकपरायणा ||३०||` | "Jaratkāru to Jaratkāru, she being overcome with anxiety and sorrow. ||30||" |
| `Line 5413: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5414: बाष्पगद्गदया वाचा मुखेन परिशुष्यता |` | "With a voice choked with tears and with a parched mouth," |
| `Line 5415: कृताञ्जलिर्वरारोहा पर्यश्रुनयना ततः ||३१||` | "With folded hands, the beautiful woman, with eyes filled with tears, then ||31||" |
| `Line 5416: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5418: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5419: न मामर्हसि धर्मज्ञ परित्यक्तुमनागसम् |` | "You ought not, O knower of dharma, to abandon me who am innocent," |
| `Line 5420: धर्मे स्थितां स्थितो धर्मे सदा प्रियहिते रताम् ||३२||` | "Me who is established in dharma, as you are established in dharma, always devoted to what is dear and beneficial. ||32||" |

| `Line 5423: तदलब्धवतीं मन्दां किं मां वक्ष्यति वासुखिः ||३३||` | "Not having achieved that, what will the unhappy one [Vāsuki] say to me, unfortunate as I am? ||33||" |
| `Line 5424: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5427: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5430: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5432: इममव्यक्तरूपं मे गर्भमाधाय सत्तम ||३६||` | "Place in me this unmanifested form of a child, O excellent one. ||36||" |

| `Line 5460: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5478: ` | [Blank line] |

| `Line 5480: आश्वासयन्ती सन्तप्तं वासुकिं पन्नगेश्वरम् ||९||` | "Consoling the distressed Vāsuki, the lord of serpents [nāga king]. ||9||" |

| `Line 5483: अस्तीत्युदरमुद्दिश्य ममेदं गतवांश्च सः ||१०||` | "Said 'It exists,' pointing to my womb, and then he departed. ||10||" |

| `Line 5489: उत्पत्स्यति हि ते पुत्रो ज्वलनार्कसमद्युतिः ||१२||` | "For a son will be born to you with radiance equal to fire and the sun. ||12||" |

| `Line 5492: तस्माद्व्येतु परं दुःखं तवेदं मनसि स्थितम् ||१३||` | "Therefore, let this extreme sorrow that dwells in your mind depart. ||13||" |

| `Line 5554: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5562: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5567: सुदर्शः सर्वभूतानामासीत्सोम इवापरः ||१०||` | "Pleasing to behold by all beings, he was like another Soma [moon deity]. ||10||" |
| `Line 5568: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5570: धनुर्वेदे च शिष्योऽभून्नृपः शारद्वतस्य सः ||११||` | "In archery, that king was a disciple of Sharadwata [sage teacher]. ||11||" |
| `Line 5571: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5573: लोकस्य चैव सर्वस्य प्रिय आसीन्महायशाः ||१२||` | "And dear to all the world was that highly renowned one. ||12||" |
| `Line 5574: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5575: परिक्षीणेषु कुरुषु उत्तरायामजायत |` | "When the Kurus were nearly extinct, he was born to Uttara [princess]," |
| `Line 5576: परिक्षिदभवत्तेन सौभद्रस्यात्मजो बली ||१३||` | "From him was born Parikshit, the mighty son of Subhadra's son [Abhimanyu]. ||13||" |
| `Line 5577: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5578: राजधर्मार्थकुशलो युक्तः सर्वगुणैर्नृपः |` | "The king was skilled in royal duty and wealth, endowed with all virtues," |
| `Line 5579: जितेन्द्रियश्चात्मवांश्च मेधावी वृद्धसेवितः ||१४||` | "With conquered senses, self-controlled, intelligent, and attended by the elders. ||14||" |
| `Line 5580: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5581: षड्वर्गविन्महाबुद्धिर्नीतिधर्मविदुत्तमः |` | "Knower of the six enemies [sensory passions], of great intellect, supreme knower of ethics and righteousness," |
| `Line 5582: प्रजा इमास्तव पिता षष्टिं वर्षाण्यपालयत् ||१५||` | "Your father protected these subjects for sixty years. ||15||" |
| `Line 5583: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5584: ततो दिष्टान्तमापन्नः सर्पेणानतिवर्तितम् ||१५||` | "Then he met his destined end, unavoidable, by a serpent. ||15||" |
| `Line 5585: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5586: ततस्त्वं पुरुषश्रेष्ठ धर्मेण प्रतिपेदिवान् |` | "Then you, O best of men, righteously obtained," |
| `Line 5587: इदं वर्षसहस्राय राज्यं कुरुकुलागतम् ||१६||` | "This kingdom descended from the Kuru lineage, for a thousand years. ||16||" |
| `Line 5588: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5589: बाल एवाभिजातोऽसि सर्वभूतानुपालकः ||१६||` | "Even as a youth, you were born noble, a protector of all beings. ||16||" |
| `Line 5590: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5591: जनमेजय उवाच||` | "Janamejaya said:" |
| `Line 5592: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5593: नास्मिन्कुले जातु बभूव राजा; यो न प्रजानां हितकृत्प्रियश्च |` | "Never in this family was there a king who was not a benefactor and beloved of his subjects," |
| `Line 5594: विशेषतः प्रेक्ष्य पितामहानां; वृत्तं महद्वृत्तपरायणानाम् ||१७||` | "Especially considering the conduct of my ancestors, who were devoted to noble behavior. ||17||" |
| `Line 5595: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5596: कथं निधनमापन्नः पिता मम तथाविधः |` | "How did my father, being of such nature, meet his death?" |
| `Line 5597: आचक्षध्वं यथावन्मे श्रोतुमिच्छामि तत्त्वतः ||१८||` | "Tell me properly, I wish to hear the truth. ||18||" |
| `Line 5598: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5599: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta said:" |
| `Line 5600: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5601: एवं सञ्चोदिता राज्ञा मन्त्रिणस्ते नराधिपम् |` | "Thus urged by the king, those ministers addressed the ruler," |
| `Line 5602: ऊचुः सर्वे यथावृत्तं राज्ञः प्रियहिते रताः ||१९||` | "All of them narrated the events as they occurred, devoted to the welfare and good of the king. ||19||" |
| `Line 5603: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5604: बभूव मृगयाशीलस्तव राजन्पिता सदा |` | "Your father, O king, was always fond of hunting," |
| `Line 5605: यथा पाण्डुर्महाभागो धनुर्धरवरो युधि ||२०||` | "Just like the illustrious Pandu [Pandava father], the foremost archer in battle. ||20||" |
| `Line 5606: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5607: अस्मास्वासज्य सर्वाणि राजकार्याण्यशेषतः ||२०||` | "Having entrusted to us all royal duties completely. ||20||" |
| `Line 5608: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5609: स कदाचिद्वनचरो मृगं विव्याध पत्रिणा |` | "Once while roaming in the forest, he pierced a deer with an arrow," |
| `Line 5610: विद्ध्वा चान्वसरत्तूर्णं तं मृगं गहने वने ||२१||` | "And after shooting it, he quickly pursued that deer in the dense forest. ||21||" |
| `Line 5611: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5612: पदातिर्बद्धनिस्त्रिंशस्ततायुधकलापवान् |` | "On foot, with sword fastened and quiver of arrows strapped," |
| `Line 5613: न चाससाद गहने मृगं नष्टं पिता तव ||२२||` | "Your father could not find the lost deer in the dense forest. ||22||" |
| `Line 5614: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5615: परिश्रान्तो वयःस्थश्च षष्टिवर्षो जरान्वितः |` | "Exhausted, advanced in age, sixty years old and affected by old age," |
| `Line 5616: क्षुधितः स महारण्ये ददर्श मुनिमन्तिके ||२३||` | "Hungry, he saw a sage nearby in the great forest. ||23||" |
| `Line 5617: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5618: स तं पप्रच्छ राजेन्द्रो मुनिं मौनव्रतान्वितम् |` | "That king [your father] asked the sage who was observing a vow of silence," |
| `Line 5619: न च किञ्चिदुवाचैनं स मुनिः पृच्छतोऽपि सन् ||२४||` | "But that sage did not say anything to him, even though he was being questioned. ||24||" |
| `Line 5620: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5621: ततो राजा क्षुच्छ्रमार्तस्तं मुनिं स्थाणुवत्स्थितम् |` | "Then the king, afflicted by hunger and fatigue, seeing that sage standing still like a post [sthāṇu]," |
| `Line 5622: मौनव्रतधरं शान्तं सद्यो मन्युवशं ययौ ||२५||` | "Who was observing a vow of silence and was peaceful, immediately came under the influence of anger. ||25||" |
| `Line 5623: ` | [Blank line] |
| `Line 5624: न बुबोध हि तं राजा मौनव्रतधरं मुनिम् |` | "The king did not understand that sage who was observing a vow of silence," |
| `Line 5625: स तं मन्युसमाविष्टो धर्षयामास ते पिता ||२६||` | "Your father, overcome with anger, insulted him. ||26||" |
| `Line 5626: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5627: मृतं सर्पं धनुष्कोट्या समुत्क्षिप्य धरातलात् |` | "Having lifted a dead serpent from the ground with the end of his bow," |
| `Line 5628: तस्य शुद्धात्मनः प्रादात्स्कन्धे भरतसत्तम ||२७||` | "He placed it on the shoulders of that pure-souled one, O best of Bharatas [noble lineage]. ||27||" |
| `Line 5629: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5631: तस्थौ तथैव चाक्रुध्यन्सर्पं स्कन्धेन धारयन् ||२८||` | "He stood just as he was, without anger, bearing the serpent on his shoulder. ||28||" |

| `Line 5641: मन्त्रिण ऊचुः||` | "The ministers said:" |
| `Line 5642: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5643: ततः स राजा राजेन्द्र स्कन्धे तस्य भुजङ्गमम् |` | "Then that king, O lord of kings, having placed the serpent on the shoulder," |
| `Line 5644: मुनेः क्षुत्क्षाम आसज्य स्वपुरं पुनराययौ ||१||` | "Of the sage who was emaciated from hunger, returned again to his city. ||1||" |
| `Line 5645: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5646: ऋषेस्तस्य तु पुत्रोऽभूद्गवि जातो महायशाः |` | "But that sage had a son, born of a cow [miraculous birth], of great fame," |
| `Line 5647: शृङ्गी नाम महातेजास्तिग्मवीर्योऽतिकोपनः ||२||` | "Shringi by name, of great splendor, of fierce power and extremely wrathful. ||2||" |
| `Line 5648: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5649: ब्रह्माणं सोऽभ्युपागम्य मुनिः पूजां चकार ह |` | "That sage, having approached Brahman [creator deity], performed worship," |
| `Line 5650: अनुज्ञातो गतस्तत्र शृङ्गी शुश्राव तं तदा ||३||` | "Having been permitted, Shringi went there and then heard about it. ||3||" |
| `Line 5651: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5652: सख्युः सकाशात्पितरं पित्रा ते धर्षितं तथा ||३||` | "From his friend about his father being thus insulted by your father. ||3||" |
| `Line 5653: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5655: वहन्तं कुरुशार्दूल स्कन्धेनानपकारिणम् ||४||` | "On the shoulder of the innocent one who carried it, O tiger among Kurus [royal epithet]. ||4||" |
| `Line 5656: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5657: तपस्विनमतीवाथ तं मुनिप्रवरं नृप |` | "That ascetic who was exceedingly the foremost among sages, O king," |

| `Line 5659: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5660: तपसा द्योतितात्मानं स्वेष्वङ्गेषु यतं तथा |` | "His self illumined by austerities, disciplined in all his limbs," |
| `Line 5661: शुभाचारं शुभकथं सुस्थिरं तमलोलुपम् ||६||` | "Of virtuous conduct, pleasant speech, steadfast and free from desires. ||6||" |
| `Line 5662: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5663: अक्षुद्रमनसूयं च वृद्धं मौनव्रते स्थितम् |` | "Not mean-minded, free from envy, aged, observing the vow of silence," |
| `Line 5664: शरण्यं सर्वभूतानां पित्रा विप्रकृतं तव ||७||` | "A refuge for all beings - was insulted by your father. ||7||" |
| `Line 5665: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5666: शशापाथ स तच्छ्रुत्वा पितरं ते रुषान्वितः |` | "Having heard that, he cursed your father, filled with anger," |
| `Line 5667: ऋषेः पुत्रो महातेजा बालोऽपि स्थविरैर्वरः ||८||` | "The sage's son of great splendor, though a child, superior to elders. ||8||" |
| `Line 5668: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5669: स क्षिप्रमुदकं स्पृष्ट्वा रोषादिदमुवाच ह |` | "He quickly touched water [purification ritual] and in anger said this," |
| `Line 5670: पितरं तेऽभिसन्धाय तेजसा प्रज्वलन्निव ||९||` | "Addressing your father, blazing as it were with energy. ||9||" |
| `Line 5671: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5672: अनागसि गुरौ यो मे मृतं सर्पमवासृजत् |` | "He who placed a dead serpent on my innocent father [guru]," |
| `Line 5673: तं नागस्तक्षकः क्रुद्धस्तेजसा सादयिष्यति ||१०||` | "Him shall the angry serpent Takshaka [serpent king] destroy with his power. ||10||" |
| `Line 5674: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5675: सप्तरात्रादितः पापं पश्य मे तपसो बलम् ||१०||` | "Within seven nights from now, O sinner, behold the power of my austerities. ||10||" |
| `Line 5676: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5677: इत्युक्त्वा प्रययौ तत्र पिता यत्रास्य सोऽभवत् |` | "Having said this, he went there where his father was," |
| `Line 5678: दृष्ट्वा च पितरं तस्मै शापं तं प्रत्यवेदयत् ||११||` | "And having seen his father, he informed him about that curse. ||11||" |
| `Line 5679: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5680: स चापि मुनिशार्दूलः प्रेषयामास ते पितुः |` | "And that tiger among sages [eminent sage] sent a message to your father:" |
| `Line 5681: शप्तोऽसि मम पुत्रेण यत्तो भव महीपते ||१२||` | "'You have been cursed by my son, be prepared, O king. ||12||'" |
| `Line 5682: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5683: तक्षकस्त्वां महाराज तेजसा सादयिष्यति ||१२||` | "'Takshaka [serpent king] will destroy you with his power, O great king.' ||12||" |
| `Line 5684: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5685: श्रुत्वा तु तद्वचो घोरं पिता ते जनमेजय |` | "Having heard those terrible words, your father, O Janamejaya," |
| `Line 5686: यत्तोऽभवत्परित्रस्तस्तक्षकात्पन्नगोत्तमात् ||१३||` | "Became vigilant and terrified of Takshaka, the foremost among serpents. ||13||" |
| `Line 5687: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5688: ततस्तस्मिंस्तु दिवसे सप्तमे समुपस्थिते |` | "Then, when the seventh day approached," |
| `Line 5689: राज्ञः समीपं ब्रह्मर्षिः काश्यपो गन्तुमैच्छत ||१४||` | "The brahmin sage Kashyapa wished to go to the king. ||14||" |
| `Line 5690: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5691: तं ददर्शाथ नागेन्द्रः काश्यपं तक्षकस्तदा |` | "Then Takshaka, the lord of serpents [naga king], saw Kashyapa," |
| `Line 5692: तमब्रवीत्पन्नगेन्द्रः काश्यपं त्वरितं व्रजन् ||१५||` | "The lord of serpents spoke to Kashyapa, who was going hurriedly. ||15||" |
| `Line 5693: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5694: क्व भवांस्त्वरितो याति किं च कार्यं चिकीर्षति ||१५||` | "'Where are you going in such haste, and what task do you wish to accomplish?' ||15||" |
| `Line 5695: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5696: काश्यप उवाच||` | "Kashyapa said:" |
| `Line 5697: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5698: यत्र राजा कुरुश्रेष्ठः परिक्षिन्नाम वै द्विज |` | "'Where the best of Kurus [Kuru dynasty], King Parikshit, is, O twice-born [brahmin]," |
| `Line 5699: तक्षकेण भुजङ्गेन धक्ष्यते किल तत्र वै ||१६||` | "'He will indeed be burned by the serpent Takshaka there. ||16||'" |
| `Line 5700: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5701: गच्छाम्यहं तं त्वरितः सद्यः कर्तुमपज्वरम् |` | "I will go to him quickly to immediately make him free from fever," |
| `Line 5702: मयाभिपन्नं तं चापि न सर्पो धर्षयिष्यति ||१७||` | "And the serpent will not harm him who is protected by me. ||17||" |
| `Line 5703: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5704: तक्षक उवाच||` | "Takshaka [serpent king] said:" |
| `Line 5705: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5706: किमर्थं तं मया दष्टं सञ्जीवयितुमिच्छसि |` | "Why do you wish to revive him who has been bitten by me?" |
| `Line 5707: ब्रूहि काममहं तेऽद्य दद्मि स्वं वेश्म गम्यताम् ||१८||` | "Tell me your desire, I shall grant it to you today. Return to your own home. ||18||" |
| `Line 5708: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5709: मन्त्रिण ऊचुः||` | "The ministers said:" |
| `Line 5710: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5712: तमुवाच महात्मानं मानयञ्श्लक्ष्णया गिरा ||१९||` | "Addressed that great soul, honoring him with gentle words: ||19||" |
| `Line 5713: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5714: यावद्धनं प्रार्थयसे तस्माद्राज्ञस्ततोऽधिकम् |` | "Whatever wealth you desire from that king, even more than that," |
| `Line 5715: गृहाण मत्त एव त्वं संनिवर्तस्व चानघ ||२०||` | "Take from me instead, and turn back, O sinless one. ||20||" |
| `Line 5716: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5717: स एवमुक्तो नागेन काश्यपो द्विपदां वरः |` | "Thus addressed by the serpent, Kashyapa [sage], the best among the twice-born [Brahmins]," |
| `Line 5718: लब्ध्वा वित्तं निववृते तक्षकाद्यावदीप्सितम् ||२१||` | "Having received from Takshaka as much wealth as he desired, turned back. ||21||" |
| `Line 5719: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5720: तस्मिन्प्रतिगते विप्रे छद्मनोपेत्य तक्षकः |` | "When that Brahmin had returned, Takshaka, approaching in disguise," |
| `Line 5721: तं नृपं नृपतिश्रेष्ठ पितरं धार्मिकं तव ||२२||` | "That king, O best of kings, your righteous father, ||22||" |
| `Line 5722: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5723: प्रासादस्थं यत्तमपि दग्धवान्विषवह्निना |` | "Though he was vigilant in his palace, (Takshaka) burned him with his poison-fire," |
| `Line 5724: ततस्त्वं पुरुषव्याघ्र विजयायाभिषेचितः ||२३||` | "Thereafter you, O tiger among men [heroic king], were crowned for victory. ||23||" |
| `Line 5725: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5726: एतद्दृष्टं श्रुतं चापि यथावन्नृपसत्तम |` | "This has been seen and heard exactly as it happened, O best of kings [royal epithet]," |
| `Line 5727: अस्माभिर्निखिलं सर्वं कथितं ते सुदारुणम् ||२४||` | "Everything has been told to you by us in full, this most terrible event. ||24||" |
| `Line 5728: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5729: श्रुत्वा चैतं नृपश्रेष्ठ पार्थिवस्य पराभवम् |` | "Having heard this, O foremost of kings [royal epithet], about the defeat of the king [your father]," |
| `Line 5730: अस्य चर्षेरुत्तङ्कस्य विधत्स्व यदनन्तरम् ||२५||` | "And of this sage Uttanka, decide what should be done next. ||25||" |
| `Line 5731: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5732: जनमेजय उवाच||` | "Janamejaya said:" |
| `Line 5733: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5734: एतत्तु श्रोतुमिच्छामि अटव्यां निर्जने वने |` | "But I wish to hear about this, in the desolate forest in the wilderness," |
| `Line 5735: संवादं पन्नगेन्द्रस्य काश्यपस्य च यत्तदा ||२६||` | "The conversation between the lord of serpents [Takshaka] and Kashyapa [sage] that took place then. ||26||" |
| `Line 5736: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5738: श्रुत्वा चाथ विधास्यामि पन्नगान्तकरीं मतिम् ||२७||` | "After hearing it, I shall then form a resolution to destroy the serpents [snake sacrifice]. ||27||" |
| `Line 5739: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5743: समागमं द्विजेन्द्रस्य पन्नगेन्द्रस्य चाध्वनि ||२८||` | "About the meeting of the foremost Brahmin [Kashyapa] and the lord of serpents on the way. ||28||" |
| `Line 5744: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5747: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5749: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5751: द्विजप्रभावाद्राजेन्द्र जीवितः सवनस्पतिः ||३०||` | "Due to the Brahmin's [twice-born] power, O lord of kings, the tree with its forest was revived. ||30||" |

| `Line 5755: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5763: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5774: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5777: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5779: काश्यपस्य प्रसादेन मन्त्रिणां सुनयेन च ||३८||` | "By the grace of Kashyapa [snake-charming sage] and through the good policy of the ministers? ||38||" |
| `Line 5780: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5783: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5786: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 5893: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5894: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5895: शौनक उवाच||` | "Shaunaka [sage-interlocutor] said:" |
| `Line 5896: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5897: सर्पसत्रे तदा राज्ञः पाण्डवेयस्य धीमतः |` | "In that serpent sacrifice [snake ritual] of the wise king, descendant of the Pandavas [Pandava lineage]," |
| `Line 5898: जनमेजयस्य के त्वासन्नृत्विजः परमर्षयः ||१||` | "Janamejaya, who were the priests and great sages? ||1||" |
| `Line 5899: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5900: के सदस्या बभूवुश्च सर्पसत्रे सुदारुणे |` | "Who were the assembly members at that terrifying serpent sacrifice," |
| `Line 5901: विषादजननेऽत्यर्थं पन्नगानां महाभये ||२||` | "In causing extreme dejection and great fear among the serpents [snake beings]. ||2||" |
| `Line 5902: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5903: सर्वं विस्तरतस्तात भवाञ्शंसितुमर्हति |` | "O dear one [term of respect], you should narrate everything in detail," |
| `Line 5904: सर्पसत्रविधानज्ञा विज्ञेयास्ते हि सूतज ||३||` | "For you are known to be knowledgeable in the procedures of the serpent sacrifice, O son of Suta [bard lineage]. ||3||" |
| `Line 5905: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5906: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5907: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5908: हन्त ते कथयिष्यामि नामानीह मनीषिणाम् |` | "Well then, I shall tell you the names of the wise men," |
| `Line 5909: ये ऋत्विजः सदस्याश्च तस्यासन्नृपतेस्तदा ||४||` | "Who were the priests [ritual officiants] and assembly members of that king at that time. ||4||" |
| `Line 5910: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5911: तत्र होता बभूवाथ ब्राह्मणश्चण्डभार्गवः |` | "There, the Hota [chief priest] was the Brahmin Chanda Bhargava," |
| `Line 5912: च्यवनस्यान्वये जातः ख्यातो वेदविदां वरः ||५||` | "Born in the lineage of Chyavana, renowned as the best among the knowers of the Vedas. ||5||" |
| `Line 5913: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5914: उद्गाता ब्राह्मणो वृद्धो विद्वान्कौत्सार्यजैमिनिः |` | "The Udgata [chanting priest] was the learned elderly Brahmin Kautsarya Jaimini," |
| `Line 5915: ब्रह्माभवच्छार्ङ्गरवो अध्वर्युर्बोधपिङ्गलः ||६||` | "Sharngrava became the Brahma [supervising priest], and Bodha Pingala was the Adhvaryu [procedural priest]. ||6||" |
| `Line 5916: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5917: सदस्यश्चाभवद्व्यासः पुत्रशिष्यसहायवान् |` | "And Vyasa became a Sadasya [assembly member], accompanied by his sons and disciples," |
| `Line 5918: उद्दालकः शमठकः श्वेतकेतुश्च पञ्चमः ||७||` | "Uddalaka, Shamathaka, and Shvetaketu the fifth. ||7||" |
| `Line 5919: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5920: असितो देवलश्चैव नारदः पर्वतस्तथा |` | "Asita, Devala, and also Narada, Parvata likewise," |
| `Line 5921: आत्रेयः कुण्डजठरो द्विजः कुटिघटस्तथा ||८||` | "Atreya, Kundajathara, the twice-born [Brahmin] Kutighata likewise. ||8||" |
| `Line 5922: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5923: वात्स्यः श्रुतश्रवा वृद्धस्तपःस्वाध्यायशीलवान् |` | "The elderly Vatsya Shrutashrava, devoted to austerities and Vedic study," |
| `Line 5924: कहोडो देवशर्मा च मौद्गल्यः शमसौभरः ||९||` | "Kahoda, Devasharma, and Maudgalya Shamasaubhara. ||9||" |
| `Line 5925: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5926: एते चान्ये च बहवो ब्राह्मणाः संशितव्रताः |` | "These and many other Brahmins of strict vows [disciplined practitioners]," |
| `Line 5927: सदस्या अभवंस्तत्र सत्रे पारिक्षितस्य ह ||१०||` | "Became assembly members there at the sacrificial session of Parikshita [Janamejaya's father], indeed. ||10||" |
| `Line 5928: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5929: जुह्वत्स्वृत्विक्ष्वथ तदा सर्पसत्रे महाक्रतौ |` | "When the priests were making offerings in that great snake sacrifice [sarpa-satra]," |
| `Line 5930: अहयः प्रापतंस्तत्र घोराः प्राणिभयावहाः ||११||` | "Terrible snakes fell there, causing fear to living beings. ||11||" |
| `Line 5931: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5932: वसामेदोवहाः कुल्या नागानां सम्प्रवर्तिताः |` | "Streams carrying fat and marrow of the serpents [nagas] flowed forth," |
| `Line 5933: ववौ गन्धश्च तुमुलो दह्यतामनिशं तदा ||१२||` | "And a tumultuous smell wafted from those being continuously burned then. ||12||" |
| `Line 5934: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5935: पततां चैव नागानां धिष्ठितानां तथाम्बरे |` | "Of the falling serpents and those stationed likewise in the sky," |
| `Line 5936: अश्रूयतानिशं शब्दः पच्यतां चाग्निना भृशम् ||१३||` | "Incessantly was heard the sound of those being intensely burned by fire. ||13||" |
| `Line 5937: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5938: तक्षकस्तु स नागेन्द्रः पुरंदरनिवेशनम् |` | "But that Takshaka, the lord of serpents [naga king], to Purandara's [Indra's] abode" |
| `Line 5939: गतः श्रुत्वैव राजानं दीक्षितं जनमेजयम् ||१४||` | "Went, having heard that King Janamejaya had been initiated [for the ritual]. ||14||" |
| `Line 5940: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5941: ततः सर्वं यथावृत्तमाख्याय भुजगोत्तमः |` | "Then, having related everything as it happened, that foremost of serpents [Takshaka]," |
| `Line 5942: अगच्छच्छरणं भीत आगस्कृत्वा पुरंदरम् ||१५||` | "Frightened, sought refuge with Purandara [Indra], having committed an offense. ||15||" |
| `Line 5943: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5944: तमिन्द्रः प्राह सुप्रीतो न तवास्तीह तक्षक |` | "To him Indra [king of gods] said, well-pleased: 'There is no reason for you, Takshaka," |
| `Line 5945: भयं नागेन्द्र तस्माद्वै सर्पसत्रात्कथञ्चन ||१६||` | "O lord of serpents [naga king], to fear from that snake sacrifice [sarpa-satra] in any way.' ||16||" |
| `Line 5946: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5947: प्रसादितो मया पूर्वं तवार्थाय पितामहः |` | "Pitamaha [Brahma, grandfather] has been propitiated by me earlier for your sake." |
| `Line 5948: तस्मात्तव भयं नास्ति व्येतु ते मानसो ज्वरः ||१७||` | "Therefore, you have no fear; let your mental fever [anxiety] depart. ||17||" |
| `Line 5949: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5950: एवमाश्वासितस्तेन ततः स भुजगोत्तमः |` | "Thus reassured by him, then that foremost of serpents [naga lord]," |
| `Line 5951: उवास भवने तत्र शक्रस्य मुदितः सुखी ||१८||` | "Dwelt there in the abode of Shakra [Indra], happy and content. ||18||" |
| `Line 5952: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5953: अजस्रं निपतत्स्वग्नौ नागेषु भृशदुःखितः |` | "As the serpents [nagas] fell incessantly into the fire, deeply distressed," |
| `Line 5954: अल्पशेषपरीवारो वासुकिः पर्यतप्यत ||१९||` | "Vasuki [naga king], with few attendants remaining, suffered greatly. ||19||" |
| `Line 5955: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5956: कश्मलं चाविशद्घोरं वासुकिं पन्नगेश्वरम् |` | "And a terrible swoon [unconsciousness] overtook Vasuki, the lord of serpents [naga king]." |
| `Line 5957: स घूर्णमानहृदयो भगिनीमिदमब्रवीत् ||२०||` | "He, with his heart reeling [dizzy], said this to his sister. ||20||" |
| `Line 5958: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5959: दह्यन्तेऽङ्गानि मे भद्रे दिशो न प्रतिभान्ति च |` | "My limbs are burning, O auspicious one [sister], and the directions do not appear clear to me." |
| `Line 5960: सीदामीव च संमोहाद्घूर्णतीव च मे मनः ||२१||` | "I seem to be sinking from confusion, and my mind seems to be whirling. ||21||" |
| `Line 5961: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5962: दृष्टिर्भ्रमति मेऽतीव हृदयं दीर्यतीव च |` | "My vision wanders excessively, and my heart seems to be breaking." |
| `Line 5963: पतिष्याम्यवशोऽद्याहं तस्मिन्दीप्ते विभावसौ ||२२||` | "Helpless, today I shall fall into that blazing fire [Agni]. ||22||" |
| `Line 5964: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5965: पारिक्षितस्य यज्ञोऽसौ वर्ततेऽस्मज्जिघांसया |` | "That sacrifice of Parikshita's son [Janamejaya] proceeds with the desire to kill us." |
| `Line 5966: व्यक्तं मयापि गन्तव्यं पितृराजनिवेशनम् ||२३||` | "Surely I too must go to the abode of the king of ancestors [Yama's realm]. ||23||" |
| `Line 5967: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5968: अयं स कालः सम्प्राप्तो यदर्थमसि मे स्वसः |` | "This is that time which has arrived, for which purpose you are my sister," |
| `Line 5969: जरत्कारोः पुरा दत्ता सा त्राह्यस्मान्सबान्धवान् ||२४||` | "Given earlier to Jaratkaru. May she save us along with our relatives. ||24||" |
| `Line 5970: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5971: आस्तीकः किल यज्ञं तं वर्तन्तं भुजगोत्तमे |` | "Astika [sage son] will indeed stop that sacrifice proceeding against the best of serpents [nagas]," |
| `Line 5972: प्रतिषेत्स्यति मां पूर्वं स्वयमाह पितामहः ||२५||` | "Pitamaha [Brahma] himself told me earlier. ||25||" |
| `Line 5973: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5974: तद्वत्से ब्रूहि वत्सं स्वं कुमारं वृद्धसंमतम् |` | "Therefore, dear one [daughter], tell your son, the youth respected by the elders," |
| `Line 5975: ममाद्य त्वं सभृत्यस्य मोक्षार्थं वेदवित्तमम् ||२६||` | "For the liberation of me and my servants today, O most knowledgeable in the Vedas. ||26||" |

| `Line 5985: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5986: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5987: तत आहूय पुत्रं स्वं जरत्कारुर्भुजङ्गमा |` | "Then Jaratkaaru [serpent woman], the serpent, having called her son," |
| `Line 5988: वासुकेर्नागराजस्य वचनादिदमब्रवीत् ||१||` | "Spoke these words at the command of Vaasuki [serpent king], the king of serpents. ||1||" |
| `Line 5989: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5990: अहं तव पितुः पुत्र भ्रात्रा दत्ता निमित्ततः |` | "O son, I was given to your father by my brother for a specific purpose," |
| `Line 5991: कालः स चायं सम्प्राप्तस्तत्कुरुष्व यथातथम् ||२||` | "And that time has now arrived; therefore, do what must be done. ||2||" |
| `Line 5992: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5993: आस्तीक उवाच||` | "Aastika [sage's name] said:" |
| `Line 5994: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5995: किंनिमित्तं मम पितुर्दत्ता त्वं मातुलेन मे |` | "For what purpose were you given to my father by my maternal uncle?" |
| `Line 5996: तन्ममाचक्ष्व तत्त्वेन श्रुत्वा कर्तास्मि तत्तथा ||३||` | "Tell me this truthfully; after hearing it, I shall act accordingly. ||3||" |
| `Line 5997: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 5998: सूत उवाच||` | "Suta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 5999: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6000: तत आचष्ट सा तस्मै बान्धवानां हितैषिणी |` | "Then she, who desired the welfare of her relatives, told him," |
| `Line 6001: भगिनी नागराजस्य जरत्कारुरविक्लवा ||४||` | "The sister of the Nāga-king [serpent ruler], the steadfast Jaratkāru. ||4||" |
| `Line 6002: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6003: भुजगानामशेषाणां माता कद्रूरिति श्रुतिः |` | "Kadrū is known as the mother of all the serpents [snake beings]," |
| `Line 6004: तया शप्ता रुषितया सुता यस्मान्निबोध तत् ||५||` | "By her, enraged, her sons were cursed - hear the reason why. ||5||" |
| `Line 6005: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6006: उच्छैःश्रवाः सोऽश्वराजो यन्मिथ्या न कृतो मम |` | "Because Uchchaihshravas, that king of horses [divine steed], was not falsely represented for me," |
| `Line 6007: विनतानिमित्तं पणिते दासभावाय पुत्रकाः ||६||` | "In the wager with Vinatā, you, my sons, were reduced to slavery. ||6||" |
| `Line 6008: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6009: जनमेजयस्य वो यज्ञे धक्ष्यत्यनिलसारथिः |` | "In Janamejaya's sacrifice, the fire [wind-charioteer] shall consume you," |
| `Line 6010: तत्र पञ्चत्वमापन्नाः प्रेतलोकं गमिष्यथ ||७||` | "There, meeting your end, you shall go to the world of the dead [afterlife realm]. ||7||" |
| `Line 6011: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6012: तां च शप्तवतीमेवं साक्षाल्लोकपितामहः |` | "And to her who had pronounced this curse, the Grandfather of the worlds [Brahmā] himself," |
| `Line 6013: एवमस्त्विति तद्वाक्यं प्रोवाचानुमुमोद च ||८||` | "Said 'So be it,' confirming her words with his approval. ||8||" |
| `Line 6014: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6015: वासुकिश्चापि तच्छ्रुत्वा पितामहवचस्तदा |` | "And Vāsuki, having heard these words of the Grandfather [Brahmā]," |
| `Line 6016: अमृते मथिते तात देवाञ्शरणमीयिवान् ||९||` | "When the nectar [immortality elixir] was churned, O dear one, sought refuge with the gods. ||9||" |
| `Line 6017: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6018: सिद्धार्थाश्च सुराः सर्वे प्राप्यामृतमनुत्तमम् |` | "And all the gods, having achieved their purpose by obtaining the supreme nectar," |
| `Line 6019: भ्रातरं मे पुरस्कृत्य प्रजापतिमुपागमन् ||१०||` | "Placing my brother at their head, approached Prajāpati [creation lord]. ||10||" |
| `Line 6020: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6021: ते तं प्रसादयामासुर्देवाः सर्वे पितामहम् |` | "All those gods propitiated the Grandfather [Brahmā]," |
| `Line 6022: राज्ञा वासुकिना सार्धं स शापो न भवेदिति ||११||` | "Along with King Vāsuki, (praying) that the curse might not come to pass. ||11||" |
| `Line 6023: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6024: वासुकिर्नागराजोऽयं दुःखितो ज्ञातिकारणात् |` | "This Vāsuki, king of serpents [Nāga ruler], distressed for the sake of his kinsmen," |
| `Line 6025: अभिशापः स मात्रास्य भगवन्न भवेदिति ||१२||` | "(Pleaded) 'O Lord, may the curse of his mother not come to pass.' ||12||" |
| `Line 6026: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6027: ब्रह्मोवाच॥` | "Brahma [creator deity] said:" |
| `Line 6028: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6029: जरत्कारुर्जरत्कारुं यां भार्यां समवाप्स्यति |` | "The Jaratkaru [sage's name] who will obtain Jaratkaru [female counterpart] as his wife," |
| `Line 6030: तत्र जातो द्विजः शापाद्भुजगान्मोक्षयिष्यति ॥१३॥` | "The twice-born [brahmin] born from that union will free the serpents from the curse. ||13||" |
| `Line 6031: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6032: जरत्कारुरुवाच॥` | "Jaratkaru [mother] said:" |
| `Line 6033: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6034: एतच्छ्रुत्वा तु वचनं वासुकिः पन्नगेश्वरः |` | "Having heard these words, Vasuki [serpent king], the lord of serpents," |
| `Line 6035: प्रादान्माममरप्रख्य तव पित्रे महात्मने ॥१४॥` | "Gave me to your noble father, who was like an immortal. ||14||" |
| `Line 6036: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6037: प्रागेवानागते काले तत्र त्वं मय्यजायथाः ॥१४॥` | "Before the appointed time arrived, you were born to me. ||14||" |
| `Line 6038: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6039: अयं स कालः सम्प्राप्तो भयान्नस्त्रातुमर्हसि |` | "Now that time has arrived; you should save us from this fear," |
| `Line 6040: भ्रातरं चैव मे तस्मात्त्रातुमर्हसि पावकात् ॥१५॥` | "And you should save my brother from that fire [sacrificial fire]. ||15||" |
| `Line 6041: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6042: अमोघं नः कृतं तत्स्याद्यदहं तव धीमते |` | "Let our efforts not be in vain, that I was given to your wise," |
| `Line 6043: पित्रे दत्ता विमोक्षार्थं कथं वा पुत्र मन्यसे ॥१६॥` | "Father for the purpose of liberation. What do you think, my son? ||16||" |
| `Line 6044: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6045: सूत उवाच॥` | "Suta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 6046: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6047: एवमुक्तस्तथेत्युक्त्वा सोऽस्तीको मातरं तदा |` | "Having been thus addressed, Astika [sage's name] said 'So be it' to his mother then," |
| `Line 6048: अब्रवीद्दुःखसन्तप्तं वासुकिं जीवयन्निव ॥१७॥` | "And spoke to the grief-stricken Vasuki, as if giving him new life. ||17||" |
| `Line 6049: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6050: अहं त्वां मोक्षयिष्यामि वासुके पन्नगोत्तम |` | "I will free you, O Vasuki, best of serpents," |
| `Line 6051: तस्माच्छापान्महासत्त्व सत्यमेतद्ब्रवीमि ते ||१८||` | "Therefore, O mighty one [great-souled being], I tell you truly about this curse. ||18||" |
| `Line 6052: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6053: भव स्वस्थमना नाग न हि ते विद्यते भयम् |` | "Be at ease in your mind, O Nāga [serpent lord], for you have nothing to fear." |
| `Line 6054: प्रयतिष्ये तथा सौम्य यथा श्रेयो भविष्यति ||१९||` | "I shall strive, O gentle one, so that good will come of it. ||19||" |
| `Line 6055: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6064: न ते मयि मनो जातु मिथ्या भवितुमर्हति ||२१||` | "Your trust in me should never prove false. ||21||" |

| `Line 6074: दीप्तादग्नेः समुत्पन्नं नाशयिष्यामि ते भयम् ||२३||` | "I shall destroy your fear arising from the blazing fire [sacrificial flames]. ||23||" |

| `Line 6124: इमे हि ते सूर्यहुताशवर्चसः; समासते वृत्रहणः क्रतुं यथा |` | "These priests with radiance like the sun and fire are seated here, as at the sacrifice of Vṛtrahana [Indra, slayer of Vṛtra]," |

| `Line 6131: प्रदक्षिणावर्तशिखः प्रदीप्तो; हव्यं तवेदं हुतभुग्वष्टि देवः ||१०||` | "With flames spiraling clockwise, brilliantly blazing, the fire-god [Agni] desires this oblation of yours. ||10||" |

| `Line 6177: होता वाक्यं नातिहृष्टान्तरात्मा; कर्मण्यस्मिंस्तक्षको नैति तावत् ||३||` | "The hotā [chief priest] spoke these words, with a not-too-pleased heart: 'In this sacrifice, Takṣaka [serpent king] has not yet come.' ||3||" |

| `Line 6181: यथा चेदं कर्म समाप्यते मे; यथा च नस्तक्षक एति शीघ्रम् |` | "So that this sacrifice of mine may be completed; and so that Takṣaka may come to us quickly," |
| `Line 6182: तथा भवन्तः प्रयतन्तु सर्वे; परं शक्त्या स हि मे विद्विषाणः ||४||` | "Let all of you strive with your utmost power; for he is my bitter enemy. ||4||" |

| `Line 6187: इन्द्रस्य भवने राजंस्तक्षको भयपीडितः ||५||` | "Takṣaka, stricken with fear, is in Indra's [king of gods] abode, O king. ||5||" |
| `Line 6188: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6190: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6191: यथा सूतो लोहिताक्षो महात्मा; पौराणिको वेदितवान्पुरस्तात् |` | "As the noble red-eyed Sūta [royal chronicler], the knower of ancient lore, had known beforehand," |
| `Line 6192: स राजानं प्राह पृष्टस्तदानीं; यथाहुर्विप्रास्तद्वदेतन्नृदेव ||६||` | "He, when asked, then told the king: 'What the Brahmins say is true, O lord of men. ||6||'" |
| `Line 6193: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6194: पुराणमागम्य ततो ब्रवीम्यहं; दत्तं तस्मै वरमिन्द्रेण राजन् |` | "Based on the Purāṇas [ancient texts], I tell you this: Indra has given him a boon, O king," |
| `Line 6195: वसेह त्वं मत्सकाशे सुगुप्तो; न पावकस्त्वां प्रदहिष्यतीति ||७||` | "'Stay here with me, well-protected; the fire shall not burn you.' ||7||" |
| `Line 6196: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6197: एतच्छ्रुत्वा दीक्षितस्तप्यमान; आस्ते होतारं चोदयन्कर्मकाले |` | "Hearing this, the consecrated one [king], burning with anticipation, sat urging the hotā [chief priest] at the time of ritual." |
| `Line 6198: होता च यत्तः स जुहाव मन्त्रै; रथो इन्द्रः स्वयमेवाजगाम ||८||` | "And the attentive hotā [chief priest] made offerings with mantras; then Indra [king of gods] himself came in his chariot. ||8||" |
| `Line 6199: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6201: बलाहकैश्चाप्यनुगम्यमानो; विद्याधरैरप्सरसां गणैश्च ||९||` | "And followed by clouds, Vidyādharas [knowledge-bearers], and groups of Apsarās [celestial nymphs]. ||9||" |
| `Line 6202: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6204: ततो राजा मन्त्रविदोऽब्रवीत्पुनः; क्रुद्धो वाक्यं तक्षकस्यान्तमिच्छन् ||१०||` | "Then the king, desiring Takshaka's end, spoke again angrily to the mantra-knowers [priests]. ||10||" |

| `Line 6207: तमिन्द्रेणैव सहितं पातयध्वं विभावसौ ||११||` | "Make him fall into the fire [sacrificial flame] together with Indra himself. ||11||" |

| `Line 6212: श्रूयतेऽस्य महान्नादो रुवतो भैरवं भयात् ||१२||` | "His loud, terrifying cry can be heard as he roars from fear. ||12||" |
| `Line 6213: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6214: नूनं मुक्तो वज्रभृता स नागो; भ्रष्टश्चाङ्कान्मन्त्रविस्रस्तकायः |` | "Surely that serpent has been released by the thunderbolt-bearer [Indra], falling from his lap, his body loosened by the mantras." |
| `Line 6215: घूर्णन्नाकाशे नष्टसञ्ज्ञोऽभ्युपैति; तीव्रान्निःश्वासान्निःश्वसन्पन्नगेन्द्रः ||१३||` | "The lord of serpents approaches, whirling in the sky, unconscious, breathing heavy breaths. ||13||" |

| `Line 6324: सप्तशीर्षा द्विशीर्षाश्च पञ्चशीर्षास्तथापरे |` | "Some with seven heads, some with two heads, and others with five heads," |
| `Line 6325: कालानलविषा घोरा हुताः शतसहस्रशः ||२०||` | "With poison [viṣa] fierce as the fire of doom [kālānala], they were sacrificed by hundreds of thousands. ||20||" |

| `Line 6328: योजनायामविस्तारा द्वियोजनसमायताः ||२१||` | "Some a yojana [measure ~9 miles] in length and breadth, others extending two yojanas. ||21||" |
| `Line 6329: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6331: दग्धास्तत्र महासत्रे ब्रह्मदण्डनिपीडिताः ||२२||` | "They were burned in that great sacrifice [mahāsatra], oppressed by the Brahmic punishment [brahmadaṇḍa]. ||22||" |

| `Line 6341: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard/narrator] said:" |
| `Line 6342: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6343: इदमत्यद्भुतं चान्यदास्तीकस्यानुशुश्रुमः |` | "We have heard of this other most wonderful deed of Āstīka [sage's name]," |
| `Line 6344: तथा वरैश्छन्द्यमाने राज्ञा पारिक्षितेन ह ||१||` | "When King Pārīkṣita [Parikshit] was being pleased with boons. ||1||" |
| `Line 6345: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6346: इन्द्रहस्ताच्च्युतो नागः ख एव यदतिष्ठत |` | "When the serpent [nāga], fallen from Indra's [king of gods] hand, remained suspended in the sky," |
| `Line 6347: ततश्चिन्तापरो राजा बभूव जनमेजयः ||२||` | "Then King Janamejaya [Parikshit's son] became filled with anxiety. ||2||" |
| `Line 6348: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6349: हूयमाने भृशं दीप्ते विधिवत्पावके तदा |` | "When the ritual fire [pāvaka] was blazing intensely, properly invoked," |
| `Line 6350: न स्म स प्रापतद्वह्नौ तक्षको भयपीडितः ||३||` | "Takṣaka [serpent king], overcome with fear, did not fall into the fire. ||3||" |
| `Line 6351: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6352: शौनक उवाच||` | "Śaunaka [sage] said:" |
| `Line 6353: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6355: न प्रत्यभात्तदाग्नौ यन्न पपात स तक्षकः ||४||` | "Not prevail in the fire, that Takṣaka [serpent king] did not fall? ||4||" |
| `Line 6356: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6357: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |

| `Line 6360: आस्तीकस्तिष्ठ तिष्ठेति वाचस्तिस्रोऽभ्युदैरयत् ||५||` | "Āstīka exclaimed three times, 'Stop! Stop!' ||5||" |
| `Line 6361: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6362: वितस्थे सोऽन्तरिक्षेऽथ हृदयेन विदूयता |` | "Then he (the serpent) remained suspended in the sky, with a tormented heart," |
| `Line 6363: यथा तिष्ठेत वै कश्चिद्गोचक्रस्यान्तरा नरः ||६||` | "As if a man were caught in the middle of a circle of cattle [gocakra]. ||6||" |
| `Line 6364: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6365: ततो राजाब्रवीद्वाक्यं सदस्यैश्चोदितो भृशम् |` | "Then the king, strongly urged by the assembly members [sadasya], spoke these words:" |
| `Line 6366: काममेतद्भवत्वेवं यथास्तीकस्य भाषितम् ||७||` | "Let it be as Āstīka has spoken. ||7||" |
| `Line 6367: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6368: समाप्यतामिदं कर्म पन्नगाः सन्त्वनामयाः |` | "Let this ritual be concluded, may the serpents [pannaga] be safe," |
| `Line 6369: प्रीयतामयमास्तीकः सत्यं सूतवचोऽस्तु तत् ||८||` | "Let this Āstīka be pleased, and let the Sūta's words be true. ||8||" |
| `Line 6370: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6372: आस्तीकस्य वरे दत्ते तथैवोपरराम च ||९||` | "And when the boon was granted to Āstīka, it (the sacrifice) came to an end. ||9||" |
| `Line 6373: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6375: प्रीतिमांश्चाभवद्राजा भारतो जनमेजयः ||१०||` | "And King Janamejaya of the Bharata lineage became pleased. ||10||" |
| `Line 6376: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6378: तेभ्यश्च प्रददौ वित्तं शतशोऽथ सहस्रशः ||११||` | "To them he gave wealth by hundreds and thousands. ||11||" |
| `Line 6379: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6391: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6397: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6398: एतच्छ्रुत्वा प्रीयमाणाः समेता; ये तत्रासन्पन्नगा वीतमोहाः |` | "Hearing this, all the serpents [pannagas] who had gathered there, now free from delusion [vītamohāḥ], were pleased;" |
| `Line 6399: तेऽऽस्तीके वै प्रीतिमन्तो बभूवु; रूचुश्चैनं वरमिष्टं वृणीष्व ||१८||` | "They became fond of Āstīka and said to him, 'Choose a desired boon.' ||18||" |
| `Line 6400: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6405: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6478: सूत उवाच||` | "Sūta [bard-narrator] said:" |
| `Line 6479: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6480: श्रुत्वा तु सर्पसत्राय दीक्षितं जनमेजयम् |` | "Having heard that Janamejaya was initiated for the serpent sacrifice [sarpasatra]," |
| `Line 6481: अभ्यागच्छदृषिर्विद्वान्कृष्णद्वैपायनस्तदा ||१||` | "The learned sage Kṛṣṇa Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] then approached. ||1||" |
| `Line 6482: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6483: जनयामास यं काली शक्तेः पुत्रात्पराशरात् |` | "Whom Kālī [Satyavatī] bore from Parāśara, the son of Śakti," |
| `Line 6484: कन्यैव यमुनाद्वीपे पाण्डवानां पितामहम् ||२||` | "While still a maiden, on an island in the Yamunā, the grandfather of the Pāṇḍavas. ||2||" |
| `Line 6485: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6486: जातमात्रश्च यः सद्य इष्ट्या देहमवीवृधत् |` | "Who, as soon as he was born, by his will made his body grow," |
| `Line 6487: वेदांश्चाधिजगे साङ्गान्सेतिहासान्महायशाः ||३||` | "And mastered the Vedas with their auxiliary texts [aṅgas] and histories [itihāsas], the greatly renowned one. ||3||" |
| `Line 6488: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6489: यं नातितपसा कश्चिन्न वेदाध्ययनेन च |` | "Whom no one could surpass, neither through austerities [tapas] nor through Vedic study," |
| `Line 6490: न व्रतैर्नोपवासैश्च न प्रसूत्या न मन्युना ||४||` | "Nor through vows, nor through fasting, nor through progeny, nor through anger. ||4||" |
| `Line 6491: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6492: विव्यासैकं चतुर्धा यो वेदं वेदविदां वरः |` | "Who, the best among knowers of the Vedas [vedavidām], divided the one Veda into four parts," |
| `Line 6493: परावरज्ञो ब्रह्मर्षिः कविः सत्यव्रतः शुचिः ||५||` | "Knower of higher and lower truths [parāvarajña], a brahmarṣi [brahmin sage], a poet, truthful in his vows, and pure. ||5||" |
| `Line 6494: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6495: यः पाण्डुं धृतराष्ट्रं च विदुरं चाप्यजीजनत् |` | "Who begot Pāṇḍu, Dhṛtarāṣṭra, and also Vidura," |
| `Line 6496: शन्तनोः सन्ततिं तन्वन्पुण्यकीर्तिर्महायशाः ||६||` | "Extending the lineage of Śantanu, he was of pure fame and great glory. ||6||" |
| `Line 6497: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6498: जनमेजयस्य राजर्षेः स तद्यज्ञसदस्तदा |` | "Then he entered the sacrificial assembly of the royal sage [rājarṣi] Janamejaya," |
| `Line 6499: विवेश शिष्यैः सहितो वेदवेदाङ्गपारगैः ||७||` | "Accompanied by his disciples who were masters of the Vedas and Vedāṅgas [auxiliary texts]. ||7||" |
| `Line 6500: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6501: तत्र राजानमासीनं ददर्श जनमेजयम् |` | "There he saw King Janamejaya seated," |
| `Line 6502: वृतं सदस्यैर्बहुभिर्देवैरिव पुरंदरम् ||८||` | "Surrounded by many assembly members, like Purandara [Indra] among the gods. ||8||" |
| `Line 6503: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6504: तथा मूर्धावसिक्तैश्च नानाजनपदेश्वरैः |` | "Also with consecrated [anointed] kings, rulers of various lands," |
| `Line 6505: ऋत्विग्भिर्देवकल्पैश्च कुशलैर्यज्ञसंस्तरे ||९||` | "And with priests [ṛtvigs] godlike in appearance, skilled in sacrificial arrangements. ||9||" |
| `Line 6506: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6507: जनमेजयस्तु राजर्षिर्दृष्ट्वा तमृषिमागतम् |` | "But the royal sage Janamejaya, seeing that sage arrive," |
| `Line 6508: सगणोऽब्युद्ययौ तूर्णं प्रीत्या भरतसत्तमः ||१०||` | "Quickly rose with his retinue in delight, that best of the Bharatas [Bharatasattama]. ||10||" |
| `Line 6509: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6510: काञ्चनं विष्टरं तस्मै सदस्यानुमते प्रभुः |` | "The lord, with the assembly's approval, arranged for him," |
| `Line 6511: आसनं कल्पयामास यथा शक्रो बृहस्पतेः ||११||` | "A golden seat, just as Śakra [Indra] would for Bṛhaspati [preceptor of gods]. ||11||" |
| `Line 6512: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6513: तत्रोपविष्टं वरदं देवर्षिगणपूजितम् |` | "Seated there, the boon-giver honored by groups of divine sages [devarṣis]," |
| `Line 6514: पूजयामास राजेन्द्रः शास्त्रदृष्टेन कर्मणा ||१२||` | "The king [rājendra] worshipped him with rituals prescribed by the scriptures [śāstras]. ||12||" |
| `Line 6515: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6516: पाद्यमाचमनीयं च अर्घ्यं गां च विधानतः |` | "The water for washing feet [pādya], water for rinsing the mouth [ācamanīya], water for respectful offering [arghya], and a cow, according to proper ritual," |
| `Line 6517: पितामहाय कृष्णाय तदर्हाय न्यवेदयत् ||१३||` | "He presented to the grandfather [pitāmaha] Krishna [Vyāsa], who was worthy of these offerings. ||13||" |
| `Line 6518: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6519: प्रतिगृह्य च तां पूजां पाण्डवाज्जनमेजयात् |` | "Having accepted that worship from Janamejaya, the Pāṇḍava [descendant]," |
| `Line 6520: गां चैव समनुज्ञाय व्यासः प्रीतोऽभवत्तदा ||१४||` | "And having accepted the cow, Vyāsa became pleased then. ||14||" |
| `Line 6521: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6522: तथा सम्पूजयित्वा तं यत्नेन प्रपितामहम् |` | "Having thus worshipped with effort his great-grandfather [prapitāmaha]," |
| `Line 6523: उपोपविश्य प्रीतात्मा पर्यपृच्छदनामयम् ||१५||` | "Sitting nearby with a pleased heart, he inquired about his well-being. ||15||" |
| `Line 6524: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6525: भगवानपि तं दृष्ट्वा कुशलं प्रतिवेद्य च |` | "The venerable one [Bhagavān], seeing him and having informed about his own welfare," |
| `Line 6526: सदस्यैः पूजितः सर्वैः सदस्यानभ्यपूजयत् ||१६||` | "Being honored by all the assembly members [sadasyas], honored the assembly members in return. ||16||" |
| `Line 6527: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6528: ततस्तं सत्कृतं सर्वैः सदस्यैर्जनमेजयः |` | "Then Janamejaya, after he [Vyāsa] was honored by all the assembly members," |
| `Line 6529: इदं पश्चाद्द्विजश्रेष्ठं पर्यपृच्छत्कृताञ्जलिः ||१७||` | "With folded hands [kṛtāñjali], asked this to the best of the twice-born [dvijaśreṣṭha]. ||17||" |
| `Line 6530: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6531: कुरूणां पाण्डवानां च भवान्प्रत्यक्षदर्शिवान् |` | "You were an eyewitness [pratyakṣadarśin] of the Kurus and the Pāṇḍavas," |
| `Line 6532: तेषां चरितमिच्छामि कथ्यमानं त्वया द्विज ||१८||` | "I wish to hear their story as narrated by you, O twice-born [dvija]. ||18||" |
| `Line 6533: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6534: कथं समभवद्भेदस्तेषामक्लिष्टकर्मणाम् |` | "How did the division arise among them of untainted deeds [akliṣṭakarman]?" |
| `Line 6535: तच्च युद्धं कथं वृत्तं भूतान्तकरणं महत् ||१९||` | "And how did that great war occur which caused the destruction of beings [bhūtāntakaraṇa]? ||19||" |
| `Line 6536: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6537: पितामहानां सर्वेषां दैवेनाविष्टचेतसाम् |` | "Of all the ancestors [pitāmahas] whose minds were possessed by fate [daiva]," |
| `Line 6538: कार्त्स्न्येनैतत्समाचक्ष्व भगवन्कुशलो ह्यसि ||२०||` | "Narrate this completely, O venerable one [bhagavan], for you are indeed skilled. ||20||" |
| `Line 6539: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6540: तस्य तद्वचनं श्रुत्वा कृष्णद्वैपायनस्तदा |` | "Having heard those words of his, Krishna Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] then," |
| `Line 6541: शशास शिष्यमासीनं वैशम्पायनमन्तिके ||२१||` | "Instructed his disciple Vaiśampāyana who was seated nearby. ||21||" |
| `Line 6542: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6543: कुरूणां पाण्डवानां च यथा भेदोऽभवत्पुरा |` | "How the division between the Kurus and the Pāṇḍavas occurred in the past," |
| `Line 6544: तदस्मै सर्वमाचक्ष्व यन्मत्तः श्रुतवानसि ||२२||` | "Tell him all that which you have heard from me. ||22||" |
| `Line 6545: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6546: गुरोर्वचनमाज्ञाय स तु विप्रर्षभस्तदा |` | "Having understood the guru's words, that foremost of brahmins [viprarṣabha] then," |
| `Line 6547: आचचक्षे ततः सर्वमितिहासं पुरातनम् ||२३||` | "Narrated the entire ancient history [itihāsa]. ||23||" |
| `Line 6548: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6549: तस्मै राज्ञे सदस्येभ्यः क्षत्रियेभ्यश्च सर्वशः |` | "To that king, to the assembly members, and to all the warriors [kṣatriyas]," |
| `Line 6550: भेदं राज्यविनाशं च कुरुपाण्डवयोस्तदा ||२४||` | "The division and the destruction of the kingdom of the Kurus and Pāṇḍavas then. ||24||" |
