| `Line 6559: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6560: वैशम्पायन उवाच||` | "Vaiśampāyana said:" |
| `Line 6561: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6562: गुरवे प्राङ्नमस्कृत्य मनोबुद्धिसमाधिभिः |` | "Having first bowed to the guru [teacher] with mind, intellect, and concentration," |
| `Line 6563: सम्पूज्य च द्विजान्सर्वांस्तथान्यान्विदुषो जनान् ||१||` | "And having honored all the twice-born [brahmins] and other learned people. ||1||" |
| `Line 6564: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6565: महर्षेः सर्वलोकेषु विश्रुतस्यास्य धीमतः |` | "Of this great sage [maharṣi], renowned in all worlds, the wise one," |
| `Line 6566: प्रवक्ष्यामि मतं कृत्स्नं व्यासस्यामिततेजसः ||२||` | "I shall proclaim the complete doctrine of Vyāsa of immeasurable splendor. ||2||" |
| `Line 6567: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6568: श्रोतुं पात्रं च राजंस्त्वं प्राप्येमां भारतीं कथाम् |` | "And you, O king, are a worthy vessel to hear this story of Bharata [epic tale]," |
| `Line 6569: गुरोर्वक्तुं परिस्पन्दो मुदा प्रोत्साहतीव माम् ||३||` | "The eagerness to speak of my guru seems to encourage me with joy. ||3||" |
| `Line 6570: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6571: शृणु राजन्यथा भेदः कुरुपाण्डवयोरभूत् |` | "Listen, O king, how the division between the Kurus and Pāṇḍavas occurred," |
| `Line 6572: राज्यार्थे द्यूतसम्भूतो वनवासस्तथैव च ||४||` | "Arising from the gambling match for the kingdom, and likewise the forest exile. ||4||" |
| `Line 6573: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6574: यथा च युद्धमभवत्पृथिवीक्षयकारकम् |` | "And how the war that caused the destruction of the earth came to be," |
| `Line 6575: तत्तेऽहं सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि पृच्छते भरतर्षभ ||५||` | "All that I shall now narrate to you who ask, O bull among the Bharatas [bharatarṣabha]. ||5||" |
| `Line 6576: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6577: मृते पितरि ते वीरा वनादेत्य स्वमन्दिरम् |` | "After their father's death, those heroes [vīrās], returning from the forest to their own palace," |
| `Line 6578: नचिरादिव विद्वांसो वेदे धनुषि चाभवन् ||६||` | "In a short time, became learned in the Vedas and skilled in archery. ||6||" |
| `Line 6579: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6580: तांस्तथा रूपवीर्यौजःसम्पन्नान्पौरसंमतान् |` | "Seeing them thus endowed with beauty, valor, and strength, respected by the citizens," |
| `Line 6581: नामृष्यन्कुरवो दृष्ट्वा पाण्डवाञ्श्रीयशोभृतः ||७||` | "The Kauravas could not tolerate the Pāṇḍavas [Pandu's sons] who were blessed with prosperity and fame. ||7||" |
| `Line 6582: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6583: ततो दुर्योधनः क्रूरः कर्णश्च सहसौबलः |` | "Then the cruel Duryodhana, along with Karṇa and Śakuni [Saubala's son]," |
| `Line 6584: तेषां निग्रहनिर्वासान्विविधांस्ते समाचरन् ||८||` | "Carried out various schemes to suppress and exile them. ||8||" |
| `Line 6585: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6586: ददावथ विषं पापो भीमाय धृतराष्ट्रजः |` | "Then the sinful son of Dhṛtarāṣṭra gave poison to Bhīma," |
| `Line 6587: जरयामास तद्वीरः सहान्नेन वृकोदरः ||९||` | "But that hero Vṛkodara [wolf-bellied] digested it along with the food. ||9||" |
| `Line 6588: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6589: प्रमाणकोट्यां संसुप्तं पुनर्बद्ध्वा वृकोदरम् |` | "Again, binding Vṛkodara who was fast asleep at the edge of the water," |
| `Line 6590: तोयेषु भीमं गङ्गायाः प्रक्षिप्य पुरमाव्रजत् ||१०||` | "He threw Bhīma into the waters of the Ganges and returned to the city. ||10||" |
| `Line 6591: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6592: यदा प्रबुद्धः कौन्तेयस्तदा सञ्छिद्य बन्धनम् |` | "When Kuntī's son [Kaunteya] awoke, he tore apart his bonds," |
| `Line 6593: उदतिष्ठन्महाराज भीमसेनो गतव्यथः ||११||` | "And rose up, O great king [mahārāja], Bhīmasena free from distress. ||11||" |
| `Line 6594: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6595: आशीविषैः कृष्णसर्पैः सुप्तं चैनमदंशयत् |` | "He (Duryodhana) had him bitten while sleeping by venomous black serpents," |
| `Line 6596: सर्वेष्वेवाङ्गदेशेषु न ममार च शत्रुहा ||१२||` | "In all those parts of his body, the enemy-slayer [śatruhā] did not die. ||12||" |
| `Line 6597: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6598: तेषां तु विप्रकारेषु तेषु तेषु महामतिः |` | "But during those various misdeeds against them, the wise one [mahāmati]," |
| `Line 6599: मोक्षणे प्रतिघाते च विदुरोऽवहितोऽभवत् ||१३||` | "Vidura remained vigilant in rescuing and protecting them. ||13||" |
| `Line 6600: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6601: स्वर्गस्थो जीवलोकस्य यथा शक्रः सुखावहः |` | "As Śakra [Indra], dwelling in heaven, brings happiness to the world of the living," |
| `Line 6602: पाण्डवानां तथा नित्यं विदुरोऽपि सुखावहः ||१४||` | "So did Vidura always bring happiness to the Pāṇḍavas. ||14||" |
| `Line 6603: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6604: यदा तु विविधोपायैः संवृतैर्विवृतैरपि |` | "But when by various means, both concealed and open," |
| `Line 6605: नाशक्नोद्विनिहन्तुं तान्दैवभाव्यर्थरक्षितान् ||१५||` | "He could not destroy those who were protected by destiny [daivabhāvya] and fate. ||15||" |
| `Line 6606: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6607: ततः संमन्त्र्य सचिवैर्वृषदुःशासनादिभिः |` | "Then, after consulting with his ministers, Vṛṣa [Duryodhana], Duḥśāsana and others," |
| `Line 6608: धृतराष्ट्रमनुज्ञाप्य जातुषं गृहमादिशत् ||१६||` | "Having obtained Dhṛtarāṣṭra's permission, he ordered a lac [flammable material] house to be built. ||16||" |
| `Line 6609: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6610: तत्र तान्वासयामास पाण्डवानमितौजसः |` | "There he made the Pāṇḍavas of immeasurable strength [amitaujas] dwell," |
| `Line 6611: अदाहयच्च विस्रब्धान्पावकेन पुनस्तदा ||१७||` | "And then tried to burn them with fire [pāvaka] while they were unsuspecting. ||17||" |
| `Line 6612: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6613: विदुरस्यैव वचनात्खनित्री विहिता ततः |` | "By Vidura's advice, a tunnel [khanitrī] was prepared," |
| `Line 6614: मोक्षयामास योगेन ते मुक्ताः प्राद्रवन्भयात् ||१८||` | "Through which they escaped by a stratagem [yoga]; freed, they fled in fear. ||18||" |
| `Line 6615: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6616: ततो महावने घोरे हिडिम्बं नाम राक्षसम् |` | "Then in a terrible great forest, the rakshasa [demon] named Hidimba," |
| `Line 6617: भीमसेनोऽवधीत्क्रुद्धो भुवि भीमपराक्रमः ||१९||` | "Bhimasena, of terrifying prowess on earth, slew in anger. ||19||" |
| `Line 6618: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6619: अथ सन्धाय ते वीरा एकचक्रां व्रजंस्तदा |` | "Then those heroes, having made a plan, proceeded to Ekacakrā [one-wheeled town]," |
| `Line 6620: ब्रह्मरूपधरा भूत्वा मात्रा सह परन्तपाः ||२०||` | "Assuming the form of Brahmins, together with their mother, those scorchers of foes [parantapāḥ]. ||20||" |
| `Line 6621: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6622: तत्र ते ब्राह्मणार्थाय बकं हत्वा महाबलम् |` | "There, for the sake of a Brahmin, having killed the mighty Baka [demon]," |
| `Line 6623: ब्राह्मणैः सहिता जग्मुः पाञ्चालानां पुरं ततः ||२१||` | "Accompanied by Brahmins, they then went to the city of the Pañcālas. ||21||" |
| `Line 6624: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6625: ते तत्र द्रौपदीं लब्ध्वा परिसंवत्सरोषिताः |` | "Having won Draupadī there, and having stayed for about a year," |
| `Line 6626: विदिता हास्तिनपुरं प्रत्याजग्मुररिंदमाः ||२२||` | "They became known and returned to Hastināpura, those destroyers of enemies [ariṃdamāḥ]. ||22||" |
| `Line 6627: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6628: त उक्ता धृतराष्ट्रेण राज्ञा शान्तनवेन च |` | "They were told by King Dhṛtarāṣṭra and by the son of Śantanu [Bhīṣma]," |
| `Line 6629: भ्रातृभिर्विग्रहस्तात कथं वो न भवेदिति ||२३||` | "'How can there not be conflict between you and your brothers [Kauravas]?' ||23||" |
| `Line 6630: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6631: अस्माभिः खाण्डवप्रस्थे युष्मद्वासोऽनुचिन्तितः ||२३||` | "'We have considered Khāṇḍavaprastha as a residence for you.' ||23||" |
| `Line 6632: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6633: तस्माज्जनपदोपेतं सुविभक्तमहापथम् |` | "'Therefore, go to Khāṇḍavaprastha, which is populated with people and has well-divided highways," |
| `Line 6634: वासाय खाण्डवप्रस्थं व्रजध्वं गतमन्यवः ||२४||` | "Go to Khāṇḍavaprastha for residence, free from anger [gatamanyavaḥ].' ||24||" |
| `Line 6635: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6636: तयोस्ते वचनाज्जग्मुः सह सर्वैः सुहृज्जनैः |` | "At the words of those two, they went together with all their well-wishers [suhṛjjana]," |
| `Line 6637: नगरं खाण्डवप्रस्थं रत्नान्यादाय सर्वशः ||२५||` | "To the city of Khāṇḍavaprastha, taking all their treasures [ratna] with them. ||25||" |
| `Line 6638: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6639: तत्र ते न्यवसन्राजन्संवत्सरगणान्बहून् |` | "There, O king [rājan], they dwelt for many years [saṃvatsara]," |
| `Line 6640: वशे शस्त्रप्रतापेन कुर्वन्तोऽन्यान्महीक्षितः ||२६||` | "Bringing other rulers [mahīkṣit] under their control through the power of their weapons [śastrapratāpa]. ||26||" |
| `Line 6641: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6642: एवं धर्मप्रधानास्ते सत्यव्रतपरायणाः |` | "Thus they, with righteousness [dharma] as their foremost principle, devoted to truthful vows [satyavrata]," |
| `Line 6643: अप्रमत्तोत्थिताः क्षान्ताः प्रतपन्तोऽहितांस्तदा ||२७||` | "Vigilant, energetic, patient, then tormented their enemies [ahita]. ||27||" |
| `Line 6644: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6645: अजयद्भीमसेनस्तु दिशं प्राचीं महाबलः |` | "The mighty [mahābala] Bhīmasena conquered the eastern direction [prācī]," |
| `Line 6646: उदीचीमर्जुनो वीरः प्रतीचीं नकुलस्तथा ||२८||` | "The heroic Arjuna the northern, and Nakula likewise the western. ||28||" |
| `Line 6647: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6648: दक्षिणां सहदेवस्तु विजिग्ये परवीरहा |` | "And Sahadeva, the slayer of enemy heroes [paravīrahā], conquered the southern direction," |
| `Line 6649: एवं चक्रुरिमां सर्वे वशे कृत्स्नां वसुन्धराम् ||२९||` | "Thus they all brought this entire earth [vasundharā] under their control. ||29||" |
| `Line 6650: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6651: पञ्चभिः सूर्यसङ्काशैः सूर्येण च विराजता |` | "With the five who were radiant like the sun [sūrya], and with the sun itself shining," |
| `Line 6652: षट्सूर्येवाबभौ पृथ्वी पाण्डवैः सत्यविक्रमैः ||३०||` | "The earth shone as if with six suns, with the Pāṇḍavas of true valor [satyavikrama]. ||30||" |
| `Line 6653: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6654: ततो निमित्ते कस्मिंश्चिद्धर्मराजो युधिष्ठिरः |` | "Then, for some reason [nimitta], King Yudhiṣṭhira, the lord of righteousness [dharmarāja]," |
| `Line 6655: वनं प्रस्थापयामास भ्रातरं वै धनञ्जयम् ||३१||` | "Sent his brother Dhanañjaya [Arjuna] to the forest. ||31||" |
| `Line 6656: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6657: स वै संवत्सरं पूर्णं मासं चैकं वनेऽवसत् |` | "He indeed dwelt in the forest for a full year and one month," |
| `Line 6658: ततोऽगच्छद्धृषीकेशं द्वारवत्यां कदाचन ||३२||` | "Then he went to Hṛṣīkeśa [Krishna] in Dvāravatī [Krishna's city] at some time. ||32||" |
| `Line 6659: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6660: लब्धवांस्तत्र बीभत्सुर्भार्यां राजीवलोचनाम् |` | "There Bībhatsu [Arjuna] obtained a lotus-eyed [rājīvalocanām] wife," |
| `Line 6661: अनुजां वासुदेवस्य सुभद्रां भद्रभाषिणीम् ||३३||` | "The younger sister of Vāsudeva [Krishna], Subhadrā, of auspicious speech. ||33||" |
| `Line 6662: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6663: सा शचीव महेन्द्रेण श्रीः कृष्णेनेव सङ्गता |` | "Like Śacī [Indra's wife] united with Mahendra [Indra], or Śrī [goddess] with Kṛṣṇa [Vishnu]," |
| `Line 6664: सुभद्रा युयुजे प्रीता पाण्डवेनार्जुनेन ह ||३४||` | "Subhadrā was happily joined with the Pāṇḍava Arjuna. ||34||" |
| `Line 6665: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6666: अतर्पयच्च कौन्तेयः खाण्डवे हव्यवाहनम् |` | "And the son of Kuntī [Arjuna] satisfied the fire [havyavāhana] in Khāṇḍava," |
| `Line 6667: बीभत्सुर्वासुदेवेन सहितो नृपसत्तम ||३५||` | "Bībhatsu [Arjuna] together with Vāsudeva [Krishna], O best of kings [nṛpasattama]. ||35||" |
| `Line 6668: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6669: नातिभारो हि पार्थस्य केशवेनाभवत्सह |` | "Indeed, no burden was too great for Pārtha [Arjuna] when with Keśava [Krishna]," |
| `Line 6670: व्यवसायसहायस्य विष्णोः शत्रुवधेष्विव ||३६||` | "Just as for Viṣṇu [supreme deity] with a resolute ally in slaying enemies. ||36||" |
| `Line 6671: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6672: पार्थायाग्निर्ददौ चापि गाण्डीवं धनुरुत्तमम् |` | "And Agni [fire god] gave to Pārtha [Arjuna] the Gāṇḍīva, that excellent bow," |
| `Line 6673: इषुधी चाक्षयैर्बाणै रथं च कपिलक्षणम् ||३७||` | "Two quivers with inexhaustible arrows, and a chariot marked with a monkey [Hanuman]. ||37||" |
| `Line 6674: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6675: मोक्षयामास बीभत्सुर्मयं तत्र महासुरम् |` | "Bībhatsu [Arjuna] there liberated Maya, the great asura [demon]," |
| `Line 6676: स चकार सभां दिव्यां सर्वरत्नसमाचिताम् ||३८||` | "He built a divine assembly hall [sabhā] filled with all kinds of jewels. ||38||" |
| `Line 6677: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6678: तस्यां दुर्योधनो मन्दो लोभं चक्रे सुदुर्मतिः |` | "In that hall, the foolish Duryodhana, of evil mind [durmati], became envious," |
| `Line 6679: ततोऽक्षैर्वञ्चयित्वा च सौबलेन युधिष्ठिरम् ||३९||` | "And then, with Saubala [Śakuni], he cheated Yudhiṣṭhira through dice [akṣa]. ||39||" |
| `Line 6680: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6681: वनं प्रस्थापयामास सप्त वर्षाणि पञ्च च |` | "He sent them to the forest [vana] for seven years and five," |
| `Line 6682: अज्ञातमेकं राष्ट्रे च तथा वर्षं त्रयोदशम् ||४०||` | "And one year incognito [ajñāta] in a kingdom, thus thirteen years in total. ||40||" |
| `Line 6683: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6684: ततश्चतुर्दशे वर्षे याचमानाः स्वकं वसु |` | "Then in the fourteenth year, when they requested their own wealth," |
| `Line 6685: नालभन्त महाराज ततो युद्धमवर्तत ||४१||` | "They did not receive it, O great king [mahārāja], and then the war began. ||41||" |
| `Line 6686: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6687: ततस्ते सर्वमुत्साद्य हत्वा दुर्योधनं नृपम् |` | "Then, having destroyed everything and killed King Duryodhana," |
| `Line 6688: राज्यं विद्रुतभूयिष्ठं प्रत्यपद्यन्त पाण्डवाः ||४२||` | "The Pāṇḍavas regained their kingdom, which was mostly in ruins [vidrutabhūyiṣṭha]. ||42||" |
| `Line 6689: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6690: एवमेतत्पुरावृत्तं तेषामक्लिष्टकर्मणाम् |` | "Thus is this ancient account of those whose deeds were untainted [akliṣṭakarma]," |
| `Line 6691: भेदो राज्यविनाशश्च जयश्च जयतां वर ||४३||` | "The division, the destruction of the kingdom, and the victory, O best of conquerors [jayatāṃ vara]. ||43||" |
| `Line 6692: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6693: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6694: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6695: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6696: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6697: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6698: ५६` | "56 [chapter number]" |
| `Line 6699: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6700: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6701: जनमेजय उवाच||` | "Janamejaya [Pāṇḍu's great-grandson] said:" |
| `Line 6702: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6703: कथितं वै समासेन त्वया सर्वं द्विजोत्तम |` | "You have indeed narrated everything in brief, O best of the twice-born [dvijottama]," |
| `Line 6704: महाभारतमाख्यानं कुरूणां चरितं महत् ||१||` | "The great narrative Mahābhārata, the magnificent history of the Kurus. ||1||" |
| `Line 6705: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6706: कथां त्वनघ चित्रार्थामिमां कथयति त्वयि |` | "O sinless one [anagha], as you narrate this story with its wonderful meanings," |
| `Line 6707: विस्तरश्रवणे जातं कौतूहलमतीव मे ||२||` | "An intense curiosity has arisen in me to hear it in full detail. ||2||" |
| `Line 6708: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6709: स भवान्विस्तरेणेमां पुनराख्यातुमर्हति |` | "You, sir, should narrate this again in detail," |
| `Line 6710: न हि तृप्यामि पूर्वेषां शृण्वानश्चरितं महत् ||३||` | "For I am not satisfied hearing the great deeds of my ancestors. ||3||" |
| `Line 6711: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6712: न तत्कारणमल्पं हि धर्मज्ञा यत्र पाण्डवाः |` | "The reason is not trivial why the Pāṇḍavas, knowers of dharma [righteousness]," |
| `Line 6713: अवध्यान्सर्वशो जघ्नुः प्रशस्यन्ते च मानवैः ||४||` | "Killed those who should not have been killed, yet are praised by people. ||4||" |
| `Line 6714: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6715: किमर्थं ते नरव्याघ्राः शक्ताः सन्तो ह्यनागसः |` | "For what reason did those tiger-like men [naravyāghrāḥ], though powerful and innocent," |
| `Line 6716: प्रयुज्यमानान्सङ्क्लेशान्क्षान्तवन्तो दुरात्मनाम् ||५||` | "They endured the afflictions [saṅkleśa] inflicted by the wicked ones [durātman]. ||5||" |
| `Line 6717: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6718: कथं नागायुतप्राणो बाहुशाली वृकोदरः |` | "How did Vṛkodara [Bhīma], strong-armed and with the strength of ten thousand elephants [nāgāyuta]," |
| `Line 6719: परिक्लिश्यन्नपि क्रोधं धृतवान्वै द्विजोत्तम ||६||` | "Even while suffering greatly, restrain his anger, O best of the twice-born [dvijottama]? ||6||" |
| `Line 6720: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6721: कथं सा द्रौपदी कृष्णा क्लिश्यमाना दुरात्मभिः |` | "How did she, Draupadī Kṛṣṇā [dark-complexioned], while being tormented by evil souls," |
| `Line 6722: शक्ता सती धार्तराष्ट्रान्नादहद्घोरचक्षुषा ||७||` | "Though capable, not burn the sons of Dhṛtarāṣṭra with her terrible gaze? ||7||" |
| `Line 6723: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6724: कथं व्यतिक्रमन्द्यूते पार्थौ माद्रीसुतौ तथा |` | "How did the two sons of Mādrī [Nakula and Sahadeva], as well as the two Pārthas [Arjuna and Bhīma]," |
| `Line 6725: अनुव्रजन्नरव्याघ्रं वञ्च्यमानं दुरात्मभिः ||८||` | "Follow the tiger among men [Yudhiṣṭhira] who was being deceived by the wicked ones in the gambling match? ||8||" |
| `Line 6726: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6727: कथं धर्मभृतां श्रेष्ठः सुतो धर्मस्य धर्मवित् |` | "How did the foremost upholder of dharma, the son of Dharma [Yudhiṣṭhira], knower of righteousness," |
| `Line 6728: अनर्हः परमं क्लेशं सोढवान्स युधिष्ठिरः ||९||` | "Though undeserving, endure that extreme suffering, that Yudhiṣṭhira? ||9||" |
| `Line 6729: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6730: कथं च बहुलाः सेनाः पाण्डवः कृष्णसारथिः |` | "And how did that Pāṇḍava [Arjuna], with Kṛṣṇa as his charioteer," |
| `Line 6731: अस्यन्नेकोऽनयत्सर्वाः पितृलोकं धनञ्जयः ||१०||` | "Shooting arrows alone, send all those numerous armies to the world of the ancestors [pitṛloka], that Dhanañjaya [Arjuna]? ||10||" |
| `Line 6732: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6733: एतदाचक्ष्व मे सर्वं यथावृत्तं तपोधन |` | "Tell me all this exactly as it happened, O wealth of austerities [tapodhana]," |
| `Line 6734: यद्यच्च कृतवन्तस्ते तत्र तत्र महारथाः ||११||` | "And whatever those great warriors [mahāratha] did in various situations. ||11||" |
| `Line 6735: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6736: वैशम्पायन उवाच॥` | "Vaiśampāyana [narrator sage] said:" |
| `Line 6737: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6738: महर्षेः सर्वलोकेषु पूजितस्य महात्मनः |` | "Of the great sage [maharṣi], who is worshipped in all worlds, the great-souled one [mahātman]," |
| `Line 6739: प्रवक्ष्यामि मतं कृत्स्नं व्यासस्यामिततेजसः ॥१२॥` | "I shall declare the complete doctrine of Vyāsa [compiler sage] of immeasurable splendor [amitatejas]. ||12||" |
| `Line 6740: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6741: इदं शतसहस्रं हि श्लोकानां पुण्यकर्मणाम् |` | "This hundred thousand verses [ślokas] of meritorious deeds [puṇyakarman]," |
| `Line 6742: सत्यवत्यात्मजेनेह व्याख्यातममितौजसा ॥१३॥` | "Has been expounded here by the son of Satyavatī [Vyāsa], of boundless energy [amitaujas]. ||13||" |
| `Line 6743: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6744: य इदं श्रावयेद्विद्वान्यश्चेदं शृणुयान्नरः |` | "The learned one who recites this, and the man who listens to this," |
| `Line 6745: ते ब्रह्मणः स्थानमेत्य प्राप्नुयुर्देवतुल्यताम् ॥१४॥` | "They, having reached the realm of Brahma [creator deity], attain equality with the gods. ||14||" |
| `Line 6746: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6747: इदं हि वेदैः समितं पवित्रमपि चोत्तमम् |` | "This is indeed equal to the Vedas [sacred texts], pure and also supreme," |
| `Line 6748: श्राव्याणामुत्तमं चेदं पुराणमृषिसंस्तुतम् ॥१५॥` | "This is the foremost of what should be heard, an ancient text [purāṇa] praised by sages. ||15||" |
| `Line 6749: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6750: अस्मिन्नर्थश्च धर्मश्च निखिलेनोपदिश्यते |` | "In this, wealth [artha] and righteousness [dharma] are taught completely," |
| `Line 6751: इतिहासे महापुण्ये बुद्धिश्च परिनैष्ठिकी ॥१६॥` | "In this highly meritorious history [itihāsa], perfect wisdom is also found. ||16||" |
| `Line 6752: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6753: अक्षुद्रान्दानशीलांश्च सत्यशीलाननास्तिकान् |` | "To those who are noble, charitable by nature, truthful, and not atheists [nāstika]," |
| `Line 6754: कार्ष्णं वेदमिमं विद्वाञ्श्रावयित्वार्थमश्नुते ॥१७॥` | "The learned one, having recited this Veda of Kṛṣṇa [Vyāsa's work], obtains wealth. ||17||" |
| `Line 6755: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6756: भ्रूणहत्याकृतं चापि पापं जह्यादसंशयम् |` | "One would undoubtedly be freed from the sin of embryo-killing [fetal murder] as well," |
| `Line 6757: इतिहासमिमं श्रुत्वा पुरुषोऽपि सुदारुणः ||१८||` | "After hearing this historical account [itihāsa], even a most cruel person. ||18||" |
| `Line 6758: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6759: जयो नामेतिहासोऽयं श्रोतव्यो विजिगीषुणा |` | "This historical account [itihāsa] named 'Jaya' [Victory] should be heard by one desiring conquest," |
| `Line 6760: महीं विजयते सर्वां शत्रूंश्चापि पराजयेत् ||१९||` | "He will conquer the entire earth and defeat his enemies as well. ||19||" |
| `Line 6761: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6762: इदं पुंसवनं श्रेष्ठमिदं स्वस्त्ययनं महत् |` | "This is the best puṃsavana [male-child ritual] and a great blessing [svastyayana]," |
| `Line 6763: महिषीयुवराजाभ्यां श्रोतव्यं बहुशस्तथा ||२०||` | "It should be heard repeatedly by the chief queen [mahiṣī] and the crown prince [yuvarāja]. ||20||" |
| `Line 6764: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6765: अर्थशास्त्रमिदं पुण्यं धर्मशास्त्रमिदं परम् |` | "This is a sacred treatise on wealth [arthaśāstra], this is the supreme treatise on righteousness [dharmaśāstra]," |
| `Line 6766: मोक्षशास्त्रमिदं प्रोक्तं व्यासेनामितबुद्धिना ||२१||` | "This is declared to be a treatise on liberation [mokṣaśāstra] by Vyāsa of immeasurable intellect. ||21||" |
| `Line 6767: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6768: सम्प्रत्याचक्षते चैव आख्यास्यन्ति तथापरे |` | "Some recite it now, and others will narrate it in the future," |
| `Line 6769: पुत्राः शुश्रूषवः सन्ति प्रेष्याश्च प्रियकारिणः ||२२||` | "Sons are obedient, and servants are pleasing in their actions. ||22||" |
| `Line 6770: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6773: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6774: भारतानां महज्जन्म शृण्वतामनसूयताम् |` | "For those who listen without envy to the great origin of the Bharatas [Bhāratānām]," |

| `Line 6776: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6777: धन्यं यशस्यमायुष्यं स्वर्ग्यं पुण्यं तथैव च |` | "This work is auspicious, fame-bestowing, life-extending, heaven-granting, and meritorious as well," |
| `Line 6778: कृष्णद्वैपायनेनेदं कृतं पुण्यचिकीर्षुणा ||२५||` | "Created by Kṛṣṇa Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] who desired to perform a meritorious deed. ||25||" |
| `Line 6779: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6782: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6785: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6786: य इदं श्रावयेद्विद्वान्ब्राह्मणानिह पर्वसु |` | "The learned one who recites this to Brahmins [priest class] during the sacred occasions [parvan]," |
| `Line 6787: धूतपाप्मा जितस्वर्गो ब्रह्मभूयं स गच्छति ||२८||` | "Becomes cleansed of sins, conquers heaven, and attains the state of Brahman [ultimate reality]. ||28||" |
| `Line 6788: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6791: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6792: अह्ना यदेनश्चाज्ञानात्प्रकरोति नरश्चरन् |` | "Whatever sin a person commits unknowingly during the day while going about," |
| `Line 6793: तन्महाभारताख्यानं श्रुत्वैव प्रविलीयते ||३०||` | "That dissolves away merely by hearing this narrative called the Mahābhārata. ||30||" |
| `Line 6794: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6796: निरुक्तमस्य यो वेद सर्वपापैः प्रमुच्यते ||३१||` | "One who knows the etymology [nirukta] of this is freed from all sins. ||31||" |
| `Line 6797: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6799: महाभारतमाख्यानं कृतवानिदमुत्तमम् ||३२||` | "Composed this supreme narrative called the Mahābhārata. ||32||" |
| `Line 6800: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6801: धर्मे चार्थे च कामे च मोक्षे च भरतर्षभ |` | "Regarding dharma [righteousness], artha [wealth], kāma [desire], and mokṣa [liberation], O bull among Bharatas [bharatarṣabha]," |

| `Line 6812: वैशम्पायन उवाच||` | "Vaiśampāyana said:" |
| `Line 6813: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6814: राजोपरिचरो नाम धर्मनित्यो महीपतिः |` | "There was a king named Rājoparicarā [sky-traveling king], ever devoted to dharma [righteousness], a ruler of the earth," |
| `Line 6815: बभूव मृगयां गन्तुं स कदाचिद्धृतव्रतः ||१||` | "Who once, having taken a vow, went hunting. ||1||" |
| `Line 6816: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6817: स चेदिविषयं रम्यं वसुः पौरवनन्दनः |` | "Vasu, the son of Pūru [Paurava dynasty], took the pleasant Cedi kingdom," |
| `Line 6818: इन्द्रोपदेशाज्जग्राह ग्रहणीयं महीपतिः ||२||` | "By Indra's instruction, the king [mahīpati] acquired this desirable land. ||2||" |
| `Line 6819: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6820: तमाश्रमे न्यस्तशस्त्रं निवसन्तं तपोरतिम् |` | "To him, who had laid down his weapons in the hermitage [āśrama], dwelling there devoted to austerities [tapas]," |
| `Line 6821: देवः साक्षात्स्वयं वज्री समुपायान्महीपतिम् ||३||` | "The god himself, the wielder of the thunderbolt [vajrī], came in person to the king. ||3||" |
| `Line 6822: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6823: इन्द्रत्वमर्हो राजायं तपसेत्यनुचिन्त्य वै |` | "Thinking 'This king is worthy of Indra's position through his austerities'," |
| `Line 6824: तं सान्त्वेन नृपं साक्षात्तपसः संन्यवर्तयत् ||४||` | "He personally dissuaded the king from his austerities with gentle words. ||4||" |
| `Line 6825: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6826: इन्द्र उवाच||` | "Indra said:" |
| `Line 6827: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6828: न सङ्कीर्येत धर्मोऽयं पृथिव्यां पृथिवीपते |` | "Let this dharma [righteous duty] not be confused on earth, O lord of the earth [pṛthivīpate]," |
| `Line 6829: तं पाहि धर्मो हि धृतः कृत्स्नं धारयते जगत् ||५||` | "Protect it, for dharma, when upheld, sustains the entire world. ||5||" |
| `Line 6830: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6831: लोक्यं धर्मं पालय त्वं नित्ययुक्तः समाहितः |` | "Protect the worldly dharma, ever vigilant and attentive," |
| `Line 6832: धर्मयुक्तस्ततो लोकान्पुण्यानाप्स्यसि शाश्वतान् ||६||` | "Established in dharma, you will then attain the eternal, meritorious worlds. ||6||" |
| `Line 6833: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6834: दिविष्ठस्य भुविष्ठस्त्वं सखा भूत्वा मम प्रियः |` | "Being my dear friend, you dwelling on earth while I dwell in heaven," |
| `Line 6835: ऊधः पृथिव्या यो देशस्तमावस नराधिप ||७||` | "Inhabit that region which is the udder [most fertile part] of the earth, O lord of men [narādhipa]. ||7||" |
| `Line 6836: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6837: पशव्यश्चैव पुण्यश्च सुस्थिरो धनधान्यवान् |` | "It is rich in cattle [paśavya], auspicious, stable, and abundant in wealth and grain," |
| `Line 6838: स्वारक्ष्यश्चैव सौम्यश्च भोग्यैर्भूमिगुणैर्युतः ||८||` | "Well-protected, pleasant, and endowed with enjoyable qualities of the land. ||8||" |
| `Line 6839: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6840: अत्यन्यानेष देशो हि धनरत्नादिभिर्युतः |` | "This country indeed surpasses others, filled with wealth, gems and other treasures," |
| `Line 6841: वसुपूर्णा च वसुधा वस चेदिषु चेदिप ||९||` | "The earth here is full of riches, so dwell among the Cedis, O king of Cedi [Cedipa]. ||9||" |
| `Line 6842: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6843: धर्मशीला जनपदाः सुसन्तोषाश्च साधवः |` | "The people are virtuous, contented, and righteous," |
| `Line 6844: न च मिथ्याप्रलापोऽत्र स्वैरेष्वपि कुतोऽन्यथा ||१०||` | "There is no false speech here, even among the independent, how could it be otherwise? ||10||" |
| `Line 6845: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6846: न च पित्रा विभज्यन्ते नरा गुरुहिते रताः |` | "Men devoted to their elders' welfare are not separated from their fathers," |
| `Line 6847: युञ्जते धुरि नो गाश्च कृशाः सन्धुक्षयन्ति च ||११||` | "They do not yoke thin cows to the plow, and they nourish them well. ||11||" |
| `Line 6848: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6849: सर्वे वर्णाः स्वधर्मस्थाः सदा चेदिषु मानद |` | "All castes [varṇas] adhere to their own duties among the Cedis, O bestower of honor [mānada]," |
| `Line 6850: न तेऽस्त्यविदितं किञ्चित्त्रिषु लोकेषु यद्भवेत् ||१२||` | "Nothing that exists in the three worlds [triloka] remains unknown to you. ||12||" |
| `Line 6851: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6852: देवोपभोग्यं दिव्यं च आकाशे स्फाटिकं महत् |` | "A divine, celestial, great crystal chariot fit for gods," |
| `Line 6853: आकाशगं त्वां मद्दत्तं विमानमुपपत्स्यते ||१३||` | "This sky-traveling [ākāśaga] aerial vehicle [vimāna] given by me will come to you. ||13||" |
| `Line 6854: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6857: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6860: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6865: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6867: इष्टप्रदानमुद्दिश्य शिष्टानां परिपालिनीम् ||१७||` | "Intended as a desired gift, protecting the righteous [śiṣṭa]. ||17||" |

| `Line 6894: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6896: भूमिदानादिभिर्दानैर्यथा पूता भवन्ति वै ||२६||` | "Just as one becomes purified through gifts of land and other donations, ||26||" |
| `Line 6897: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6899: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 6901: पालयामास धर्मेण चेदिस्थः पृथिवीमिमाम् ||२७||` | "Protected this earth righteously while residing in Cedi. ||27||" |
| `Line 6902: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6903: इन्द्रप्रीत्या भूमिपतिश्चकारेन्द्रमहं वसुः ||२७||` | "Out of devotion to Indra, King Vasu performed the Indra festival. ||27||" |
| `Line 6904: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6905: पुत्राश्चास्य महावीर्याः पञ्चासन्नमितौजसः |` | "And his sons were five, of great valor and immeasurable strength," |
| `Line 6906: नानाराज्येषु च सुतान्स सम्राडभ्यषेचयत् ||२८||` | "And the emperor installed his sons in various kingdoms. ||28||" |
| `Line 6907: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6908: महारथो मगधराड्विश्रुतो यो बृहद्रथः |` | "The great chariot-warrior [mahāratha], the renowned king of Magadha, who was Bṛhadratha," |
| `Line 6909: प्रत्यग्रहः कुशाम्बश्च यमाहुर्मणिवाहनम् ||२९||` | "Pratyagraha, and Kuśāmba whom they called Maṇivāhana [jewel-bearer], ||29||" |
| `Line 6910: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6911: मच्छिल्लश्च यदुश्चैव राजन्यश्चापराजितः ||२९||` | "And Macchilla and Yadu, the unconquered prince. ||29||" |
| `Line 6912: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6913: एते तस्य सुता राजन्राजर्षेर्भूरितेजसः |` | "These were the sons, O king, of that royal sage [rājarṣi] of abundant splendor," |
| `Line 6914: न्यवेशयन्नामभिः स्वैस्ते देशांश्च पुराणि च ||३०||` | "They established countries and cities named after themselves. ||30||" |
| `Line 6915: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6916: वासवाः पञ्च राजानः पृथग्वंशाश्च शाश्वताः ||३०||` | "The five Vāsava kings [celestial rulers] and their separate eternal lineages. ||30||" |
| `Line 6917: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6918: वसन्तमिन्द्रप्रासादे आकाशे स्फाटिके च तम् |` | "Him residing in Indra's palace [divine abode] in the crystal sky," |
| `Line 6919: उपतस्थुर्महात्मानं गन्धर्वाप्सरसो नृपम् ||३१||` | "The Gandharvas [celestial musicians] and Apsaras [heavenly nymphs] attended upon that great-souled king. ||31||" |
| `Line 6920: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6921: राजोपरिचरेत्येवं नाम तस्याथ विश्रुतम् ||३१||` | "Thus his name became renowned as Rājoparicarā [one who travels above]. ||31||" |
| `Line 6922: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6923: पुरोपवाहिनीं तस्य नदीं शुक्तिमतीं गिरिः |` | "The mountain blocked his city-flowing river Śuktimatī [pearl-rich]," |
| `Line 6924: अरौत्सीच्चेतनायुक्तः कामात्कोलाहलः किल ||३२||` | "Indeed, the conscious mountain Kolāhala [tumultuous] willfully obstructed it out of desire. ||32||" |
| `Line 6925: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6926: गिरिं कोलाहलं तं तु पदा वसुरताडयत् |` | "But Vasu struck that mountain Kolāhala with his foot," |
| `Line 6927: निश्चक्राम नदी तेन प्रहारविवरेण सा ||३३||` | "And the river flowed out through the opening made by that blow. ||33||" |
| `Line 6928: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6929: तस्यां नद्यामजनयन्मिथुनं पर्वतः स्वयम् |` | "In that river, the mountain himself produced a pair [male-female]," |
| `Line 6930: तस्माद्विमोक्षणात्प्रीता नदी राज्ञे न्यवेदयत् ||३४||` | "Pleased with her release, the river presented them to the king. ||34||" |
| `Line 6931: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6932: यः पुमानभवत्तत्र तं स राजर्षिसत्तमः |` | "The male child who was born there, that best of royal sages [rājarṣi]," |
| `Line 6933: वसुर्वसुप्रदश्चक्रे सेनापतिमरिंदमम् ||३५||` | "Vasu, the bestower of wealth, made him the enemy-subduing commander of his army. ||35||" |
| `Line 6934: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6935: चकार पत्नीं कन्यां तु दयितां गिरिकां नृपः ||३५||` | "And the king made the beloved daughter, Girikā [mountain girl], his wife. ||35||" |
| `Line 6936: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6937: वसोः पत्नी तु गिरिका कामात्काले न्यवेदयत् |` | "Vasu's wife Girikā, out of desire, informed him at the proper time," |
| `Line 6938: ऋतुकालमनुप्राप्तं स्नाता पुंसवने शुचिः ||३६||` | "That her fertile period [ṛtukāla] had arrived, having bathed in the puṃsavana ritual [male-child ceremony], purified. ||36||" |
| `Line 6939: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6940: तदहः पितरश्चैनमूचुर्जहि मृगानिति |` | "That very day, the ancestors [pitaras] told him, 'Hunt the deer,'" |
| `Line 6941: तं राजसत्तमं प्रीतास्तदा मतिमतां वरम् ||३७||` | "They were pleased with that best of kings [rājasattama], the foremost among the wise. ||37||" |
| `Line 6942: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6943: स पितृणां नियोगं तमव्यतिक्रम्य पार्थिवः |` | "That king [pārthiva], not disobeying the command of the ancestors," |
| `Line 6944: चचार मृगयां कामी गिरिकामेव संस्मरन् ||३८||` | "Went hunting, filled with desire, thinking only of Girikā. ||38||" |
| `Line 6945: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6946: अतीव रूपसम्पन्नां साक्षाच्छ्रियमिवापराम् ||३८||` | "Who was exceedingly beautiful, like another Śrī [goddess of fortune] incarnate. ||38||" |
| `Line 6947: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6948: तस्य रेतः प्रचस्कन्द चरतो रुचिरे वने |` | "His semen was discharged as he wandered in the beautiful forest," |
| `Line 6949: स्कन्नमात्रं च तद्रेतः वृक्षपत्रेण भूमिपः ||३९||` | "And as soon as it was discharged, the king [bhūmipa] caught that semen on a leaf. ||39||" |
| `Line 6950: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6951: प्रतिजग्राह मिथ्या मे न स्कन्देद्रेत इत्युत |` | "He caught it thinking, 'May my semen not be wasted in vain,'" |
| `Line 6952: ऋतुश्च तस्याः पत्न्या मे न मोघः स्यादिति प्रभुः ||४०||` | "And 'May my wife's fertile period not go fruitless,' thought the lord [prabhu]. ||40||" |
| `Line 6953: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6954: सञ्चिन्त्यैवं तदा राजा विचार्य च पुनः पुनः |` | "Having thought thus, the king pondered again and again," |
| `Line 6955: अमोघत्वं च विज्ञाय रेतसो राजसत्तमः ||४१||` | "And understanding the need for his semen not to be wasted, that best of kings [rājasattama]. ||41||" |
| `Line 6956: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6957: शुक्रप्रस्थापने कालं महिष्याः प्रसमीक्ष्य सः |` | "Having carefully observed the proper time for releasing semen [śukra] in his queen [mahiṣī]," |
| `Line 6958: अभिमन्त्र्याथ तच्छुक्रमारात्तिष्ठन्तमाशुगम् ||४२||` | "He consecrated that semen with mantras, and the swift one [āśuga] stood nearby. ||42||" |
| `Line 6959: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6960: सूक्ष्मधर्मार्थतत्त्वज्ञो ज्ञात्वा श्येनं ततोऽब्रवीत् ||४२||` | "Knowing the subtle principles of dharma and artha, he then spoke to the falcon [śyena]. ||42||" |
| `Line 6961: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6962: मत्प्रियार्थमिदं सौम्य शुक्रं मम गृहं नय |` | "For my beloved's sake, O gentle one [saumya], take this semen to my home," |
| `Line 6963: गिरिकायाः प्रयच्छाशु तस्या ह्यार्तवमद्य वै ||४३||` | "And quickly give it to Girikā, for today is indeed her fertile period [ārtava]. ||43||" |
| `Line 6964: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6965: गृहीत्वा तत्तदा श्येनस्तूर्णमुत्पत्य वेगवान् |` | "Taking it then, the swift falcon rose up quickly," |
| `Line 6966: जवं परममास्थाय प्रदुद्राव विहङ्गमः ||४४||` | "And attaining its highest speed, the bird [vihaṅgama] flew away. ||44||" |
| `Line 6967: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6968: तमपश्यदथायान्तं श्येनं श्येनस्तथापरः |` | "Then another falcon saw that falcon coming," |
| `Line 6969: अभ्यद्रवच्च तं सद्यो दृष्ट्वैवामिषशङ्कया ||४५||` | "And immediately attacked it, having seen it and suspecting prey [āmiṣa]. ||45||" |
| `Line 6970: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6971: तुण्डयुद्धमथाकाशे तावुभौ सम्प्रचक्रतुः |` | "Then both of them engaged in a beak-battle [tuṇḍayuddha] in the sky," |
| `Line 6972: युध्यतोरपतद्रेतस्तच्चापि यमुनाम्भसि ||४६||` | "And as they fought, the semen fell into the waters of the Yamunā. ||46||" |
| `Line 6973: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6974: तत्राद्रिकेति विख्याता ब्रह्मशापाद्वराप्सराः |` | "There, the excellent apsarā [celestial nymph] named Adrikā, cursed by Brahmā," |
| `Line 6975: मीनभावमनुप्राप्ता बभूव यमुनाचरी ||४७||` | "Had attained the form of a fish [mīna] and was dwelling in the Yamunā. ||47||" |
| `Line 6976: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6977: श्येनपादपरिभ्रष्टं तद्वीर्यमथ वासवम् |` | "Then that seed of Vāsava [Indra], which had fallen from the falcon's claw," |
| `Line 6978: जग्राह तरसोपेत्य साद्रिका मत्स्यरूपिणी ||४८||` | "Was quickly swallowed by Adrikā in the form of a fish [matsyarūpiṇī]. ||48||" |
| `Line 6979: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6980: कदाचिदथ मत्सीं तां बबन्धुर्मत्स्यजीविनः |` | "Then once, that female fish was caught by fishermen [matsyajīvinaḥ]," |
| `Line 6981: मासे च दशमे प्राप्ते तदा भरतसत्तम ||४९||` | "And when the tenth month arrived, O best of Bharatas [bharatasattama], ||49||" |
| `Line 6982: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6983: उज्जह्रुरुदरात्तस्याः स्त्रीपुमांसं च मानुषम् ||४९||` | "They extracted from her belly a human male and female. ||49||" |
| `Line 6984: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6985: आश्चर्यभूतं मत्वा तद्राज्ञस्ते प्रत्यवेदयन् |` | "Considering this a marvel [āścaryabhūtam], they reported to the king," |
| `Line 6986: काये मत्स्या इमौ राजन्सम्भूतौ मानुषाविति ||५०||` | "'O king, these two human beings have been born in the body of a fish.' ||50||" |
| `Line 6987: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6988: तयोः पुमांसं जग्राह राजोपरिचरस्तदा |` | "Then King Uparicara [royal name] took the male of the two," |
| `Line 6989: स मत्स्यो नाम राजासीद्धार्मिकः सत्यसङ्गरः ||५१||` | "He became a king named Matsya [Fish], righteous and true to his promises. ||51||" |
| `Line 6990: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6991: साप्सरा मुक्तशापा च क्षणेन समपद्यत |` | "And the Apsarā [celestial nymph], freed from the curse, was restored in an instant," |
| `Line 6992: पुरोक्ता या भगवता तिर्यग्योनिगता शुभे ||५२||` | "She who had been previously told by the Lord [bhagavata], 'O auspicious one, having entered animal birth [tiryagyoni], ||52||" |
| `Line 6993: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6994: मानुषौ जनयित्वा त्वं शापमोक्षमवाप्स्यसि ||५२||` | "After giving birth to human beings, you shall obtain release from the curse.' ||52||" |
| `Line 6995: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6996: ततः सा जनयित्वा तौ विशस्ता मत्स्यघातिना |` | "Then, after giving birth to those two, she was killed by a fisherman [matsyaghātin]," |
| `Line 6997: सन्त्यज्य मत्स्यरूपं सा दिव्यं रूपमवाप्य च ||५३||` | "And abandoning her fish form, she attained a divine form. ||53||" |
| `Line 6998: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 6999: सिद्धर्षिचारणपथं जगामाथ वराप्सराः ||५३||` | "Then that excellent apsara [celestial nymph] went to the realm of Siddhas, Rishis, and Charanas [celestial beings]. ||53||" |
| `Line 7000: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7001: या कन्या दुहिता तस्या मत्स्या मत्स्यसगन्धिनी |` | "The girl who was her daughter, Matsya [fish-born], had the scent of fish," |
| `Line 7002: राज्ञा दत्ताथ दाशाय इयं तव भवत्विति ||५४||` | "Was given by the king to the fisherman [dāśa], saying, 'Let her be yours.' ||54||" |
| `Line 7003: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7004: रूपसत्त्वसमायुक्ता सर्वैः समुदिता गुणैः ||५४||` | "She was endowed with beauty and character, adorned with all virtues. ||54||" |
| `Line 7005: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7006: सा तु सत्यवती नाम मत्स्यघात्यभिसंश्रयात् |` | "She was named Satyavati, and because of her association with the fisherman [matsyaghātin]," |
| `Line 7007: आसीन्मत्स्यसगन्धैव कञ्चित्कालं शुचिस्मिता ||५५||` | "She had the scent of fish for some time, though she had a pure smile. ||55||" |
| `Line 7008: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7009: शुश्रूषार्थं पितुर्नावं तां तु वाहयतीं जले |` | "While she was rowing a boat in the water to serve her father," |
| `Line 7010: तीर्थयात्रां परिक्रामन्नपश्यद्वै पराशरः ||५६||` | "Parashara, who was traveling on a pilgrimage [tīrthayātrā], saw her. ||56||" |
| `Line 7011: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7012: अतीव रूपसम्पन्नां सिद्धानामपि काङ्क्षिताम् |` | "Exceedingly beautiful, desired even by the Siddhas [accomplished beings]," |
| `Line 7013: दृष्ट्वैव च स तां धीमांश्चकमे चारुदर्शनाम् ||५७||` | "Seeing her, that wise one desired the lovely-looking woman. ||57||" |
| `Line 7014: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7015: विद्वांस्तां वासवीं कन्यां कार्यवान्मुनिपुङ्गवः ||५७||` | "That learned and purposeful foremost sage [munipuṅgava] (recognized) her as a maiden of divine origin [vāsavī]. ||57||" |
| `Line 7016: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7017: साब्रवीत्पश्य भगवन्पारावारे ऋषीन्स्थितान् |` | "She said, 'Look, O lord [bhagavan], at the sages [ṛṣis] standing on the opposite shore," |
| `Line 7018: आवयोर्दृश्यतोरेभिः कथं नु स्यात्समागमः ||५८||` | "How can we unite while being observed by them?' ||58||" |
| `Line 7019: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7020: एवं तयोक्तो भगवान्नीहारमसृजत्प्रभुः |` | "Thus addressed by her, the lord [bhagavan], the master, created a mist," |
| `Line 7021: येन देशः स सर्वस्तु तमोभूत इवाभवत् ||५९||` | "By which that entire place became as if covered in darkness. ||59||" |
| `Line 7022: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7023: दृष्ट्वा सृष्टं तु नीहारं ततस्तं परमर्षिणा |` | "Seeing the mist created by that great sage [paramarṣi]," |
| `Line 7024: विस्मिता चाब्रवीत्कन्या व्रीडिता च मनस्विनी ||६०||` | "The thoughtful maiden spoke, astonished and embarrassed: ||60||" |
| `Line 7025: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7026: विद्धि मां भगवन्कन्यां सदा पितृवशानुगाम् |` | "'Know me, O lord [bhagavan], as a maiden always obedient to her father," |
| `Line 7027: त्वत्संयोगाच्च दुष्येत कन्याभावो ममानघ ||६१||` | "And through union with you, my maidenhood would be defiled, O sinless one [anagha]. ||61||" |
| `Line 7028: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7029: कन्यात्वे दूषिते चापि कथं शक्ष्ये द्विजोत्तम |` | "With my maidenhood defiled, how shall I be able, O best of the twice-born [dvijottama]," |
| `Line 7030: गन्तुं गृहं गृहे चाहं धीमन्न स्थातुमुत्सहे ||६२||` | "To return home, and in my home, O wise one [dhīman], I would not have the courage to remain. ||62||" |
| `Line 7031: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7032: एतत्सञ्चिन्त्य भगवन्विधत्स्व यदनन्तरम् ||६२||` | "Considering this, O lord [bhagavan], determine what should follow.' ||62||" |
| `Line 7033: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7034: एवमुक्तवतीं तां तु प्रीतिमानृषिसत्तमः |` | "To her who had spoken thus, the pleased best of sages [ṛṣisattama]," |
| `Line 7035: उवाच मत्प्रियं कृत्वा कन्यैव त्वं भविष्यसि ||६३||` | "Said, 'After doing what pleases me, you shall remain a maiden still.' ||63||" |
| `Line 7036: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7037: वृणीष्व च वरं भीरु यं त्वमिच्छसि भामिनि |` | "Choose a boon, O timid one [bhīru], whichever you desire, O beautiful lady [bhāminī]," |
| `Line 7038: वृथा हि न प्रसादो मे भूतपूर्वः शुचिस्मिते ||६४||` | "For my favor has never before been given in vain, O pure-smiling one [śucismite]. ||64||" |
| `Line 7039: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7040: एवमुक्ता वरं वव्रे गात्रसौगन्ध्यमुत्तमम् |` | "Thus addressed, she chose the boon of supreme bodily fragrance [gātrasaugandhya]," |
| `Line 7041: स चास्यै भगवान्प्रादान्मनसः काङ्क्षितं प्रभुः ||६५||` | "And the lord [bhagavān], the master [prabhuḥ], granted her the heart's desire. ||65||" |
| `Line 7042: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7043: ततो लब्धवरा प्रीता स्त्रीभावगुणभूषिता |` | "Then, having received the boon, she was pleased, adorned with feminine qualities [strībhāvaguṇa]," |
| `Line 7044: जगाम सह संसर्गमृषिणाद्भुतकर्मणा ||६६||` | "And she had union with the sage [ṛṣi] of wonderful deeds [adbhutakarmaṇā]. ||66||" |
| `Line 7045: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7046: तेन गन्धवतीत्येव नामास्याः प्रथितं भुवि |` | "Therefore, the name 'Gandhavatī' [fragrant one] became famous for her on earth," |
| `Line 7047: तस्यास्तु योजनाद्गन्धमाजिघ्रन्ति नरा भुवि ||६७||` | "And men on earth could smell her fragrance from a yojana [distance measure] away. ||67||" |
| `Line 7048: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7049: ततो योजनगन्धेति तस्या नाम परिश्रुतम् |` | "Thus, the name 'Yojanagandha' [yojana-fragrant] became well-known for her," |
| `Line 7050: पराशरोऽपि भगवाञ्जगाम स्वं निवेशनम् ||६८||` | "And the venerable [bhagavān] Parāśara also went to his own dwelling. ||68||" |
| `Line 7051: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7052: इति सत्यवती हृष्टा लब्ध्वा वरमनुत्तमम् |` | "Thus Satyavatī, delighted after obtaining the excellent boon," |
| `Line 7053: पराशरेण संयुक्ता सद्यो गर्भं सुषाव सा ||६९||` | "Having united with Parāśara, immediately gave birth to a child. ||69||" |
| `Line 7054: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7055: जज्ञे च यमुनाद्वीपे पाराशर्यः स वीर्यवान् ||६९||` | "And on an island [dvīpa] in the Yamunā was born that mighty [vīryavān] son of Parāśara. ||69||" |
| `Line 7056: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7057: स मातरमुपस्थाय तपस्येव मनो दधे |` | "After attending to his mother, he set his mind on austerities [tapas]," |
| `Line 7058: स्मृतोऽहं दर्शयिष्यामि कृत्येष्विति च सोऽब्रवीत् ||७०||` | "And he said, 'When remembered, I shall appear for important tasks [kṛtya].' ||70||" |
| `Line 7059: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7060: एवं द्वैपायनो जज्ञे सत्यवत्यां पराशरात् |` | "Thus was Dvaipāyana born to Satyavatī from Parāśara," |
| `Line 7061: द्वीपे न्यस्तः स यद्बालस्तस्माद्द्वैपायनोऽभवत् ||७१||` | "Since as a child he was placed on an island [dvīpa], therefore he became known as Dvaipāyana [island-born]. ||71||" |
| `Line 7062: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7063: पादापसारिणं धर्मं विद्वान्स तु युगे युगे |` | "That learned one, observing dharma [righteousness] diminishing quarter by quarter in each age [yuga]," |
| `Line 7064: आयुः शक्तिं च मर्त्यानां युगानुगमवेक्ष्य च ||७२||` | "And seeing the lifespan and strength of mortals declining with each passing age [yuga]. ||72||" |
| `Line 7065: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7066: ब्रह्मणो ब्राह्मणानां च तथानुग्रहकाम्यया |` | "Out of compassion for Brahma and the Brahmins [brāhmaṇa]," |
| `Line 7067: विव्यास वेदान्यस्माच्च तस्माद्व्यास इति स्मृतः ||७३||` | "He divided [vivyāsa] the Vedas, and therefore he is remembered as Vyāsa [compiler]. ||73||" |
| `Line 7068: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7069: वेदानध्यापयामास महाभारतपञ्चमान् |` | "He taught the Vedas with the Mahābhārata as the fifth," |
| `Line 7070: सुमन्तुं जैमिनिं पैलं शुकं चैव स्वमात्मजम् ||७४||` | "To Sumantu, Jaimini, Paila, and Śuka, his own son. ||74||" |
| `Line 7071: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7072: प्रभुर्वरिष्ठो वरदो वैशम्पायनमेव च |` | "The master [prabhu], most excellent, bestower of boons, (taught) Vaiśampāyana as well," |
| `Line 7073: संहितास्तैः पृथक्त्वेन भारतस्य प्रकाशिताः ||७५||` | "By them separately the collections [saṃhitā] of the Bhārata were published. ||75||" |
| `Line 7074: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7075: तथा भीष्मः शान्तनवो गङ्गायाममितद्युतिः |` | "Similarly, Bhīṣma, son of Śantanu, of immeasurable splendor [amitadyuti], was born to Gaṅgā," |
| `Line 7076: वसुवीर्यात्समभवन्महावीर्यो महायशाः ||७६||` | "From Vasuvīrya was born the mighty-powered [mahāvīrya] and greatly renowned [mahāyaśāḥ] one. ||76||" |
| `Line 7077: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7078: शूले प्रोतः पुराणर्षिरचोरश्चोरशङ्कया |` | "An ancient sage [purāṇarṣi] was impaled on a stake, though not a thief [acora], but suspected of theft," |
| `Line 7079: अणीमाण्डव्य इति वै विख्यातः सुमहायशाः ||७७||` | "He was known as Aṇīmāṇḍavya, of great renown [sumahāyaśāḥ]. ||77||" |
| `Line 7080: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7081: स धर्ममाहूय पुरा महर्षिरिदमुक्तवान् |` | "That great sage [maharṣi] summoned Dharma [justice deity] and said this:" |
| `Line 7082: इषीकया मया बाल्यादेका विद्धा शकुन्तिका ||७८||` | "In my childhood, I pierced a small bird [śakuntikā] with a blade of grass [iṣīkā]. ||78||" |
| `Line 7083: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7084: तत्किल्बिषं स्मरे धर्म नान्यत्पापमहं स्मरे |` | "I remember that sin [kilbiṣa], O Dharma, I remember no other sin," |
| `Line 7085: तन्मे सहस्रसमितं कस्मान्नेहाजयत्तपः ||७९||` | "Why has my penance [tapas], equal to a thousand, not overcome that sin here? ||79||" |
| `Line 7086: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7087: गरीयान्ब्राह्मणवधः सर्वभूतवधाद्यतः |` | "Since killing a Brahmin [brāhmaṇavadha] is more grievous than killing any other being," |
| `Line 7088: तस्मात्त्वं किल्बिषादस्माच्छूद्रयोनौ जनिष्यसि ||८०||` | "Therefore, because of this sin, you shall be born in a Śūdra womb [śūdrayoni]. ||80||" |
| `Line 7089: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7090: तेन शापेन धर्मोऽपि शूद्रयोनावजायत |` | "By that curse [śāpa], even Dharma was born in a Śūdra womb," |
| `Line 7091: विद्वान्विदुररूपेण धार्मी तनुरकिल्बिषी ||८१||` | "As the wise Vidura [royal advisor], righteous [dhārmī] and sinless [akilbiṣī]. ||81||" |
| `Line 7092: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7093: सञ्जयो मुनिकल्पस्तु जज्ञे सूतो गवल्गणात् |` | "Sañjaya, sage-like [munikalpa], was born as a charioteer [sūta] from Gavalgaṇa," |
| `Line 7094: सूर्याच्च कुन्तिकन्यायां जज्ञे कर्णो महारथः ||८२||` | "And from Sūrya [sun god] and Kuntī [princess], was born Karṇa, the great warrior [mahāratha]. ||82||" |
| `Line 7095: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7096: सहजं कवचं बिभ्रत्कुण्डलोद्द्योतिताननः ||८२||` | "Wearing natural armor [sahaja kavaca], with his face illuminated by earrings [kuṇḍala]. ||82||" |
| `Line 7097: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7098: अनुग्रहार्थं लोकानां विष्णुर्लोकनमस्कृतः |` | "For the benefit [anugraha] of the worlds, Viṣṇu [preserver deity], who is worshipped by all worlds," |
| `Line 7099: वसुदेवात्तु देवक्यां प्रादुर्भूतो महायशाः ||८३||` | "Was born of great fame from Vasudeva through Devakī. ||83||" |
| `Line 7100: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7101: अनादिनिधनो देवः स कर्ता जगतः प्रभुः |` | "That god without beginning or end [anādinidhanā], the creator, the lord of the universe," |
| `Line 7102: अव्यक्तमक्षरं ब्रह्म प्रधानं निर्गुणात्मकम् ||८४||` | "The unmanifest [avyakta], imperishable Brahman [akṣara], the supreme, beyond all qualities [nirguṇa]. ||84||" |
| `Line 7103: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7104: आत्मानमव्ययं चैव प्रकृतिं प्रभवं परम् |` | "The immutable self [avyaya], primordial nature [prakṛti], the supreme source," |
| `Line 7105: पुरुषं विश्वकर्माणं सत्त्वयोगं ध्रुवाक्षरम् ||८५||` | "The cosmic person [puruṣa], creator of all [viśvakarmāṇa], united with purity [sattvayoga], the eternal imperishable [dhruvākṣara]. ||85||" |
| `Line 7106: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7107: अनन्तमचलं देवं हंसं नारायणं प्रभुम् |` | "The infinite [ananta], immovable god, the swan [haṃsa], Nārāyaṇa [Supreme Lord], the master," |
| `Line 7108: धातारमजरं नित्यं तमाहुः परमव्ययम् ||८६||` | "The creator [dhātāra], ageless, eternal - him they call the supreme immutable one. ||86||" |
| `Line 7109: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7110: पुरुषः स विभुः कर्ता सर्वभूतपितामहः |` | "That cosmic person [puruṣa], the all-pervading creator, the great-grandfather of all beings," |
| `Line 7111: धर्मसंवर्धनार्थाय प्रजज्ञेऽन्धकवृष्णिषु ||८७||` | "Was born among the Andhaka-Vṛṣṇis [Yādava clans] for the purpose of upholding dharma [righteousness]. ||87||" |
| `Line 7112: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7113: अस्त्रज्ञौ तु महावीर्यौ सर्वशस्त्रविशारदौ |` | "Two mighty warriors [mahāvīryau] skilled in weapons [astra], expert in all arms [śastra]," |
| `Line 7114: सात्यकिः कृतवर्मा च नारायणमनुव्रतौ ||८८||` | "Sātyaki and Kṛtavarmā, both devoted followers of Nārāyaṇa. ||88||" |
| `Line 7115: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7116: सत्यकाद्धृदिकाच्चैव जज्ञातेऽस्त्रविशारदौ ||८८||` | "From Satyaka and Hṛdika were born two experts in weapons [astraviśāradau]. ||88||" |
| `Line 7117: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7118: भरद्वाजस्य च स्कन्नं द्रोण्यां शुक्रमवर्धत |` | "And the seed [śukra] of Bharadvāja that fell [skanna] grew in Droṇī [Droṇa's mother]," |
| `Line 7119: महर्षेरुग्रतपसस्तस्माद्द्रोणो व्यजायत ||८९||` | "From that great sage [maharṣi] of fierce austerities [ugratapas], Droṇa was born. ||89||" |
| `Line 7120: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7121: गौतमान्मिथुनं जज्ञे शरस्तम्बाच्छरद्वतः |` | "From Gautama was born a pair [mithuna], and from a clump of reeds [śarastamba] was born Śaradvat," |
| `Line 7122: अश्वत्थाम्नश्च जननी कृपश्चैव महाबलः ||९०||` | "The mother of Aśvatthāman and the mighty [mahābala] Kṛpa. ||90||" |
| `Line 7123: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7124: अश्वत्थामा ततो जज्ञे द्रोणादस्त्रभृतां वरः ||९०||` | "Then from Droṇa was born Aśvatthāman, the best among weapon-bearers [astrabhr̥tāṃ vara]. ||90||" |
| `Line 7125: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7126: तथैव धृष्टद्युम्नोऽपि साक्षादग्निसमद्युतिः |` | "Likewise, Dhṛṣṭadyumna too, with radiance equal to fire [agnisama-dyuti] itself," |
| `Line 7127: वैताने कर्मणि तते पावकात्समजायत ||९१||` | "Was born from the fire [pāvaka] during the performance of a sacrificial ritual [vaitāna karmaṇi]. ||91||" |
| `Line 7128: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7129: वीरो द्रोणविनाशाय धनुषा सह वीर्यवान् ||९१||` | "The heroic [vīra] and powerful one [vīryavān] was born with a bow to destroy Droṇa. ||91||" |
| `Line 7130: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7131: तथैव वेद्यां कृष्णापि जज्ञे तेजस्विनी शुभा |` | "Similarly, Kṛṣṇā [Draupadī] too was born from the altar [vedyām], radiant [tejasvinī] and auspicious [śubhā]," |
| `Line 7132: विभ्राजमाना वपुषा बिभ्रती रूपमुत्तमम् ||९२||` | "Shining with her form [vapuṣā], bearing supreme beauty [rūpam uttamam]. ||92||" |
| `Line 7133: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7134: प्रह्रादशिष्यो नग्नजित्सुबलश्चाभवत्ततः |` | "Nagnajit was a disciple of Prahlāda, and then came Subala," |
| `Line 7135: तस्य प्रजा धर्महन्त्री जज्ञे देवप्रकोपनात् ||९३||` | "His progeny [prajā], destroyers of dharma [dharmahantrī], were born due to the gods' anger [devaprakopanāt]. ||93||" |
| `Line 7136: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7137: गान्धारराजपुत्रोऽभूच्छकुनिः सौबलस्तथा |` | "Śakuni was the son of the Gāndhāra king, also known as Saubala [son of Subala]," |
| `Line 7138: दुर्योधनस्य माता च जज्ञातेऽर्थविदावुभौ ||९४||` | "And Duryodhana's mother - both were born knowledgeable in matters of wealth [arthavidau]. ||94||" |
| `Line 7139: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7140: कृष्णद्वैपायनाज्जज्ञे धृतराष्ट्रो जनेश्वरः |` | "From Kṛṣṇa Dvaipāyana [Vyāsa] was born Dhṛtarāṣṭra, the ruler of people [janeśvara]," |
| `Line 7141: क्षेत्रे विचित्रवीर्यस्य पाण्डुश्चैव महाबलः ||९५||` | "In the field [kṣetra] of Vicitravīrya, and also Pāṇḍu of great strength [mahābala]. ||95||" |
| `Line 7142: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7143: पाण्डोस्तु जज्ञिरे पञ्च पुत्रा देवसमाः पृथक् |` | "To Pāṇḍu were born five sons equal to gods [devasamāḥ], each from different sources," |
| `Line 7144: द्वयोः स्त्रियोर्गुणज्येष्ठस्तेषामासीद्युधिष्ठिरः ||९६||` | "Of the two wives, Yudhiṣṭhira was the eldest in virtue [guṇajyeṣṭha] among them. ||96||" |
| `Line 7145: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7146: धर्माद्युधिष्ठिरो जज्ञे मारुतात्तु वृकोदरः |` | "Yudhiṣṭhira was born from Dharma [justice deity], and Vṛkodara [Bhīma] from Maruta [wind god]," |
| `Line 7147: इन्द्राद्धनञ्जयः श्रीमान्सर्वशस्त्रभृतां वरः ||९७||` | "From Indra was born the illustrious Dhanañjaya [Arjuna], the best among all weapon-bearers [śastrabhṛtām]. ||97||" |
| `Line 7148: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7149: जज्ञाते रूपसम्पन्नावश्विभ्यां तु यमावुभौ |` | "From the Aśvins [divine twins] were born the twins, both endowed with beauty [rūpasampanna]," |
| `Line 7150: नकुलः सहदेवश्च गुरुशुश्रूषणे रतौ ||९८||` | "Nakula and Sahadeva, both devoted to serving their elders [guruśuśrūṣaṇe]. ||98||" |
| `Line 7151: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7152: तथा पुत्रशतं जज्ञे धृतराष्ट्रस्य धीमतः |` | "Likewise, a hundred sons were born to the wise Dhṛtarāṣṭra [dhīmataḥ]," |
| `Line 7153: दुर्योधनप्रभृतयो युयुत्सुः करणस्तथा ||९९||` | "Duryodhana and others, as well as Yuyutsu and Karaṇa. ||99||" |
| `Line 7154: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7155: अभिमन्युः सुभद्रायामर्जुनादभ्यजायत |` | "Abhimanyu was born to Subhadrā from Arjuna," |
| `Line 7156: स्वस्रीयो वासुदेवस्य पौत्रः पाण्डोर्महात्मनः ||१००||` | "The nephew of Vāsudeva [Krishna] and grandson of the noble-souled Pāṇḍu. ||100||" |
| `Line 7157: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7158: पाण्डवेभ्योऽपि पञ्चभ्यः कृष्णायां पञ्च जज्ञिरे |` | "From the five Pāṇḍavas, five sons were born to Kṛṣṇā [Draupadī]," |
| `Line 7159: कुमारा रूपसम्पन्नाः सर्वशस्त्रविशारदाः ||१०१||` | "Princes endowed with beauty and skilled in all weapons. ||101||" |
| `Line 7160: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7161: प्रतिविन्ध्यो युधिष्ठिरात्सुतसोमो वृकोदरात् |` | "Prativindhya from Yudhiṣṭhira, Sutasoma from Vṛkodara [Bhīma]," |
| `Line 7162: अर्जुनाच्छ्रुतकीर्तिस्तु शतानीकस्तु नाकुलिः ||१०२||` | "Śrutakīrti from Arjuna, and Śatānīka from Nakula. ||102||" |
| `Line 7163: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7164: तथैव सहदेवाच्च श्रुतसेनः प्रतापवान् |` | "And likewise from Sahadeva, the valiant Śrutasena," |
| `Line 7165: हिडिम्बायां च भीमेन वने जज्ञे घटोत्कचः ||१०३||` | "And from Bhīma and Hiḍimbā was born Ghaṭotkaca in the forest. ||103||" |
| `Line 7166: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7167: शिखण्डी द्रुपदाज्जज्ञे कन्या पुत्रत्वमागता |` | "Śikhaṇḍī was born to Drupada, a daughter who attained the state of a son," |
| `Line 7168: यां यक्षः पुरुषं चक्रे स्थूणः प्रियचिकीर्षया ||१०४||` | "Whom the Yakṣa [supernatural being] Sthūṇa transformed into a man out of desire to please. ||104||" |

| `Line 7186: जनमेजय उवाच||` | "Janamejaya said:" |

| `Line 7188: य एते कीर्तिता ब्रह्मन्ये चान्ये नानुकीर्तिताः |` | "These who have been mentioned, O Brahmin [brahman], and others who have not been enumerated," |
| `Line 7189: सम्यक्ताञ्श्रोतुमिच्छामि राज्ञश्चान्यान्सुवर्चसः ||१||` | "I wish to hear about them properly, and about other splendid [suvarcas] kings. ||1||" |
| `Line 7190: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7192: भुवि तन्मे महाभाग सम्यगाख्यातुमर्हसि ||२||` | "On earth - that, O fortunate one [mahābhāga], you should properly explain to me. ||2||" |
| `Line 7193: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7194: वैशम्पायन उवाच||` | "Vaiśampāyana said:" |
| `Line 7195: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7196: रहस्यं खल्विदं राजन्देवानामिति नः श्रुतम् |` | "This is indeed a secret of the gods [devas], O king [rājan], as we have heard," |
| `Line 7197: तत्तु ते कथयिष्यामि नमस्कृत्वा स्वयम्भुवे ||३||` | "But I shall tell it to you, after bowing to the Self-born One [Brahmā]. ||3||" |
| `Line 7198: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7199: त्रिःसप्तकृत्वः पृथिवीं कृत्वा निःक्षत्रियां पुरा |` | "After making the earth devoid of Kshatriyas [warriors] twenty-one times in the past," |
| `Line 7200: जामदग्न्यस्तपस्तेपे महेन्द्रे पर्वतोत्तमे ||४||` | "Jāmadagnya [Paraśurāma] performed austerities on Mahendra, the best of mountains. ||4||" |
| `Line 7201: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7202: तदा निःक्षत्रिये लोके भार्गवेण कृते सति |` | "When the world was made devoid of Kshatriyas by Bhārgava [Paraśurāma]," |
| `Line 7203: ब्राह्मणान्क्षत्रिया राजन्गर्भार्थिन्योऽभिचक्रमुः ||५||` | "The Kshatriya women [warrior women] desiring offspring approached the Brahmins, O king. ||5||" |
| `Line 7204: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7205: ताभिः सह समापेतुर्ब्राह्मणाः संशितव्रताः |` | "The Brahmins of strict vows [saṃśitavratāḥ] united with these women," |
| `Line 7206: ऋतावृतौ नरव्याघ्र न कामान्नानृतौ तथा ||६||` | "Only during their fertile season [ṛtu], O tiger among men [naravyāghra], not out of lust nor in their infertile period. ||6||" |
| `Line 7207: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7208: तेभ्यस्तु लेभिरे गर्भान्क्षत्रियास्ताः सहस्रशः |` | "From them, those Kshatriya women conceived thousands of embryos," |
| `Line 7209: ततः सुषुविरे राजन्क्षत्रियान्वीर्यसंमतान् ||७||` | "Then, O king, they gave birth to Kshatriyas endowed with valor [vīrya]. ||7||" |
| `Line 7210: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7211: कुमारांश्च कुमारीश्च पुनः क्षत्राभिवृद्धये ||७||` | "Both boys and girls, for the increase of the Kshatriya race again. ||7||" |
| `Line 7212: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7213: एवं तद्ब्राह्मणैः क्षत्रं क्षत्रियासु तपस्विभिः |` | "Thus the Kshatriya race [kṣatra] was born from ascetic Brahmins [tapasvi] and Kshatriya women," |
| `Line 7214: जातमृध्यत धर्मेण सुदीर्घेणायुषान्वितम् ||८||` | "Born and flourishing righteously [dharmeṇa], endowed with very long life. ||8||" |
| `Line 7215: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7216: चत्वारोऽपि तदा वर्णा बभूवुर्ब्राह्मणोत्तराः ||८||` | "At that time, all four varṇas [social classes] existed with Brahmins [brahmaṇa] as the foremost. ||8||" |
| `Line 7217: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7218: अभ्यगच्छन्नृतौ नारीं न कामान्नानृतौ तथा |` | "Men approached women only during their fertile season [ṛtu], not out of mere desire, nor outside the proper time." |
| `Line 7219: तथैवान्यानि भूतानि तिर्यग्योनिगतान्यपि ||९||` | "Similarly, other beings, even those born in animal species [tiryagyoni], also (followed this rule). ||9||" |
| `Line 7220: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7222: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7223: ततोऽवर्धन्त धर्मेण सहस्रशतजीविनः |` | "Thus they flourished righteously, living for hundreds and thousands (of years)," |
| `Line 7224: ताः प्रजाः पृथिवीपाल धर्मव्रतपरायणाः ||१०||` | "Those people, O protector of the earth [pṛthivīpāla], were devoted to righteous vows [dharmavrata]. ||10||" |
| `Line 7225: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7227: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7230: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7232: ब्राह्मणाद्यास्तदा वर्णा लेभिरे मुदमुत्तमाम् ||१२||` | "Then all the varṇas, beginning with the Brahmins, attained supreme happiness. ||12||" |
| `Line 7233: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7234: कामक्रोधोद्भवान्दोषान्निरस्य च नराधिपाः |` | "The kings [narādhipā], having cast aside the faults arising from desire and anger," |
| `Line 7235: दण्डं दण्ड्येषु धर्मेण प्रणयन्तोऽन्वपालयन् ||१३||` | "Righteously administered punishment [daṇḍa] to those deserving it, and thus protected (the people). ||13||" |
| `Line 7236: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7237: तथा धर्मपरे क्षत्रे सहस्राक्षः शतक्रतुः |` | "Thus, when the kṣatriyas [warrior class] were devoted to dharma [righteousness], Sahasrākṣa [thousand-eyed Indra] Śatakratu [performer of hundred sacrifices]," |

| `Line 7239: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7240: न बाल एव म्रियते तदा कश्चिन्नराधिप |` | "No child died prematurely in those days, O ruler of men [narādhipa]," |
| `Line 7241: न च स्त्रियं प्रजानाति कश्चिदप्राप्तयौवनः ||१५||` | "And no one knew a woman [carnally] before attaining youth [proper age]. ||15||" |
| `Line 7242: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7244: इयं सागरपर्यन्ता समापूर्यत मेदिनी ||१६||` | "This earth, bounded by the ocean, became completely filled. ||16||" |
| `Line 7245: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7248: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7250: न च शूद्रसमाभ्याशे वेदानुच्चारयन्त्युत ||१८||` | "Nor did they recite the Vedas [sacred texts] in the proximity of śūdras [servant class]. ||18||" |
| `Line 7251: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7254: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7256: न कूटमानैर्वणिजः पण्यं विक्रीणते तदा ||२०||` | "Merchants did not sell goods using false measures [kūṭamāna] at that time. ||20||" |
| `Line 7257: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7258: कर्माणि च नरव्याघ्र धर्मोपेतानि मानवाः |` | "And, O tiger among men [naravyāghra], humans performed actions that were in accordance with dharma [righteousness]," |
| `Line 7259: धर्ममेवानुपश्यन्तश्चक्रुर्धर्मपरायणाः ||२१||` | "Seeing only dharma, they acted devoted to dharma [dharmaparāyaṇa]. ||21||" |
| `Line 7260: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7262: एवं तदा नरव्याघ्र धर्मो न ह्रसते क्वचित् ||२२||` | "Thus, O tiger among men [naravyāghra], dharma did not diminish anywhere at that time. ||22||" |
| `Line 7263: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7264: काले गावः प्रसूयन्ते नार्यश्च भरतर्षभ |` | "Cows and women gave birth in their proper time, O bull among Bharatas [Bharatarṣabha]," |
| `Line 7265: फलन्त्यृतुषु वृक्षाश्च पुष्पाणि च फलानि च ||२३||` | "And trees bore flowers and fruits in their proper seasons. ||23||" |
| `Line 7266: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7267: एवं कृतयुगे सम्यग्वर्तमाने तदा नृप |` | "Thus, O king [nṛpa], when the Kṛta Yuga [golden age] was properly functioning," |
| `Line 7268: आपूर्यत मही कृत्स्ना प्राणिभिर्बहुभिर्भृशम् ||२४||` | "The entire earth became abundantly filled with many living beings. ||24||" |
| `Line 7269: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7270: ततः समुदिते लोके मानुषे भरतर्षभ |` | "Then, when the human world was prospering, O bull among Bharatas [Bharatarṣabha]," |
| `Line 7271: असुरा जज्ञिरे क्षेत्रे राज्ञां मनुजपुङ्गव ||२५||` | "Asuras [demons] were born in the realm of kings, O foremost among men [manujapuṅgava]. ||25||" |
| `Line 7272: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7273: आदित्यैर्हि तदा दैत्या बहुशो निर्जिता युधि |` | "For the Daityas [demon clan], repeatedly defeated in battle by the Ādityas [gods]," |
| `Line 7274: ऐश्वर्याद्भ्रंशिताश्चापि सम्बभूवुः क्षिताविह ||२६||` | "And deprived of their sovereignty, took birth here on earth. ||26||" |
| `Line 7275: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7276: इह देवत्वमिच्छन्तो मानुषेषु मनस्विनः |` | "Here, desiring divinity [devatva], the intelligent ones [manasvinaḥ] among humans," |
| `Line 7277: जज्ञिरे भुवि भूतेषु तेषु तेष्वसुरा विभो ||२७||` | "Were born on earth among various beings, and among them were the Asuras [demons], O mighty one [vibho]. ||27||" |
| `Line 7278: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7280: क्रव्यादेषु च भूतेषु गजेषु च मृगेषु च ||२८||` | "And among carnivorous [kravyāda] creatures, elephants, and wild animals. ||28||" |
| `Line 7281: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7283: न शशाकात्मनात्मानमियं धारयितुं धरा ||२९||` | "This earth [dharā] was unable to sustain herself by herself. ||29||" |
| `Line 7284: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7286: दितेः पुत्रा दनोश्चैव तस्माल्लोकादिह च्युताः ||३०||` | "Sons of Diti and Danu, fallen here from that world [celestial realm]. ||30||" |
| `Line 7287: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7289: इमां सागरपर्यन्तां परीयुररिमर्दनाः ||३१||` | "Roamed this earth bounded by oceans, crushing their enemies [arimardanāḥ]. ||31||" |
| `Line 7290: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7291: ब्राह्मणान्क्षत्रियान्वैश्याञ्शूद्रांश्चैवाप्यपीडयन् |` | "They oppressed Brahmins, Kshatriyas, Vaishyas, and Shudras," |
| `Line 7292: अन्यानि चैव भूतानि पीडयामासुरोजसा ||३२||` | "And other beings too they tormented with their might [ojasā]. ||32||" |
| `Line 7293: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7295: विचेरुः सर्वतो राजन्महीं शतसहस्रशः ||३३||` | "They wandered all over the earth, O king [rājan], in hundreds of thousands. ||33||" |
| `Line 7296: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7297: आश्रमस्थान्महर्षींश्च धर्षयन्तस्ततस्ततः |` | "Violating the great sages [maharṣis] dwelling in hermitages [āśramas] here and there," |
| `Line 7298: अब्रह्मण्या वीर्यमदा मत्ता मदबलेन च ||३४||` | "Impious [abrahmaṇya], intoxicated with their strength, and maddened by the power of their arrogance. ||34||" |
| `Line 7299: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7300: एवं वीर्यबलोत्सिक्तैर्भूरियं तैर्महासुरैः |` | "Thus, this earth, oppressed by those mighty demons [mahāsuras] swollen with the pride of their power," |
| `Line 7301: पीड्यमाना महीपाल ब्रह्माणमुपचक्रमे ||३५||` | "Approached Brahmā [creator deity], O protector of the earth [mahīpāla]. ||35||" |
| `Line 7302: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7303: न हीमां पवनो राजन्न नागा न नगा महीम् |` | "Neither the wind [pavana], O king, nor the serpents [nāgas], nor the mountains [nagas] could then," |
| `Line 7304: तदा धारयितुं शेकुराक्रान्तां दानवैर्बलात् ||३६||` | "Support this earth forcibly overrun by the demons [dānavas]. ||36||" |
| `Line 7305: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7306: ततो मही महीपाल भारार्ता भयपीडिता |` | "Then the earth [mahī], O protector of the earth [mahīpāla], distressed by the burden and afflicted with fear," |
| `Line 7307: जगाम शरणं देवं सर्वभूतपितामहम् ||३७||` | "Went for refuge to the god who is the grandfather of all beings [sarvabhūtapitāmaha]. ||37||" |
| `Line 7308: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7309: सा संवृतं महाभागैर्देवद्विजमहर्षिभिः |` | "She saw the god Brahmā surrounded by the illustrious [mahābhāga] gods, twice-born [dvija], and great sages [maharṣis]," |
| `Line 7310: ददर्श देवं ब्रह्माणं लोककर्तारमव्ययम् ||३८||` | "The imperishable [avyaya] creator of the worlds [lokakartā]. ||38||" |
| `Line 7311: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7312: गन्धर्वैरप्सरोभिश्च बन्दिकर्मसु निष्ठितैः |` | "With Gandharvas [celestial musicians] and Apsaras [celestial nymphs] skilled in the art of praise," |
| `Line 7313: वन्द्यमानं मुदोपेतैर्ववन्दे चैनमेत्य सा ||३९||` | "Being praised by them filled with joy, she approached and bowed to him. ||39||" |
| `Line 7314: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7315: अथ विज्ञापयामास भूमिस्तं शरणार्थिनी |` | "Then the Earth [bhūmi], seeking refuge [śaraṇārthinī], made her petition to him," |
| `Line 7316: संनिधौ लोकपालानां सर्वेषामेव भारत ||४०||` | "in the presence of all the Lokapālas [world guardians], O Bhārata [descendant of Bharata]. ||40||" |
| `Line 7317: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7318: तत्प्रधानात्मनस्तस्य भूमेः कृत्यं स्वयम्भुवः |` | "The purpose of that supreme being, the Self-born [Svayambhu/Brahmā], regarding Earth's plight," |
| `Line 7319: पूर्वमेवाभवद्राजन्विदितं परमेष्ठिनः ||४१||` | "was already known beforehand, O King, to the Supreme Lord [Parameṣṭhin]. ||41||" |
| `Line 7320: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7321: स्रष्टा हि जगतः कस्मान्न सम्बुध्येत भारत |` | "For how could the Creator [Sraṣṭā] of the universe not understand, O Bhārata," |
| `Line 7322: सुरासुराणां लोकानामशेषेण मनोगतम् ||४२||` | "the thoughts of all the worlds of gods and demons [surāsura] completely? ||42||" |
| `Line 7323: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7324: तमुवाच महाराज भूमिं भूमिपतिर्विभुः |` | "The all-pervading Lord [Vibhu], master of the earth, spoke to Earth, O great king," |
| `Line 7325: प्रभवः सर्वभूतानामीशः शम्भुः प्रजापतिः ||४३||` | "He who is the origin of all beings, the ruler, the benevolent one [Śambhu], the lord of creatures [Prajāpati]. ||43||" |
| `Line 7326: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7327: यदर्थमसि सम्प्राप्ता मत्सकाशं वसुन्धरे |` | "'For the purpose that you have come to me, O Earth [Vasundharā]," |
| `Line 7328: तदर्थं संनियोक्ष्यामि सर्वानेव दिवौकसः ||४४||` | "for that purpose I shall engage all the celestial beings [divaukas].' ||44||" |
| `Line 7329: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7330: इत्युक्त्वा स महीं देवो ब्रह्मा राजन्विसृज्य च |` | "Having spoken thus to Earth and dismissing her, O King, the god Brahmā," |
| `Line 7331: आदिदेश तदा सर्वान्विबुधान्भूतकृत्स्वयम् ||४५||` | "the creator of beings [bhūtakṛt] himself then instructed all the gods [vibudha]. ||45||" |
| `Line 7332: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7333: अस्या भूमेर्निरसितुं भारं भागैः पृथक्पृथक् |` | "'To remove the burden of this Earth with your respective portions [bhāga]," |
| `Line 7334: अस्यामेव प्रसूयध्वं विरोधायेति चाब्रवीत् ||४६||` | "take birth on this very Earth to counter (the burden),' thus he spoke. ||46||" |
| `Line 7335: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7336: तथैव च समानीय गन्धर्वाप्सरसां गणान् |` | "Similarly, having assembled the hosts of Gandharvas [celestial musicians] and Apsaras [heavenly dancers]," |
| `Line 7337: उवाच भगवान्सर्वानिदं वचनमुत्तमम् ||४७||` | "The Lord [Bhagavān] spoke these excellent words to all of them: ||47||" |
| `Line 7338: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7339: स्वैरंशैः सम्प्रसूयध्वं यथेष्टं मानुषेष्विति ||४७||` | "'Be born among humans as you wish, through your own portions [aṃśa],' he said. ||47||" |
| `Line 7340: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7341: अथ शक्रादयः सर्वे श्रुत्वा सुरगुरोर्वचः |` | "Then Śakra [Indra] and all the others, having heard the words of the preceptor of the gods [Suraguru]," |
| `Line 7342: तथ्यमर्थ्यं च पथ्यं च तस्य ते जगृहुस्तदा ||४८||` | "Accepted his words then, which were truthful, meaningful, and beneficial. ||48||" |
| `Line 7343: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7344: अथ ते सर्वशोंऽशैः स्वैर्गन्तुं भूमिं कृतक्षणाः |` | "Then they, having found the right moment to go to earth with portions of themselves," |
| `Line 7345: नारायणममित्रघ्नं वैकुण्ठमुपचक्रमुः ||४९||` | "Approached Nārāyaṇa [Supreme Lord], the destroyer of enemies, the lord of Vaikuṇṭha [divine abode]. ||49||" |
| `Line 7346: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7347: यः स चक्रगदापाणिः पीतवासासितप्रभः |` | "He who holds the discus and mace in his hands, dressed in yellow garments, of dark radiance," |
| `Line 7348: पद्मनाभः सुरारिघ्नः पृथुचार्वञ्चितेक्षणः ||५०||` | "With a lotus in his navel [Padmanābha], destroyer of the enemies of gods, with large, beautiful, curved eyes. ||50||" |
| `Line 7349: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7350: तं भुवः शोधनायेन्द्र उवाच पुरुषोत्तमम् |` | "To him, for the purification of the earth, Indra [king of gods] spoke to that Supreme Person [Puruṣottama]:" |
| `Line 7351: अंशेनावतरस्वेति तथेत्याह च तं हरिः ||५१||` | "'Descend with a portion [of yourself],' and Hari [Viṣṇu] replied to him, 'So be it.' ||51||" |

| `Line 7361: वैशम्पायन उवाच||` | "Vaiśampāyana said:" |
| `Line 7362: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7363: अथ नारायणेनेन्द्रश्चकार सह संविदम् |` | "Then Indra [king of gods] made an agreement with Nārāyaṇa [Supreme Lord]," |
| `Line 7364: अवतर्तुं महीं स्वर्गादंशतः सहितः सुरैः ||१||` | "To descend to earth from heaven in partial form [aṃśataḥ], accompanied by the gods [suras]. ||1||" |
| `Line 7365: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7366: आदिश्य च स्वयं शक्रः सर्वानेव दिवौकसः |` | "And Śakra [Indra] himself, having instructed all the heaven-dwellers [divaukasas]," |
| `Line 7367: निर्जगाम पुनस्तस्मात्क्षयान्नारायणस्य ह ||२||` | "Departed again from that abode [kṣaya] of Nārāyaṇa. ||2||" |
| `Line 7368: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7369: तेऽमरारिविनाशाय सर्वलोकहिताय च |` | "They, for the destruction of the enemies of immortals [amarāri] and for the welfare of all worlds," |
| `Line 7370: अवतेरुः क्रमेणेमां महीं स्वर्गाद्दिवौकसः ||३||` | "Descended in succession to this earth from heaven, the celestial beings [divaukasas]. ||3||" |
| `Line 7371: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7372: ततो ब्रह्मर्षिवंशेषु पार्थिवर्षिकुलेषु च |` | "Then in the lineages of brahmarṣis [sage-seers] and in the families of royal sages [pārthivarṣi]," |
| `Line 7373: जज्ञिरे राजशार्दूल यथाकामं दिवौकसः ||४||` | "The celestial beings [divaukasas] were born according to their wishes, O tiger among kings [rājaśārdūla]. ||4||" |
| `Line 7374: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7375: दानवान्राक्षसांश्चैव गन्धर्वान्पन्नगांस्तथा |` | "The Dānavas [demon class], Rākṣasas [night-wanderers], Gandharvas [celestial musicians], and Pannagas [serpent beings] as well," |
| `Line 7376: पुरुषादानि चान्यानि जघ्नुः सत्त्वान्यनेकशः ||५||` | "And they killed many other man-eating [puruṣāda] creatures repeatedly. ||5||" |
| `Line 7377: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7378: दानवा राक्षसाश्चैव गन्धर्वाः पन्नगास्तथा |` | "Dānavas [demon class], Rākṣasas [night-wanderers], Gandharvas [celestial musicians], and Pannagas [serpents] as well," |
| `Line 7379: न तान्बलस्थान्बाल्येऽपि जघ्नुर्भरतसत्तम ||६||` | "They did not kill them even in childhood when they were in their full strength, O best of the Bharatas [bharatasattama]. ||6||" |
| `Line 7380: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7381: जनमेजय उवाच||` | "Janamejaya said:" |
| `Line 7382: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7383: देवदानवसङ्घानां गन्धर्वाप्सरसां तथा |` | "Of the hosts of Devas [gods] and Dānavas [demons], of Gandharvas [celestial musicians] and Apsarās [celestial nymphs] as well," |
| `Line 7384: मानवानां च सर्वेषां तथा वै यक्षरक्षसाम् ||७||` | "Of all humans [mānavas] and indeed of Yakṣas [wealth-spirits] and Rākṣasas [night-wanderers]. ||7||" |
| `Line 7385: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7387: प्राणिनां चैव सर्वेषां सर्वशः सर्वविद्ध्यसि ||८||` | "And of all living beings in every respect, for you know everything [sarvaviddhyasi]. ||8||" |

| `Line 7392: सुरादीनामहं सम्यग्लोकानां प्रभवाप्ययम् ||९||` | "The proper origin and dissolution of the worlds, beginning with the gods [suras] and others. ||9||" |
| `Line 7393: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7396: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7405: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7408: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7411: ` | "[Blank line]" |

| `Line 7414: ` | "[Blank line]" |
