| `Line 7444: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7445: अन्यौ तु खलु देवानां सूर्याचन्द्रमसौ स्मृतौ ||२६||` | "But indeed, two others named Sūrya and Candramasa are remembered among the gods [devas]. ||26||" |
| `Line 7446: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7447: इमे च वंशे प्रथिताः सत्त्ववन्तो महाबलाः |` | "And these renowned in the lineage, endowed with strength [sattvavanta] and great power [mahābalāḥ]," |
| `Line 7448: दनुपुत्रा महाराज दश दानवपुङ्गवाः ||२७||` | "Are ten foremost Dānavas [dānavapuṅgavāḥ], sons of Danu, O great king [mahārāja]. ||27||" |
| `Line 7449: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7450: एकाक्षो मृतपा वीरः प्रलम्बनरकावपि |` | "Ekākṣa, Mṛtapā the hero [vīra], Pralamba and Naraka too," |
| `Line 7451: वातापिः शत्रुतपनः शठश्चैव महासुरः ||२८||` | "Vātāpi, Śatrutapana, and Śaṭha the great demon [mahāsura]. ||28||" |
| `Line 7452: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7453: गविष्ठश्च दनायुश्च दीर्घजिह्वश्च दानवः |` | "Gaviṣṭha, Danāyu, and the long-tongued [dīrghajihva] Dānava," |
| `Line 7454: असङ्ख्येयाः स्मृतास्तेषां पुत्राः पौत्राश्च भारत ||२९||` | "Innumerable [asaṅkhyeyāḥ] are remembered to be their sons and grandsons, O Bhārata. ||29||" |
| `Line 7455: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7456: सिंहिका सुषुवे पुत्रं राहुं चन्द्रार्कमर्दनम् |` | "Siṃhikā gave birth to a son, Rāhu, the tormentor of the moon and sun [candrārkamardana]," |
| `Line 7457: सुचन्द्रं चन्द्रहन्तारं तथा चन्द्रविमर्दनम् ||३०||` | "And to Sucandra, Candrahantāra, and also Candravimardana. ||30||" |
| `Line 7458: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7459: क्रूरस्वभावं क्रूरायाः पुत्रपौत्रमनन्तकम् |` | "The cruel-natured [krūrasvabhāva] offspring and descendants of the cruel one [krūrāyāḥ] are endless," |
| `Line 7460: गणः क्रोधवशो नाम क्रूरकर्मारिमर्दनः ||३१||` | "A group called Krodhavaśa, performing cruel deeds and crushing enemies [krūrakarmārimardana]. ||31||" |
| `Line 7461: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7462: अनायुषः पुनः पुत्राश्चत्वारोऽसुरपुङ्गवाः |` | "The sons of Anāyuṣa were four eminent asuras [asurapuṅgava]," |
| `Line 7463: विक्षरो बलवीरौ च वृत्रश्चैव महासुरः ||३२||` | "Vikṣara, Bala and Vīra, and also Vṛtra, the great asura [mahāsura]. ||32||" |
| `Line 7464: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7465: कालायाः प्रथिताः पुत्राः कालकल्पाः प्रहारिणः |` | "The renowned sons of Kālā were like death [kālakalpa] in their striking power," |
| `Line 7466: भुवि ख्याता महावीर्या दानवेषु परन्तपाः ||३३||` | "Famous on earth for their great valor, scorchers of enemies [parantapa] among the Dānavas. ||33||" |
| `Line 7467: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7468: विनाशनश्च क्रोधश्च हन्ता क्रोधस्य चापरः |` | "Vināśana, Krodha, and another destroyer of anger [hantā krodhasya]," |
| `Line 7469: क्रोधशत्रुस्तथैवान्यः कालेया इति विश्रुताः ||३४||` | "And yet another named Krodhaśatru—these are known as the Kāleyas. ||34||" |
| `Line 7470: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7471: असुराणामुपाध्यायः शुक्रस्त्वृषिसुतोऽभवत् |` | "Śukra, the son of a sage [ṛṣisuta], became the preceptor of the Asuras," |
| `Line 7472: ख्याताश्चोशनसः पुत्राश्चत्वारोऽसुरयाजकाः ||३५||` | "And the four renowned sons of Uśanas became the priests [yājaka] of the Asuras. ||35||" |
| `Line 7473: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7474: त्वष्टावरस्तथात्रिश्च द्वावन्यौ मन्त्रकर्मिणौ |` | "Tvaṣṭāvara and Atri, and two others skilled in mantras [mantrakarmin]," |
| `Line 7475: तेजसा सूर्यसङ्काशा ब्रह्मलोकप्रभावनाः ||३६||` | "Radiant like the sun [sūryasaṅkāśa] and glorifying the world of Brahma [brahmaloka]. ||36||" |
| `Line 7476: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7477: इत्येष वंशप्रभवः कथितस्ते तरस्विनाम् |` | "Thus this lineage origin has been narrated to you of the mighty ones [tarasvinām]," |
| `Line 7478: असुराणां सुराणां च पुराणे संश्रुतो मया ||३७||` | "Of the Asuras [demons] and Suras [gods], as I have heard it in the Purāṇa [ancient text]. ||37||" |
| `Line 7479: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7480: एतेषां यदपत्यं तु न शक्यं तदशेषतः |` | "Their progeny, however, cannot be enumerated completely," |
| `Line 7481: प्रसङ्ख्यातुं महीपाल गुणभूतमनन्तकम् ||३८||` | "O protector of the earth [mahīpāla], for they are innumerable [anantakam] and manifold. ||38||" |
| `Line 7482: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7483: तार्क्ष्यश्चारिष्टनेमिश्च तथैव गरुडारुणौ |` | "Tārkṣya, Ariṣṭanemi, and likewise Garuḍa and Aruṇa," |
| `Line 7484: आरुणिर्वारुणिश्चैव वैनतेया इति स्मृताः ||३९||` | "Āruṇi and Vāruṇi - these are known as the sons of Vinatā [Vainateyās]. ||39||" |
| `Line 7485: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7486: शेषोऽनन्तो वासुकिश्च तक्षकश्च भुजङ्गमः |` | "Śeṣa, Ananta, Vāsuki, and Takṣaka the serpent [bhujaṅgama]," |
| `Line 7487: कूर्मश्च कुलिकश्चैव काद्रवेया महाबलाः ||४०||` | "And Kūrma and Kulika - these are the mighty sons of Kadrū [Kādraveyās]. ||40||" |
| `Line 7488: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7489: भीमसेनोग्रसेनौ च सुपर्णो वरुणस्तथा |` | "Bhīmasena, Ugrasena, Suparṇa, and Varuṇa as well," |
| `Line 7490: गोपतिर्धृतराष्ट्रश्च सूर्यवर्चाश्च सप्तमः ||४१||` | "Gopati, Dhṛtarāṣṭra, and Sūryavarcā as the seventh. ||41||" |
| `Line 7491: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7492: पत्रवानर्कपर्णश्च प्रयुतश्चैव विश्रुतः |` | "Patravān, Arkaparṇa, and the renowned Prayuta," |
| `Line 7493: भीमश्चित्ररथश्चैव विख्यातः सर्वविद्वशी ||४२||` | "Bhīma and Citraratha, the famous one who controls all [sarvavidvaśī]. ||42||" |
| `Line 7494: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7495: तथा शालिशिरा राजन्प्रद्युम्नश्च चतुर्दशः |` | "Also Śāliśira, O king [rājan], and Pradyumna as the fourteenth," |
| `Line 7496: कलिः पञ्चदशश्चैव नारदश्चैव षोडशः ||४३||` | "Kali is the fifteenth and Nārada is the sixteenth. ||43||" |
| `Line 7497: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7498: इत्येते देवगन्धर्वा मौनेयाः परिकीर्तिताः ||४३||` | "Thus these divine Gandharvas [celestial musicians], born of Muni [sage], have been enumerated. ||43||" |
| `Line 7499: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7500: अतस्तु भूतान्यन्यानि कीर्तयिष्यामि भारत |` | "Now, O Bhārata [Yudhiṣṭhira], I shall describe other beings," |
| `Line 7501: अनवद्यामनुवशामनूनामरुणां प्रियाम् ||४४||` | "Anavadyā, Anuvaśā, Anūnā, and Aruṇā the beloved. ||44||" |
| `Line 7502: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7503: अनूपां सुभगां भासीमिति प्रावा व्यजायत ||४४||` | "Anūpā, Subhagā, and Bhāsī - these were born to Pravā. ||44||" |
| `Line 7504: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7505: सिद्धः पूर्णश्च बर्ही च पूर्णाशश्च महायशाः |` | "Siddha, Pūrṇa, Barhi, and Pūrṇāśa of great fame," |
| `Line 7506: ब्रह्मचारी रतिगुणः सुपर्णश्चैव सप्तमः ||४५||` | "Brahmacārī [celibate], Ratiguṇa, and Suparṇa as the seventh. ||45||" |
| `Line 7507: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7508: विश्वावसुश्च भानुश्च सुचन्द्रो दशमस्तथा |` | "Viśvāvasu, Bhānu, and Sucandra as the tenth," |
| `Line 7509: इत्येते देवगन्धर्वाः प्रावेयाः परिकीर्तिताः ||४६||` | "Thus these divine Gandharvas [celestial musicians], born of Pravā, have been enumerated. ||46||" |
| `Line 7510: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7511: इमं त्वप्सरसां वंशं विदितं पुण्यलक्षणम् |` | "Now this lineage of Apsarās [celestial nymphs], known for auspicious characteristics," |
| `Line 7512: प्रावासूत महाभागा देवी देवर्षितः पुरा ||४७||` | "The blessed goddess Pravā bore them from the divine sage [devarṣi] in ancient times. ||47||" |
| `Line 7513: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7514: अलम्बुसा मिश्रकेषी विद्युत्पर्णा तुलानघा |` | "Alambuṣā, Miśrakeśī, Vidyutparṇā, Tulānaghā," |
| `Line 7515: अरुणा रक्षिता चैव रम्भा तद्वन्मनोरमा ||४८||` | "Aruṇā, Rakṣitā, and Rambhā, likewise Manoramā. ||48||" |
| `Line 7516: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7517: असिता च सुबाहुश्च सुव्रता सुभुजा तथा |` | "Asitā, Subāhu, Suvratā, and Subhujā as well," |
| `Line 7518: सुप्रिया चातिबाहुश्च विख्यातौ च हहाहुहू ||४९||` | "Supriyā, Atibāhu, and the two renowned ones, Hahā and Huhū. ||49||" |
| `Line 7519: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7520: तुम्बुरुश्चेति चत्वारः स्मृता गन्धर्वसत्तमाः ||४९||` | "And Tumburu—these four are remembered as the foremost among Gandharvas [celestial musicians]. ||49||" |
| `Line 7521: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7522: अमृतं ब्राह्मणा गावो गन्धर्वाप्सरसस्तथा |` | "The nectar [amṛta], the Brahmins [brāhmaṇa], the cows [gāvo], and the Gandharvas and Apsaras as well," |
| `Line 7523: अपत्यं कपिलायास्तु पुराणे परिकीर्तितम् ||५०||` | "Are declared in the Purāṇas [ancient texts] to be the offspring of Kapilā [divine cow]. ||50||" |
| `Line 7524: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7525: इति ते सर्वभूतानां सम्भवः कथितो मया |` | "Thus has the origin of all beings been narrated by me to you," |
| `Line 7526: यथावत्परिसङ्ख्यातो गन्धर्वाप्सरसां तथा ||५१||` | "Enumerated properly, including that of the Gandharvas and Apsaras. ||51||" |
| `Line 7527: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7528: भुजगानां सुपर्णानां रुद्राणां मरुतां तथा |` | "Of the serpents [bhujaga], of the Suparṇas [divine birds], of the Rudras [storm deities], of the Maruts [wind gods] as well," |
| `Line 7529: गवां च ब्राह्मणानां च श्रीमतां पुण्यकर्मणाम् ||५२||` | "Of the cows and of the Brahmins, who are illustrious and of virtuous deeds. ||52||" |
| `Line 7530: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7531: आयुष्यश्चैव पुण्यश्च धन्यः श्रुतिसुखावहः |` | "This account is life-extending, meritorious, blessed, and brings pleasure when heard," |
| `Line 7532: श्रोतव्यश्चैव सततं श्राव्यश्चैवानसूयता ||५३||` | "It should be listened to constantly and should be recited without malice. ||53||" |
| `Line 7533: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7534: इमं तु वंशं नियमेन यः पठे; न्महात्मनां ब्राह्मणदेवसंनिधौ |` | "Whoever regularly recites this genealogy [vaṃśa] in the presence of great souls, Brahmins, and deities," |
| `Line 7535: अपत्यलाभं लभते स पुष्कलं; श्रियं यशः प्रेत्य च शोभनां गतिम् ||५४||` | "Obtains abundant offspring, prosperity, fame, and after death, an auspicious destination. ||54||" |

| `Line 7544: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7545: वैशम्पायन उवाच||` | "Vaiśampāyana said:" |
| `Line 7546: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7547: ब्रह्मणो मानसाः पुत्रा विदिताः षण्महर्षयः |` | "The six great sages [maharṣis] are known as the mind-born [mānasa] sons of Brahmā," |
| `Line 7548: एकादश सुताः स्थाणोः ख्याताः परममानसाः ||१||` | "And the eleven sons of Sthāṇu [Śiva] are renowned as supremely spiritual beings [paramamānasa]. ||1||" |
| `Line 7549: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7550: मृगव्याधश्च शर्वश्च निरृतिश्च महायशाः |` | "Mṛgavyādha, Śarva, and the greatly renowned Nirṛti," |
| `Line 7551: अजैकपादहिर्बुध्न्यः पिनाकी च परन्तपः ||२||` | "Ajaikapāda, Ahirbudhnya, and Pināki the scorcher of enemies [parantapa]. ||2||" |
| `Line 7552: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7553: दहनोऽथेश्वरश्चैव कपाली च महाद्युतिः |` | "Dahana, then Īśvara, and Kapālī of great splendor [mahādyuti]," |
| `Line 7554: स्थाणुर्भवश्च भगवान्रुद्रा एकादश स्मृताः ||३||` | "Sthāṇu and the divine Bhava—these are remembered as the eleven Rudras [Śiva forms]. ||3||" |
| `Line 7555: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7556: मरीचिरङ्गिरा अत्रिः पुलस्त्यः पुलहः क्रतुः |` | "Marīci, Aṅgirā, Atri, Pulastya, Pulaha, and Kratu," |
| `Line 7557: षडेते ब्रह्मणः पुत्रा वीर्यवन्तो महर्षयः ||४||` | "These six are Brahmā's sons, powerful great sages [maharṣis]. ||4||" |
| `Line 7558: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7559: त्रयस्त्वङ्गिरसः पुत्रा लोके सर्वत्र विश्रुताः |` | "Three sons of Aṅgiras are renowned throughout the world," |
| `Line 7560: बृहस्पतिरुतथ्यश्च संवर्तश्च धृतव्रताः ||५||` | "Bṛhaspati, Utathya, and Saṃvarta, all firm in their vows [dhṛtavratāḥ]. ||5||" |
| `Line 7561: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7562: अत्रेस्तु बहवः पुत्राः श्रूयन्ते मनुजाधिप |` | "Many sons of Atri are known, O ruler of men [manujādhipa]," |
| `Line 7563: सर्वे वेदविदः सिद्धाः शान्तात्मानो महर्षयः ||६||` | "All knowers of the Vedas [vedavidaḥ], accomplished ones [siddhāḥ], peaceful-souled great sages. ||6||" |
| `Line 7564: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7565: राक्षसास्तु पुलस्त्यस्य वानराः किंनरास्तथा |` | "The Rākṣasas [demons] belong to Pulastya, as well as monkeys [vānarāḥ] and Kiṃnaras [half-human beings]," |
| `Line 7566: पुलहस्य मृगाः सिंहा व्याघ्राः किम्पुरुषास्तथा ||७||` | "To Pulaha belong deer, lions, tigers, and Kimpuruṣas [horse-headed beings] as well. ||7||" |
| `Line 7567: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7568: क्रतोः क्रतुसमाः पुत्राः पतङ्गसहचारिणः |` | "Kratu's sons are like sacrifices [kratu-samāḥ], companions of the sun [pataṅga]," |
| `Line 7569: विश्रुतास्त्रिषु लोकेषु सत्यव्रतपरायणाः ||८||` | "Famous in the three worlds, devoted to truthful vows [satyavrata-parāyaṇāḥ]. ||8||" |
| `Line 7570: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7571: दक्षस्त्वजायताङ्गुष्ठाद्दक्षिणाद्भगवानृषिः |` | "The venerable sage Dakṣa was born from the right thumb [dakṣiṇād aṅguṣṭhād]," |
| `Line 7572: ब्रह्मणः पृथिवीपाल पुत्रः पुत्रवतां वरः ||९||` | "Of Brahmā, O protector of the earth [pṛthivīpāla], a son foremost among those having sons. ||9||" |
| `Line 7573: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7574: वामादजायताङ्गुष्ठाद्भार्या तस्य महात्मनः |` | "From the left thumb [vāmād aṅguṣṭhād] was born the wife of that great-souled one," |
| `Line 7575: तस्यां पञ्चाशतं कन्याः स एवाजनयन्मुनिः ||१०||` | "In her, that sage himself begot fifty daughters. ||10||" |
| `Line 7576: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7577: ताः सर्वास्त्वनवद्याङ्ग्यः कन्याः कमललोचनाः |` | "All those maidens with flawless limbs [anavadyāṅgyaḥ] and lotus-like eyes [kamala-locanāḥ]," |
| `Line 7578: पुत्रिकाः स्थापयामास नष्टपुत्रः प्रजापतिः ||११||` | "The Prajāpati [creation lord], having lost his sons, established as his daughters [putrikāḥ]. ||11||" |
| `Line 7579: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7580: ददौ स दश धर्माय सप्तविंशतिमिन्दवे |` | "He gave ten to Dharma and twenty-seven to Indu [Moon god]," |
| `Line 7581: दिव्येन विधिना राजन्कश्यपाय त्रयोदश ||१२||` | "And thirteen to Kaśyapa through divine arrangement, O King [rājan]. ||12||" |
| `Line 7582: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7583: नामतो धर्मपत्न्यस्ताः कीर्त्यमाना निबोध मे |` | "Learn from me the names of Dharma's wives as I enumerate them:" |
| `Line 7584: कीर्तिर्लक्ष्मीर्धृतिर्मेधा पुष्टिः श्रद्धा क्रिया तथा ||१३||` | "Kīrti [Fame], Lakṣmī [Fortune], Dhṛti [Steadfastness], Medhā [Intelligence], Puṣṭi [Nourishment], Śraddhā [Faith], and Kriyā [Ritual action] as well. ||13||" |
| `Line 7585: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7586: बुद्धिर्लज्जा मतिश्चैव पत्न्यो धर्मस्य ता दश |` | "Buddhi [Intellect], Lajjā [Modesty], and Mati [Thought] - these are the ten wives of Dharma," |
| `Line 7587: द्वाराण्येतानि धर्मस्य विहितानि स्वयम्भुवा ||१४||` | "These are the portals [dvārāṇi] of Dharma established by Svayambhū [Self-born one]. ||14||" |
| `Line 7588: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7589: सप्तविंशति सोमस्य पत्न्यो लोके परिश्रुताः |` | "The twenty-seven wives of Soma [Moon god] are renowned in the world," |
| `Line 7590: कालस्य नयने युक्ताः सोमपत्न्यः शुभव्रताः ||१५||` | "The wives of Soma, of auspicious vows [śubha-vratāḥ], are engaged in guiding time [kāla]. ||15||" |
| `Line 7591: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7592: सर्वा नक्षत्रयोगिन्यो लोकयात्राविधौ स्थिताः ||१५||` | "All are connected with the constellations [nakṣatra-yoginyaḥ], established in the regulation of worldly affairs. ||15||" |
| `Line 7593: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7594: पितामहो मुनिर्देवस्तस्य पुत्रः प्रजापतिः |` | "The Pitāmaha [Grandfather, Brahmā] is the divine sage, his son is Prajāpati [creation lord]," |
| `Line 7595: तस्याष्टौ वसवः पुत्रास्तेषां वक्ष्यामि विस्तरम् ||१६||` | "His eight sons are the Vasus [elemental deities]; I shall describe them in detail. ||16||" |
| `Line 7596: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7597: धरो ध्रुवश्च सोमश्च अहश्चैवानिलोऽनलः |` | "Dhara [earth-bearer], Dhruva [steadfast one], Soma [moon deity], Aha [day], and also Anila [wind] and Anala [fire]," |
| `Line 7598: प्रत्यूषश्च प्रभासश्च वसवोऽष्टाविति स्मृताः ||१७||` | "Pratyūṣa [dawn] and Prabhāsa [radiance] - these are remembered as the eight Vasus [divine beings]. ||17||" |
| `Line 7599: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7600: धूम्रायाश्च धरः पुत्रो ब्रह्मविद्यो ध्रुवस्तथा |` | "Dhara is the son of Dhūmrā [smoke-colored], and similarly Dhruva is (the son) of Brahmavidyā [Vedic knowledge]," |
| `Line 7601: चन्द्रमास्तु मनस्विन्याः श्वसायाः श्वसनस्तथा ||१८||` | "Chandramās [moon] is (the son) of Manasvinī [thoughtful one], and similarly Śvasana [breath] is (the son) of Śvasā. ||18||" |
| `Line 7602: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7603: रतायाश्चाप्यहः पुत्रः शाण्डिल्याश्च हुताशनः |` | "Aha [day] is the son of Ratā [beloved], and Hutāśana [fire-consumer] is (the son) of Śāṇḍilyā," |
| `Line 7604: प्रत्यूषश्च प्रभासश्च प्रभातायाः सुतौ स्मृतौ ||१९||` | "Pratyūṣa and Prabhāsa are remembered as the two sons of Prabhātā [dawn]. ||19||" |
| `Line 7605: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7606: धरस्य पुत्रो द्रविणो हुतहव्यवहस्तथा |` | "Dhara's son is Draviṇa, and also Hutahavyavaha [fire-offering carrier]," |
| `Line 7607: ध्रुवस्य पुत्रो भगवान्कालो लोकप्रकालनः ||२०||` | "Dhruva's son is the illustrious Kāla [Time deity], the illuminator of worlds. ||20||" |
| `Line 7608: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7609: सोमस्य तु सुतो वर्चा वर्चस्वी येन जायते |` | "Soma's [Moon god] son is Varchā, through whom one becomes radiant [varchasvī]," |
| `Line 7610: मनोहरायाः शिशिरः प्राणोऽथ रमणस्तथा ||२१||` | "From Manoharā [mind-captivating goddess] were born Śiśira [cool season], Prāṇa [life-breath], and Ramaṇa [delighter]. ||21||" |
| `Line 7611: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7612: अह्नः सुतो स्मृतो ज्योतिः श्रमः शान्तस्तथा मुनिः |` | "The son of Ahan [Day] is remembered as Jyotis [light], Śrama [exertion], Śānta [peace], and Muni [sage]," |
| `Line 7613: अग्नेः पुत्रः कुमारस्तु श्रीमाञ्शरवणालयः ||२२||` | "Agni's [fire god] son is Kumāra [youth-deity], the illustrious one who dwells in reed-beds [Śaravaṇālaya]. ||22||" |
| `Line 7614: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7615: तस्य शाखो विशाखश्च नैगमेशश्च पृष्ठजः |` | "His (Kumāra's) sons are Śākha, Viśākha, Naigameśa, and Pṛṣṭhaja [born from the back]," |
| `Line 7616: कृत्तिकाभ्युपपत्तेश्च कार्त्तिकेय इति स्मृतः ||२३||` | "And due to his association with the Kṛttikās [Pleiades stars], he is remembered as Kārttikeya [son of Kṛttikās]. ||23||" |
| `Line 7617: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7618: अनिलस्य शिवा भार्या तस्याः पुत्रः पुरोजवः |` | "Anila's [wind god] wife is Śivā, and her son is Purojava [swift-moving]," |
| `Line 7619: अविज्ञातगतिश्चैव द्वौ पुत्रावनिलस्य तु ||२४||` | "And Avijñātagati [of unknown course] - these two are the sons of Anila. ||24||" |
| `Line 7620: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7621: प्रत्यूषस्य विदुः पुत्रमृषिं नाम्नाथ देवलम् |` | "They know Pratyūṣa's [dawn] son as the sage named Devala [divine one]," |
| `Line 7622: द्वौ पुत्रौ देवलस्यापि क्षमावन्तौ मनीषिणौ ||२५||` | "And Devala also has two sons, both patient and wise. ||25||" |
| `Line 7623: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7624: बृहस्पतेस्तु भगिनी वरस्त्री ब्रह्मचारिणी |` | "Bṛhaspati's [preceptor of gods] sister is an excellent woman, a celibate [brahmacharini]," |
| `Line 7625: योगसिद्धा जगत्सर्वमसक्तं विचरत्युत ||२६||` | "Accomplished in yoga, she wanders throughout the entire world, unattached. ||26||" |
| `Line 7626: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7627: प्रभासस्य तु भार्या सा वसूनामष्टमस्य ह ॥२६॥` | "She was the wife of Prabhāsa [radiance deity], the eighth of the Vasus [divine beings]. ||26||" |
| `Line 7628: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7629: विश्वकर्मा महाभागो जज्ञे शिल्पप्रजापतिः |` | "Viśvakarmā [universal architect], the greatly fortunate one, was born as the lord of crafts [śilpa-prajāpati]," |
| `Line 7630: कर्ता शिल्पसहस्राणां त्रिदशानां च वर्धकिः ॥२७॥` | "The creator of thousands of crafts and the carpenter of the thirty [tridaśa] gods. ||27||" |
| `Line 7631: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7632: भूषणानां च सर्वेषां कर्ता शिल्पवतां वरः |` | "The maker of all ornaments and the best among craftsmen," |
| `Line 7633: यो दिव्यानि विमानानि देवतानां चकार ह ॥२८॥` | "Who created the divine aerial chariots [vimāna] for the deities. ||28||" |
| `Line 7634: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7635: मनुष्याश्चोपजीवन्ति यस्य शिल्पं महात्मनः |` | "And humans subsist upon the craftsmanship of that great-souled one [mahātman]," |
| `Line 7636: पूजयन्ति च यं नित्यं विश्वकर्माणमव्ययम् ||२९||` | "And whom they worship daily as Viśvakarmā [universal architect], the imperishable one. ||29||" |
| `Line 7637: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7638: स्तनं तु दक्षिणं भित्त्वा ब्रह्मणो नरविग्रहः |` | "Breaking through the right breast of Brahmā [creator deity], in human form," |
| `Line 7639: निःसृतो भगवान्धर्मः सर्वलोकसुखावहः ||३०||` | "Emerged the illustrious Dharma [righteousness], who brings happiness to all worlds. ||30||" |
| `Line 7640: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7641: त्रयस्तस्य वराः पुत्राः सर्वभूतमनोहराः |` | "He has three excellent sons who captivate the minds of all beings:" |
| `Line 7642: शमः कामश्च हर्षश्च तेजसा लोकधारिणः ||३१||` | "Śama [tranquility], Kāma [desire], and Harṣa [joy], who sustain the worlds with their splendor. ||31||" |
| `Line 7643: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7644: कामस्य तु रतिर्भार्या शमस्य प्राप्तिरङ्गना |` | "Kāma's wife is Rati [pleasure], Śama's wife is Prāpti [attainment]," |
| `Line 7645: नन्दी तु भार्या हर्षस्य यत्र लोकाः प्रतिष्ठिताः ||३२||` | "And Harṣa's wife is Nandī [delight], in whom the worlds are established. ||32||" |
| `Line 7646: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7647: मरीचेः कश्यपः पुत्रः कश्यपस्य सुरासुराः |` | "From Marīchi [light-ray sage] was born Kaśyapa, and from Kaśyapa were born the Suras [gods] and Asuras [demons]," |
| `Line 7648: जज्ञिरे नृपशार्दूल लोकानां प्रभवस्तु सः ||३३||` | "They were born, O tiger among kings [nṛpaśārdūla], and he (Kaśyapa) is the progenitor of the worlds. ||33||" |
| `Line 7649: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7650: त्वाष्ट्री तु सवितुर्भार्या वडवारूपधारिणी |` | "Tvāṣṭrī [daughter of Tvaṣṭṛ], the wife of Savitṛ [sun deity], who took the form of a mare [vaḍavā]," |
| `Line 7651: असूयत महाभागा सान्तरिक्षेऽश्विनावुभौ ||३४||` | "The blessed one [mahābhāgā] gave birth to both the Aśvins [divine physicians] in the sky [antarikṣa]. ||34||" |
| `Line 7652: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7653: द्वादशैवादितेः पुत्राः शक्रमुख्या नराधिप |` | "Aditi [boundless goddess] had twelve sons with Śakra [Indra] as their chief, O lord of men [narādhipa]," |
| `Line 7654: तेषामवरजो विष्णुर्यत्र लोकाः प्रतिष्ठिताः ||३५||` | "Among them, the youngest is Viṣṇu [all-pervader], in whom the worlds are established. ||35||" |
| `Line 7655: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7656: त्रयस्त्रिंशत इत्येते देवास्तेषामहं तव |` | "These are the thirty-three gods, and I shall now tell you" |
| `Line 7657: अन्वयं सम्प्रवक्ष्यामि पक्षैश्च कुलतो गणान् ||३६||` | "their lineage, along with their groups classified by families and divisions. ||36||" |
| `Line 7658: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7659: रुद्राणामपरः पक्षः साध्यानां मरुतां तथा |` | "Another division consists of the Rudras [storm deities], the Sādhyas [celestial beings], and the Maruts [wind-gods]," |
| `Line 7660: वसूनां भार्गवं विद्याद्विश्वेदेवांस्तथैव च ||३७||` | "Know the Bhārgava [Bhṛgu's lineage] to be of the Vasus, and likewise the Viśvedevas [universal gods]. ||37||" |
| `Line 7661: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7662: वैनतेयस्तु गरुडो बलवानरुणस्तथा |` | "Garuḍa, the son of Vinatā [Vainateya], the mighty one, and also Aruṇa," |
| `Line 7663: बृहस्पतिश्च भगवानादित्येष्वेव गण्यते ||३८||` | "And the illustrious Bṛhaspati [preceptor of gods] are counted among the Ādityas [solar deities]. ||38||" |
| `Line 7664: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7665: अश्विभ्यां गुह्यकान्विद्धि सर्वौषध्यस्तथा पशून् |` | "Know the Guhyakas [hidden beings] to be from the Aśvins [divine twins], as well as all medicinal herbs and animals." |
| `Line 7666: एष देवगणो राजन्कीर्तितस्तेऽनुपूर्वशः ||३९||` | "Thus, O King, the host of deities has been described to you in proper sequence. ||39||" |
| `Line 7667: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7668: यं कीर्तयित्वा मनुजः सर्वपापैः प्रमुच्यते ||३९||` | "By reciting which [this divine genealogy], a human being becomes freed from all sins. ||39||" |
| `Line 7669: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7670: ब्रह्मणो हृदयं भित्त्वा निःसृतो भगवान्भृगुः |` | "The illustrious Bhṛgu [sage-progenitor] emerged by piercing through the heart of Brahmā [creator deity]," |
| `Line 7671: भृगोः पुत्रः कविर्विद्वाञ्शुक्रः कविसुतो ग्रहः ||४०||` | "Bhṛgu's son was the wise Kavi, and Śukra [Venus deity], the planet, was Kavi's son. ||40||" |
| `Line 7672: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7673: त्रैलोक्यप्राणयात्रार्थे वर्षावर्षे भयाभये |` | "For the sustenance of the three worlds [triloka], in rain and drought, in fear and safety," |
| `Line 7674: स्वयम्भुवा नियुक्तः सन्भुवनं परिधावति ||४१||` | "Being appointed by Svayambhuva [self-born Brahmā], he revolves around the world. ||41||" |
| `Line 7675: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7676: योगाचार्यो महाबुद्धिर्दैत्यानामभवद्गुरुः |` | "He became the Yogācārya [yoga teacher], of great intellect, and the guru of the Daityas [demon clan]," |
| `Line 7677: सुराणां चापि मेधावी ब्रह्मचारी यतव्रतः ||४२||` | "And also for the Surās [gods], he was wise, celibate, and of controlled vows. ||42||" |
| `Line 7678: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7679: तस्मिन्नियुक्ते विभुना योगक्षेमाय भार्गवे |` | "When that Bhārgava [Śukra] was appointed by the Lord [Vibhu] for the welfare of all," |
| `Line 7680: अन्यमुत्पादयामास पुत्रं भृगुरनिन्दितम् ||४३||` | "Bhṛgu produced another blameless son. ||43||" |
| `Line 7681: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7682: च्यवनं दीप्ततपसं धर्मात्मानं मनीषिणम् |` | "Chyavana, of blazing austerities, righteous soul, and wise," |
| `Line 7683: यः स रोषाच्च्युतो गर्भान्मातुर्मोक्षाय भारत ||४४||` | "Who fell [chyuta] from the womb due to anger, for the liberation of his mother, O Bhārata [Yudhiṣṭhira]. ||44||" |
| `Line 7684: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7685: आरुषी तु मनोः कन्या तस्य पत्नी मनीषिणः |` | "Āruṣī, the daughter of Manu, was the wife of that wise one [Chyavana]," |
| `Line 7686: और्वस्तस्यां समभवदूरुं भित्त्वा महायशाः ||४५||` | "Aurva [great sage] of great fame was born from her, breaking through the thigh [ūru]. ||45||" |
| `Line 7687: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7688: महातपा महातेजा बाल एव गुणैर्युतः ||४५||` | "He was of great austerity [mahātapā], great splendor [mahātejā], endowed with virtues even as a child. ||45||" |
| `Line 7689: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7690: ऋचीकस्तस्य पुत्रस्तु जमदग्निस्ततोऽभवत् |` | "Ṛcīka was his son, and from him was born Jamadagni," |
| `Line 7691: जमदग्नेस्तु चत्वार आसन्पुत्रा महात्मनः ||४६||` | "And to Jamadagni, the great-souled one [mahātman], were born four sons. ||46||" |
| `Line 7692: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7693: रामस्तेषां जघन्योऽभूदजघन्यैर्गुणैर्युतः |` | "Rāma [Paraśurāma] was the youngest among them, yet endowed with qualities that were not inferior," |
| `Line 7694: सर्वशस्त्रास्त्रकुशलः क्षत्रियान्तकरो वशी ||४७||` | "Skilled in all weapons [śastra] and missiles [astra], the destroyer of Kṣatriyas, and self-controlled. ||47||" |
| `Line 7695: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7696: और्वस्यासीत्पुत्रशतं जमदग्निपुरोगमम् |` | "Aurva [sage descendant of Bhṛgu] had a hundred sons with Jamadagni [famous sage] as the foremost," |
| `Line 7697: तेषां पुत्रसहस्राणि बभूवुर्भृगुविस्तरः ||४८||` | "They had thousands of sons, thus expanding the Bhṛgu [sage lineage] family. ||48||" |
| `Line 7698: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7699: द्वौ पुत्रौ ब्रह्मणस्त्वन्यौ ययोस्तिष्ठति लक्षणम् |` | "There are two other sons of Brahmā [creator deity], whose characteristics remain," |
| `Line 7700: लोके धाता विधाता च यौ स्थितौ मनुना सह ||४९||` | "In the world they are Dhātā [establisher] and Vidhātā [ordainer], who remain with Manu [progenitor of mankind]. ||49||" |
| `Line 7701: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7702: तयोरेव स्वसा देवी लक्ष्मीः पद्मगृहा शुभा |` | "Their sister is the auspicious goddess Lakṣmī [prosperity deity], who dwells in the lotus [padmagṛhā]," |
| `Line 7703: तस्यास्तु मानसाः पुत्रास्तुरगा व्योमचारिणः ||५०||` | "Her mind-born [mānasa] sons are the horses [turaga] that move through the sky [vyomacāriṇaḥ]. ||50||" |
| `Line 7704: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7705: वरुणस्य भार्या ज्येष्ठा तु शुक्राद्देवी व्यजायत |` | "Varuṇa's [water deity] eldest wife, the goddess, was born from Śukra [Venus deity]," |
| `Line 7706: तस्याः पुत्रं बलं विद्धि सुरां च सुरनन्दिनीम् ||५१||` | "Know her son to be Bala [strength personified], and Surā [liquor goddess], the delighter of gods [Suranandini]. ||51||" |
| `Line 7707: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7708: प्रजानामन्नकामानामन्योन्यपरिभक्षणात् |` | "From the mutual devouring of creatures desiring food," |
| `Line 7709: अधर्मस्तत्र सञ्जातः सर्वभूतविनाशनः ||५२||` | "Adharma [unrighteousness] was born there, the destroyer of all beings. ||52||" |
| `Line 7710: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7711: तस्यापि निरृतिर्भार्या नैरृता येन राक्षसाः |` | "His wife is Nirṛti [destruction], from whom came the Nairṛtas [destructive beings], the Rākṣasas [demons]," |
| `Line 7712: घोरास्तस्यास्त्रयः पुत्राः पापकर्मरताः सदा ||५३||` | "She has three terrible sons, always engaged in sinful acts. ||53||" |
| `Line 7713: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7714: भयो महाभयश्चैव मृत्युर्भूतान्तकस्तथा ||५३||` | "Bhaya [fear], Mahābhaya [great fear], and Mṛtyu [death], the ender of beings [Bhūtāntaka]. ||53||" |
| `Line 7715: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7716: काकीं श्येनीं च भासीं च धृतराष्ट्रीं तथा शुकीम् |` | "Kākī [crow-mother], Śyenī [hawk-mother], Bhāsī [light-bird], Dhṛtarāṣṭrī [goose-mother], and also Śukī [parrot-mother]," |
| `Line 7717: ताम्रा तु सुषुवे देवी पञ्चैता लोकविश्रुताः ||५४||` | "These five world-renowned ones were born to the goddess Tāmrā [copper-colored]. ||54||" |
| `Line 7718: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7719: उलूकान्सुषुवे काकी श्येनी श्येनान्व्यजायत |` | "Kākī gave birth to owls [ulūka], Śyenī produced hawks [śyena]," |
| `Line 7720: भासी भासानजनयद्गृध्रांश्चैव जनाधिप ||५५||` | "Bhāsī generated vultures [gṛdhra] and Bhāsa birds, O ruler of people [janādhipa]. ||55||" |
| `Line 7721: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7722: धृतराष्ट्री तु हंसांश्च कलहंसांश्च सर्वशः |` | "Dhṛtarāṣṭrī gave birth to swans [haṃsa] and all types of flamingos [kalahaṃsa]," |
| `Line 7723: चक्रवाकांश्च भद्रं ते प्रजज्ञे सा तु भामिनी ||५६||` | "And that radiant lady [bhāminī] bore chakravāka birds [ruddy geese] as well, may good fortune be yours. ||56||" |
| `Line 7724: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7725: शुकी विजज्ञे धर्मज्ञ शुकानेव मनस्विनी |` | "The thoughtful [manasvinī] Śukī gave birth to parrots [śuka] only, O knower of dharma [dharmajña]," |
| `Line 7726: कल्याणगुणसम्पन्ना सर्वलक्षणपूजिता ||५७||` | "Endowed with auspicious qualities and honored with all favorable marks. ||57||" |
| `Line 7727: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7728: नव क्रोधवशा नारीः प्रजज्ञेऽप्यात्मसम्भवाः |` | "Nine women born of anger [krodhavaśā] were produced from his own self," |
| `Line 7729: मृगीं च मृगमन्दां च हरिं भद्रमनामपि ||५८||` | "Mṛgī [doe], Mṛgamandā [deer-like], Hari [tawny], and also Bhadramanā [auspicious-minded]. ||58||" |
| `Line 7730: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7731: मातङ्गीमथ शार्दूलीं श्वेतां सुरभिमेव च |` | "Mātaṅgī [elephant-woman], then Śārdūlī [tigress], Śvetā [white one], and Surabhi [fragrant] as well," |
| `Line 7732: सर्वलक्षणसम्पन्नां सुरसां च यशस्विनीम् ||५९||` | "And Surasā [well-flavored], endowed with all auspicious marks and glorious. ||59||" |
| `Line 7733: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7734: अपत्यं तु मृगाः सर्वे मृग्या नरवरात्मज |` | "O son of the best of men [naravaratmaja], all deer are the offspring of Mṛgī," |
| `Line 7735: ऋक्षाश्च मृगमन्दायाः सृमराश्चमरा अपि ||६०||` | "And bears, as well as yaks [sṛmara] and chamaras [bushy-tailed], are the offspring of Mṛgamandā. ||60||" |
| `Line 7736: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7737: ततस्त्वैरावतं नागं जज्ञे भद्रमना सुतम् |` | "Then Bhadramanā [auspicious-minded] gave birth to the elephant Airāvata [cloud-born] as her son," |
| `Line 7738: ऐरावतः सुतस्तस्या देवनागो महागजः ||६१||` | "Airāvata, her son, is the divine elephant [deva-nāga], the great tusker. ||61||" |
| `Line 7739: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7740: हर्याश्च हरयोऽपत्यं वानराश्च तरस्विनः |` | "The offspring of Haryā [tawny one] are the Harayas [tawny beings] and the energetic monkeys [vānaras]," |
| `Line 7741: गोलाङ्गूलांश्च भद्रं ते हर्याः पुत्रान्प्रचक्षते ||६२||` | "And the Golāṅgūlas [cow-tailed monkeys], blessings to you, are declared to be the sons of Haryā. ||62||" |
| `Line 7742: ` | "[Blank line]" |
| `Line 7743: प्रजज्ञे त्वथ शार्दूली सिंहान्व्याघ्रांश्च भारत |` | "And then, O Bhārata [descendant of Bharata], Śārdūlī [tigress] gave birth to lions and tigers," |
| `Line 7744: द्वीपिनश्च महाभाग सर्वानेव न संशयः ||६३||` | "And leopards [dvīpins] as well, O fortunate one [mahābhāga], indeed all of them, without doubt. ||63||" |
